athāyuṣmān pūrṇastasyā eva rātreratyayāt pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya śrāvastīṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat | [Divyāv, 2 389]
śrāvastīṃ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyaḥ paścādbhaktapiṇḍapātraḥ pratikrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 390]
yathāparibhuktaśayanāsanaṃ pratisamayya samādāya pātracīvaram yena śroṇāparāntakā janapadāstena cārikāṃ carañ śroṇāparāntakāñ janapadānanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 391]
athāyuṣmān pūrṇaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya śroṇāparāntakaṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat | [Divyāv, 2 392]
anyatamaśca lubdhako dhanuṣpāṇirmṛgayāṃ nirgacchati | [Divyāv, 2 393]
tena dṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 394]
sa saṃlakṣayati amaṅgalo 'yaṃ muṇḍakaḥ śramaṇako mayā dṛṣṭa iti viditvā ā karṇād dhanuḥ pūrayitvā yenāyuṣmān pūrṇastena pradhāvitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 395]
sa āyuṣmatā pūrṇena dṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 396]
dṛṣṭvā cottarāsaṅgaṃ vivartya kathayati bhadramukha asya duṣpūrasyārthe praviśāmi atra prahareti | [Divyāv, 2 397]
gāthāṃ ca bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 2 398]
yasyārthe gahane caranti vihagā gacchanti bandhaṃ mṛgāḥ saṃgrāme śaraśaktitomaradharā naśyantyajasraṃ narāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 399.1]
dīnā durdinacāriṇaśca kṛpaṇā matsyā grasantyāyasam asyārthe udarasya pāpakalile dūrādihābhyāgataḥ iti | [Divyāv, 2 399.2]
sa saṃlakṣayati ayaṃ pravrajita īdṛśena kṣāntisaurabhyena samanvāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 400]
kimasya praharāmīti matvā abhiprasannaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 401]
tato 'syāyuṣmatā pūrṇena dharmo deśitaḥ śaraṇagamanaśikṣāpadeśeṣu ca pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 402]
anyāni ca pañcopāsakaśatāni kṛtāni pañcopāsikāśatāni | [Divyāv, 2 403]
pañcavihāraśatāni kāritāni anekāni ca mañcapīṭhavṛṣikoccakabimbopadhānacaturasrakaśatāni anupradāpitāni | [Divyāv, 2 404]
tasyaiva ca trimāsasyātyayāt tisro vidyāḥ kāyena sākṣātkṛtāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 405]
arhan saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 406]
traidhātukavītarāgo yāvat sendropendrāṇāṃ devānāṃ pūjyo mānyo 'bhivādyaśca saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 407]
yāvadapareṇa samayena dārukarṇibhrātrorbhogāstanutvaṃ parikṣayaṃ paryādānaṃ gatāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 408]
tau kathayataḥ gato 'sau asmākaṃ gṛhāt kālakarṇiprakhyaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 409]
āgaccha ekadhye prativasāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 410]
sa kathayati kataro 'sau kālakarṇiprakhyaḥ tau kathayataḥ pūrṇakaśrīḥ | [Divyāv, 2 411]
sā mama gṛhānniṣkrāntā | [Divyāv, 2 412]
nāsau kālakarṇiprakhyaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 413]
tau kathayataḥ śrīrvā bhavatu kālakarṇī vā āgaccha ekadhye prativasāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 414]
sa kathayati yuvayoranyāyopārjitaṃ dhanam mama nyāyopārjitam | [Divyāv, 2 415]
nāham yuvābhyāṃ sārdhamekadhye vāsaṃ kalpayāmīti | [Divyāv, 2 416]
tau kathayataḥ tena dāsīputreṇa mahāsamudramavatīryāvatīrya bhogāḥ samudānītā yena tvaṃ bhuñjāno vikatthase | [Divyāv, 2 417]
kutastava sāmarthyaṃ mahāsamudramavatartumiti | [Divyāv, 2 418]
sa tābhyāṃ mānaṃ grāhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 419]
sa saṃlakṣayati ahamapi mahāsamudramavatarāmi | [Divyāv, 2 420]
pūrvavat yāvanmahāsamudramavatīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 421]
yāvattadvahanaṃ vāyunā gośīrṣacandanavanam anupreritam | [Divyāv, 2 422]
karṇadhāraḥ kathayati bhavantaḥ yattat śrūyate gośīrṣacandanavanamiti idaṃ tat | [Divyāv, 2 423]
gṛhṇantu atra yatsāramiti | [Divyāv, 2 424]
tena khalu samayena gośīrṣacandanavanaṃ maheśvarasya yakṣasya parigraho 'bhūt | [Divyāv, 2 425]
sa ca yakṣāṇām yakṣasamitiṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 426]
tato gośīrṣacandanavane pañcamātrāṇi kuṭhāraśatāni voḍhumārabdhāni | [Divyāv, 2 427]
adrākṣīdapriyākhyo yo yakṣo gośīrṣacandanavane pañcamātrāṇi kuṭhāraśatāni vahataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 428]
dṛṣṭvā ca yena maheśvaro yakṣaḥ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 429]
upasaṃkramya maheśvaram yakṣamidamavocat yat khalu grāmaṇīrjānīyā gośīrṣacandanavane pañcamātrāṇi kuṭhāraśatāni vahanti | [Divyāv, 2 430]
yatte kṛtyaṃ vā karaṇīyaṃ vā tatkuruṣveti | [Divyāv, 2 431]
atha maheśvaro yakṣo yakṣāṇāṃ samitimasamitiṃ kṛtvā saṃjātāmarṣo mahāntaṃ kālikāvātabhayaṃ saṃjanya yena gośīrṣacandanavanaṃ tena samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 432]
karṇadhāreṇārocitam śṛṇvantu bhavanto jāmbudvīpakā vaṇijaḥ yattat śrūyate mahākālikāvātabhayamiti idaṃ tat | [Divyāv, 2 433]
kiṃ manyadhvamiti tataste vaṇijo bhītāstrastāḥ saṃvignā āhṛṣṭaromakūpā devatāyācanaṃ kartumārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 434]
śivavaruṇakuberaśakrabrahmādyāsuramanujoragayakṣadānavendrāḥ vyasanamatibhayaṃ vayaṃ prapannā vigatabhayā hi bhavantu no 'dya nāthāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 435]
kecinnamasyanti śacīpatiṃ narā brahmāṇamanye hariśaṃkarāvapi | [Divyāv, 2 436]
bhūmyāśritān vṛkṣavanāśritāṃśca trāṇārthino vātapiśācadasthāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 437]
dārukarṇī alpotsukastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 2 438]
vaṇijaḥ kathayanti sārthavāha vayaṃ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhaprāptāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 439]
kimarthamalpotsukastiṣṭhasīti sa kathayati bhavantaḥ ahaṃ bhrātrā abhihitaḥ mahāsamudro 'lpāsvādo bahvādīnavaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 440]
tṛṣṇāndhā bahavo 'vataranti svalpā vyutthāsyanti | [Divyāv, 2 441]
na tvayā kenacit prakāreṇa mahāsamudramavatartavyamiti | [Divyāv, 2 442]
so 'haṃ tasya vacanamavacanaṃ kṛtvā mahāsamudramavatīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 443]
kimidānīṃ karomi kastava bhrātā pūrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 444]
vaṇijaḥ kathayanti bhavantaḥ sa evāryapūrṇaḥ puṇyamaheśākhyaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 445]
tameva śaraṇaṃ prapadyāma iti | [Divyāv, 2 446]
tairekasvareṇa sarvairevaṃ nādo muktaḥ namastasmai āryāya pūrṇāya namo namastasmai āryāya pūrṇāyeti | [Divyāv, 2 447]
atha yā devatā āyuṣmatī pūrṇe 'bhiprasannā sā yenāyuṣmān pūrṇastenopasaṃkrāntā | [Divyāv, 2 448]
upasaṃkramya āyuṣmantaṃ pūrṇamidamavocat ārya bhrātā te kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhaprāptaḥ samanvāhareti | [Divyāv, 2 449]
tena samanvāhṛtam | [Divyāv, 2 450]
tata āyuṣmān pūrṇastadrūpaṃ samādhiṃ samāpanno yathā samāhite citte śroṇāparāntake 'ntarhito mahāsamudre vahanasīmāyāṃ paryaṅkaṃ baddhvā avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 451]
tato 'sau kālikāvātaḥ sumerupratyāhata iva pratinivṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 452]
atha maheśvaro yakṣaḥ saṃlakṣayati pūrvam yat kiṃcidvahanaṃ kālikāvātena spṛśyate tattūlapicuvat kṣipyate viśīryate ca | [Divyāv, 2 453]
idānīṃ ko yogo yena kālikāvātaḥ sumerupratyāhata iva pratinivṛttaḥ sa itaścāmutaśca pratyavekṣitumārabdho yāvat paśyati āyuṣmantaṃ pūrṇaṃ vahanasīmāyāṃ paryaṅkaṃ baddhvāvasthitam | [Divyāv, 2 454]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ kathayati ārya pūrṇa kiṃ viheṭhayasīti āyuṣmān pūrṇaḥ kathayati jarādharmo 'ham | [Divyāv, 2 455]
kiṃ māmeva viheṭhayasi yadi mayedṛśā guṇagaṇā nādhigatāḥ syurbhrātā me tvayā nāmāvaśeṣaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt | [Divyāv, 2 456]
maheśvaro yakṣaḥ kathayati ārya idaṃ gośīrṣacandanavanaṃ rājñaścakravartino 'rthāya dhāryate | [Divyāv, 2 457]
kiṃ manyase grāmaṇīḥ kiṃ varaṃ rājā cakravartī uta tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddhaḥ kim ārya bhagavāṃlloka utpannaḥ utpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 458]
yadi evam yadaparipūrṇaṃ tatparipūryatām | [Divyāv, 2 459]
tataste vaṇijo gatapratyāgataprāṇā āyuṣmati pūrṇe cittamabhiprasādya tadvahanaṃ gośīrṣacandanasya pūrayitvā samprasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 460]
anupūrveṇa sūrpārakaṃ nagaramanuprāptāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 461]
tata āyuṣmān pūrṇo bhrātuḥ kathayati yasya nāmnā vahanaṃ saṃsiddhayānapātramāgacchati tattasya gamyaṃ bhavati | [Divyāv, 2 462]
tvameṣāṃ vaṇijāṃ ratnasaṃvibhāgaṃ kuru | [Divyāv, 2 463]
ahamanena gośīrṣacandanena bhagavato 'rthāya candanamālaṃ prāsādaṃ kārayāmīti | [Divyāv, 2 464]
tena teṣāṃ vaṇijāṃ ratnaiḥ saṃvibhāgaḥ kṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 465]
tata āyuṣmān pūrṇo gośīrṣacandanena prāsādaṃ māpayitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 466]
tena śilpānāhūyoktāḥ bhavantaḥ kiṃ divase divase pañca kārṣāpaṇaśatāni gṛhṇīdhvamāhosvit gośīrṣacandanacūrṇasya biḍālapadam te kathayanti ārya gośīrṣacandanacūrṇasya biḍālapadam | [Divyāv, 2 467]
yāvat alpīyasā kālena candanamālaḥ prāsādaḥ kṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 468]
rājā kathayati bhavantaḥ śobhanaṃ prāsādam | [Divyāv, 2 469]
sarvajātakṛtaniṣṭhataḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 470]
yattatra saṃkalikā cūrṇaṃ cāvaśiṣṭam tat piṣṭvā tatraiva pralepo dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 471]
te ca bhrātaraḥ parasparaṃ sarve kṣamitā uktāśca buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghamupanimantrya bhojayata | [Divyāv, 2 472]
ārya kutra bhagavān śrāvastyām | [Divyāv, 2 473]
kiyaddūramitaḥ śrāvastī sātirekam yojanaśatam | [Divyāv, 2 474]
rājānaṃ tāvadavalokayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 475]
evaṃ kuruta | [Divyāv, 2 476]
te rājñaḥ sakāśamupasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 477]
upasaṃkramya śirasā praṇāmaṃ kṛtvā kathayanti deva icchāmo vayaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghamupanimantrya bhojayitum | [Divyāv, 2 478]
devo 'smākaṃ sāhāyyaṃ kalpayatu | [Divyāv, 2 479]
rājā kathayati tataḥ śobhanam | [Divyāv, 2 480]
tathā bhavatu | [Divyāv, 2 481]
kalpayāmi | [Divyāv, 2 482]
tata āyuṣmān pūrṇaḥ śaraṇapṛṣṭhamabhiruhya jetavanābhimukhaṃ sthitvā ubhe jānumaṇḍale pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya puṣpāṇi kṣiptvā dhūpaṃ saṃcārya ārāmikena ca sauvarṇabhṛṅgāraṃ grāhayitvā ārādhituṃ pravṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 483]
viśuddhaśīla suviśuddhabuddhe bhaktābhisāre satatārthadarśin | [Divyāv, 2 484.1]
anāthabhūtān prasamīkṣya sādho kṛtvā kṛpāmāgamanaṃ kuruṣva | [Divyāv, 2 484.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 2 484.3]
tatastāni puṣpāṇi buddhānāṃ buddhānubhāvena devatānāṃ ca devatānubhāvenopari puṣpamaṇḍapaṃ kṛtvā jetavane gatvā sthitāni dhūpo 'bhrakūṭavadudakaṃ vaidūryaśalākāvat | [Divyāv, 2 485]
āyuṣmānānando nimittakuśalaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 486]
sa kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha kuto bhagavan nimantraṇamāgatam sūrpārakāt ānanda nagarāt | [Divyāv, 2 487]
kiyaddūre bhadanta sūrpārakaṃ nagaram sātirekam ānanda yojanaśatam | [Divyāv, 2 488]
gacchāmaḥ ānanda bhikṣūnārocaya yo yuṣmākamutsahate śvaḥ sūrpārakaṃ nagaraṃ gatvā bhoktum sa śalākāṃ gṛhṇātu iti | [Divyāv, 2 489]
evaṃ bhadanteti āyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya śalākāṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purastāt sthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 490]
bhagavatā śalākā gṛhītā sthavirasthaviraiśca bhikṣubhiḥ | [Divyāv, 2 491]
tena khalu samayenāyuṣmān pūrṇaḥ kuṇḍopadhānīyakaḥ sthaviraḥ prajñāvimuktas tasyāmeva pariṣadi saṃniṣaṇṇo 'bhūt | [Divyāv, 2 492]
saṃnipatitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 493]
so 'pi śalākāṃ gṛhītumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 494]
tamāyuṣmānānando gāthayā pratyabhāṣata | [Divyāv, 2 495]
naitadbhoktavyamāyuṣman kośalādhipatergṛhe | [Divyāv, 2 496.1]
agāre vā sujātasya mṛgārabhavane 'thavā | [Divyāv, 2 496.2]
sādhikam yojanaśataṃ sūrpārakamitaḥ puram | [Divyāv, 2 497]
ṛddhibhiryatra gantavyaṃ tūṣṇīṃ tvaṃ bhava pūrṇaka | [Divyāv, 2 498.1]
iti | [Divyāv, 2 498.2]
sa prajñāvimuktaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 499]
tena ṛddhir notpāditā | [Divyāv, 2 500]
tasyaitadabhavat yena mayā sakalaṃ kleśagaṇaṃ vāntaṃ charditaṃ tyaktaṃ pratiniḥsṛṣṭam so 'haṃ tīrthikasādhāraṇāyām ṛddhyāṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 501]
tena vīryamāsthāya ṛddhimutpādya yāvadāyuṣmānānandas tṛtīyasthavirasya śalākāṃ na dadāti tāvat tena gajabhujasadṛśaṃ bāhumabhiprasārya śalākā gṛhītā | [Divyāv, 2 502]
tato gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 2 503]
vapuṣmattayā śrutena vā na balātkāraguṇaiśca gautama | [Divyāv, 2 504.1]
prabalairapi vāṅmanorathaiḥ ṣaḍabhijñatvamihādhigamyate | [Divyāv, 2 504.2]
śamaśīlavipaśyanābalairvividhairdhyānabalaiḥ parīkṣitāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 505.1]
jarayā hi nipīḍitayauvanāḥ ṣaḍabhijñā hi bhavanti madvidhāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 505.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 2 505.3]
tatra bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma eṣo 'gro me bhikṣavo bhikṣūṇāṃ mama śrāvakāṇāṃ caityaśalākāgrahaṇe | [Divyāv, 2 506]
tatprathamataḥ śalākāṃ gṛhṇatām yaduta pūrṇaḥ kuṇḍopadhānīyakaḥ sthaviraḥ | [Divyāv, 2 507]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate gaccha ānanda bhikṣūṇāmārocaya | [Divyāv, 2 508]
kiṃ cāpi uktaṃ mayā praticchannakalyāṇairvo bhikṣavo vihartavyaṃ vivṛtapāpairiti api tu tīrthikāvastabdhaṃ tannagaram | [Divyāv, 2 509]
yo vo yasyā ṛddherlābhī tena tayā tatra sūrpārakaṃ nagaraṃ gatvā bhoktavyamiti | [Divyāv, 2 510]
evaṃ bhadanteti āyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya bhikṣūṇāmārocayati āyuṣmantaḥ bhagavānevamāha kiṃ cāpi uktaṃ mayā praticchannakalyāṇairvo bhikṣavo vihartavyamiti pūrvavat yāvat gatvā bhoktavyamiti | [Divyāv, 2 511]
tataḥ sūrpārakarājñā sūrpārakanagaramapagatapāṣāṇaśarkarakaṭhallaṃ vyavasthāpitaṃ candanavāripariṣiktaṃ nānāvidhasurabhidhūpaghaṭikāsamalaṃkṛtam āmuktapaṭṭadāmakalāpaṃ nānāpuṣpābhikīrṇaṃ ramaṇīyam | [Divyāv, 2 512]
sūrpārakasya nagarasyāṣṭādaśa dvārāṇi | [Divyāv, 2 513]
tasyāpi rājñaḥ saptadaśa putrāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 514]
pratyekamekaikasmin dvāre paramayā vibhūtyā rājaputrā vyavasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 515]
mūladvāre ca mahatā rājānubhāvena sūrpārakādhipatī rājā āyuṣmān pūrṇo dārukarṇī stavakarṇī trapukarṇī ca vyavasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 516]
yāvat patracārikā ṛddhyā haritacārikā bhājanacārikāścāgatāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 517]
tān dṛṣṭvā rājā kathayati bhadanta pūrṇa kiṃ bhagavānāgataḥ āyuṣmān pūrṇaḥ kathayati mahārāja patracārikā haritacārikā bhājanacārikāścaite na tāvat bhagavān | [Divyāv, 2 518]
yāvat sthavirasthavirā bhikṣavo 'nekavidhābhirdhyānasamāpattibhiḥ samprāptāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 519]
punarapi pṛcchati bhadanta pūrṇa kiṃ bhagavānāgataḥ āyuṣmān pūrṇaḥ kathayati mahārāja na bhagavān api tu khalu sthavirasthavirā eva te bhikṣava iti | [Divyāv, 2 520]
athānyatamopāsakastasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 2 521]
siṃhavyāghragajāśvanāgavṛṣabhānāśritya kecit śubhān kecidratnavimānaparvatatarūṃścitrān rathāṃścojjvalān | [Divyāv, 2 522.1]
anye toyadharā ivāmbaratale vidyullatālaṃkṛtā ṛddhyā devapurīmiva pramuditā gantuṃ samabhyudyatāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 522.2]
gāṃ bhittvā hyutpatantyeke patantyanye nabhastalāt | [Divyāv, 2 523.1]
āsane nirmitāścaike paśya ṛddhimatāṃ balam | [Divyāv, 2 523.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 2 523.3]
tato bhagavān bahirvihārasya pādau prakṣālya vihāraṃ praviśya ṛjuṃ kāyaṃ praṇidhāya pratimukhaṃ smṛtimupasthāpya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 524]
yāvad bhagavatā gandhakuṭyāṃ sābhisaṃskāraṃ pādo nyastaḥ ṣaḍvikāraḥ pṛthivīkampo jātaḥ iyaṃ mahāpṛthivī calati saṃcalati saṃpracalati vyadhati pravyadhati saṃpravyadhati | [Divyāv, 2 525]
pūrvadigbhāga unnamati paścimo 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 2 526]
paścima unnamati pūrvo 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 2 527]
dakṣiṇa unnamati uttaro 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 2 528]
uttara unnamati dakṣiṇo 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 2 529]
anta unnamati madhyo 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 2 530]
madhya unnamati anto 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 2 531]
rājā āyuṣmantaṃ pūrṇaṃ pṛcchati ārya pūrṇa kimetat sa kathayati mahārāja bhagavatā gandhakuṭyāṃ sābhisaṃskāraḥ pādo nyastaḥ tena ṣaḍvikāraḥ pṛthivīkampo jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 532]
tato bhagavatā kanakamarīcivarṇaprabhā utsṛṣṭā yayā jambudvīpo vilīnakanakāvabhāsaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 533]
punarapi rājā vismayotphullalocanaḥ pṛcchati ārya pūrṇa idaṃ kim sa kathayati mahārāja bhagavatā kanakamarīcivarṇaprabhā utsṛṣṭeti | [Divyāv, 2 534]
tato bhagavān dānto dāntaparivāraḥ śāntaḥ śāntaparivāraḥ pañcabhirarhacchataiḥ sārdhaṃ sūrpārakābhimukhaḥ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 535]
atha yā jetavananivāsinī devatā sā bakulaśākhāṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataśchāyāṃ kurvantī pṛṣṭhataḥ samprasthitā | [Divyāv, 2 536]
tasyā bhagavatā āśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī caturāryasatyasamprativedhakī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā tayā devatayā viṃśatiśikharasamudgataṃ satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ jñānavajreṇa bhittvā srotaāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 2 537]
yāvadanyatamasmin pradeśe pañcamātrāṇi ghariṇīśatāni prativasanti | [Divyāv, 2 538]
adrākṣustā buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam aśītyānuvyañjanairvirājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamamiva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [Divyāv, 2 539]
sahadarśanācca tāsāṃ bhagavati mahāprasāda utpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 540]
dharmataiṣā na tathā dvādaśavarṣābhyastaḥ śamathaścittasya kalyatāṃ janayati aputrasya ca putralābho daridrasya vā nidhidarśanaṃ rājyābhinandino vā rājyābhiṣeko yathopacitakuśalamūlahetukasya sattvasya tatprathamato buddhadarśanam | [Divyāv, 2 541]
tato bhagavāṃstāsāṃ vinayakālamavekṣya purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 542]
tā api bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 543]
tato bhagavatā tāsāmāśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā yāvat srotaāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 2 544]
tā dṛṣṭasatyās trirudānamudānayanti idamasmākaṃ bhadanta na mātrā kṛtaṃ na pitrā kṛtaṃ na rājñā neṣṭasvajanabandhuvargeṇa na devatābhir na pūrvapretair na śramaṇabrāhmaṇairyad bhagavatāsmākaṃ tatkṛtam | [Divyāv, 2 545]
ucchoṣitā rudhirāśrusamudrāḥ laṅghitā asthiparvatāḥ pihitānyapāyadvārāṇi pratiṣṭhāpitā vayaṃ devamanuṣyeṣu atikrāntātikrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 546]
etā vayaṃ bhagavataṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmo dharmaṃ ca bhikṣusaṃghaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 2 547]
upāsikāścāsmān bhagavān dhārayatu | [Divyāv, 2 548]
tata utthāyāsanāt yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocan aho bata bhagavānasmākaṃ kiṃcidatra prayacchet yatra vayaṃ kārāṃ kariṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 549]
tato bhagavatā ṛddhyā keśanakhamutsṛṣṭam | [Divyāv, 2 550]
tābhirbhagavataḥ keśanakhastūpaḥ pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 551]
tatastayā jetavananivāsinyā tasmin stūpe yaṣṭyāṃ sā bakulaśākhāropitā | [Divyāv, 2 552]
bhagavāṃścoktaḥ bhagavan ahamasmin stūpe kārāṃ kurvantī tiṣṭhāmīti | [Divyāv, 2 553]
sā tatraiva āsthitā | [Divyāv, 2 554]
tatra kecit ghariṇīstūpa iti saṃjānate kecit bakulamedhīti yamadyāpi caityavandakā bhikṣavo vandante | [Divyāv, 2 555]
tato bhagavān samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 556]
yāvadanyasminnāśramapade pañca ṛṣiśatāni prativasanti | [Divyāv, 2 557]
tatteṣāmāśramapadaṃ puṣpaphalasalilasampannam | [Divyāv, 2 558]
te tena madena mattā na kiṃcinmanyante | [Divyāv, 2 559]
tato bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ vinayakālamavekṣya tadāśramapadamupasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 560]
upasaṃkramya tasmādāśramapadāt puṣpaphalamṛddhyā śāmitam salilaṃ śoṣitam haritaśāḍvalaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sthaṇḍilāni pātitāni | [Divyāv, 2 561]
tataste ṛṣayaḥ kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparā vyavasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 562]
tato bhagavatā abhihitāḥ maharṣayaḥ kimarthaṃ cintāparāstiṣṭhateti | [Divyāv, 2 563]
te kathayanti bhagavaṃstvaṃ dvipādakaṃ puṇyakṣetramiha praviṣṭo 'smākaṃ cedṛśī samavasthā | [Divyāv, 2 564]
bhagavānāha kim te kathayanti bhagavan puṣpaphalasalilasampannam āśramapadaṃ vinaṣṭam yathāpaurāṇaṃ bhavatu | [Divyāv, 2 565]
bhavatu ityāha bhagavān | [Divyāv, 2 566]
tato bhagavatā ṛddhiḥ prasrabdhā yathāpaurāṇaṃ saṃvṛttam | [Divyāv, 2 567]
tataste paraṃ vismayamupagatā bhagavati cittam abhiprasādayāmāsuḥ | [Divyāv, 2 568]
tato bhagavatā teṣāmāśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī caturāryasatyasamprativedhikī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā taiḥ pañcabhirṛṣiśatairanāgāmiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam ṛddhiścābhinirhṛtā | [Divyāv, 2 569]
tato yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocan labhema vayaṃ bhadanta svākhyāte dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasampadaṃ bhikṣubhāvam | [Divyāv, 2 570]
carema vayaṃ bhagavato 'ntike brahmacaryam | [Divyāv, 2 571]
tataste bhagavatā ehibhikṣukayā ābhāṣitāḥ eta bhikṣavaścarata brahmacaryamiti | [Divyāv, 2 572]
bhagavato vācāvasāne muṇḍāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ saṃghāṭiprāvṛtāḥ pātrakaravyagrahastāḥ saptāhāvaropitakeśaśmaśravo varṣaśatopasaṃpannasya bhikṣorīryāpathena avasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 573]
ehīti coktā hi tathāgatena muṇḍāśca saṃghāṭiparītadehāḥ sadyaḥ praśāntendriyā eva tasthurevaṃ sthitā buddhamanorathena | [Divyāv, 2 574]
tairyujyamānairghaṭamānair vyāyacchamānairidameva pañcagaṇḍakaṃ pūrvavat yāvadabhivādyāśca saṃvṛttāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 575]
yasteṣām ṛṣiravavādakaḥ sa kathayati bhagavan mayā anena veṣeṇa mahājanakāyo vipralabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 576]
tam yāvadabhiprasādayāmi paścāt pravrajiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 2 577]
tato bhagavān pañcabhirṛṣiśataiḥ pūrvakaiśca pañcabhirbhikṣuśatair ardhacandrākāropagūḍhastat eva ṛddhyā upari vihāyasā prakrānto 'nupūrveṇa musalakaṃ parvatamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 578]
tena khalu samayena musalake parvate vakkalī nāma ṛṣiḥ prativasati | [Divyāv, 2 579]
adrākṣīt sa ṛṣirbhagavantaṃ dūrādeva dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaṃ pūrvavat yāvat samantato bhadrakam | [Divyāv, 2 580]
sahadarśanāccānena bhagavato 'ntike cittamabhiprasāditam | [Divyāv, 2 581]
sa prasādajātaścintayati yannvahaṃ parvatādavatīrya bhagavantaṃ darśanāyopasaṃkramiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 2 582]
bhagavān vaineyāpekṣayā atikramiṣyati | [Divyāv, 2 583]
yannvahamātmānaṃ parvatānmuñceyamiti | [Divyāv, 2 584]
tena parvatādātmā muktaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 585]
asaṃmoṣadharmāṇo buddhā bhagavantaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 586]
bhagavatā ṛddhyā pratīṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 587]
tato 'sya bhagavatā āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā vakkalinā anāgāmiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam ṛddhiścābhinirhṛtā | [Divyāv, 2 588]
tato bhagavantamidamavocat labheyāhaṃ bhadanta svākhyāte dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasampadaṃ bhikṣubhāvaṃ pūrvavat yāvat bhagavatā ehibhikṣukayā pravrājito yāvadevaṃ sthito buddhamanorathena | [Divyāv, 2 589]
tatra bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma eṣo 'gro me bhikṣavo bhikṣūṇāṃ mama śraddhādhimuktānām yaduta vakkalī bhikṣuriti | [Divyāv, 2 590]
tato bhagavān bhikṣusahasraparivṛto vicitrāṇi prātihāryāṇi kurvan sūrpārakaṃ nagaramanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 591]
bhagavān saṃlakṣayati yadi ekena dvāreṇa praviśāmi apareṣāṃ bhaviṣyati anyathātvam | [Divyāv, 2 592]
yannvaham ṛddhyaiva praviśeyamiti | [Divyāv, 2 593]
tata ṛddhyā upari vihāyasā madhye sūrpārakasya nagarasyāvatīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 594]
tataḥ sūrpārakādhipatī rājā āyuṣmān pūrṇo dārukarṇī stavakarṇī trapukarṇī te ca saptadaśa putrāḥ svakasvakena parivāreṇa yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ anekāni ca prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi | [Divyāv, 2 595]
tato bhagavānanekaiḥ prāṇiśatasahasrairanugamyamāno yena candanamālaḥ prāsādas tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 596]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 597]
sa janakāyo bhagavantamapaśyaṃścandanamālaṃ prāsādaṃ bhettumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 598]
bhagavān saṃlakṣayati yadi candanamālaḥ prāsādo bhetsyate dātṝṇāṃ puṇyāntarāyo bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 2 599]
yannvahamenaṃ sphaṭikamayaṃ nirminuyāmiti | [Divyāv, 2 600]
sa bhagavatā sphaṭikamayo nirmitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 601]
tato bhagavatā tasyāḥ pariṣada āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā anekaiḥ prāṇiśatasahasrairmahān viśeṣo 'dhigataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 602]
kaiścinmokṣabhāgīyāni kuśalamūlāni utpāditāni kaiścinnirvedhabhāgīyāni kaiścit srotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam kaiścit sakṛdāgāmiphalam kaiścidanāgāmiphalam kaiścit sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam kaiścit śrāvakabodhau cittānyutpāditāni kaiścit pratyekabodhau kaiścidanuttarāyāṃ samyaksambodhau cittānyutpāditāni | [Divyāv, 2 603]
yadbhūyasā sā parṣad buddhanimnā dharmapravaṇā saṃghaprāgbhārā vyavasthāpitā | [Divyāv, 2 604]
atha dārukarṇī stavakarṇī trapukarṇī ca praṇītaṃ khādanīyaṃ bhojanīyaṃ samudānīya āsanāni prajñāpya bhagavato dūtena kālamārocayanti samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālam manyata iti | [Divyāv, 2 605]
tena khalu samayena kṛṣṇagautamakau nāgarājau mahāsamudre prativasataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 606]
tau saṃlakṣayataḥ bhagavān sūrpārake nagare dharmaṃ deśayati | [Divyāv, 2 607]
gacchāvaḥ dharmaṃ śroṣyāva iti | [Divyāv, 2 608]
tatastau pañcanāgaśataparivārau pañcanadīśatāni saṃjanya sūrpārakaṃ nagaraṃ samprasthitau | [Divyāv, 2 609]
asaṃmoṣadharmāṇo buddhā bhagavantaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 610]
bhagavān saṃlakṣayati imau kṛṣṇagautamau nāgarājau yadi sūrpārakaṃ nagaramāgamiṣyataḥ agocarīkariṣyataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 611]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ mahāmaudgalyāyanamāmantrayate pratigṛhāṇa mahāmaudgalyāyana tathāgatasyātyayikapiṇḍapātam | [Divyāv, 2 612]
tatkasya hetoḥ pañca me maudgalyāyana ātyayikapiṇḍapātāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 613]
katame pañca āgantukasya gamikasya glānasya glānopasthāyakasyopadhivārikasya ca | [Divyāv, 2 614]
asmiṃstvarthe bhagavānupādhau vartate | [Divyāv, 2 615]
atha bhagavān maudgalyāyanasahāyo yena kṛṣṇagautamakau nāgarājau tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 616]
tau kathayataḥ samanvāharata nāgendrau sūrpārakaṃ nagaramagocarībhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 2 617]
tau kathayataḥ tādṛśena bhadanta prasādena vayamāgatā yanna śakyamasmābhiḥ kuntapipīlikasyāpi prāṇinaḥ pīḍāmutpādayituṃ prāgeva sūrpārakanagaranivāsino janakāyasyeti | [Divyāv, 2 618]
tato bhagavatā kṛṣṇagautamakayor nāgarājayostādṛśo dharmo yaṃ śrutvā buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatau dharmaṃ saṃghaṃ ca śaraṇaṃ gatau śikṣāpadāni ca gṛhītāni | [Divyāv, 2 619]
bhagavān bhaktakṛtyaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 620]
ekaiko nāgaḥ saṃlakṣayati aho bata bhagavān mama pānīyaṃ pibatu iti | [Divyāv, 2 621]
bhagavān saṃlakṣayati yadi ekasyaiva pānīyaṃ pāsyāmi eṣāṃ bhaviṣyati anyathātvam | [Divyāv, 2 622]
upāyasaṃvidhānaṃ kartavyamiti | [Divyāv, 2 623]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ mahāmaudgalyāyanamāmantrayate gaccha maudgalyāyana yatra pañcānāṃ nadīśatānāṃ saṃbhedaḥ tasmādudakasya pātrapūramānaya | [Divyāv, 2 624]
evaṃ bhadanteti āyuṣmān mahāmaudgalyāyano bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya yatra pañcānāṃ nadīśatānāṃ saṃbhedastatrodakasya pātrapūramādāya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 625]
upasaṃkramya bhagavata udakasya pātrapūramupanāmayati | [Divyāv, 2 626]
bhagavatā gṛhītvā paribhuktam | [Divyāv, 2 627]
āyuṣmān mahāmaudgalyāyanaḥ saṃlakṣayati pūrvamuktaṃ bhagavatā duṣkarakārakau hi bhikṣavaḥ putrasya mātāpitarau āpyāyakau poṣakau saṃvardhakau stanyasya dātārau citrasya jambudvīpasya darśayitārau | [Divyāv, 2 628]
ekenāṃśena putro mātaraṃ dvitīyena pitaraṃ pūrṇavarṣaśataṃ paricaret yadvā asyāṃ mahāpṛthivyāṃ maṇayo muktā vaidūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpamaśmagarbho musāragalvo lohitikā dakṣiṇāvarta iti evaṃrūpe vā vividhaiśvaryādhipatye pratiṣṭhāpayen neyatā putreṇa mātāpitroḥ kṛtaṃ vā syādupakṛtaṃ vā | [Divyāv, 2 629]
yastu asāvaśrāddhaṃ mātāpitaraṃ śraddhāsampadi samādāpayati vinayati niveśayati pratiṣṭhāpayati duḥśīlaṃ śīlasampadi matsariṇaṃ tyāgasampadi duṣprajñaṃ prajñāsampadi samādāpayati vinayati niveśayati pratiṣṭhāpayati iyatā putreṇa mātāpitroḥ kṛtaṃ vā syādupakṛtaṃ veti | [Divyāv, 2 630]
mayā ca mātur na kaścidupakāraḥ kṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 631]
yadahaṃ samanvāhareyaṃ kutra me mātā upapanneti | [Divyāv, 2 632]
samanvāhartuṃ saṃvṛttaḥ paśyati marīcike lokadhātau upapannā | [Divyāv, 2 633]
sa saṃlakṣayati kasya vineyā paśyati bhagavataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 634]
tasyaitadabhavat dūraṃ vayamihāgatāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 635]
yannvahametamarthaṃ bhagavato nivedayeyamiti bhagavantamidamavocat uktaṃ bhadanta bhagavatā pūrvam duṣkarakārakau hi bhikṣavaḥ putrasya mātāpitarau iti | [Divyāv, 2 636]
tanmama mātā marīcike lokadhātau upapannā sā ca bhagavato vineyā | [Divyāv, 2 637]
tadarhati bhagavāṃs tāṃ vinetumanukampāmupādāyeti | [Divyāv, 2 638]
bhagavān kathayati maudgalyāyana kasya ṛddhyā gacchāmaḥ bhagavan madīyayā | [Divyāv, 2 639]
tato bhagavānāyuṣmāṃśca mahāmaudgalyāyanaḥ sumerumūrdhni pādān sthāpayantau samprasthitau | [Divyāv, 2 640]
saptame divase marīcikaṃ lokadhātumanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 641]
adrākṣīt sā bhadrakanyā āyuṣmantaṃ mahāmaudgalyāyanaṃ dūrādeva | [Divyāv, 2 642]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ sasambhramāt tatsakāśamupasaṃkramya kathayati cirādbata putrakaṃ paśyāmīti | [Divyāv, 2 643]
tato janakāyaḥ kathayati bhadanto 'yaṃ pravrajito vṛddhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 644]
iyaṃ ca kanyā | [Divyāv, 2 645]
kathamasya mātā bhavatīti āyuṣmān maudgalyāyanaḥ kathayati bhavantaḥ mama ime skandhā anayā saṃvṛddhāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 646]
tena mameyaṃ māteti | [Divyāv, 2 647]
tato bhagavatā tasyā bhadrakanyāyā āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī caturāryasatyasamprativedhikī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā tayā bhadrakanyayā viṃśatiśikharasamudgataṃ satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ jñānavajreṇa bhittvā srotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 2 648]
sā dṛṣṭasatyā trirudānamudānayati pūrvavat yāvat pratiṣṭhāpitā devamanuṣyeṣu | [Divyāv, 2 649]
āha ca | [Divyāv, 2 650]
tavānubhāvātpihitaḥ sughoro hyapāyamārgo bahudoṣaduṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 651]
apāvṛtā svargagatiḥ supuṇyā nirvāṇamārgaṃ ca mayopalabdham | [Divyāv, 2 652]
tvadāśrayāccāptamapetadoṣaṃ mamādya śuddhaṃ suviśuddhacakṣuḥ | [Divyāv, 2 653]
prāptaṃ ca kāntaṃ padamāryakāntaṃ tīrṇā ca duḥkhārṇavapāramasmi | [Divyāv, 2 654]
jagati daityanarāmarapūjita vigatajanmajarāmaraṇāmaya | [Divyāv, 2 655.1]
bhavasahasrasudurlabhadarśana saphalamadya mune tava darśanam | [Divyāv, 2 655.2]
atikrāntāhaṃ bhadanta atikrāntā eṣāhaṃ bhagavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi dharmaṃ ca bhikṣusaṃghaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 2 656]
upāsikāṃ ca māṃ dhāraya adyāgreṇa yāvajjīvaṃ prāṇopetāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāmabhiprasannām | [Divyāv, 2 657]
adhivāsayatu me bhagavānadya piṇḍapātena sārdhamāryamahāmaudgalyāyaneneti | [Divyāv, 2 658]
adhivāsayati bhagavāṃstasyā bhadrakanyāyāstūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 2 659]
atha sā bhadrakanyā bhagavantamāyuṣmantaṃ ca mahāmaudgalyāyanaṃ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpya saṃpravārya bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastam apanītapātraṃ nīcataramāsanaṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purastānniṣaṇṇā dharmaśravaṇāya | [Divyāv, 2 660]
bhagavatā tasyā dharmo deśitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 661]
āyuṣmān mahāmaudgalyāyano bhagavataḥ pātragrāhakaḥ pātraṃ niryātayati | [Divyāv, 2 662]
bhagavatā abhihitaḥ maudgalyāyana gacchāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 663]
gacchāmo bhagavan | [Divyāv, 2 664]
kasya ṛddhyā tathāgatasya bhagavataḥ | [Divyāv, 2 665]
yadi evam samanvāhara jetavanam | [Divyāv, 2 666]
āgatāḥ smo bhagavan āgatāḥ | [Divyāv, 2 667]
maudgalyāyanastato vismayāvarjitamatiḥ kathayati kiṃ nāmeyaṃ bhagavann ṛddhir manojavā maudgalyāyana | [Divyāv, 2 668]
na mayā bhadanta vijñātamevaṃ gambhīramevaṃ gambhīrā buddhadharmā iti | [Divyāv, 2 669]
yadi vijñātamabhaviṣyat tilaśo 'pi me saṃcūrṇitaśarīreṇānuttarāyāḥ samyaksambodheścittaṃ vyāvartitamabhaviṣyat | [Divyāv, 2 670]
idānīṃ kiṃ karomi dagdhendhana iti | [Divyāv, 2 671]
tato bhikṣavaḥ saṃśayajātāḥ sarvasaṃśayacchettāraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ papracchuḥ kiṃ bhadanta āyuṣmatā pūrṇena karma kṛtam yenāḍhye mahādhane mahābhoge kule jātaḥ kiṃ karma kṛtam yena dāsyāḥ kukṣau upapannaḥ pravrajya ca sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam bhagavānāha pūrṇena bhikṣavo bhikṣuṇā karmāṇi kṛtāni upacitāni labdhasambhārāṇi pariṇatapratyayāni oghavatpratyupasthitāni avaśyambhāvīni | [Divyāv, 2 672]
pūrṇena karmāṇi kṛtāni upacitāni | [Divyāv, 2 673]
ko 'nyaḥ pratyanubhaviṣyati na bhikṣavaḥ karmāṇi kṛtāni upacitāni bāhye pṛthivīdhātau vipacyante nābdhātau na tejodhātau na vāyudhātau api tūpātteṣveva skandhadhātvāyataneṣu karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni vipacyante śubhānyaśubhāni ca | [Divyāv, 2 674]
na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi api kalpaśatairapi | [Divyāv, 2 675.1]
sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti khalu dehinām | [Divyāv, 2 675.2]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'sminneva bhadrakalpe viṃśativarṣasahasrāyuṣi prajāyāṃ kāśyapo nāma samyaksambuddho loka udapādi vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [Divyāv, 2 676]
buddho bhagavān vārāṇasīṃ nagarīmupaniśritya viharati | [Divyāv, 2 677]
tasyāyaṃ śāsane pravrajitaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 678]
tripiṭakasaṃghasya ca dharmavaiyāvṛtyaṃ karoti | [Divyāv, 2 679]
yāvadanyatamasyārhata upadhivāraḥ prāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 680]
sa vihāraṃ saṃmarṣṭumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 681]
vāyunetaścāmutaśca saṃkāro nīyate | [Divyāv, 2 682]
sa saṃlakṣayati tiṣṭhatu tāvad yāvadvāyurupaśamaṃ gacchatīti | [Divyāv, 2 683]
vaiyāvṛtyakareṇāsaṃmṛṣṭo vihāro dṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 684]
tena tīvreṇa paryavasthānena kharavākkarma niścāritam kasya dāsīputrasyopadhivāra iti | [Divyāv, 2 685]
tena arhatā śrutam | [Divyāv, 2 686]
sa saṃlakṣayati paryavasthito 'yam | [Divyāv, 2 687]
tiṣṭhatu tāvat | [Divyāv, 2 688]
paścāt saṃjñāpayiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 2 689]
yadā asya paryavasthānaṃ vigataṃ tadā tasya sakāśamupasaṃkramya kathayati jānīṣe tvaṃ ko 'hamiti sa kathayati jāne tvaṃ kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasya śāsane pravrajito 'hamapīti | [Divyāv, 2 690]
sa kathayati yadyapyevaṃ tathāpi tu yanmayā pravrajya caraṇīyaṃ tatkṛtam ahaṃ sakalabandhanābaddhaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 691]
kharaṃ te vākkarma niścāritam | [Divyāv, 2 692]
atyayamatyayato deśaya | [Divyāv, 2 693]
apyevaitatkarma tanutvaṃ parikṣayaṃ paryādānaṃ gacchediti | [Divyāv, 2 694]
tenātyayamatyayato deśitam | [Divyāv, 2 695]
yattena naraka upapadya dāsīputreṇa bhavitavyam tannarake nopapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 696]
pañca tu janmaśatāni dāsyāḥ kukṣau upapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 697]
yāvadetarhyapi carame bhave dāsyā eva kukṣau upapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 698]
yat saṃghasyopasthānaṃ kṛtam tenāḍhye mahādhane mahābhoge kule jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 699]
yattatra paṭhitaṃ svādhyāyitaṃ skandhakauśalaṃ ca kṛtam tena mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 2 700]
iti hi bhikṣava ekāntakṛṣṇānāṃ karmaṇāmekāntakṛṣṇo vipākaḥ ekāntaśuklānāṃ karmaṇāmekāntaśuklo vipākaḥ vyatimiśrāṇāṃ vyatimiśraḥ | [Divyāv, 2 701]
tasmāt tarhi bhikṣava ekāntakṛṣṇāni karmāṇyapāsya vyatimiśrāṇi ca ekāntaśukleṣveva karmasvābhogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [Divyāv, 2 702]
ityevaṃ vo bhikṣavaḥ śikṣitavyam | [Divyāv, 2 703]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 2 704]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandanniti | [Divyāv, 2 705]
{Divyāv, 3}
yadā rājñā māgadhena ajātaśatruṇā vaidehīputreṇa naukramo mātāpitrormāpitastadā vaiśālakairlicchavibhirbhagavato 'rthe naukramo māpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 1]
nāgāḥ saṃlakṣayanti vayaṃ vinipatitaśarīrā yannu vayaṃ phaṇasaṃkrameṇa bhagavantaṃ nadīm gaṅgāmuttārayema iti | [Divyāv, 3 2]
taiḥ phaṇasaṃkramo māpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 3]
tatra bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma rājagṛhāt śrāvastīṃ gantum yo yuṣmākaṃ bhikṣava utsahate rājño māgadhasyājātaśatrorvaidehīputrasya nausaṃkrameṇa nadīgaṅgāmuttartum sa tena taratu yo vā bhikṣavo vaiśālakānāṃ licchavīnāṃ nausaṃkrameṇa so 'pi tenottaratu | [Divyāv, 3 4]
ahamapi āyuṣmatā ānandena bhikṣuṇā sārdhaṃ nāgānāṃ phaṇasaṃkrameṇa nadīṃ gaṅgāmuttariṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 3 5]
tatra kecit rājño māgadhasyājātaśatrorvaidehīputrasya nausaṃkrameṇottīrṇāḥ kecit vaiśālikānāṃ licchavīnāṃ nausaṃkrameṇa | [Divyāv, 3 6]
bhagavānapi āyuṣmatā ānandena sārdhaṃ nāgānāṃ phaṇasaṃkrameṇottīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 7]
athānyatamopāsakastasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 3 8]
ye tarantyarṇavaṃ saraḥ setuṃ kṛtvā visṛjya palvalāni | [Divyāv, 3 9.1]
kolaṃ hi janāḥ prabandhitā uttīrṇā medhāvino janāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 9.2]
uttīrṇo bhagavān buddho brāhmaṇastiṣṭhati sthale | [Divyāv, 3 10.1]
bhikṣavo 'tra parisnānti kolaṃ badhnanti śrāvakāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 10.2]
kiṃ kuryādudapānena āpaścet sarvato yadi | [Divyāv, 3 11.1]
chittveha mūlaṃ tṛṣṇāyāḥ kasya paryeṣaṇāṃ caret | [Divyāv, 3 11.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 3 12]
adrākṣīdbhagavānanyatamasmin bhūbhāge unnatonnataṃ pṛthivīpradeśam | [Divyāv, 3 13]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarāyuṣmantamāmantrayate icchasi tvamānanda yo 'sau yūpa ūrdhvaṃ vyāmasahasraṃ tiryak ṣoḍaśapravedho nānāratnavicitro divyaḥ sarvasauvarṇo rājñā mahāpraṇādena dānāni dattvā puṇyāni kṛtvā nadyāṃ gaṅgāyāṃ āplāvitaḥ taṃ draṣṭum etasya bhagavan kālaḥ etasya sugata samayaḥ yo 'yaṃ bhagavān yūpamucchrāpayet bhikṣavaḥ paśyeyuḥ | [Divyāv, 3 14]
tato bhagavatā cakrasvastikanandyāvartena jālāvanaddhenānekapuṇyaśatanirjātena bhītānāmāśvāsanakareṇa pṛthivī parāmṛṣṭā | [Divyāv, 3 15]
nāgāḥ saṃlakṣayanti kimarthaṃ bhagavatā pṛthivī parāmṛṣṭeti yāvat paśyanti yūpaṃ draṣṭukāmāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 16]
tatastairucchrāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 17]
bhikṣavo yūpaṃ draṣṭumārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 18]
āyuṣmānapi bhaddālī alpotsukaḥ pāṃsukūlaṃ sīvyati | [Divyāv, 3 19]
tatra bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma ārohapariṇāhaṃ nimittaṃ bhikṣavo yūpasya gṛhṇīta antardhāsyatīti | [Divyāv, 3 20]
antarhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 21]
bhikṣavo buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ papracchuḥ paśya bhadanta bhikṣavo yūpaṃ paśyanti | [Divyāv, 3 22]
āyuṣmānapi bhaddālī alpotsukaḥ pāṃsukūlaṃ sīvyati | [Divyāv, 3 23]
kiṃ tāvat vītarāgatvādāhosvit paryupāsitapūrvatvāt tadyadi tāvad vītarāgatvāt santyanye 'pi vītarāgāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 24]
atha paryupāsitapūrvatvāt kutra kena paryupāsitamiti | [Divyāv, 3 25]
bhagavānāha api bhikṣavo vītarāgatvādapi paryupāsitapūrvatvāt | [Divyāv, 3 26]
kutrānena paryupāsitam | [Divyāv, 3 27]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo rājābhūt praṇādo nāma śakrasya devendrasya vayasyakaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 28]
so 'putraḥ putrābhinandī kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ anekadhanasamudito 'hamaputraśca | [Divyāv, 3 29]
mamātyayād rājavaṃśasamucchedo bhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 3 30]
tataḥ śakreṇa dṛṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭaśca mārṣa kasmāt tvaṃ kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparastiṣṭhasīti sa kathayati kauśila anekadhanasamudito 'hamaputraśca | [Divyāv, 3 31]
mamātyayād rājavaṃśasyocchedo bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 32]
śakraḥ kathayati mārṣa mā tvaṃ cintāparastiṣṭha | [Divyāv, 3 33]
yadi kaścit cyavanadharmā devaputro bhaviṣyati tatte putratve samādāpayiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 3 34]
dharmatā khalu cyavanadharmaṇo devaputrasya pañca pūrvanimittāni prādurbhavanti akliṣṭāni vāsāṃsi saṃkliśyanti amlānāni mālyāni mlāyante daurgandhaṃ mukhānniścarati ubhābhyāṃ kakṣābhyāṃ svedaḥ pragharati sve cāsane dhṛtiṃ na labhate | [Divyāv, 3 35]
yāvadanyatamasya devaputrasya pañca pūrvanimittāni prādurbhūtāni | [Divyāv, 3 36]
sa śakreṇa devendreṇoktaḥ mārṣa praṇādasya rājño 'gramahiṣyāḥ kukṣau pratisaṃdhiṃ gṛhāṇeti | [Divyāv, 3 37]
sa kathayati pramādasthānaṃ kauśika | [Divyāv, 3 38]
bahukilbiṣakāriṇo hi kauśika rājānaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 39]
mā adharmeṇa rājyaṃ kṛtvā narakaparāyaṇo bhaviṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 3 40]
śakraḥ kathayati mārṣa ahaṃ te smārayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 3 41]
pramattāḥ kauśika devā ratibahulāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 42]
evametanmārṣa | [Divyāv, 3 43]
tathāpi tvahaṃ bhavantaṃ smārayāmi | [Divyāv, 3 44]
tena praṇādasya rājño 'gramahiṣyāḥ kukṣau pratisaṃdhirgṛhītā | [Divyāv, 3 45]
yasminneva divase pratisaṃdhirgṛhītā tasmin divase mahājanakāyena praṇādo muktaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 46]
sā aṣṭānāṃ vā navānāṃ vā māsānāmatyayāt prasūtā | [Divyāv, 3 47]
dārako jāto 'bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādiko gauraḥ kanakavarṇaśchatrākāraśirāḥ pralambabāhurvistīrṇalalāṭaḥ saṃgatabhrūstuṅganāsaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 48]
tasya jñātayaḥ saṃgamya samāgamya nāmadheyaṃ vyavasthāpayanti kiṃ bhavatu dārakasya nāmeti | [Divyāv, 3 49]
jñātaya ūcur yasminneva divase 'yaṃ dārako mātuḥ kukṣimavakrāntaḥ tasminneva divase mahājanakāyena nādo muktaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 50]
yasminneva divase jātastasminneva divase mahājanakāyena nādo muktaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 51]
tasmāt bhavatu dārakasya mahāpraṇāda iti nāma | [Divyāv, 3 52]
tasya mahāpraṇāda iti nāmadheyaṃ vyavasthāpitam | [Divyāv, 3 53]
mahāpraṇādo dārako 'ṣṭābhyo dhātrībhyo 'nupradatto dvābhyām aṃsadhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ maladhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ kṣīradhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ krīḍanikābhyām | [Divyāv, 3 54]
so 'ṣṭābhirdhātrībhirunnīyate vardhyate kṣīreṇa dadhnā navanītena sarpiṣā sarpimaṇḍenānyaiścottaptottaptairupakaraṇaviśeṣaiḥ | [Divyāv, 3 55]
āśu vardhate hradasthamiva paṅkajam | [Divyāv, 3 56]
yadā mahān saṃvṛttastadā lipyāmupanyastaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 57]
saṃkhyāyāṃ gaṇanāyāṃ mudrāyāmuddhāre nyāse nikṣepe vastuparīkṣāyāṃ dāruparīkṣāyāṃ ratnaparīkṣāyāṃ hastiparīkṣāyāmaśvaparīkṣāyāṃ kumāraparīkṣāyāṃ kumārīparīkṣāyām so 'ṣṭāsu parīkṣāsūdghaṭṭako vācakaḥ paṭupracāraḥ paṇḍitaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 58]
sa yāni tāni rājñāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mūrdhnābhiṣiktānāṃ janapadaiśvaryasthāmavīryam anuprāptānāṃ mahāntaṃ pṛthivīmaṇḍalam abhinirjityādhyāsatāṃ pṛthag bhavanti śilpasthānakarmasthānāni tadyathā hastiśikṣāyāmaśvapṛṣṭhe rathe śare dhanuṣi prayāṇe niryāṇe 'ṅkuśagrahe pāśagrahe tomaragrahe yaṣṭibandhe padabandhe śikhābandhe dūravedhe marmavedhe 'kṣuṇṇavedhe dṛḍhaprahāritāyāṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu kṛtāvī saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 59]
dharmatā khalu na tāvat putrasya nāma prajñāyate yāvat tāto jīvati | [Divyāv, 3 60]
apareṇa samayena praṇādo rājā kālagataḥ | [Divyāv, 3 61]
mahāpraṇādo rājye pratiṣṭhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 62]
sa yāvattāvad dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kārayitvā adharmeṇa kārayituṃ pravṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 63]
tataḥ śakreṇa devendreṇoktaḥ mārṣa mayā tvaṃ praṇādasya rājñaḥ samādāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 64]
mā adharmeṇa rājyaṃ kāraya mā narakaparāyaṇo bhaviṣyasīti | [Divyāv, 3 65]
sa yāvattāvad dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kārayitvā punarapi adharmeṇa rājyaṃ kārayituṃ pravṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 66]
dvirapi śakreṇoktaḥ mārṣa mayā tvaṃ praṇādasya rājñaḥ putratve samādāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 67]
mā adharmeṇa rājyaṃ kāraya mā narakaparāyaṇo bhaviṣyasīti | [Divyāv, 3 68]
sa kathayati kauśika vayaṃ rājānaḥ pramattā iti ratibahulāḥ kṣaṇād vismarāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 69]
kiṃcittvamasmākaṃ cihnaṃ sthāpaya yaṃ dṛṣṭvā dānāni dāsyāmaḥ puṇyāni kārayiṣyāma iti | [Divyāv, 3 70]
na ca śakyate vinā nimittena puṇyaṃ kartum | [Divyāv, 3 71]
tataḥ śakreṇa devendreṇa viśvakarmaṇo devaputrasyājñā dattā gaccha tvaṃ viśvakarman rājño mahāpraṇādasya niveśane | [Divyāv, 3 72]
divyaṃ maṇḍalavāṭaṃ nirmiṇu yūpaṃ cocchrāpaya ūrdhvaṃ vyāmasahasreṇa tiryak ṣoḍaśapravedhaṃ nānāratnavicitraṃ sarvasauvarṇamiti | [Divyāv, 3 73]
tato viśvakarmaṇā devaputreṇa mahāpraṇādasya rājño niveśane divyo maṇḍalavāṭo nirmito yūpaścocchritaḥ ūrdhvaṃ vyāmasahasraṃ nānāratnavicitro divyaḥ sarvasauvarṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 74]
tato mahāpraṇādena rājñā dānaśālā māpitā | [Divyāv, 3 75]
tasya mātulo 'śoko nāma yūpasya paricārako vyavasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 76]
tato yūpadarśanodyuktaḥ sarva eva jambudvīpanivāsī janakāya āgatya bhuktvā yūpaṃ paśyati svakarmānuṣṭhānaṃ na karoti | [Divyāv, 3 77]
tataḥ kṛṣikarmāntāḥ samucchinnāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 78]
rājñaḥ karapratyāyā nottiṣṭhante | [Divyāv, 3 79]
amātyaiḥ stokāḥ karapratyāyā upanītāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 80]
mahāpraṇādo rājā pṛcchati bhavantaḥ kasmāt stokāḥ karapratyāyā upanītāḥ deva jambudvīpanivāsī janakāya āgatya bhuktvā yūpaṃ paśyati svakarmānuṣṭhānaṃ na karoti | [Divyāv, 3 81]
kṛṣikarmāntāḥ samucchinnāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 82]
rājñaḥ karapratyāyā nottiṣṭhanta iti | [Divyāv, 3 83]
rājā kathayati samucchidyatāṃ dānaśāleti | [Divyāv, 3 84]
taiḥ samucchinnā | [Divyāv, 3 85]
tato 'pyasau janakāyaḥ svapathyadanamādāya bhuktvā yūpaṃ nirīkṣamāṇastiṣṭhati svakarmānuṣṭhānaṃ na karoti | [Divyāv, 3 86]
kṛṣikarmāntāḥ samucchinnāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 87]
tathāpi karapratyāyā nottiṣṭhante | [Divyāv, 3 88]
rājā pṛcchati bhavantaḥ dānaśālāḥ samucchinnāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 89]
idānīṃ karapratyāyā nottiṣṭhanta iti | [Divyāv, 3 90]
amātyāḥ kathayanti deva janakāyaḥ svapathyadanamādāya bhuktvā yūpaṃ nirīkṣamāṇastiṣṭhati svakarmānuṣṭhānaṃ na karoti | [Divyāv, 3 91]
kṛṣikarmāntāḥ samucchinnāḥ yataḥ karapratyāyā nottiṣṭhante | [Divyāv, 3 92]
tato rājñā mahāpraṇādena dānāni dattvā puṇyāni kṛtvā sa yūpo nadyāṃ gaṅgāyāmāplāvitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 93]
kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau mahāpraṇādasyāśoko nāma mātulaḥ eṣa evāsau bhaddālī bhikṣuḥ | [Divyāv, 3 94]
tatrānena paryupāsitapūrvaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 95]
kutra bhadantāsau yūpo vilayaṃ gamiṣyati bhaviṣyanti bhikṣavo 'nāgate 'dhvani aśītivarṣasahasrāyuṣo manuṣyāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 96]
aśītivarṣasahasrāyuṣāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ śaṅkho nāma rājā bhaviṣyati saṃyamanī cakravartī caturantavijetā dhārmiko dharmarājā saptaratnasamanvāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 3 97]
tasyemānyevaṃrūpāṇi sapta ratnāni bhaviṣyanti | [Divyāv, 3 98]
tadyathā cakraratnaṃ hastiratnamaśvaratnaṃ maṇiratnaṃ strīratnaṃ gṛhapatiratnaṃ pariṇāyakaratnameva saptamam | [Divyāv, 3 99]
pūrṇaṃ cāsya bhaviṣyati sahasraṃ putrāṇāṃ śūrāṇāṃ vīrāṇāṃ varāṅgarūpiṇāṃ parasainyapramardakānām | [Divyāv, 3 100]
sa imāmeva samudraparyantāṃ pṛthivīmakhilām akaṇṭakām anutpīḍām adaṇḍenāśastreṇa dharmeṇa samayena abhinirjityādhyāvasiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 101]
śaṅkhasya rājño brahmāyur nāma brāhmaṇaḥ purohito bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 102]
tasya brahmavatī nāma patnī bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 103]
sā maitreyāṃśena sphuritvā putraṃ janayiṣyati maitreyaṃ nāma | [Divyāv, 3 104]
brahmāyurmāṇavo 'śītimāṇavakaśatāni brāhmaṇakān mantrān vācayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 105]
sa tān māṇavakān maitreyāya anupradāsyati | [Divyāv, 3 106]
maitreyo māṇavo 'śītimāṇavakasahasrāṇi brāhmaṇakān mantrān vācayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 107]
atha catvāro mahārājāścaturmahānidhisthāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 108]
piṅgalaśca kaliṅgeṣu mithilāyāṃ ca pāṇḍukaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 109.1]
elāpatraśca gāndhāre śaṅkho vārāṇasīpure | [Divyāv, 3 109.2]
enaṃ ca yūpamādāya śaṅkhasya rājña upanāmayiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 3 110]
śaṅkho 'pi rājā brahmāyuṣe brāhmaṇāyānupradāsyati | [Divyāv, 3 111]
brahmāyurapi brāhmaṇo maitreyāya māṇavāyānupradāsyati | [Divyāv, 3 112]
maitreyo 'pi māṇavasteṣāṃ māṇavakānāmanupradāsyati | [Divyāv, 3 113]
tataste māṇavakāstam yūpaṃ khaṇḍaṃ khaṇḍaṃ chittvā bhājayiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 3 114]
tato maitreyo māṇavakastasya yūpasyānityatāṃ dṛṣṭvā tenaiva saṃvegena vanaṃ saṃśrayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 115]
yasminneva divase vanaṃ saṃśrayiṣyati tasminneva divase maitreyāṃśena sphuritvā anuttaraṃ jñānamadhigamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 116]
tasya maitreyaḥ samyaksambuddha iti saṃjñā bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 117]
yasminneva divase maitreyaḥ samyaksambuddho 'nuttarajñānamadhigamiṣyati tasminneva divase śaṅkhasya rājñaḥ saptaratnānyantardhāsyante | [Divyāv, 3 118]
śaṅkho 'pi rājā aśītikoṭṭarājasahasraparivāro maitreyaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ pravrajitamanupravrajiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 119]
yadapyasya strīratnaṃ viśākhā nāma sāpi aśītistrīsahasraparivārā maitreyaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ pravrajitamanupravrajiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 120]
tato maitreyaḥ samyaksambuddho 'śītibhikṣukoṭiparivāro yena gurupādakaḥ parvatastenopasaṃkramiṣyati yatra kāśyapasya bhikṣorasthisaṃghāto 'vikopitastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 3 121]
gurupādakaparvato maitreyāya samyaksambuddhāya vivaramanupradāsyati | [Divyāv, 3 122]
yato maitreyaḥ samyaksambuddhaḥ kāśyapasya bhikṣoravikopitam asthisaṃghātaṃ dakṣiṇena pāṇinā gṛhītvā vāme pāṇau pratiṣṭhāpya evaṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ dharmaṃ deśayiṣyati yo 'sau bhikṣavo varṣaśatāyuṣi prajāyāṃ śākyamunir nāma śāstā loka utpannastasyāyaṃ śrāvakaḥ kāśyapo nāmnā alpecchānāṃ saṃtuṣṭānāṃ dhūtaguṇavādināmagro nirdiṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 123]
śākyamuneḥ parinirvṛtasyānena śāsanasaṃgītiḥ kṛtā iti | [Divyāv, 3 124]
te dṛṣṭvā saṃvegamāpatsyante kathamidānīmīdṛśenātmabhāvenedṛśā guṇagaṇā adhigatā iti | [Divyāv, 3 125]
te tenaiva saṃvegenārhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyanti | [Divyāv, 3 126]
ṣaṇṇavatikoṭyo 'rhatāṃ bhaviṣyanti dhūtaguṇasākṣātkṛtāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 127]
yaṃ ca saṃvegamāpatsyante tatrāsau yūpo vilayaṃ gamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 128]
ko bhadanta hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo dvayo ratnayoryugapalloke prādurbhāvāya bhagavānāha praṇidhānavaśāt | [Divyāv, 3 129]
kutra bhagavan praṇidhānaṃ kṛtam | [Divyāv, 3 130]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani madhyadeśe vāsavo nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati ṛddhaṃ sphītaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 3 131]
tasya sadāpuṣpaphalā vṛkṣāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 132]
devaḥ kālena kālaṃ samyagvāridhārāmanuprayacchati | [Divyāv, 3 133]
atīva śasyasampattirbhavati | [Divyāv, 3 134]
uttarāpathe dhanasaṃmato nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati ṛddhaṃ ca sphītaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 3 135]
tasyāpi sadāpuṣpaphalā vṛkṣāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 136]
devaḥ kālena kālaṃ samyagvāridhārāmanuprayacchatīti | [Divyāv, 3 137]
atīva śasyasampattirbhavati | [Divyāv, 3 138]
yāvadapareṇa samayena vāsavasya rājñaḥ putro jāto ratnapratyuptayā śikhayā | [Divyāv, 3 139]
tasya vistareṇa jātimahaṃ kṛtvā ratnaśikhīti nāmadheyaṃ vyavasthāpitam | [Divyāv, 3 140]
so 'pareṇa samayena jīrṇāturamṛtasaṃdarśanādudvigno vanaṃ saṃśritaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 141]
yasminneva divase vanaṃ saṃśritastasminneva divase 'nuttaraṃ jñānamadhigatam | [Divyāv, 3 142]
tasya ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddha iti saṃjñodapādi | [Divyāv, 3 143]
athāpareṇa samayena dhanasaṃmato rājā upariprāsādatalagato 'mātyagaṇaparivṛtastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 3 144]
so 'mātyānāmantrayate bhavantaḥ kasyacidanyasyāpi rājño rājyamevamṛddhaṃ ca sphītaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 3 145]
sadāpuṣpaphalā vṛkṣāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 146]
devaḥ kālena kālaṃ samyagvāridhārāmanuprayacchatīti | [Divyāv, 3 147]
atīva śasyasampattirbhavati yathā asmākamiti madhyadeśād vaṇijaḥ paṇyamādāyottarāpathaṃ gatāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 148]
te kathayanti asti deva madhyadeśe vāsavo nāma rājā iti | [Divyāv, 3 149]
sahaśravaṇādeva dhanasaṃmatasya rājño 'marṣa utpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 150]
sa saṃjātāmarṣo 'mātyānāmantrayate saṃnāhayantu bhavantaścaturaṅgaṃ balakāyam | [Divyāv, 3 151]
rāṣṭrāpamardanamasya kariṣyāma iti | [Divyāv, 3 152]
tato dhanasaṃmato rājā caturaṅgaṃ balakāyaṃ saṃnāhya hastikāyamaśvakāyaṃ rathakāyaṃ pattikāyaṃ madhyadeśamāgatya gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe kūle 'vasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 153]
aśrauṣīdvāsavo rājā dhanasaṃmato rājā caturaṅgaṃ balakāyaṃ saṃnāhya hastikāyamaśvakāyaṃ rathakāyaṃ pattikāyaṃ madhyadeśamāgatya gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe kūle 'vasthita iti | [Divyāv, 3 154]
śrutvā ca punaḥ so 'pi caturaṅgaṃ balakāyaṃ saṃnāhya hastikāyamaśvakāyaṃ rathakāyaṃ pattikāyaṃ gaṅgāyā uttare kūle 'vasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 155]
atha ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhastayorvinayakālaṃ jñātvā nadyā gaṅgāyāstīre rātriṃ vāsamupagataḥ | [Divyāv, 3 156]
ratnaśikhinā samyaksambuddhena laukikaṃ cittamutpāditam | [Divyāv, 3 157]
dharmatā khalu yadā buddhā bhagavanto laukikaṃ cittamutpādayanti tasmin samaye śakrabrahmādayo devā bhagavataścetasā cittamājānanti | [Divyāv, 3 158]
atha śakrabrahmādayo devā yena ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 159]
upasaṃkramya ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 3 160]
teṣāṃ varṇānubhāvena mahānudārāvabhāsaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 161]
dhanasaṃmatena rājñā dṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 162]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaramātyān pṛcchati kimayaṃ bhavanto vāsavasya rājño vijite mahānudārāvabhāsaḥ te kathayanti deva vāsavasya rājño vijite ratnaśikhī nāma samyaksambuddha utpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 163]
tasya śakrabrahmādayo devā darśanāyopasaṃkramanti | [Divyāv, 3 164]
tenaivodārāvabhāsaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 165]
maharddhiko 'sau mahānubhāvaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 166]
tasyāyamanubhāva iti | [Divyāv, 3 167]
dhanasaṃmato rājā kathayati bhavantaḥ yasya vijite īdṛśaṃ dvipādakaṃ puṇyakṣetramutpannam yaṃ śakrabrahmādayo 'pi devā darśanāyopasaṃkrāmanti tasyāhaṃ kīdṛśamanarthaṃ kariṣyāmi tena tasya dūto 'nupreṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 168]
vayasyāgaccha | [Divyāv, 3 169]
na te 'haṃ kiṃcit kariṣyāmi iti | [Divyāv, 3 170]
puṇyamaheśākhyastvam yasya vijite dvipādakaṃ puṇyakṣetraṃ ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddho 'yam | [Divyāv, 3 171]
śakrabrahmādayo devā darśanāyopasaṃkrāmanti | [Divyāv, 3 172]
kiṃtu kaṇṭhāśleṣaṃ te dattvā gamiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 3 173]
evamāvayoḥ parasparaṃ cittasaumanasyaṃ bhavatīti | [Divyāv, 3 174]
vāsavo rājā viśvāsaṃ na gacchati | [Divyāv, 3 175]
sa yena ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 176]
upasaṃkramya ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 177]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇo vāsavo rājā ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhamidamavocat mama bhadanta dhanasaṃmatena rājñā saṃdiṣṭam priyavayasyāgaccha na te 'haṃ kiṃcit kariṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 3 178]
kaṇṭhāśleṣaṃ dattvā gamiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 3 179]
evamāvayoḥ parasparaṃ cittasaumanasyaṃ bhavatīti | [Divyāv, 3 180]
tatra mayā kathaṃ pratipattavyam ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhaḥ kathayati gaccha mahārāja śobhanaṃ bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 181]
bhagavan kiṃ mayā tasya pādayor nipatitavyam mahārāja balaśreṣṭhā hi rājānaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 182]
atha vāsavo rājā ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā utthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 184]
yena dhanasaṃmato rājā tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 185]
upasaṃkramya dhanasaṃmatasya rājñaḥ pādayor nipatitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 186]
tato dhanasaṃmatena rājñā kaṇṭhe śleṣaṃ dattvā viśvāsamutpādya preṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 187]
atha vāsavo rājā yena ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 188]
upasaṃkramya ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 189]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇo vāsavo rājā ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhamidamavocat kasya bhadanta sarve rājānaḥ pādayor nipatanti rājño mahārāja cakravartinaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 190]
atha vāsavo rājā utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena ratnaśikhī tathāgataḥ samyaksambuddhastenāñjaliṃ praṇamya ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhamidamavocat adhivāsayatu me bhagavāñ śvo 'ntargṛhe bhaktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena | [Divyāv, 3 191]
atha vāsavo rājā tāmeva rātriṃ śuci praṇītaṃ khādanīyaṃ bhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyamevotthāya āsanāni prajñāpya udakamaṇīn pratiṣṭhāpya ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya dūtena kālamārocayati samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyate iti | [Divyāv, 3 192]
atha ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣusaṃghaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena rājño vāsavasya bhaktābhisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 193]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 194]
atha rājā vāsavo ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpayati saṃpravārayati | [Divyāv, 3 195]
anekaparyāyeṇa śucinā khādanīyena bhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpya saṃpravārya bhagavantaṃ ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastamapanītapātraṃ pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ anenāhaṃ bhadanta kuśalamūlena rājā syāṃ cakravartīti | [Divyāv, 3 196]
tatsamanantaraṃ ca śaṅkha āpūritaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 197]
tato ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddho vāsavaṃ rājānamidamavocat bhaviṣyasi mahārāja aśītivarṣasahasrāyuṣi prajāyāṃ śaṅkho nāma rājā cakravartīti | [Divyāv, 3 198]
tata uccaśabdo mahāśabdo jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 199]
dhanasaṃmato rājā kolāhalaśabdaṃ śrutvā amātyān pṛcchati kimeṣa bhavanto vāsavasya rājño vijite kolāhalaśabdaḥ śrūyate iti tairāgamya niveditam deva ratnaśikhinā samyaksambuddhena vāsavo rājā cakravartirājye vyākṛta iti janakāyo hṛṣṭatuṣṭapramuditaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 200]
tena kolāhalaśabdo jāta iti | [Divyāv, 3 201]
atha dhanasaṃmato rājā yena ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 202]
upasaṃkramya ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 203]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇo dhanasaṃmato rājā ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhamidamavocat kasya bhadanta sarve cakravartinaḥ pādayor nipatanti tathāgatasya mahārāja arhataḥ samyaksambuddhasya | [Divyāv, 3 204]
atha dhanasaṃmato rājā utthāyāsanādekāṃsam uttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhastenāñjalim praṇamya ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhamidamavocat adhivāsayatu me bhagavāñ śvo 'ntargṛhe bhaktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena | [Divyāv, 3 205]
adhivāsayati ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddho dhanasaṃmatasya rājño 'pi tūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 3 206]
atha dhanasaṃmato rājā ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanaṃ viditvā ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasyāntikāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 207]
atha dhanasaṃmato rājā tāmeva rātriṃ śuci praṇītaṃ khādanīyaṃ bhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyamevotthāya āsanāni prajñapya udakamaṇīn pratiṣṭhāpya ratnaśikhinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya dūtena kālamārocayati samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyate iti | [Divyāv, 3 208]
atha ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena dhanasaṃmatasya rājño bhaktābhisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 209]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 3 210]
atha dhanasaṃmato rājā sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ tatpramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena svahastena saṃtarpayati saṃpravārayati | [Divyāv, 3 211]
anekaparyāyeṇa śucinā praṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena svahastena saṃtarpya saṃpravārya ratnaśikhinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastamapanītapātraṃ pādayor nipatya sarvamimaṃ lokaṃ maitreṇāṃśena sphuritvā praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena śāstā loke bhaveyaṃ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddha iti | [Divyāv, 3 212]
ratnaśikhī samyaksambuddhaḥ kathayati bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ mahārāja aśītivarṣasahasrāyuṣi prajāyāṃ maitreyo nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddha iti | [Divyāv, 3 213]
tatpraṇidhānavaśād dvayo ratnayorloke prādurbhāvo bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 3 214]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 3 215]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 3 216]
{Divyāv, 4}
bhagavān nyagrodhikāmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 1]
atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya nyagrodhikāṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat | [Divyāv, 4 2]
kapilavastuno brāhmaṇasya dārikā nyagrodhikāyāṃ niviṣṭā | [Divyāv, 4 3]
adrākṣīt sā brāhmaṇadārikā bhagavantaṃ dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam aśītyānuvyañjanairvirājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamamiva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [Divyāv, 4 4]
sahadarśanādasyā etadabhavat ayaṃ sa bhagavāñ śākyakulanandanaścakravartikulād rājyamapahāya sphītamantaḥpuraṃ sphītāni ca kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇi pravrajita idānīṃ bhikṣāmaṭate | [Divyāv, 4 5]
yadi mamāntikātsaktukabhikṣāṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt ahamasmai dadyāmiti | [Divyāv, 4 6]
tato bhagavatā tasyāścetasā cittamājñāya pātramupanāmitam yadi te bhagini parityaktam ākīryatāmasmin pātra iti | [Divyāv, 4 7]
tato bhūyasyā mātrayā tasyāḥ prasāda utpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 8]
jānāti me bhagavāṃścetasā cittamiti viditvā tīvreṇa prasādena bhagavate saktubhikṣāṃ dattavatī | [Divyāv, 4 9]
tato bhagavatā smitamupadarśitam | [Divyāv, 4 10]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātāḥ puṣparāgapadmarāgavajravaiḍūryamusāragalvārkalohitakādakṣiṇāvartaśaṅkhaśilāpravālajātarūparajatavarṇā arciṣo mukhānniścārya kāścidadhastādgacchanti kāścidupariṣṭādgacchanti | [Divyāv, 4 11]
yā adhastādgacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanamavīcimarbudaṃ nirarbudamaṭaṭaṃ hahavahuhuvamutpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmamavīciparyantān narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakāsteṣu śītībhūtvā nipatanti ye śītanarakāsteṣūṣṇībhūtvā nipatanti | [Divyāv, 4 12]
tenānugatāsteṣāṃ sattvānāṃ tasmin kṣaṇe kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ te pratiprasrabhyante | [Divyāv, 4 13]
teṣāmevaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaścyutā āhosvidanyatropapannā iti | [Divyāv, 4 14]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavānnirmitam visarjayati | [Divyāv, 4 15]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati na hyeva vayaṃ bhavanta itaścyutāḥ nāpyanyatropapannā iti | [Divyāv, 4 16]
te nirmite cittamabhiprasādya tannarakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisaṃdhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 4 17]
yā upariṣṭādgacchanti tāścāturmahārājikān devān gatvā trāyastriṃśān yāmāṃstuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino devān brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhānābhāsvarān parīttaśubhānapramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnānanabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhānatapān sudṛśān sudarśānakaniṣṭhaparyantān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyamanātmetyudghoṣayanti | [Divyāv, 4 18]
gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [Divyāv, 4 19]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [Divyāv, 4 20.1]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāramiva kuñjaraḥ | [Divyāv, 4 20.2]
yo hyasmin dharmavinaye apramattaścariṣyati | [Divyāv, 4 21.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 4 21.2]
atha tā arciṣastrisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātumanvāhiṇḍya bhagavantameva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddhā gacchanti | [Divyāv, 4 22]
tadyadi bhagavānatītaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 23]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastādantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 24]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 25]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyāmantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 26]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 27]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunorantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 28]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 29]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 30]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 31]
pratyekabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyāmantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 32]
yadi anuttarāṃ samyaksambodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 4 33]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtyorṇāyāmantarhitāḥ | [Divyāv, 4 34]
athāyuṣmānānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [Divyāv, 4 35]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarānniṣkramitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 36.1]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantāt divākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [Divyāv, 4 36.2]
gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 4 37]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagatyuttamahetubhūtāḥ | [Divyāv, 4 38.1]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitamupadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 38.2]
tatkālaṃ svayamadhigamya dhīrabuddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [Divyāv, 4 39.1]
dhīrābhirmunivṛṣa vāgbhiruttamābhirutpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [Divyāv, 4 39.2]
nākasmāllavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitamupadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [Divyāv, 4 40.1]
yasyārthe smitamupadarśayanti dhīrāstaṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [Divyāv, 4 40.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 4 41]
bhagavānāha evametadānanda evametat | [Divyāv, 4 42]
nāhetupratyayam ānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksambuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [Divyāv, 4 43]
dṛṣṭā tavaiṣā sā ānanda brāhmaṇadārikā yayā prasādajātayā mahyaṃ saktubhikṣānupradattā dṛṣṭā bhadanta | [Divyāv, 4 44]
asāvānanda brāhmaṇadārikā anena kuśalamūlena trayodaśa kalpān vinipātaṃ na gamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 4 45]
kiṃ tarhi devāṃśca manuṣyāṃśca saṃvācya saṃsṛtya paścime bhave paścime nikete paścime samucchraye paścima ātmabhāvapratilambhe supraṇihito nāma pratyekabuddho bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 4 46]
sāmantakena śabdo visṛtaḥ amukayā brāhmaṇadārikayā prasādajātayā bhagavate saktubhikṣā pratipāditā sā bhagavatā pratyekāyāṃ bodhau vyākṛteti | [Divyāv, 4 47]
tasyāśca svāmī puṣpasamidhāmarthāyāraṇyaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 4 48]
tena śrutaṃ mama patnyā śramaṇāya gautamāya saktubhikṣā pratipāditā sā ca śramaṇena gautamena pratyekāyāṃ bodhau vyākṛtā iti | [Divyāv, 4 49]
śrutvā punaḥ saṃjātāmarṣo yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 50]
bhagavatā sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃmodanīṃ saṃrañjanīṃ vividhāṃ kathāṃ vyatisārya bhagavantamidamavocat agamadbhavān gautamo 'smākaṃ niveśanam agamaṃ brāhmaṇa satyaṃ bhavate tayā mama patnyā saktubhikṣā pratipāditā sā ca tvayā pratyekāyāṃ bodhau vyākṛtā iti satyaṃ brāhmaṇa | [Divyāv, 4 51]
tvaṃ gautama cakravartirājyamapahāya pravrajitaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 52]
kathaṃ nāma tvametarhi saktubhikṣāhetoḥ samprajānan mṛṣāvādaṃ sambhāṣase kaste śraddhāsyati iyatpramāṇasya bījasyeyat phalamiti tena hi brāhmaṇa tvāmeva prakṣyāmi yathā te kṣamate tathaivaṃ vyākuru | [Divyāv, 4 53]
kiṃ manyase brāhmaṇa asti kaścittvayā āścaryādbhuto dharmo dṛṣṭas tiṣṭhantu tāvat bho gautama anye āścaryādbhutā dharmāḥ | [Divyāv, 4 54]
yo mayā asyāmeva nyagrodhikāyāmāścaryādbhuto dharmo dṛṣṭaḥ sa tāvacchrūyatām | [Divyāv, 4 55]
asyāṃ bho gautama nyagrodhikāyāṃ pūrveṇa nyagrodho vṛkṣo yasya nāmneyaṃ nyagrodhikā tasyādhastāt pañca śakaṭaśatāni asaṃsaktāni tiṣṭhanti anyonyāsambādhamānāni | [Divyāv, 4 56]
kiyatpramāṇaṃ tasya nyagrodhasya phalam kiyat tāvat kedāramātram | [Divyāv, 4 57]
no bho gautama kiliñjamātram | [Divyāv, 4 58]
tailikacakramātram | [Divyāv, 4 59]
śakaṭacakramātram | [Divyāv, 4 60]
gopiṭakamātram | [Divyāv, 4 61]
bilvamātram | [Divyāv, 4 62]
kapitthamātram no bho gautama sarṣapacatuṣṭayabhāgamātram | [Divyāv, 4 63]
kaste śraddhāsyati iyatpramāṇasya bījasyāyaṃ mahāvṛkṣo nirvṛtta iti śraddadhātu me bhavān gautamo mā vā | [Divyāv, 4 64]
naitat pratyakṣaṃ kṣetram | [Divyāv, 4 65]
tāvadbho gautama nirupahataṃ snigdhamadhuramṛttikāpradeśaṃ bījaṃ ca navasāraṃ sukhāropitam | [Divyāv, 4 66]
kālena ca kālaṃ devo vṛṣyate tenāyaṃ mahānyagrodhavṛkṣo 'bhinirvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 67]
atha bhagavānasminnutpanne gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 4 68]
yathā kṣetre ca bījena pratyakṣastvamiha dvija | [Divyāv, 4 69.1]
evaṃ karmavipākeṣu pratyakṣā hi tathāgatāḥ | [Divyāv, 4 69.2]
yathā tvayā brāhmaṇa dṛṣṭametadalpaṃ ca bījaṃ sumahāṃśca vṛkṣaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 70.1]
evaṃ mayā brāhmaṇa dṛṣṭametat alpaṃ ca bījaṃ mahatī ca saṃpat | [Divyāv, 4 70.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 4 71]
tato bhagavatā mukhāt jihvāṃ nirnamayya sarvaṃ mukhamaṇḍalamācchāditam yāvat keśaparyantam upādāya sa ca brāhmaṇo 'bhihitaḥ kiṃ manyase brāhmaṇa yasya mukhāt jihvāṃ niścārya sarvam mukhamaṇḍalamācchādayati api tvasau cakravartirājyaśatasahasrahetorapi samprajānan mṛṣāvādaṃ bhāṣeta no bho gautama | [Divyāv, 4 72]
tato 'nveva gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 4 73]
apyeva hi syādanṛtābhidhāyinī mameha jihvārjavasatyavāditā | [Divyāv, 4 74.1]
tadevametanna yathā hi brāhmaṇa tathāgato 'smītyavagantumarhasi | [Divyāv, 4 74.2]
atha sa brāhmaṇo 'bhiprasannaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 75]
tato 'sya bhagavatā āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī caturāryasatyasamprativedhikī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā brāhmaṇena viṃśatiśikharasamudgataṃ satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ jñānavajreṇa bhittvā srotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam atikrānto 'haṃ bhadanta atikrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 76]
eṣo 'haṃ bhagavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi dharmaṃ ca bhikṣusaṃghaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 4 77]
upāsakaṃ ca māṃ dhāraya adyāgreṇa yāvajjīvaṃ prāṇopetaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatamabhiprasannam | [Divyāv, 4 78]
atha sa brāhmaṇo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhinandyānumodya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā utthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 4 79]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 4 80]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 4 81]
{Divyāv, 5}
atha bhagavān hastināpuramanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 1]
anyatamo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ dūrādeva dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam aśītyānuvyañjanairvirājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamamiva parvataṃ samantato bhadrakaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca punarbhagavantamabhigamya gāthābhiḥ stotumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 2]
suvarṇavarṇo nayanābhirāmaḥ prītyākaraḥ sarvaguṇairupetaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 3.1]
devātidevo naradamyasārathis tīrṇo 'si pāraṃ bhavasāgarasya | [Divyāv, 5 3.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 5 4]
tato bhagavatā smitamupadarśitam | [Divyāv, 5 5]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti pūrvavad yāvad bhagavata ūrṇāyāmantarhitāḥ | [Divyāv, 5 6]
athāyuṣmānānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [Divyāv, 5 7]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarānniṣkramitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 8.1]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantāddivākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [Divyāv, 5 8.2]
gāthāṃ ca bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 5 9]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagatyuttamahetubhūtāḥ | [Divyāv, 5 10.1]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitamupadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 10.2]
tatkālaṃ svayamadhigamya dhīrabuddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [Divyāv, 5 11.1]
dhīrābhirmunivṛṣa vāgbhiruttamābhirutpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [Divyāv, 5 11.2]
nākasmāllavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitamupadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [Divyāv, 5 12.1]
yasyārthe smitamupadarśayanti dhīrāstaṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [Divyāv, 5 12.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 5 13]
bhagavānāha evametadānanda evametat | [Divyāv, 5 14]
nāhetupratyayamānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksambuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [Divyāv, 5 15]
dṛṣṭaste ānanda brāhmaṇo yena tathāgato gāthayā abhiṣṭutaḥ dṛṣṭo bhadanta | [Divyāv, 5 16]
asau anena kuśalamūlena viṃśatikalpaṃ vinipātaṃ na gamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 5 17]
kiṃtu devāṃśca manuṣyāṃśca gatvā saṃsṛtya paścime nikete paścime samucchraye paścime ātmabhāvapratilambhe stavārho nāma pratyekabuddho bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 5 18]
bhikṣavaḥ saṃśayajātāḥ sarvasaṃśayacchettāraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ pṛcchanti paśya bhadanta anena brāhmaṇena bhagavānekayā gāthayā stuto bhagavatā ca pratyekāyāṃ bodhau vyākṛta iti | [Divyāv, 5 19]
bhagavānāha na bhikṣava etarhi yathā atīte 'dhvani anenāhamekayā gāthayā stutaḥ mayā ca pañcasu grāmavareṣu pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 20]
tacchṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye | [Divyāv, 5 21]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani vārāṇasyāṃ nagaryāṃ brahmadatto nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati ṛddhaṃ ca sphītaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 5 22]
sa cātīva kavipriyaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 23]
vārāṇasyāmanyatamo brāhmaṇaḥ kaviḥ | [Divyāv, 5 24]
sa brāhmaṇyocyate brāhmaṇa śītakālo vartate | [Divyāv, 5 25]
gaccha asya rājñaḥ kaccidanukūlaṃ bhāṣitaṃ kṛtvā kadācit kiṃcit śītatrāṇaṃ saṃpadyata iti | [Divyāv, 5 26]
sa samprasthitaḥ yāvadrājā hastiskandhārūḍho nirgacchati | [Divyāv, 5 27]
sa brāhmaṇaḥ saṃlakṣayati kiṃ tāvadrājānaṃ stunomi āhosviddhastināgamiti | [Divyāv, 5 28]
tasyaitadabhavat ayaṃ hastināgaḥ sarvalokasya priyo manāpaśca | [Divyāv, 5 29]
tiṣṭhatu tāvadrājā hastināgaṃ tāvadabhiṣṭaumīti | [Divyāv, 5 30]
gāthāṃ ca bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 5 31]
airāvaṇasyākṛtitulyadeho rūpopapanno varalakṣaṇaiśca | [Divyāv, 5 32.1]
lakṣe praśasto 'si mahāgajendra varṇapramāṇena surūparūpa | [Divyāv, 5 32.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 5 33]
tato rājā abhiprasanno gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 5 34]
yo me gajendro dayito manāpaḥ prītiprado dṛṣṭiharo narāṇām | [Divyāv, 5 35.1]
taṃ bhāṣase varṇapadāni tasya dadāmi te grāmavarāṇi pañca | [Divyāv, 5 35.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 5 36]
kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau hastināgaḥ ahameva tena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 5 37]
tadāpyahamanenaikayā gāthayā stutaḥ mayā cāyaṃ pañcagrāmavareṣu pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 5 38]
etarhi anenaikagāthayā stutaḥ mayāpi cāyaṃ pratyekabodhau vyākṛta iti | [Divyāv, 5 39]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 5 40]
āttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 5 41]
{Divyāv, 6}
bhagavāñśrughnāmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 1]
śrughnāyāmindro nāma brāhmaṇaḥ prativasati | [Divyāv, 6 2]
sa ca rūpayauvanaśrutamanuprāpto na mamāsti kaścit tulya ityatīva vikatthate | [Divyāv, 6 3]
bhagavāṃścānyatamasmin pradeśe purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇo dharmaṃ deśayati | [Divyāv, 6 4]
aśrauṣīdindro nāma brāhmaṇaḥ śramaṇo gautamaḥ śrughnāmanuprāpta iti | [Divyāv, 6 5]
tasyaitadabhavat śramaṇo gautamaḥ śrūyate 'bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādika iti | [Divyāv, 6 6]
gacchāmi paśyāmi kiṃ mamāntikādabhirūpatara āhosvinneti | [Divyāv, 6 7]
sa nirgato yāvat paśyati bhagavantaṃ dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtamaśītyā cānuvyañjanairvirājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamamiva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [Divyāv, 6 8]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarasyaitadabhavat kiṃ cāpi śramaṇo gautamo mamāntikādabhirūpataraḥ noccatara iti | [Divyāv, 6 9]
sa bhagavato mūrdhānamavalokayitumārabdho yāvanna paśyati | [Divyāv, 6 10]
sa ūrdhvataraṃ pradeśamārūḍhaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 11]
tatra bhagavānindraṃ brāhmaṇamāmantrayate alaṃ brāhmaṇa khedamāpatsyase | [Divyāv, 6 12]
yadi sumerumūrdhānamapi abhiruhya tathāgatasya mūrdhānamavalokayasi tathā sutarāṃ khedamāpatsyase na ca drakṣyasi | [Divyāv, 6 13]
api tu na tvayā śrutaṃ sasurāsurajagadanavalokitamūrdhāno buddhā bhagavanta iti api tu yadīpsasi tathāgatasya śarīrapramāṇaṃ draṣṭum tava gṛhe 'gnihotrakuṇḍaṃ tasyādhastādgośīrṣacandanamayī yaṣṭirupatiṣṭhate tāmuddhṛtya māpaya | [Divyāv, 6 14]
tattathāgatamātāpaitṛkasyāśrayasya pramāṇamiti | [Divyāv, 6 15]
indro brāhmaṇaḥ saṃlakṣayati etadasyāścaryaṃ na kadācinmayā śrutam gacchāmi paśyāmīti | [Divyāv, 6 16]
tvaritatvaritagato 'gnihotrakuṇḍakasyādhastāt khanitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 17]
sarvaṃ tathaiva | [Divyāv, 6 18]
so 'bhiprasannaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 19]
sa saṃlakṣayati nūnaṃ śramaṇo gautamaḥ sarvajñaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 20]
gacchāmi paryupāsitumiti | [Divyāv, 6 21]
sa prasādajāto yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 22]
upasaṃkramya bhagavatā sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃmodanīṃ saṃrañjanīṃ vividhāṃ kathāṃ vyatisārya ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 23]
tato bhagavatā āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī caturāryasatyasamprativedhikī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yathendreṇa brāhmaṇena viṃśatiśikharasamudgataṃ satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ jñānavajreṇa bhittvā srotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 6 24]
sa dṛṣṭasatyaḥ kathayati atikrānto 'haṃ bhadanta atikrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 25]
eṣo 'haṃ bhagavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchāmi dharmaṃ ca bhikṣusaṃghaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 6 26]
upāsakaṃ ca māṃ dhāraya adyāgreṇa yāvajjīvaṃ prāṇopetaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatam | [Divyāv, 6 27]
abhiprasanno 'thendro brāhmaṇa utthāyāsanāt ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocat yadi bhagavānanujānīyāt ahaṃ gośīrṣacandanamayyā yaṣṭyā mahaṃ prajñapayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 6 28]
bhagavānāha gaccha brāhmaṇa anujñātaṃ prajñapayasi | [Divyāv, 6 29]
tatastena viviktāvakāśe mahatā satkāreṇāsau yaṣṭirucchrāpitā mahaśca prajñapitaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 30]
anyairapi brāhmaṇagṛhapatibhiḥ kuśalamadhiṣṭhānāya bhavatviti viditvā kulā baddhā | [Divyāv, 6 31]
indreṇa brāhmaṇena yaṣṭyā mahaḥ prajñapita iti indramaha indramaha iti saṃjñā saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 6 32]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate āgamaya ānanda yena toyikā | [Divyāv, 6 33]
evaṃ bhadanteti āyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt | [Divyāv, 6 34]
atha bhagavāṃstoyikāmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 35]
tasmiṃśca pradeśe brāhmaṇo lāṅgalaṃ vāhayati | [Divyāv, 6 36]
athāsau dadarśa buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtamaśītyā cānuvyañjanairvirājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamamiva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [Divyāv, 6 37]
dṛṣṭvā saṃlakṣayati yadi bhagavantaṃ gautamamupetyābhivādayiṣyāmi karmaparihāṇirme bhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 6 38]
atha nopetyābhivādayiṣyāmi puṇyaparihāṇirbhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 6 39]
tat ko 'sau upāyaḥ syāt yena me karmaparihāṇir na syānnāpi puṇyaparihāṇiriti | [Divyāv, 6 40]
tasya buddhirutpannā atrastha evābhivādanaṃ karomi | [Divyāv, 6 41]
evaṃ na karmaparihāṇir na puṇyaparihāṇiriti | [Divyāv, 6 42]
tena yathāgṛhītayaiva pratodayaṣṭyā tatrasthenaivābhivādanaṃ kṛtam abhivādaye buddhaṃ bhagavantamiti | [Divyāv, 6 43]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate bhavakṣayakaraḥ kṣaṇam eṣa brāhmaṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 44]
sacedasyaivaṃ samyaksampratyayajñānadarśanaṃ pravartate etasmin pradeśe kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasyāvikopito 'sthisaṃghātastiṣṭhatīty ahamanenopakrameṇa vandito bhaveyam evamanena dvābhyāṃ samyaksambuddhābhyāṃ vandanā kṛtā bhavet | [Divyāv, 6 45]
tatkasya hetoḥ asminnānanda pradeśe kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasyāvikopito 'sthisaṃghātastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 6 46]
athāyuṣmānānando laghulaghveva caturguṇamuttarāsaṅgaṃ prajñapya bhagavantamidamavocat niṣīdatu bhagavān prajñapta evāsane | [Divyāv, 6 47]
evamayaṃ pṛthivīpradeśo dvābhyāṃ samyaksambuddhābhyāṃ paribhukto bhaviṣyati yacca kāśyapena samyaksambuddhena yaccaitarhi bhagavatā iti | [Divyāv, 6 48]
niṣaṇṇo bhagavān prajñapta evāsane | [Divyāv, 6 49]
niṣadya bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma icchatha yūyaṃ bhikṣavaḥ kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasya śarīrasaṃghātam avikopitaṃ draṣṭum etasya bhagavan kālaḥ etasya sugata samayaḥ yaṃ bhagavān bhikṣūṇāṃ kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasyāvikopitaṃ śarīrasaṃghātamupadarśayet | [Divyāv, 6 50]
dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaścittamabhiprasādayiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 6 51]
tato bhagavatā laukikaṃ cittamutpāditam | [Divyāv, 6 52]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavanto laukikaṃ cittamutpādayanti tasmin samaye kuntapipīlikā api prāṇino bhagavataścetasā cittamājānanti | [Divyāv, 6 53]
nāgāḥ saṃlakṣayanti kiṃ kāraṇaṃ bhagavatā laukikacittamutpāditamiti paśyanti kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasya śarīrasaṃghātamavikopitaṃ draṣṭukāma iti | [Divyāv, 6 54]
tatastaiḥ kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasyāvikopitaśarīrasaṃghāta ucchrāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 55]
tatra bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma udgṛhṇīta bhikṣavo nimittam | [Divyāv, 6 56]
antardhāsyati | [Divyāv, 6 57]
antarhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 58]
rājñā prasenajitā śrutaṃ bhagavatā śrāvakāṇāṃ darśanāyāvikopitaṃ kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasya śarīrasaṃghātaṃ samucchritamiti | [Divyāv, 6 59]
śrutvā ca punaḥ kutūhalajātaḥ sahāntaḥpureṇa kumārairamātyairbhaṭabalāgrair naigamajānapadaiśca draṣṭuṃ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 60]
evaṃ virūḍhakaḥ anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatiḥ ṛṣidattaḥ purāṇaḥ sthapatiḥ viśākhā mṛgāramātā anekāni ca prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi kutūhalajātāni draṣṭuṃ samprasthitāni pūrvakaiśca kuśalamūlaiḥ saṃcodyamānāni | [Divyāv, 6 61]
yāvadasau antarhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 62]
taiḥ śrutam antarhito 'sau bhagavataḥ kāśyapasya samyaksambuddhasya śarīrasaṃghātadhātur avikopita iti | [Divyāv, 6 63]
śrutvā ca punasteṣāṃ duḥkhadaurmanasyamutpannam vṛthā asmākamāgamanaṃ jātamiti | [Divyāv, 6 64]
athānyatamena copāsakena sa pradeśaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 65]
evaṃ ca cetasā cittamabhisaṃskṛtam asmānme padāvihārāt kiyat puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 6 66]
atha bhagavāṃstasya mahājanakāyasyāvipratisārasaṃjananārthaṃ tasya copāsakasya cetasā cittamājñāya gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 6 67]
śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇaniṣkā jāmbūnadā nāsya samā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 6 68.1]
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacittaḥ padāvihāraṃ prakaroti vidvān | [Divyāv, 6 68.2]
anyatamena upāsakena tasmin pradeśe mṛttikāpiṇḍo dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 69]
evaṃ ca cittamabhisaṃskṛtam padāvihārasya tāvadiyat puṇyamākhyātaṃ bhagavatā anyatra | [Divyāv, 6 70]
mṛttikāpiṇḍasya kiyat puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti atha bhagavāṃstasyāpi cetasā cittamājñāya bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 6 71]
śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇaniṣkā jāmbūnadā nāsya samā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 6 72.1]
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitta āropayenmṛttikapiṇḍamekam | [Divyāv, 6 72.2]
tataḥ śrutvā anekaiḥ prāṇiśatasahasrairmṛttikāpiṇḍasamāropaṇaṃ kṛtam | [Divyāv, 6 73]
aparaistatra muktapuṣpāṇyavakṣiptāni evaṃ ca cittamabhisaṃskṛtam padāvihārasya mṛttikāpiṇḍasya ceyat puṇyamuktaṃ bhagavatā asmākaṃ tu muktapuṣpāṇāṃ kiyat puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti atha bhagavāṃsteṣāmapi cetasā cittamājñāya gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 6 74]
śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇaniṣkā jāmbūnadā nāsya samā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 6 75]
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacittaḥ āropayenmuktasupuṣparāśim | [Divyāv, 6 76]
aparaistatra mālāvihāraḥ kṛtaḥ cittaṃ cābhisaṃskṛtam muktapuṣpāṇāṃ bhagavatā iyat puṇyamuktam | [Divyāv, 6 77]
asmākaṃ mālāvihārasya kiyatpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti atha bhagavāṃsteṣāmapi cetasā cittamājñāya gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 6 78]
śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇavāhā jāmbūnadā nāsya samā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 6 79.1]
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitto mālāvihāraṃ prakaroti vidvān | [Divyāv, 6 79.2]
aparaistatra pradīpamālā dattā cittaṃ cābhisaṃskṛtam mālāvihārasya bhagavatā iyat puṇyamuktam | [Divyāv, 6 80]
asmākaṃ pradīpadānasya kiyatpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti atha bhagavāṃsteṣāmapi cetasā cittamājñāya gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 6 81]
śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇakoṭyo jāmbūnadā nāsya samā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 6 82.1]
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacittaḥ pradīpadānaṃ prakaroti vidvān | [Divyāv, 6 82.2]
aparaistatra gandhābhiṣeko dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 83]
evaṃ cetasā cittamabhisaṃskṛtam pradīpasya bhagavatā iyat puṇyamuktam | [Divyāv, 6 84]
asmākaṃ gandhābhiṣekasya kiyatpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti atha bhagavāṃsteṣāmapi cetasā cittamājñāya gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 6 85]
śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇarāśayo jāmbūnadā nāsya samā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 6 86.1]
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitto gandhābhiṣekaṃ prakaroti vidvān | [Divyāv, 6 86.2]
aparaistatra chatradhvajapatākāropaṇaṃ kṛtam | [Divyāv, 6 87]
evaṃ ca cetasā cittamājñāya gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 6 88]
tiṣṭhantaṃ pūjayedyaśca yaścāpi parinirvṛtam | [Divyāv, 6 89.1]
samaṃ cittaṃ prasādyeha nāsti puṇyaviśeṣatā | [Divyāv, 6 89.2]
evaṃ hyacintiyā buddhā buddhadharmāpyacintiyā | [Divyāv, 6 90.1]
acintiye prasannānāṃ vipāko 'pi acintiyaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 90.2]
teṣām acintiyānām apratihatadharmacakravartinām | [Divyāv, 6 91.1]
samyaksambuddhānāṃ nālaṃ guṇapāramadhigantum | [Divyāv, 6 91.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 6 92.1]
tato bhagavatā tasya mahājanakāyasya tathāvidhā dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā anekaiḥ prāṇiśatasahasrairmahān viśeṣo 'dhigataḥ | [Divyāv, 6 93]
kaiścicchrāvakabodhau cittānyutpāditāni kaiścit pratyekabodhau kaiścidanuttarāyāṃ samyaksambodhau kaiścinmūrdhāgatāni kaiścinmūrdhānaḥ kaiściduṣṇagatānyāsāditāni kaiścit satyānulomāḥ kṣāntayaḥ kaiścitsrotaāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam kaiścit sakṛdāgāmiphalam kaiścit sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam yadbhūyasā buddhanimnā dharmapravaṇāḥ saṃghaprāgbhārā vyavasthāpitāḥ | [Divyāv, 6 94]
atha anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatirbhagavantamidamavocat yadi bhagavānanujānīyāt atra mahaṃ prajñāpayeyam | [Divyāv, 6 95]
anujānāmi gṛhapate prajñāpayitavyam | [Divyāv, 6 96]
tato 'nāthapiṇḍadena gṛhapatinā mahaḥ prajñāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 6 97]
toyikāmaha iti saṃjñā saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 6 98]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 6 99]
āttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 6 100]
{Divyāv, 7}
atha bhagavān kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ carañ śrāvastīmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 1]
śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [Divyāv, 7 2]
aśrauṣīdanāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatiḥ bhagavān kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ carañ śrāvastīmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 3]
śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍadasyārāma iti | [Divyāv, 7 4]
śrutvā ca punaryena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 5]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 6]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇamanāthapiṇḍadaṃ gṛhapatiṃ bhagavān dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 7 7]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 7 8]
anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatir utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṃgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocat adhivāsayatu me bhagavāñ śvo 'ntargṛhe bhuktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena iti | [Divyāv, 7 9]
adhivāsayati bhagavānanāthapiṇḍadasya gṛhapatestūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 7 10]
anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatirbhagavatas tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavato bhāṣitamabhinandyānumodya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato 'ntikāt prakrānto yena svaniveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 11]
upasaṃkramya dauvārikaṃ puruṣamāmantrayate na tāvadbhoḥ puruṣa tīrthyānāṃ praveśo dātavyo yāvad buddhapramukhena bhikṣusaṃghena bhuktaṃ bhavati | [Divyāv, 7 12]
tataḥ paścādahaṃ tīrthyānāṃ dāsyāmīti | [Divyāv, 7 13]
evamāryeti dauvārikaḥ puruṣo 'nāthapiṇḍadasya gṛhapateḥ pratyaśrauṣīt | [Divyāv, 7 14]
anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatistāmeva rātriṃ śuci praṇītaṃ khādanīyabhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyamevotthāya āsanāni prajñapya udakamaṇīn pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālamārocayati samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyata iti | [Divyāv, 7 15]
