atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena anāthapiṇḍadasya gṛhapaterbhaktābhisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 16]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 17]
atha anāthapiṇḍado gṛhapatiḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpayati saṃpravārayati | [Divyāv, 7 18]
anekaparyāyeṇa śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpya saṃpravārya bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastamapanītapātraṃ nīcataramāsanaṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purastānniṣaṇṇo dharmaśravaṇāya | [Divyāv, 7 19]
athāyuṣmān mahākāśyapo 'nyatamasmādāraṇyakācchayanāsanāt dīrghakeśaśmaśrurlūhacīvaro jetavanaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 7 20]
sa paśyati jetavanaṃ śūnyam | [Divyāv, 7 21]
tenopadhivārikaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kutra buddhapramukho bhikṣusaṃgha iti | [Divyāv, 7 22]
tena samākhyātam anāthapiṇḍadena gṛhapatinopanimantrita iti | [Divyāv, 7 23]
sa saṃlakṣayati gacchāmi tatraiva piṇḍapātaṃ paribhokṣyāmi buddhapramukhaṃ ca bhikṣusaṃghaṃ paryupāsiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 7 24]
so 'nāthapiṇḍadasya gṛhapater niveśanaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 7 25]
ato dauvārikena uktaḥ ārya tiṣṭha mā pravekṣyasi | [Divyāv, 7 26]
kasyārthāya anāthapiṇḍadena gṛhapatinā ājñā dattā mā tāvat tīrthyānāṃ praveśaṃ dāsyasi yāvadbuddhapramukhena bhikṣusaṃghena bhuktam | [Divyāv, 7 27]
tataḥ paścāt tīrthyānāṃ dāsyāmi iti | [Divyāv, 7 28]
athāyuṣmān mahākāśyapaḥ saṃlakṣayati tasya me lābhāḥ sulabdhāḥ yanmāṃ śrāddhā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ śramaṇaśākyaputrīya iti na jānante | [Divyāv, 7 29]
gacchāmi kṛpaṇajanasyānugrahaṃ karomīti viditvā udyānaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 7 30]
sa saṃlakṣayati adya mayā kasyānugrahaḥ kartavya iti | [Divyāv, 7 31]
yāvadanyatamā nagarāvalambikā kuṣṭhābhidrutā sarujārtā pakvagātrā bhikṣāmaṭati | [Divyāv, 7 32]
sa tasyāḥ sakāśamupasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 33]
tasyāśca bhikṣāyāmāyāsaḥ sampannaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 34]
tayā āyuṣmān mahākāśyapo dṛṣṭaḥ kāyaprāsādikaścittaprāsādikaḥ śāntena īryāpathena | [Divyāv, 7 35]
sā saṃlakṣayati nūnaṃ mayā evaṃvidhe dakṣiṇīye kārā kṛtā yena me iyamevaṃrūpā samavasthā | [Divyāv, 7 36]
yadi āryo mahākāśyapo mamāntikādanukampāmupādāya ācāmaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt ahamasmai dadyāmiti | [Divyāv, 7 37]
tata āyuṣmatā mahākāśyapena tasyāścetasā cittamājñāya pātramupanāmitam yadi te bhagini parityaktam dīyatāmasmin pātra iti | [Divyāv, 7 38]
tatastayā cittamabhiprasādya tasmin pātre dattam | [Divyāv, 7 39]
makṣikā ca patitā | [Divyāv, 7 40]
sā tāmapanetumārabdhā | [Divyāv, 7 41]
tasyāstasminnācāme 'ṅguliḥ patitā | [Divyāv, 7 42]
saṃlakṣayati kiṃcāpyāryeṇa mama cittānurakṣayā na choritaḥ api tu na paribhokṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 7 43]
athāyuṣmatā mahākāśyapena tasyāścetasā cittamājñāya tasyā eva pratyakṣamanyatamaṃ kuḍyamūlaṃ niśritya paribhuktam | [Divyāv, 7 44]
sā saṃlakṣayati kiṃcāpi āryeṇa mama cittānurakṣayā paribhuktam nānenāhāreṇāhārakṛtyaṃ kariṣyati iti | [Divyāv, 7 45]
athāyuṣmān mahākāśyapastasyāścittamājñāya tāṃ nagarāvalambikāmidamavocat bhagini prāmodyamutpādayasi ahaṃ tvadīyenāhāreṇa rātriṃdivasamatināmayiṣyāmi iti | [Divyāv, 7 46]
tasyā atīva audbilyamutpannam mamāryeṇa mahākāśyapena piṇḍapātaḥ pratigṛhīta iti | [Divyāv, 7 47]
tata āyuṣmatī mahākāśyape cittamabhiprasādya kālaṃ gatā tuṣite devanikāye upapannā | [Divyāv, 7 48]
sā śakreṇa devendreṇa dṛṣṭā ācāmaṃ pratipādayantī cittamabhiprasādayantī kālaṃ ca kurvāṇā | [Divyāv, 7 49]
no tu dṛṣṭā kutropapannā iti | [Divyāv, 7 50]
sa narakān vyavalokayitumārabdho na paśyati tiryak ca pretaṃ ca manuṣyāṃścāturmahārājikān devāṃstrāyastriṃśān yāvanna paśyati | [Divyāv, 7 51]
tathā hyadhastāddevānāṃ jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate no tūpariṣṭāt | [Divyāv, 7 52]
atha śakro devānāmindro yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 53]
upasaṃkramya gāthābhigītena praśnaṃ papraccha | [Divyāv, 7 54]
carataḥ piṇḍapātaṃ hi kāśyapasya mahātmanaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 55.1]
kutrāsau modate nārī kāśyapācāmadāyikā | [Divyāv, 7 55.2]
bhagavānāha | [Divyāv, 7 56]
tuṣitā nāma te devāḥ sarvakāmasamṛddhayaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 57.1]
yatrāsau modate nārī kāśyapācāmadāyikā | [Divyāv, 7 57.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 7 58]
atha śakrasya devānāmindrasyaitadabhavat ime ca tāvanmanuṣyāḥ puṇyāpuṇyānām apratyakṣadarśino dānāni dadati puṇyāni kurvanti | [Divyāv, 7 59]
ahaṃ pratyakṣadarśanena puṇyānāṃ svapuṇyaphale vyavasthitaḥ kasmāt dānāni na dadāmi puṇyāni vā na karomi ayamāryo mahākāśyapo dīnānāthakṛpaṇavanīpakānukampī | [Divyāv, 7 60]
yannvahamenaṃ piṇḍakena pratipādayeyam | [Divyāv, 7 61]
iti viditvā kṛpaṇavīthyāṃ gṛhaṃ nirmitavān avacīravicīrakaṃ kākābhilīnakaṃ nātiparamarūpaṃ kuvindaṃ cātmānamabhinirmāya udūḍhaśiraskaḥ saṇaśāṭikānivāsitaḥ sphaṭitapāṇipādo vastraṃ vāyitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 62]
śacī api devakanyā kuvindanaryā veśadhāriṇī tasarikāṃ kartumārabdhā | [Divyāv, 7 63]
pārśve cāsyā divyā sudhā sajjīkṛtā tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 7 64]
athāyuṣmān mahākāśyapaḥ kṛpaṇānāthavanīpakajanānukampako 'nupūrveṇa tadgṛhamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 65]
duḥkhitako 'yamiti kṛtvā dvāre sthitena pātraṃ prasāditam | [Divyāv, 7 66]
śakreṇa devānāmindreṇa divyayā sudhayā pūritam | [Divyāv, 7 67]
athāyuṣmato mahākāśyapasyaitadabhavat | [Divyāv, 7 68]
divyaṃ cāsya sudhābhaktam ayaṃ ca gṛhavistaraḥ | [Divyāv, 7 69.1]
suviruddhamiti kṛtvā jāto me hṛdi saṃśayaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 69.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 7 70]
dharmatā hyeṣā asamanvāhṛtya arhatāṃ jñānadarśanaṃ na pravartate | [Divyāv, 7 71]
sa samanvāhartuṃ pravṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 72]
yāvat paśyati śakraṃ devendram | [Divyāv, 7 73]
sa kathayati kauśika kiṃ duḥkhitajanasyāntarāyaṃ karoṣi yasya te bhagavatā dīrgharātrānugato vicikitsākathaṃkathāśalyaḥ samūla ārūḍho yathāpi tattathāgatenārhatā samyaksambuddhena | [Divyāv, 7 74]
ārya mahākāśyapa kiṃ duḥkhitajanasyāntarāyaṃ karomi ime tāvat manuṣyāḥ puṇyānām apratyakṣadarśino dānāni dadati puṇyāni kurvanti | [Divyāv, 7 75]
ahaṃ pratyakṣadarśī eva puṇyānāṃ kathaṃ dānāni na dadāmi nanu coktaṃ bhagavatā | [Divyāv, 7 76]
karaṇīyāni puṇyāni duḥkhā hyakṛtapuṇyatā | [Divyāv, 7 77.1]
kṛtapuṇyāni modante asmiṃlloke paratra ca | [Divyāv, 7 77.2]
tataḥ prabhṛti āyuṣmān mahākāśyapaḥ samanvāhṛtya kulāni piṇḍapātaṃ praveṣṭumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 78]
atha śakro devendra ākāśasthaścāyuṣmato mahākāśyapasya piṇḍapātaṃ carato divyayā sudhayā pātraṃ pūrayati | [Divyāv, 7 79]
āyuṣmānapi mahākāśyapaḥ pātramadhomukhaṃ karoti | [Divyāv, 7 80]
annapānaṃ choryate | [Divyāv, 7 81]
etat prakaraṇaṃ bhikṣavo bhagavata ārocayanti | [Divyāv, 7 82]
bhagavānāha tasmādanujānāmi piṇḍopadhānaṃ dhārayitavyamiti | [Divyāv, 7 83]
sāmantakena śabdo visṛtaḥ amukayā nagarāvalambikayā āryo mahākāśyapa ācāmena pratipāditaḥ sā ca tuṣite devanikāye upapannā iti | [Divyāv, 7 84]
rājñā prasenajitā kauśalena śrutam amukayā nagarāvalambikayā āryo mahākāśyapa ācāmena pratipāditaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 85]
sā tuṣite deve upapannā iti | [Divyāv, 7 86]
śrutvā ca punaryena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 87]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 88]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇaṃ rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalaṃ bhagavān dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 7 89]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśala utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocat adhivāsayatu me bhagavānāryamahākāśyapamuddiśya bhaktaṃ saptāhena iti | [Divyāv, 7 90]
adhivāsayati bhagavān rājñaḥ prasenajitas tūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 7 91]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo bhagavatas tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavato 'ntikāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 92]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalastāmeva rātriṃ praṇītaṃ khādanīyaṃ bhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyamevotthāya āsanāni prajñāpya udakamaṇīn pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālamārocayati samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyata iti | [Divyāv, 7 93]
atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya bhaktābhisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 94]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 95]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpayati saṃpravārayati | [Divyāv, 7 96]
anyatamaśca kroḍamallako vṛddhānte cittamabhiprasādayaṃstiṣṭhati ayaṃ rājā pratyakṣadarśī eva puṇyānāṃ sve puṇyaphale pratiṣṭhāpito 'tṛpta eva puṇyairdānāni dadāti puṇyāni karoti | [Divyāv, 7 97]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo 'nekaparyāyeṇa buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ śucinā praṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpya saṃpravārya bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastamapanītapātraṃ nīcataramāsanaṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purastāt niṣaṇṇo dharmaśravaṇāya | [Divyāv, 7 98]
tato bhagavatā abhihitaḥ mahārāja kasya nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiśāmi kiṃ tava āhosvidyena tavāntikāt prabhūtataraṃ puṇyaṃ prasūtamiti rājā saṃlakṣayati māṃ bhagavān piṇḍapātaṃ paribhuṅkte | [Divyāv, 7 99]
ko 'nyo mamāntikāt prabhūtataraṃ puṇyaṃ prasaviṣyatīti viditvā kathayati bhagavan yena mamāntikāt prabhūtataraṃ puṇyaṃ prasūtaṃ tasya bhagavān nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiśatu iti | [Divyāv, 7 100]
tato bhagavatā kroḍamallakasya nāmnā dakṣiṇā ādiṣṭā | [Divyāv, 7 101]
evam yāvat ṣaḍdivasān | [Divyāv, 7 102]
tato 'nyadivase rājā kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ mama bhagavān piṇḍapātaṃ paribhuṅkte kroḍamallakasya nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiśati iti | [Divyāv, 7 103]
so 'mātyairdṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 104]
te kathayanti kimarthaṃ kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthita iti rājā kathayati bhavantaḥ kathaṃ na cintāparastiṣṭhāmi yatredānīṃ sa bhagavān mama piṇḍapātaṃ paribhuṅkte kroḍamallakasya nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiśatīti tatraiko vṛddho 'mātyaḥ kathayati alpotsuko bhavatu | [Divyāv, 7 105]
vayaṃ tathā kariṣyāmo yathā śvo bhagavān devasyaiva nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiśatīti | [Divyāv, 7 106]
taiḥ pauruṣeyāṇāmājñā dattā yataḥ śvo bhavadbhiḥ praṇīta āhāraḥ sajjīkartavyaḥ prabhūtaścaiva samudānayitavyo yathopārdhaṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ pātre patati upārdhaṃ bhūmau iti | [Divyāv, 7 107]
amātyairaparasmin divase prabhūta āhāraḥ sajjīkṛtaḥ praṇītaśca | [Divyāv, 7 108]
tataḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ pariveṣitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 109]
upārdhaṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ pātre patati upārdhaṃ bhūmau | [Divyāv, 7 110]
tataḥ kroḍamallakāḥ pradhāvitāḥ bhūmau nipatitaṃ gṛhṇīma iti | [Divyāv, 7 111]
te pariveṣakair nivāritāḥ | [Divyāv, 7 112]
tataḥ kroḍamallakaḥ kathayati yadyasya rājñaḥ prabhūtamannam svāpateyamasti santyanye 'pi asmadvidhā duḥkhitakā ākāṅkṣante | [Divyāv, 7 113]
kimarthaṃ na dīyate kimanenāparibhogaṃ choritena iti | [Divyāv, 7 114]
tasya kroḍamallakasya cittavikṣepo jātaḥ na śakyaṃ tena tathā cittaṃ prasādayitum yathāpūrvam | [Divyāv, 7 115]
tato rājā buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ bhojayitvā na mama nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiśatīti viditvā dakṣiṇāmaśrutvaiva praviṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 116]
tato bhagavatā rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya nāmnā dakṣiṇā ādiṣṭā | [Divyāv, 7 117]
hastyaśvarathapattiyāyino bhuñjānasya puraṃ sanairgamaṃ paśyasi phalaṃ hi rūkṣikāyā alavaṇikāyāḥ kulmāṣapiṇḍakāyāḥ | [Divyāv, 7 118]
athāyuṣmānānando bhagavantamidamavocat bahuśo bahuśo bhadanta bhagavatā rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya niveśane bhuktvā nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiṣṭā | [Divyāv, 7 119]
nābhijānāmi kadācidevaṃrūpāṃ dakṣiṇāmādiṣṭapūrvām | [Divyāv, 7 120]
bhagavānāha icchasi tvamānanda rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasyālavaṇikāṃ kulmāṣapiṇḍakām ārabhya karmaplotiṃ śrotum etasya bhagavan kālaḥ etasya sugata samayaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 121]
ayaṃ bhagavān rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasyālavaṇikāṃ kulmāṣapiṇḍakāmārabhya karmaplotiṃ varṇayet bhagavataḥ śrutvā bhikṣavo dhārayiṣyanti iti | [Divyāv, 7 122]
tatra bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma | [Divyāv, 7 123]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'nyatamasmin karpaṭake gṛhapatiḥ prativasati | [Divyāv, 7 124]
tena sadṛśāt kulāt kalatramānītam | [Divyāv, 7 125]
sa tayā sārdhaṃ krīḍati ramate paricārayati | [Divyāv, 7 126]
tasya krīḍato ramamāṇasya paricārayataḥ putro jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 127]
sa unnīto vardhitaḥ paṭuḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 128]
yāvadasau gṛhapatiḥ patnīmāmantrayate bhadre jāto 'smākamṛṇahārako dhanahārakaśca | [Divyāv, 7 129]
gacchāmi paṇyamādāya deśāntaramiti | [Divyāv, 7 130]
sā kathayati āryaputra etat kuruṣva iti | [Divyāv, 7 131]
sa paṇyamādāya deśāntaraṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 7 132]
tatraivānayena vyasanamāpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 133]
alpaparicchado 'sau gṛhapatiḥ | [Divyāv, 7 134]
tasya gṛhapaterdhanajātaṃ parikṣīṇam | [Divyāv, 7 135]
so 'sya putro duḥkhito jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 136]
tasya gṛhapatervayasyakaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 137]
tena tasya dārakasya mātā abhihitā ayaṃ tava putraḥ kṣetraṃ rakṣatu ahamasya sukhaṃ bhuktena yogodvahanaṃ kariṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 7 138]
evaṃ bhavatu | [Divyāv, 7 139]
sa tasya kṣetraṃ rakṣitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 140]
sa tasya sukhaṃ bhaktakena yogodvahanaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 141]
yāvadapareṇa samayena parvaṇī pratyupasthitā | [Divyāv, 7 142]
tasya dārakasya mātā saṃlakṣayati adya gṛhapatipatnī suhṛtsambandhibāndhavaiḥ saha śramaṇabrāhmaṇabhojanena vyagrā bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 7 143]
gacchāmi sānukālaṃ tasya dārakasya bhaktaṃ nayāmi iti | [Divyāv, 7 144]
sā sānukālaṃ gatvā gṛhapatipatnyā etamarthaṃ niveśayati | [Divyāv, 7 145]
sā ruṣitā kathayati na tāvacchramaṇabrāhmaṇebhyo dadāmi jñātīnāṃ vā tāvat preṣyamanuṣyāya dadāmi adya tāvat tiṣṭhatu śvo dviguṇaṃ dāsyāmīti | [Divyāv, 7 146]
tatastasya dārakasya mātā saṃlakṣayati mā me putro bubhukṣitakaḥ sthāsyatīti | [Divyāv, 7 147]
tayā ātmano 'rthe 'lavaṇikā kulmāṣapiṇḍakā sampāditā | [Divyāv, 7 148]
sā tāmādāya gatā | [Divyāv, 7 149]
tena dārakeṇa dūrata eva dṛṣṭā | [Divyāv, 7 150]
sa kathayati amba asti kiṃcinmṛṣṭaṃ mṛṣṭam sā kathayati putra yadeva prātidaivasikaṃ tadapyadya nāsti | [Divyāv, 7 151]
mayā ātmano 'rthe 'lavaṇikā kulmāṣapiṇḍikā sādhitā | [Divyāv, 7 152]
tāmahaṃ gṛhītvā āgatā | [Divyāv, 7 153]
etāṃ paribhuṅkṣveti | [Divyāv, 7 154]
sa kathayati sthāpayitvā gacchasveti | [Divyāv, 7 155]
sā sthāpayitvā prakrāntā | [Divyāv, 7 156]
asati buddhānāmutpāde pratyekabuddhā loke utpadyante hīnadīnānukampakāḥ prāntaśayanāsanabhaktā ekadakṣiṇīyā lokasya | [Divyāv, 7 157]
yāvadanyatamaḥ pratyekabuddhastatpradeśamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 158]
sa tena dṛṣṭaḥ kāyaprāsādikaścittaprāsādikaśca śānteryāpathavartī | [Divyāv, 7 159]
sa saṃlakṣayati nūnaṃ mayā evaṃvidhe sadbhūte dakṣiṇīye kārā na kṛtā yena me īdṛśī samavasthā | [Divyāv, 7 160]
yadyayaṃ mamāntikād alavaṇikāṃ kulmāṣapiṇḍikāṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt ahamasmai dadyāmiti | [Divyāv, 7 161]
tato 'sau pratyekabuddhastasya daridrapuruṣasya cetasā cittamājñāya pātraṃ prasāritavān bhadramukha sacette parityaktam dīyatāmasmin pātra iti | [Divyāv, 7 162]
tatastena tīvreṇa prasādena sā alavaṇikā kulmāṣapiṇḍakā tasmai pratyekabuddhāya pratipāditā | [Divyāv, 7 163]
kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau daridrapuruṣaḥ eṣa evāsau rājā prasenajit kauśalastena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 7 164]
yadanena pratyekabuddhāyālavaṇikā kulmāṣapiṇḍakā pratipāditā tena karmaṇā ṣaṭkṛtvo deveṣu trāyastriṃśeṣu rājyaiśvaryādhipatyaṃ kāritavān ṣaṭkṛtvo 'syāmeva śrāvastyāṃ rājā kṣatriyo mūrdhnābhiṣiktaḥ tenaiva ca karmaṇā avaśeṣeṇa etarhi rājā kṣatriyo mūrdhnābhiṣiktaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 165]
so 'sya tamahaṃ saṃdhāya kathayāmi | [Divyāv, 7 166]
hastyaśvarathapattiyāyino bhuñjānasya puraṃ sanairgamanam | [Divyāv, 7 167]
paśyasi phalaṃ hi rūkṣikāyā alavaṇikāyā kulmāṣapiṇḍakāyāḥ iti | [Divyāv, 7 168]
sāmantakena śabdo visṛtaḥ bhagavatā rājñaḥ prasenajito 'lavaṇikāṃ kulmāṣapiṇḍakāmārabhya karmaplotirvyākṛtā iti | [Divyāv, 7 169]
rājñāpi prasenajitā śrutam | [Divyāv, 7 170]
sa yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 171]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 172]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇaṃ rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalaṃ bhagavān dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 7 173]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 7 174]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśala utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā bhagavantamidamavocat adhivāsayatu me bhagavāṃstraimāsīṃ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃgheneti | [Divyāv, 7 175]
adhivāsayati bhagavān rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya tūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 7 176]
tato rājñā prasenajitā kauśalena buddhamukhāya bhikṣusaṃghāya traimāsyaṃ śatarasaṃ bhojanaṃ dattam | [Divyāv, 7 177]
ekaikaśca bhikṣuḥ śatasahasreṇa vastreṇācchāditaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 178]
tailasya ca kumbhakoṭiṃ samudānīya dīpamālā abhyudyato dātum | [Divyāv, 7 179]
tatra bhakte pūjāyāṃ ca mahān kolāhalo jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 180]
yāvadanyatamā nagarāvalambikā atīva duḥkhitā | [Divyāv, 7 181]
tayā kroḍamallakena bhikṣāmaṭantyā uccaśabdaḥ śrutaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 182]
śrutvā ca punaḥ pṛcchati bhavantaḥ kimeṣa uccaśabdo mahāśabda iti | [Divyāv, 7 183]
aparaiḥ samākhyātam rājñā prasenajitā kauśalena buddhapramukho bhikṣusaṃghastraimāsyaṃ bhojitaḥ ekaikaśca bhikṣuḥ śatasahasreṇa vastreṇa ācchāditaḥ tailasya kumbhakoṭiṃ ca samudānīya dīpamālā abhyudyato dātumiti | [Divyāv, 7 184]
tatastasyā nagarāvalambikāyā etadabhavat ayaṃ tāvadrājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ puṇyairatṛpto 'dyāpi dānāni dadāti puṇyāni karoti | [Divyāv, 7 185]
yannvahamapi kutaścit samudānīya bhagavataḥ pradīpaṃ dadyāmiti | [Divyāv, 7 186]
tayā khaṇḍamallake tailasya stokam yācayitvā pradīpaṃ prajvālya bhagavataścaṅkrame dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 187]
pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ kṛtam anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena yathāyaṃ bhagavāñ śākyamunirvarṣaśatāyuṣi prajāyāṃ śākyamunir nāma śāstā loka utpannaḥ evamahamapi varṣaśatāyuṣi prajāyāṃ śākyamunireva śāstā bhaveyam | [Divyāv, 7 188]
yathā cāsya śāriputramaudgalyāyanāgrayugaṃ bhadrayugamānando bhikṣurupasthāyakaḥ śuddhodanaḥ pitā mātā mahāmāyā rāhulabhadraḥ kumāraḥ putraḥ | [Divyāv, 7 189]
yathāyaṃ bhagavān dhātuvibhāgaṃ kṛtvā parinirvāsyati evamahamapi dhātuvibhāgaṃ kṛtvā parinirvāpayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 7 190]
yāvat sarve te dīpā nairvāṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 7 191]
sa tayā prajvalitaḥ pradīpaḥ prajvalatyeva | [Divyāv, 7 192]
dharmatā khalu buddhānāṃ bhagavatām na tāvadupasthāyakāḥ pratisaṃlīyante na yāvadbuddhā bhagavantaḥ pratisaṃlīnā iti | [Divyāv, 7 193]
athāyuṣmānānandaḥ saṃlakṣayati asthānamanavakāśo yadbuddhā bhagavanta āloke śayyāṃ kalpayanti | [Divyāv, 7 194]
yannvahaṃ dīpam nirvāpayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 7 195]
sa hastena nirvāpayitumārabdho na śaknoti | [Divyāv, 7 196]
tataścīvarakarṇikena tato vyajanena tathāpi na śaknoti nirvāpayitum | [Divyāv, 7 197]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate kimetadānandeti | [Divyāv, 7 198]
sa kathayati bhagavan mama buddhirutpannā asthānamanavakāśo yadbuddhā bhagavanta āloke śayyāṃ kalpayanti | [Divyāv, 7 199]
yannvahaṃ dīpaṃ nirvāpayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 7 200]
so 'haṃ hastena nirvāpayitumārabdho na śaknomi tataścīvarakarṇikena tato vyajanena tathāpi na śaknomīti | [Divyāv, 7 201]
bhagavānāha khedamānanda āpatsyase | [Divyāv, 7 202]
yadi vairambhakā api vāyavo vāyeyuḥ te 'pi na śaknuyur nirvāpayituṃ prāgeva hastagataścīvarakarṇiko vyajanaṃ vā | [Divyāv, 7 203]
tathā hi ayaṃ pradīpastayā dārikayā mahatā cittābhisaṃskāreṇa prajvalitaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 204]
api tu ānanda bhaviṣyatyasau dārikā varṣaśatāyuṣi prajāyāṃ śākyamunir nāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddhaḥ | [Divyāv, 7 205]
śāriputramaudgalyāyanau tasyāgrayugaṃ bhadrayugam ānando bhikṣurupāsakaḥ śuddhodanaḥ pitā mahāmāyā mātā kapilavastu nagaram rāhulabhadraḥ kumāraḥ putraḥ | [Divyāv, 7 206]
sāpi dhātuvibhāgaṃ kṛtvā parinirvāsyatīti | [Divyāv, 7 207]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 7 208]
āttamanasaste ca bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 7 209]
{Divyāv, 8}
buddho bhavāñ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍadasyārāme satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrairdhanibhiḥ paurairbrāhmaṇairgṛhapatibhiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhairdevair nāgairyakṣairasurairgaruḍaiḥ kinnarairmahoragairiti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavāṃllābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 1]
tatra khalu varṣāvāsaṃ bhagavānupagato jetavane anāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [Divyāv, 8 2]
atha tadaiva pravāraṇāyāṃ pratyupasthitāyāṃ saṃbahulāḥ śrāvastīnivāsino vaṇijo yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 3]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 4]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇān saṃbahulāñśrāvastīnivāsino vaṇijo bhagavān dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 8 5]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 8 6]
atha saṃbahulāḥ śrāvastīnivāsino vaṇijo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhinandyānumodya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato 'ntikāt prakrāntāḥ yenāyuṣmānānandastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 7]
upasaṃkramyāyuṣmata ānandasya pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 8]
saṃbahulāñ śrāvastīnivāsino vaṇija āyuṣmānānando dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 8 9]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 8 10]
atha te vaṇija utthāyāsanebhya ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yenāyuṣmānānandastenāñjaliṃ praṇamya āyuṣmantamānandamidamavocan kiṃcitte āryānanda śrutaṃ varṣoṣito bhagavān katameṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cariṣyatīti yadvayaṃ tadyātrikaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ samudānīmahe dharmatā caiṣā ṣaṇmahānagaranivāsino vaṇijo yasyāṃ diśi buddhā bhagavanto gantukāmā bhavanti tadyātrikabhāṇḍaṃ samudānayanti | [Divyāv, 8 11]
sa kathayati buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ kiṃ na pṛcchatha durāsadā hi buddhā bhagavanto duṣprasahāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 12]
na śaknumo vayaṃ bhagavantaṃ praṣṭum | [Divyāv, 8 13]
mamāpi bhavanto durāsadā hi buddhā bhagavanto duṣprasahāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 14]
ahamapi na śaknomi bhagavantaṃ praṣṭum | [Divyāv, 8 15]
yadi bhadantānandasyāpi durāsadā buddhā bhagavanto duṣprasahāḥ kathaṃ bhadantānando jānīte 'mukāṃ diśaṃ bhagavān gamiṣyatīti nimittena vā bhavantaḥ parikathayā vā | [Divyāv, 8 16]
kathaṃ nimittena yāṃ diśaṃ bhagavān gantukāmastato 'bhimukho niṣīdati evaṃ nimittena | [Divyāv, 8 17]
kathaṃ parikathayā teṣāṃ janapadānāṃ varṇaṃ bhāṣate evaṃ parikathayā | [Divyāv, 8 18]
kutomukho bhadantānanda bhagavān niṣīdati katameṣāṃ ca janapadānāṃ varṇaṃ bhāṣate magadhābhimukho bhavanto bhagavān niṣīdati māgadhakānāṃ janapadānāṃ varṇaṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 8 19]
api tu bhavanto 'ṣṭādaśānuśaṃsā buddhacārikāyām | [Divyāv, 8 20]
katame 'ṣṭādaśa nāgnibhayaṃ nodakabhayaṃ na siṃhabhayaṃ na vyāghrabhayaṃ na dvīpitarakṣuparacakrabhayaṃ na caurabhayaṃ na gulmatarapaṇyātiyātrābhayaṃ na manuṣyāmanuṣyabhayam | [Divyāv, 8 21]
kālena ca kālaṃ divyāni rūpāṇi dṛśyante divyāḥ śabdāḥ śrūyante udārāś cāvabhāsāḥ prajñāyante ātmavyākaraṇāni ca śrūyante dharmasambhoga āmiṣasambhogo 'lpābādhā ca buddhacārikā | [Divyāv, 8 22]
atha saṃbahulāḥ śrāvastīnivāsino vaṇijaḥ āyuṣmataḥ ānandasya bhāṣitamabhinandyānumodya āyuṣmata ānandasya pādau śirasā vanditvā utthāyāsanāt prakrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 23]
dharmatā khalu buddhā bhagavanto jīvanto dhriyanto yāpayanto mahākaruṇayā saṃcodyamānāḥ parānugrahapravṛttāḥ kālena kālamaraṇyacārikāṃ caranti nadīcārikāṃ parvatacārikāṃ śmaśānacārikāṃ janapadacārikāṃ caranti | [Divyāv, 8 24]
asmiṃstvarthe buddho bhagavān magadheṣu janapadacārikāṃ cartukāmastadeva pravāraṇāṃ pravārayitvā āyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate sma gaccha ānanda bhikṣūṇāmārocaya itaḥ saptame divase tathāgato magadheṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cariṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 25]
yo yuṣmākam utsahate tathāgatena sārdhaṃ janapadacārikāṃ cartum sa cīvarakarma karotu | [Divyāv, 8 26]
evaṃ bhadantetyāyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya bhikṣūṇāmārocayati bhagavānāyuṣmanta itaḥ saptame divase magadheṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cariṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 27]
yo yuṣmākamutsahate bhagavatā sārdhaṃ magadheṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cartum sa cīvarakarma karotu | [Divyāv, 8 28]
atha bhagavān bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaḥ saṃbahulaiśca śrāvastīnivāsibhirvaṇigbrāhmaṇagṛhapatibhiḥ sārdhaṃ magadheṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 29]
atha saṃbahulāśca śrāvastīnivāsino vaṇijo yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 30]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavantamidamavocan adhivāsayatvasmākaṃ bhagavān yāvacca śrāvastī yāvacca rājagṛham atrāntarā cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena | [Divyāv, 8 31]
adhivāsayati bhagavān saṃbahulānāṃ śrāvastīnivāsināṃ vaṇijāṃ tūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 8 32]
atha saṃbahulāḥ śrāvastīnivāsino vaṇijo bhagavatas tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavato 'ntikāt prakrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 33]
atha samprasthite buddhe bhagavati antarā ca śrāvastīmantarā ca rājagṛham atrāntarānmahāṭavyāṃ caurasahasraṃ prativasati | [Divyāv, 8 34]
adrākṣīttaccaurasahasraṃ bhagavantaṃ sārthaparivṛtaṃ bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtam | [Divyāv, 8 35]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ parasparaṃ kathayanti gacchatu bhagavān saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 36]
śeṣaṃ sārthaṃ muṣiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 37]
ityanuvicintya sarve javena prasṛtā yena sārthaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 38]
bhagavatā abhihitāḥ kimetadbhavantaḥ samārabdham caurāḥ kathayanti vayaṃ smo bhadanta caurā aṭavīcarāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 39]
nāsmākaṃ kṛṣir na vāṇijyā na gaurakṣyam | [Divyāv, 8 40]
anenopakrameṇa jīvikāṃ kalpayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 41]
gacchatu bhagavān saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 42]
śeṣaṃ sārthaṃ muṣiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 43]
bhagavānāha mamaiṣa sārthaḥ saṃniśritaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 44]
api tu sakalasya sārthasya parigaṇayya suvarṇaṃ gṛhṇīdhvam | [Divyāv, 8 45]
tathā bhavatviti caurasahasreṇa pratijñātam | [Divyāv, 8 46]
asmin sārthe ye upāsakā vaṇijastaiḥ kṛtsnasya sārthasya mūlyaṃ gaṇayya caurāṇāṃ niveditam iyanti śatāni sahasrāṇi ceti | [Divyāv, 8 47]
tatasteṣāṃ caurāṇāṃ sārthaniṣkrayārthaṃ bhagavatā nidhānaṃ darśitam | [Divyāv, 8 48]
tatastena caurasahasreṇa sārthamūlyapramāṇaṃ suvarṇaṃ gṛhītam avaśiṣṭaṃ tatraivāntarhitam | [Divyāv, 8 49]
evaṃ bhagavatā sārthaścaurasahasrāt pratimokṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 50]
anupūrveṇa bhagavān rājagṛhamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 51]
punarapi bhagavān sārthaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto rājagṛhāt śrāvastīṃ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 52]
tathaiva caurasahasrasakāśāt sārtho niṣkrītaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 53]
evaṃ dvitricatuṣpañcaṣaḍvārāṃśca caurasahasrasakāśād āgamanagamanena sārthaḥ paritrāto mūlyaṃ cānupradattam | [Divyāv, 8 54]
saptamaṃ tu vāraṃ bhagavān sārtharahito bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaḥ śrāvastyā rājagṛhaṃ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 55]
adrākṣīccaurasahasraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ sārthavirahitaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaparivṛtam | [Divyāv, 8 56]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ parasparaṃ saṃlapanti bhagavān gacchatu bhikṣusaṃghaṃ muṣiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 57]
tatkasya hetoḥ eṣo hi bhagavān suvarṇapradaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 58]
ityuktvā sarvajavena pradhāvitā bhikṣūn muṣitumārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 59]
bhagavatā cābhihitāḥ vatsāḥ mama ete śrāvakāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 60]
caurāḥ kathayanti jānāsyeva bhagavan vayaṃ caurā aṭavīcarāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 61]
nāsmākaṃ kṛṣir na vaṇijyā na gaurakṣyam | [Divyāv, 8 62]
anena vayaṃ jīvikāṃ kalpayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 63]
tato bhagavatā caurāṇāṃ mahānidhānaṃ darśitam evaṃ coktāḥ vatsāḥ yāvadāptaṃ dhanaṃ gṛhṇītheti | [Divyāv, 8 64]
tatastena caurasahasreṇa tasmānmahānidhānādyāvadāptaṃ suvarṇamādattam avaśiṣṭaṃ tatraivāntarhitam | [Divyāv, 8 65]
atha bhagavāṃstaccaurasahasram yāvadāptaṃ dhanena saṃtarpayitvā tato 'nupūrveṇa rājagṛhamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 66]
tatasteṣāṃ caurāṇāṃ buddhirutpannā yā kācidasmākaṃ śrīsaubhāgyasampat sarvāsau buddhaṃ bhagavantamāgamya | [Divyāv, 8 67]
yannu vayaṃ bhagavantaṃ saśrāvakasaṃghamasmin pradeśe bhojayema iti | [Divyāv, 8 68]
atrāntare nāsti kiṃcidbuddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ mahākāruṇikānām ekarakṣāṇām ekavīrāṇām advayavādināṃ śamathavipaśyanāvihāriṇāṃ trividhadamathavastukuśalānāṃ caturṛddhipādacaraṇatalasupratiṣṭhitānāṃ caturoghottīrṇānāṃ caturṣu saṃgrahavastuṣu dīrgharātrakṛtaparicayānāṃ daśabalabalināṃ caturvaiśāradyaviśāradānām udārārṣabhasamyaksiṃhanādanādināṃ pañcāṅgaviprahīṇānāṃ pañcaskandhavimocakānāṃ pañcagatisamatikrāntānāṃ ṣaḍāyatanabhedakānāṃ saṃghātavihāriṇāṃ ṣaṭpāramitāparipūrṇayaśasāṃ saptabodhyaṅgakusumāḍhyānāṃ saptasamādhipariṣkāradāyakānām āryāṣṭāṅgamārgadeśikānām āryamārgapudgalanāyakānāṃ navānupūrvasamāpattikuśalānāṃ navasaṃyojanavisaṃyojanakānāṃ daśadikparipūrṇayaśasāṃ daśaśatavaśavartiprativiśiṣṭānām | [Divyāv, 8 69.1]
trī rātrestrirdivasasya ṣaṭkṛtvo rātriṃdivasena buddhacakṣuṣā lokam vyavalokayanti kasyānavaropitāni kuśalamūlānyavaropayāmi kasyāvaropitāni vivardhayāmi kaḥ kṛcchraprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃkaṭaprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃbādhaprāptaḥ kaḥ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhaprāptaḥ kaṃ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhāt parimocayāmi ko 'pāyanimnaḥ ko 'pāyapravaṇaḥ ko 'pāyaprāgbhāraḥ kamahamapāyād vyutthāpya svarge mokṣaphale ca pratiṣṭhāpayāmi kasya kāmapaṅkanimagnasya hastoddhāramanuprayacchāmi kasya buddhotpādavibhūṣitaṃ lokaṃ saphalīkaromi kamāryadhanavirahitam āryadhanaiśvaryādhipatye pratiṣṭhāpayeyam ko hīyate ko vardhate | [Divyāv, 8 69.2]
apyevātikramedvelāṃ sāgaro makarālayaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 70.1]
na tu vaineyavatsānāṃ buddho velāmatikramet | [Divyāv, 8 70.2]
yathā hi mātā priyamekaputrakaṃ hyavekṣate rakṣati cāsya jīvitam | [Divyāv, 8 71.1]
tathaiva vaineyajanaṃ tathāgato hyavekṣate rakṣati cāsya saṃtatim | [Divyāv, 8 71.2]
sarvajñasaṃtānanivāsinī hi kāruṇyadhenurmṛgayatyakhinnā | [Divyāv, 8 72.1]
vaineyavatsān bhavaduḥkhanaṣṭān vatsān praṇaṣṭāniva vatsalā gauḥ | [Divyāv, 8 72.2]
tato bhagavāṃsteṣāṃ caurāṇāṃ vaineyakālamapekṣya rājagṛhādanupūrveṇa bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣugaṇapuraskṛto dānto dāntaparivāraḥ śāntaḥ śāntaparivāraścandanaścandanaparivāro mukto muktaparivāra āśvasta āśvastaparivāraḥ pūrvavat yāvanmahākaruṇayā samanvāgatas tāṃ sālāṭavīmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 73]
adrākṣīttaccaurasahasraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ saśrāvakasaṃghaṃ dūrādevāgacchantam | [Divyāv, 8 74]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaścittānyabhiprasādya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 75]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya bhagavantamidamavocan adhivāsayatu asmākaṃ bhagavāñ śvo 'ntargṛhe bhaktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena | [Divyāv, 8 76]
adhivāsayati bhagavāṃstasya caurasahasrasya tūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 8 77]
atha caurasahasraṃ bhagavatas tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavato'ntikāt prakrāntam | [Divyāv, 8 78]
atha taccaurasahasraṃ tāmeva rātriṃ śuci praṇītaṃ khādanīyabhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyamevotthāya āsanāni prajñapya udakamaṇīn pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālamārocayati samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyase | [Divyāv, 8 79]
atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena tasya caurasahasrasya bhaktābhisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 80]
atha taccaurasahasraṃ buddhapramukhasya bhikṣusaṃghasya candanodakena pādau prakṣālayāmāsa | [Divyāv, 8 81]
atha bhagavān prakṣālitapāṇipādaḥ purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 82]
niṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpya saṃpravārya bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastamapanītapātraṃ nīcatarāṇyāsanāni gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purastānniṣaṇṇā dharmaśravaṇāya | [Divyāv, 8 83]
atha bhagavatā teṣāmāśayānuśayaṃ viditvā dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā tena caurasahasreṇa tasminnevāsane niṣaṇṇena viṃśatiśikharasamudgataṃ satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ jñānavajreṇa bhittvā srotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 8 84]
dṛṣṭasatyāśca kathayanti idamasmākaṃ bhadanta na mātrā kṛtaṃ na pitrā kṛtaṃ na rājñā na devatābhir na pūrvapretair na śramaṇabrāhmaṇair neṣṭair na svajanabandhuvargeṇa yadasmābhirbhagavantaṃ kalyāṇamitramāgamya | [Divyāv, 8 85]
uddhṛto narakatiryakpretebhyaḥ pādaḥ pratiṣṭhāpito devamanuṣyeṣu paryantīkṛtaḥ saṃsāraḥ ucchoṣitā rudhirāśrusamudrāḥ uttīrṇā aśrusāgarāḥ laṅghitā asthiparvatāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 86]
labhema vayaṃ bhadanta svākhyāte dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasampadaṃ bhikṣubhāvam | [Divyāv, 8 87]
carema vayaṃ bhagavato 'ntike brahmacaryam | [Divyāv, 8 88]
tato bhagavatā brāhmeṇa svareṇābhihitāḥ eta vatsāḥ carata brahmacaryam | [Divyāv, 8 89]
vācāvasāne bhagavato muṇḍāḥ saṃvṛttāstraidhātukavītarāgāḥ samaloṣṭakāñcanā ākāśapāṇitalasamacittā vāsīcandanakalpā vidyāvidāritāṇḍakośā vidyābhijñāpratisaṃvitprāptā bhavalābhalobhasatkāraparāṅmukhāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 90]
sendropendrāṇāṃ devānāṃ pūjyā mānyā abhivādyāśca saṃvṛttāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 91]
bhikṣavaḥ saṃśayajātāḥ sarvasaṃśayacchettāraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ papracchuḥ paśya bhadanta bhagavatā idaṃ caurasahasraṃ saptavāraṃ dhanena saṃtarpayitvā atyantaniṣṭhe 'nuttare yogakṣeme nirvāṇe pratiṣṭhāpitam | [Divyāv, 8 92]
bhagavānāha na bhikṣava etarhi yathā atīte 'pyadhvani mayā asyaiva caurasahasrasya sakāśādanekabhāṇḍasahasraḥ sārtho niṣkrītaḥ na ca śakitāḥ saṃtarpayitum | [Divyāv, 8 93]
tato mayā anekairduṣkaraśatasahasrairdevamanuṣyaduṣprāpyāṃ śakrabrahmādyairapi duradhigamāṃ badaradvīpayātrāṃ varṣaśatena sādhayitvā etadeva caurasahasramārabhya kṛtsno jāmbudvīpaḥ suvarṇarajatavaiḍūryasphaṭikādyai ratnaviśeṣairmanorathepsitaiścopakaraṇaviśeṣaiḥ saṃtarpayitvā daśabhiḥ kuśalaiḥ karmapathaiḥ pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 94]
tacchṛṇuta bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani asminneva jambudvīpe vārāṇasyāṃ nagaryāṃ brahmadatto nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati sma ṛddhaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca praśāntakalikalahaḍimbaḍamarataskaradurbhikṣarogāpagatam | [Divyāv, 8 95]
priyamivaikaputrakamiva rājyaṃ kārayati | [Divyāv, 8 96]
tena khalu samayena vārāṇasyāṃ priyaseno nāma sārthavāhaḥ prativasati āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vaiśravaṇadhanapratispardhī | [Divyāv, 8 97]
tena sadṛśāt kulāt kalatramānītam | [Divyāv, 8 98]
sa tayā sārdhaṃ krīḍate ramate paricārayati | [Divyāv, 8 99]
atha anyatama udārapuṇyamaheśākhyaḥ sattvo 'nyatamasmāt praṇītāddevanikāyāccyutvā tasyāḥ prajāpatyāḥ kukṣimavakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 100]
pañcāveṇīyā dharmā ihaikatye paṇḍitajātīye mātṛgrāme | [Divyāv, 8 101]
katame pañca raktaṃ puruṣaṃ jānāti kālaṃ jānāti ṛtuṃ jānāti garbhamavakrāntaṃ jānāti yasyāḥ sakāśādgarbho 'vakrāmati taṃ jānāti dārakaṃ jānāti dārikāṃ jānāti | [Divyāv, 8 102]
saceddārako bhavati dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣiṃ niśritya tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 8 103]
saceddārikā bhavati vāmaṃ kukṣiṃ niśritya tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 8 104]
sā āttamanāḥ svāmina ārocayati diṣṭyā āryaputra vardhasva āpannasattvāsmi saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 8 105]
yathā ca me dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣiṃ niśritya tiṣṭhati niyataṃ dārako bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 106]
so 'pyāttamanā āttamanā udānamudānayati apyevāhaṃ cirakālābhilaṣitaṃ putramukhaṃ paśyeyam | [Divyāv, 8 107]
jāto me syānnāvajātaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 108]
kṛtyāni me kuryāt | [Divyāv, 8 109]
bhṛtaḥ pratibharet | [Divyāv, 8 110]
dāyādyaṃ pratipadyeta | [Divyāv, 8 111]
kulavaṃśo me cirasthitikaḥ syāt | [Divyāv, 8 112]
asmākaṃ cāpyatītakālagatānām uddiśya dānāni dattvā puṇyāni kṛtvā nāmnā dakṣiṇāmādiśet idaṃ tayor yatra tatropapannayorgacchator anugacchatviti | [Divyāv, 8 113]
āpannasattvāṃ caināṃ viditvā upariprāsādatalagatām ayantritāṃ dhārayati uṣṇa uṣṇopakaraṇaiḥ śīte śītopakaraṇair vaidyaprajñaptairāhārair nātiśītair nātyuṣṇair nātitiktair nātyamlair nātilavaṇair nātimadhurair nātikaṭukair nātikaṣāyais tiktāmlalavaṇamadhurakaṭukakaṣāyavivarjitair āhāraiḥ hārārdhahāravibhūṣitagātrīmapsarasamiva nandanavanacāriṇīṃ mañcānmañcaṃ pīṭhātpīṭham avatarantīm adharimāṃ bhūmim | [Divyāv, 8 114]
na cāsyāḥ kiṃcidamanojñaśabdaśravaṇam yāvadeva garbhasya paripākāya | [Divyāv, 8 115]
sā aṣṭānāṃ vā navānāṃ vā māsānāmatyayāt prasūtā | [Divyāv, 8 116]
dārako jāto 'bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādiko gauraḥ kanakavarṇaśchatrākāraśirāḥ pralambabāhurvistīrṇalalāṭaḥ saṃgatabhrūstuṅganāso dṛḍhakaṭhinaśarīro mahānagrabalaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 117]
tasya jñātayaḥ saṃgamya samāgamya trīṇi saptakānyekaviṃśatirātriṃdivasāni tasya jātasya jātamahaṃ kṛtvā nāmadheyaṃ vyavasthāpayanti kiṃ bhavatu dārakasya nāma ayaṃ dārakaḥ priyasenasya sārthavāhasya putraḥ | [Divyāv, 8 118]
tadbhavatu dārakasya nāma supriya iti | [Divyāv, 8 119]
supriyo dārako 'ṣṭābhyo dhātrībhya upanyasto dvābhyāṃ kṣīradhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāmaṃsadhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ maladhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ krīḍanikābhyāṃ dhātrībhyām | [Divyāv, 8 120]
so 'ṣṭābhirdhātrībhirunnīyate vardhyate kṣīreṇa dadhnā navanītena sarpiṣā sarpimaṇḍena anyaiścottaptottaptairupakaraṇaviśeṣaiḥ | [Divyāv, 8 121]
āśu vardhate hradasthamiva paṅkajam | [Divyāv, 8 122]
yadā mahān saṃvṛttastadā lipyāmupanyastaḥ saṃkhyāyāṃ gaṇanāyāṃ mudrāyāmuddhāre nyāse nikṣepe hastiparīkṣāyāmaśvaparīkṣāyāṃ ratnaparīkṣāyāṃ dāruparīkṣāyāṃ vastraparīkṣāyāṃ puruṣaparīkṣāyāṃ strīparīkṣāyām nānāpaṇyaparīkṣāsu paryavadātaḥ sarvaśāstrajñaḥ sarvakalābhijñaḥ sarvaśilpajñaḥ sarvabhūtarutajñaḥ sarvagatigatijña udghaṭṭako vācakaḥ paṇḍitaḥ paṭupracāraḥ paramatīkṣṇaniśitabuddhiḥ saṃvṛtto 'gnikalpa iva jñānena | [Divyāv, 8 123]
sa yāni tāni rājñāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mūrdhnābhiṣiktānāṃ janapadaiśvaryasthāmavīryam anuprāptānāṃ mahāntaṃ pṛthivīmaṇḍalamabhinirjityādhyāvasatāṃ pṛthagbhavanti śilpasthānakarmasthānāni tadyathā hastigrīvāyām aśvapṛṣṭhe rathe tsarudhanuḥṣu upayāne niryāṇe 'ṅkuśagrahe tomaragrahe chedye bhedye muṣṭibandhe padabandhe dūravedhe śabdavedhe'kṣuṇṇavedhe marmavedhe dṛḍhaprahāritāyām pañcasu sthāneṣu kṛtāvī saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 124]
dharmatā caiṣā na tāvat putrasya nāma nirgacchati yāvat pitā dhriyate | [Divyāv, 8 125]
athāpareṇa samayena priyasenaḥ sārthavāho glānībhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 126]
sa mūlagaṇḍaputrapuṣpaphalabhaiṣajyairupasthīyamāno hīyata eva | [Divyāv, 8 127]
sarve kṣayāntā nicayāḥ patanāntāḥ samucchrayāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 128.1]
saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ ca jīvitam | [Divyāv, 8 128.2]
iti sa kāladharmeṇa saṃyuktaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 129]
kālagate priyasene sārthavāhe brahmadattena kāśirājñā supriyo mahāsārthavāhatve 'bhiṣiktaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 130]
tena sārthavāhabhūtena iyamevaṃrūpā mahāpratijñā kṛtā sarvasattvā mayā dhanena saṃtarpayitavyāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 131]
alpaṃ ca deyaṃ bahavaśca yācakāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 132]
tato 'lpairahobhistaddhanaṃ parikṣayaṃ paryādānaṃ gatam | [Divyāv, 8 133]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ saṃlakṣayati alpaṃ ca deyaṃ bahavaśca yācakāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 134]
tato 'lpairahobhistaddhanaṃ parikṣayaṃ paryādānaṃ gatam | [Divyāv, 8 135]
yannvahaṃ sāmudram yānapātraṃ samudānīya mahāsamudramavatareyaṃ dhanahārikaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 136]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ sāmudrayānapātraṃ samudānīya pañcamātrairvaṇikśataiḥ sārdhaṃ mahāsamudramavatīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 137]
tato 'nupūrveṇa ratnadvīpaṃ gatvā ratnasaṃgrahaṃ kṛtvā svastikṣemābhyāṃ mahāsamudrāduttīrya sthalajairvahitrairbhāṇḍamāropya vārāṇasyabhimukhaḥ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 138]
aṭavīkāntāramadhyagataścaurasahasreṇāsāditaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 139]
tataste caurā muṣitukāmāḥ sarvajavena prasṛtāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 140]
supriyeṇa ca sārthavāhenāvalokyābhihitāḥ kimetadbhavantaḥ samārabdham caurāḥ kathayanti sārthavāha tvamekaḥ svastikṣemābhyāṃ gaccha avaśiṣṭaṃ sārthaṃ muṣiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 141]
sārthavāhaḥ kathayati mamaiṣa bhavantaḥ sārthaḥ saṃniśritaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 142]
nārhanti bhavanto muṣitum evamuktāścaurāḥ kathayanti vayaṃ smaḥ sārthavāhacaurā aṭavīcarāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 143]
nāsmākaṃ kṛṣir na vāṇijyā na gaurakṣyam | [Divyāv, 8 144]
anena vayaṃ jīvikāṃ kalpayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 145]
teṣāṃ supriyaḥ sārthavāhaḥ kathayati sārthasya mūlyaṃ bhavanto gaṇyatām | [Divyāv, 8 146]
ahameṣāmarthe mūlyaṃ dāsyāmīti | [Divyāv, 8 147]
tataste vaṇijaḥ parasparaṃ mūlyaṃ gaṇayitvā caurāṇāṃ nivedayanti iyanti śatāni sahasrāṇi ceti | [Divyāv, 8 148]
tataḥ supriyeṇa sārthavāhena bhāṇḍaniṣkrayārthe svaṃ dravyamanupradattam | [Divyāv, 8 149]
caurasakāśāt sārthaḥ paritrātaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 150]
evaṃ dvistriścatuḥpañcaṣaḍvārāṃs tasyaiva caurasahasrasya sakāśāt supriyeṇa sārthavāhena sārthaḥ paritrāto mūlyaṃ cānupradattam | [Divyāv, 8 151]
yāvat saptamaṃ tu vāraṃ supriyaḥ sārthavāho mahāsamudramavatīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 152]
tataḥ saṃsiddhayānapātro 'bhyāgato 'ṭavīkāntāramadhyagatastenaiva caurasahasreṇāsāditaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 153]
tataste caurā muṣitukāmāḥ sarvajavena prasṛtāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 154]
supriyeṇa ca sārthavāhenāvalokyābhihitāḥ supriyo 'haṃ bhavantaḥ sārthavāhaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 155]
caurāḥ kathayanti jānāsyeva mahāsārthavāha vayaṃ caurā aṭavīcarāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 156]
nāsmākaṃ kṛṣir na vāṇijyaṃ na gaurakṣyam | [Divyāv, 8 157]
anena vayaṃ jīvikāṃ kalpayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 158]
tataḥ supriyeṇa sārthavāhena pūrvikāṃ pratijñāmanusmṛtya dṛḍhapratijñena tasya caurasahasrasya bhāṇḍamanupradattam | [Divyāv, 8 159]
supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ saṃlakṣayati ime caurā labdhaṃ labdhamarthajātasaṃnicayaṃ kurvanti | [Divyāv, 8 160]
mayā ca mahatī pratijñā kṛtā sarvasattvā dhanena mayā saṃtarpayitavyā iti | [Divyāv, 8 161]
so 'hamimaṃ caurasahasraṃ na śaknomi dhanena saṃtarpayitum | [Divyāv, 8 162]
kathaṃ punaḥ sarvasattvān dhanena saṃtarpayiṣyāmīti cintāparo middhamavakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 163]
atha tasya mahātmana udārapuṇyamaheśākhyasyodāracetasopapannasya sarvasattvamanorathaparipūrakasya lokahitārthamabhyudgatasya anyatarā maheśākhyā devatā upasaṃkramya samāśvāsayati mā tvaṃ sārthavāha khedamāpadyasva | [Divyāv, 8 164]
ṛddhiṣyati te praṇidhiriti | [Divyāv, 8 165]
asti khalu mahāsārthavāha asminneva jambudvīpe badaradvīpo nāma mahāpattano 'manuṣyāvacarito maheśākhyamanuṣyādhiṣṭhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 166]
santi tasmin badaradvīpe pradhānāni ratnāni sarvasattvavicitramanorathaparipūrakāṇi | [Divyāv, 8 167]
yadi mahāsārthavāho badaradvīpayātrāṃ sādhayet evamimāṃ mahatīṃ pratijñāṃ pratinistareta | [Divyāv, 8 168]
iyaṃ hi mahāpratijñā śakrabrahmādīnāmapi dustarā prāgeva manuṣyabhūtasya | [Divyāv, 8 169]
ityuktvā sā devatā tatraivāntarhitā | [Divyāv, 8 170]
na ca śakitā supriyeṇa mahāsārthavāhena sā devatā praṣṭum katarasyāṃ diśi badaradvīpaḥ kathaṃ vā tatra gamyata iti | [Divyāv, 8 171]
atha supriyasya sārthavāhasya suptapratibuddhasya etadabhavat aho bata me sā devatā punarapi darśayet diśaṃ copāyaṃ ca vyapadiśed badaradvīpamahāpattanasya gamanāyeti cintāparo middhamavakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 172]
atha sā devatā tasya mahātmana udārapuṇyamaheśākhyasya dṛḍhodārapratijñasyodāravīryaparākramatām anikṣiptotsāhatāṃ viditvā upasaṃkramya evamāha mā tvaṃ sārthavāha khedamāpadyasva | [Divyāv, 8 173]
asti khalu mahāsārthavāha paścime digbhāge pañcāntaradvīpaśatāni samatikramya sapta mahāparvatāḥ uccāśca pragṛhītāśca sapta ca mahānadyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 174]
tān vīryabalena laṅghayitvā antaroddānam anulomapratilomadvayamāvartaḥ śaṅkhanābhaḥ śaṅkhanābhī ca nīlodastārakākṣaśca parvatau nīlagrīva eva ca vairambhā tāmrāṭavī veṇugulmaḥ sapta parvatāḥ sakaṇṭakāḥ kṣāranadī triśaṅkur ayaskilam aṣṭādaśavakro nadī ślakṣṇa eva ca dhūmanetramudakaṃ saptāśīviṣaparvatā nadī bhavati paścimā | [Divyāv, 8 175]
anulomapratilomo nāma mahāsamudraḥ | [Divyāv, 8 176]
anulomapratilome mahāsamudre manuṣyānavacarite anulomapratilomā vāyavo vānti | [Divyāv, 8 177]
tatra yo 'sau puruṣo bhavati maheśākhyo maheśākhyadevatāparigṛhītaḥ sa mahatā puṇyabalena vīryabalena cittabalena mahāntaṃ plavamāsthāya anulomapratilomamahāsamudram avatarati | [Divyāv, 8 178]
sa yanmāsena gacchati tadekena divasena pratyāhriyate | [Divyāv, 8 179]
evaṃ dvis triḥ | [Divyāv, 8 180]
hriyamāṇaśca pratyāhriyamāṇaśca yadi madhyamāmudakadhārāṃ pratipadyate evamasau maitrībalaparigṛhīto lokahitārthamabhyudgamyottarati nistarati abhiniṣkramati | [Divyāv, 8 181]
anulomapratilomaṃ mahāsamudraṃ samatikramya anulomapratilomo nāma parvataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 182]
anulomapratilome mahāparvate 'manuṣyāvacarite 'nulomapratilomā nāma vāyavo vānti yaiḥ puruṣastimirīkṛtanetro naṣṭasaṃjñaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [Divyāv, 8 183]
sa vīryabalenātmānaṃ saṃdhārya tasmādeva mahāparvatādamoghāṃ nāmauṣadhīṃ samanviṣya gṛhītvā netre añjayitvā śirasi baddhvā samālabhya anulomapratilomaṃ nāma mahāparvatamabhiniṣkramitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 184]
sacedetaṃ vidhimanutiṣṭhate nāsya saṃmoho bhavati svastikṣemeṇātikramatyanulomapratilomaṃ mahāparvatam | [Divyāv, 8 185]
sacedevaṃ vidhiṃ vā nānutiṣṭhati auṣadhīṃ vā na labhate labdhvā vā na gṛhṇāti sa ṣaṇmāsān muhyati unmādamapi prāpnoti ucchritya vā kālaṃ karoti | [Divyāv, 8 186]
anulomapratilomaṃ mahāparvataṃ samatikramya āvarto nāma mahāsamudraḥ | [Divyāv, 8 187]
tatra vairambhakā vāyavo vānti yaistadudakaṃ bhrāmyate | [Divyāv, 8 188]
tatra yo 'sau puruṣo bhavatyudārapuṇyavipākamaheśākhyo devatāparigṛhītaḥ sa mahatā puṇyabalena vīryabalena cittabalena kāyabalena mahāntaṃ plavamāsthāya āvartaṃ mahāsamudramavatarati | [Divyāv, 8 189]
sa ekasminnāvarte saptakṛtvo bhrāmayitvā nirudhyate | [Divyāv, 8 190]
yojanaṃ gatvā dvitīye āvarte unmajjate | [Divyāv, 8 191]
sa tasminnapyāvarte saptakṛtvo bhrāmayitvā nirudhyate | [Divyāv, 8 192]
evaṃ dvitīye tṛtīye caturthe pañcame ṣaṣṭhe āvarte saptakṛtvo bhrāmayitvā nirudhyate yojanaṃ gatvā unmajjate | [Divyāv, 8 193]
evamasau maitrībalaparigṛhīto lokahitārthamabhyudgata uttarati nistaratyabhiniṣkrāmati | [Divyāv, 8 194]
āvartaṃ mahāsamudramabhiniṣkramya āvarto nāma parvato 'manuṣyāvacaritaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 195]
tatra śaṅkho nāma rākṣasaḥ prativasati raudraḥ paraprāṇaharo mahābalo mahākāyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 196]
tasyopariṣṭādyojanamātre śaṅkhanābhī nāmauṣadhī divā dhūmāyate rātrau prajvalati | [Divyāv, 8 197]
sā nāgaparigṛhītā tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 8 198]
sa khalu nāgo divā svapiti rātrau carati | [Divyāv, 8 199]
tatra tena puruṣeṇa divā sukhasuptasya nāgasya ātmānaṃ samanurakṣatā nāgaśarīramaviheṭhayatā auṣadhibalena mantrabalena puṇyabalena śaṅkhanābhī auṣadhī grahītavyā | [Divyāv, 8 200]
gṛhītvā netre añjayitvā śirasi baddhvā samālabhya āvartaḥ parvato 'dhiroḍhavyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 201]
sacedetāṃ vidhimanutiṣṭhati svastikṣemeṇātikrāmati āvartaṃ parvatam aviheṭhitaḥ śaṅkhanābhena rākṣasena | [Divyāv, 8 202]
sacedetāṃ vidhiṃ nānutiṣṭhati auṣadhīṃ vā na labhate labdhāṃ vā na gṛhṇāti tamenaṃ śaṅkhanābho rākṣasaḥ pañcatvamāpādayati | [Divyāv, 8 203]
āvartaṃ parvatamatikramya nīlodo nāma mahāsamudraḥ | [Divyāv, 8 204]
gambhīro 'yaṃ gambhīrāvabhāsaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 205]
nīlode mahāsamudre tārākṣo nāma rākṣasaḥ prativasati raktanetraḥ pradīptaśiroruho vikṛtacaraṇadaśananayanaḥ parvatāyatakukṣiḥ | [Divyāv, 8 206]
sacet svapiti vivṛtānyasya netrāṇi bhavanti tadyathā acirodito bhāskaraḥ | [Divyāv, 8 207]
audārikāścāsya āśvāsapraśvāsā gurugurukāḥ pravartante yathā meghasya garjato 'śanyāṃ ca sphūrjatyāṃ śabdaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 208]
yadā jāgarti nimīlitānyasya bhavanti netrāṇi | [Divyāv, 8 209]
tatra tena puruṣeṇa tasmādeva samudrakūlān mahāmakarīnām auṣadhīṃ samanviṣya gṛhya netre añjayitvā śirasi baddhvā samālabhya mahāntaṃ plavamāsthāya suptaṃ tārākṣaṃ dakarākṣasaṃ viditvā pūrvabuddhabhāṣitāmeraṇḍāṃ nāma mahāvidyāmuccārayatā mantrapadāṃ dakarākṣasasamīpena gantavyam | [Divyāv, 8 210]
sacedetāṃ vidhiṃ nānutiṣṭhati auṣadhīṃ vā na labhate labdhāṃ vā na gṛhṇāti tamenaṃ tārākṣo dakarākṣasa ojaṃ vā ghaṭṭayati cittaṃ vā kṣipati sarveṇa vā sarvaṃ jīvitādvyaparopayati | [Divyāv, 8 211]
nīlodaṃ mahāsamudraṃ samatikramya nīlodo nāma mahāparvataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 212]
tatra nīlagrīvo nāma rākṣasaḥ prativasati pañcaśataparivāra ugratejā raudraḥ paraprāṇaharaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 213]
nīlodo mahāparvata ekanīlo 'khaṇḍo 'cchidro 'suṣiraḥ saṃvṛta ekaghanaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 214]
apīdānīmanimiṣaṃ paśyato netrāṇi vyābādhayate mūrcchāṃ ca saṃjanayati | [Divyāv, 8 215]
tasyopariṣṭādyojanamātre 'moghā nāmauṣadhī vicitrarūpā | [Divyāv, 8 216]
sā nāgaparigṛhītā tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 8 217]
sa khalu nāgo dṛṣṭiviṣo 'pi śvāsaviṣo 'pi sparśaviṣo 'pi daṃṣṭrāviṣo 'pi | [Divyāv, 8 218]
yadā svapiti tadā dhūmāyate | [Divyāv, 8 219]
yaḥ khalu tena dhūmena mṛgo vā pakṣī vā spṛśyate sa pañcatvamāpadyate | [Divyāv, 8 220]
tatra tena puruṣeṇa śiraḥsnātenopoṣitena maitrāyatā karuṇāyatā avyāpannena cittenātmānaṃ samanurakṣatā nāgaśarīram aviheṭhayatā auṣadhī grahītavyā | [Divyāv, 8 221]
netre añjayitvā śirasi baddhvā samālabhya anena vidhinā jānatānuṣṭhitena nīlodaḥ parvato 'bhiroḍhavyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 222]
timiraṃ na bhaviṣyati mūrcchā ca na bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 223]
na cāsya guhyakāḥ śarīre prahariṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 224]
sacedetāṃ vidhiṃ nānutiṣṭhati auṣadhīṃ vā na labhate labdhāṃ vā na gṛhṇāti tamenaṃ nīlagrīvo rākṣasaḥ pañcatvamāpādayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 225]
nīlodaṃ parvataṃ samatikramya vairambho nāma mahāsamudraḥ | [Divyāv, 8 226]
vairambhe mahāsamudre vairambhā nāma vāyavo vānti yaistadudakaṃ kṣobhyate yatrāgatir makarakacchapavallakaśiśumārādīnāṃ pretapiśācakumbhāṇḍakaṭapūtanādīnāṃ kaḥ punarvādo manuṣyāṇām | [Divyāv, 8 227]
tamutsṛjya uttareṇa vairambhasya mahāsamudrasya mahatī tāmrāṭavī anekayojanāyāmavistārā | [Divyāv, 8 228]
tasyāstāmrāṭavyā madhye mahat sālavanaṃ mahaccodapānam | [Divyāv, 8 229]
tatra tāmrākṣo nāma ajagaraḥ prativasati raudraḥ paraprāṇaharaḥ paramadurgandhaḥ pañcayojanāyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 230]
sa ṣaṇmāsān svapiti | [Divyāv, 8 231]
yadā svapiti tadā asya yojanaṃ sāmantakena lālāsya spharitvā tiṣṭhati yadā jāgarti alpāsya lālā bhavati | [Divyāv, 8 232]
tasyopariṣṭānmahān veṇugulmaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 233]
tasmin veṇugulme mahatyaśmaśilā | [Divyāv, 8 234]
tāṃ vīryabalena utpāṭya guhā | [Divyāv, 8 235]
tasyāṃ guhāyāṃ saṃmohanī nāmauṣadhī | [Divyāv, 8 236]
sā rātriṃdivasaṃ prajvalati | [Divyāv, 8 237]
tāṃ gṛhītvā netre añjayitvā śirasi baddhvā samālabhya suptaṃ tāmrākṣamajagaraṃ viditvā auṣadhībalena mantrabalena vā ajagarabhavanasamīpena gantavyam | [Divyāv, 8 238]
sacedetāṃ vidhimanutiṣṭhati svastikṣemābhyāmatikramya aviheṭhitas tāmrākṣeṇājagareṇa tataḥ paścānmūlaphalāni bhakṣayatā gantavyam | [Divyāv, 8 239]
mahatīṃ tāmrāṭavīmatikramya sapta parvatāḥ kaṇṭakaveṇupraticchannāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 240]
tatra tena puruṣeṇa tāmrapaṭṭaiḥ pādau baddhvā tān parvatān vīryabalena laṅghayitvā sapta kṣāranadyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 241]
tāsāṃ tīre mahāśālmalīvanam | [Divyāv, 8 242]
tataḥ śālmalīphalakaiḥ plavaṃ baddhvā abhiruhyātikramitavyā aspṛśatā pānīyam | [Divyāv, 8 243]
sacet spṛśet tadaṅgaṃ śīryate | [Divyāv, 8 244]
sapta kṣāranadīḥ samatikramya triśaṅkur nāma parvataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 245]
triśaṅkau parvate triśaṅkavo nāma kaṇṭakāstīkṣṇāḥ sutīkṣṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 246]
tatastena puruṣeṇa tāmrapaṭṭairvetrapāśaiḥ pādau baddhvā atikramitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 247]
triśaṅkuparvatamatikramya triśaṅkur nāma nadī | [Divyāv, 8 248]
triśaṅkavo nāma kaṇṭakāstīkṣṇā aṣṭādaśāṅgulā udake 'ntargatāstiṣṭhanti | [Divyāv, 8 249]
tatra tena puruṣeṇa śālmalīphalakaiḥ plavaṃ baddhvā atikramitavyam aspṛśatā pānīyam | [Divyāv, 8 250]
sacet patati tatraivānayena vyasanamāpadyate | [Divyāv, 8 251]
yathā triśaṅkuḥ parvataḥ evaṃ triśaṅkukā nāma nadī | [Divyāv, 8 252]
evamayaskilaḥ parvato 'yaskilā nāma nadī | [Divyāv, 8 253]
ayaskilānadīmatikramya aṣṭādaśavakro nāma parvataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 254]
ucchritaśca sarvataḥ saṃvṛto 'dvārakaśca | [Divyāv, 8 255]
asya na kiṃcit nistaraṇamanyatra vṛkṣāgrād vṛkṣamadhiruhya gantavyam | [Divyāv, 8 256]
aṣṭādaśavakraṃ parvatamatikramya aṣṭādaśavakrikā nāma nadī grāhamakarākulā saṃvṛtā ca | [Divyāv, 8 257]
tatra vetrapāśaṃ baddhvā atikramitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 258]
sacet patati anayena vyasanamāpadyate | [Divyāv, 8 259]
aṣṭādaśavakrikāṃ nadīmatikramya ślakṣṇo nāma parvataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 260]
ślakṣṇaḥ parvato mṛdurucchrito 'dvārakaśca | [Divyāv, 8 261]
na cāsya kiṃcinnistaraṇam | [Divyāv, 8 262]
tatrāyaskīlānāṃ koṭyātikramitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 263]
ślakṣṇaṃ parvatamatikramya ślakṣṇā nāma nadī grāhamakarākulā | [Divyāv, 8 264]
saṃvṛtā ca sā nadī | [Divyāv, 8 265]
tatra vetrapāśān baddhvā atikramitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 266]
sacet patati anayena vyasanamāpadyate | [Divyāv, 8 267]
ślakṣṇāṃ nadīmatikramya dhūmanetro nāma parvato dhūmāyate saṃdhūmāyate | [Divyāv, 8 268]
yena khalu tena dhūmena mṛgā vā pakṣiṇo vā spṛśyante pañcatvamāpadyante | [Divyāv, 8 269]
dhūmanetraḥ parvata ucchrito mahāprapāto 'dvārakaśca | [Divyāv, 8 270]
tatra tena puruṣeṇa guhā paryeṣitavyā | [Divyāv, 8 271]
guhāṃ samanviṣya tenātra guhādvāramauṣadhibalena mantrabalena ca moktavyam | [Divyāv, 8 272]
sā ca khalu guhā āśīviṣaparipūrṇā tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 8 273]
te khalu āśīviṣā dṛṣṭiviṣā api sparśaviṣā api | [Divyāv, 8 274]
dhūmanetrasya parvatasyopariṣṭānmahadudakapalvalam | [Divyāv, 8 275]
tasminnudakapalvale mahatyaśmaśilā | [Divyāv, 8 276]
tāṃ vīryabalenotpāṭya guhā | [Divyāv, 8 277]
tasyāṃ guhāyāṃ saṃjīvanī nāmauṣadhī jyotīrasaśca maṇirdīpaprabhāsaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 278]
tāmauṣadhīṃ gṛhītvā saśīrṣapādaṃ samālabhya tāṃ cauṣadhīṃ gṛhītvā guhā praveṣṭavyā | [Divyāv, 8 279]
auṣadhībalena mantrabalena auṣadhīprabhāvāccāśīviṣāḥ kāye na kramiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 280]
evaṃ hi tasmāt parvatānnistaraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 281]
dhūmanetraparvatamatikramya saptāśīviṣaparvatāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 282]
auṣadhībalena mantrabalena ca saptāśīviṣaparvatā atikramitavyāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 283]
saptāśīviṣaparvatānatikramya saptāśīviṣanadyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 284]
tīkṣṇagandhā nāma tatrāśīviṣāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 285]
tatra tena puruṣeṇa māṃsapeśyanveṣitavyā | [Divyāv, 8 286]
tāsāmāśīviṣanadīnāṃ tīre śālmalīvanam | [Divyāv, 8 287]
tataḥ śālmalīphalakaiḥ plavaṃ baddhvā māṃsapeśyā ātmānamācchādya adhiroḍhavyam | [Divyāv, 8 288]
tatasta āśīviṣā māṃsagandhena pārāt pāraṃ gamiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 289]
saptāśīviṣamatikramya mahān sudhāvadātaḥ parvataḥ uccaśca pragṛhītaśca | [Divyāv, 8 290]
so 'dhiroḍhavyas tatra drakṣyasi mahāntaṃ sauvarṇabhūmiṃ pṛthivīpradeśaṃ puṣpaphalacchāyāvṛkṣopaśobhitam | [Divyāv, 8 291]
rohitakāñ janapadān ṛddhāṃśca kṣemāṃśca subhikṣāṃśca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṃśca | [Divyāv, 8 292]
rohitakaṃ ca mahānagaraṃ dvādaśayojanāyāmaṃ saptayojanavistṛtaṃ saptaprākāraparikṣiptaṃ dvāṣaṣṭidvāropaśobhitaṃ bhavanaśatasahasravirājitaṃ suviviktarathyāvīthicatvaraśṛṅgāṭakāntarāpaṇam | [Divyāv, 8 293]
vīṇāvallikāmahatīsughoṣakaiḥ śrotrābhirāmaiśca gītadhvanibhiranuparataprayogaṃ nānāpaṇyasaṃvṛddhaṃ nityapramuditajanaughasaṃkulaṃ tridaśendropendrasadṛśodyānasabhāpuṣkariṇīsampannaṃ kādambahaṃsakāraṇḍavacakravākopaśobhitataḍāgaṃ rohitakaṃ mahārājādhyuṣitaṃ mahāpuruṣavaṇiṅniṣevitam | [Divyāv, 8 294]
yatra maghaḥ sārthavāhaḥ prativasati abhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ paṇḍito vyakto medhāvī āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vistīrṇaviśālaparigraho vaiśravaṇadhanasamudito vaiśravaṇadhanapratispardhī dvīpāntaradvīpagamanavidhijño mahāsamudrayānapātrayāyī | [Divyāv, 8 295]
sa te badaradvīpamahāpattanasya pravṛttimākhyāsyati nimittāni ca darśayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 296]
yathoktaṃ ca vidhimanuṣṭhāsyasi na ca khedamāpatsyase | [Divyāv, 8 297]
evaṃ mahāsārthavāha paramaduṣkarakāraka imāṃ sumerumalayamandarasadṛśīṃ dṛḍhāṃ pratijñāṃ nistariṣyasi | [Divyāv, 8 298]
iyaṃ ca mahāpratijñā śakrabrahmādīnāmapi duṣkarā prāgeva manuṣyabhūtānām | [Divyāv, 8 299]
ityuktvā sā devatā tatraivāntarhitā | [Divyāv, 8 300]
atha supriyaḥ sārthavāhaḥ suptapratibuddho devatāvacanaṃ śrutvā paramavismayamāpannaścintayati nūnamanayā devatayā anekairevaṃvidhaiḥ paramaduṣkaraśatasahasrairbadaradvīpayātrā sādhitapūrvā bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 301]
yadi tāvat sādhitā duṣkarakārikā iyaṃ devatā | [Divyāv, 8 302]
atha sādhyamānā dṛṣṭāḥ paramaduṣkarakārakāste manuṣyāḥ yairanekairduṣkaraśatasahasrairbadaradvīpayātrā sādhitā | [Divyāv, 8 303]
atiduṣkaraṃ caitadasmābhiḥ karaṇīyam | [Divyāv, 8 304]
athavā yadyapyahaṃ lokahitārthe pratipadyeyam saphalo me pariśramaḥ syāt | [Divyāv, 8 305]
yathā anekairduṣkaraśatasahasrair badaradvīpamahāpattanayātrāṃ sādhayiṣyāmi paraṃ lokānugrahaṃ kariṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 8 306]
te 'pi manuṣyāḥ yairanekairduṣkaraśatasahasrairbadaradvīpayātrā sādhitapūrvā | [Divyāv, 8 307]
ahamapi manuṣyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 308]
taiḥ sādhitā | [Divyāv, 8 309]
kasmādahaṃ na sādhayiṣyāmītyanuvicintya supriyo mahāsārthavāho dṛḍhapratijño dṛḍhavīryaparākramo 'nikṣiptotsāha udārapuṇyavipākamaheśākhyo lokahitārthamabhyudgato yathopadiṣṭoddeśasmṛtiparigṛhīto dṛḍhapratijñāṃ samanusmṛtya mahatā vīryabalena ekākī advitīyavyavasāyo yathopadiṣṭāni pañcāntaradvīpaśatāni samatikrāmati | [Divyāv, 8 310]
sapta mahāparvatān sapta mahānadyo vistareṇa sarvāṇi saṃkaṭāni yathoktena vidhinā mūlakandaphalāhāro guṇavati phalake baddhvā paripūrṇairdvādaśabhirvarṣai rohitakaṃ mahānagaramanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 311]
udyāne sthitvā anyatamaṃ puruṣamāmantrayate kaścidbhoḥ puruṣa asmin rohitake mahānagare magho nāma sārthavāhaḥ parivasati sa evamāha asti bhoḥ puruṣa | [Divyāv, 8 312]
kiṃ tarhi mahāvyādhinā grastaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 313]
sthānametadvidyate yattenaivābādhena kālaṃ kariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 8 314]
atha supriyasya mahāsārthavāhasyaitadabhavat mā haiva magho mahāsārthavāho 'dṛṣṭa eva kālaṃ kuryāt | [Divyāv, 8 315]
ko me vyapadeśaṃ kariṣyati tasya badaradvīpamahāpattanasya gamanāyeti viditvā tvaritatvaritam yena maghasya sārthavāhasya niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 316]
sa dvāre nivāryate na labhate praveśaṃ mahāsārthavāhadarśanāya | [Divyāv, 8 317]
dharmatā khalu kuśalā bodhisattvāsteṣu teṣu śilpasthānakarmasthāneṣu | [Divyāv, 8 318]
tato vaidyasaṃjñāṃ ghoṣayitvā praviṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 319]
adrākṣīt supriyo mahāsārthavāho 'riṣṭādhyāyeṣu viditavṛttāntaḥ maghaḥ sārthavāhaḥ ṣaḍbhirmāsaiḥ kālaṃ kariṣyatīti viditvā supriyo mahāsārthavāho 'dhītya vaidyamatāni svayameva mūlagaṇḍapatrapuṣpaphalabhaiṣajyānyānulomikāni vyapadiśati sma vyādhivyupaśamārtham | [Divyāv, 8 320]
paraṃ cainaṃ toṣayati citrākṣaravyañjanapadābhidhānaiḥ śāstrabaddhābhiḥ kathābhiḥ nānāśrutimanorathākhyāyikābhiḥ saṃrañjayati | [Divyāv, 8 321]
dākṣyadākṣiṇyacāturyamādhuryopetamupasthānakarmaṇi satputra iva pitaraṃ bhaktyā gauraveṇa śuśrūṣate | [Divyāv, 8 322]
tato maghasya sārthavāhasya kṣemaṇīyataraṃ cābhūdyāpanīyataraṃ ca | [Divyāv, 8 323]
saṃjñā anena pratilabdhā | [Divyāv, 8 324]
atha magho mahāsārthavāhaḥ pratilabdhasaṃjñaḥ supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhamidamavocat kuto bhavāñ jñānavijñānasampanno 'bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ paṇḍito vyakto medhāvī paṭupracāraḥ sarvaśāstrajñaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ sarvakalābhijñaḥ sarvabhūtarutajña iṅgitajñaḥ kiṃ jātyā bhavān kiṃgotraḥ kena vā kāraṇena amanuṣyāvacaritaṃ deśamabhyāgataḥ evamuktaḥ supriyaḥ sārthavāhaḥ kathayati sādhu sādhu mahāsārthavāha | [Divyāv, 8 325]
kāle 'smi mahāsārthavāhena jātikulagotrāgamanaprayojanaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 326]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāho maghāya sārthavāhāya jātikulagotrāgamanaprayojanaṃ vistareṇārocayati sma paraṃ cainaṃ vijñāpayati sārthavāhānubhāvādahaṃ badaradvīpamahāpattanaṃ paśyeyam | [Divyāv, 8 327]
evamahaṃ syāt paripūrṇamanoratho nistīrṇadṛḍhapratijñaḥ sarvasattvamanorathaparipūrakaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 328]
atha magho mahāsārthavāhaḥ supriyasya mahāsārthavāhasyāśrutapūrvāṃ parahitārthamabhyudyatāṃ dṛḍhapratijñāṃ śrutvā paramavismayajāto 'nimiṣadṛṣṭiḥ suciraṃ nirīkṣya supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhamidamavocat taruṇaśca bhavān dharmakāmaśca | [Divyāv, 8 329]
āścaryamamānuṣaparākramaṃ te paśyāmi yo nāma bhavāñ jambudvīpādamanuṣyāvacaritaṃ parvatasamudranadyottaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ihāgataḥ yatrāmanuṣyāḥ pralayaṃ gacchanti prāgeva manuṣyāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 330]
devaṃ tadbhavantaṃ paśyāmi devānyatamaṃ vā manuṣyaveṣadhāriṇam | [Divyāv, 8 331]
na te kiṃciddustaramasādhyaṃ vā | [Divyāv, 8 332]
api tu ahaṃ mahāvyādhinā grasto mumūrṣuḥ | [Divyāv, 8 333]
bhavāṃścāyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 334]
api tu ko bhavato 'rthe parahitārthe 'bhyudyatasyātmaparityāgamapi na kuryāt tena hi vatsa kṣipraṃ maṅgalapotaṃ samudānaya saṃvaraṃ cāropaya yadāvayoryātrāyanaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 8 335]
evaṃ sārthavāheti supriyo mahāsārthavāho maghāya mahāsārthavāhāya pratiśrutya maṅgalapotaṃ samudānīya saṃvaraṃ cāropya yena magho mahāsārthavāhastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 336]
upasaṃkramya maghaṃ sārthavāhamidamavocat deva samudānīto maṅgalapotaḥ saṃvaraṃ cāropitam yasyedānīṃ mahāsārthavāhaḥ kālaṃ manyate | [Divyāv, 8 337]
atha magho mahāsārthavāho badaradvīpamahāpattanagamanakṛtabuddhiḥ svajanabandhuvargaputradāramitrāmātyajñātisālohitaiḥ sabhṛtyavargeṇa ca rohitakarājñā ca nivāryamāṇo 'pi guṇavati phalake baddhvā āśu supriyasārthavāhasahāyo maṅgalapotamabhiruhya mahāsamudramavatīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 338]
atha magho mahāsārthavāhaḥ supriyasya mahāsārthavāhasya kathayati ahaṃ bāḍhaglāno na śakyāmi sthito gantum | [Divyāv, 8 339]
tadarhasi śayyāṃ kalpayitum yatrāhamapāśrito gamiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 8 340]
api tu asmin mahāsamudre yāvadevaṃvidhāni nimittāni bhavanti udakasya varṇasaṃsthānāni ca mama nivedayitavyāni | [Divyāv, 8 341]
yathā anekāni yojanaśatāni gatvā adrākṣīt supriyo mahāsārthavāha ekapāṇḍaraṃ pānīyam | [Divyāv, 8 342]
dṛṣṭvā punarmaghāya sārthavāhāyārocayati yatkhalu mahāsārthavāha jānīyāḥ ekapāṇḍaraṃ pānīyaṃ paśyāmi | [Divyāv, 8 343]
evamukte maghaḥ sārthavāhaḥ kathayati naitanmahāsārthavāha ekapāṇḍaraṃ pānīyam | [Divyāv, 8 344]
api tu paśyasi tvaṃ dakṣiṇakena mahatsudhāparvatam yadidaṃ tasyaitadanubhāvena pānīyaṃ rañjitam | [Divyāv, 8 345]
yatraikaviṃśatidhātugotrāṇi yaṃ paktvā suvarṇarūpyavaiḍūryānyabhinirvartante yadeke jāmbudvīpakā manuṣyā ratnānyādāya pratinivartante | [Divyāv, 8 346]
idaṃ badaradvīpamahāpattanasya prathamanimittam | [Divyāv, 8 347]
punarapi gacchan paśyati supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ śastravarṇaṃ pānīyam | [Divyāv, 8 348]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarmaghāya sārthavāhāyārocayati yat khalu mahāsārthavāha jānīyāḥ śastravarṇaṃ pānīyaṃ dṛśyate | [Divyāv, 8 349]
maghaḥ sārthavāhaḥ kathayati naitacchastravarṇaṃ pānīyam | [Divyāv, 8 350]
paśyasi tvaṃ dakṣiṇakeṇa mahacchastraparvatam | [Divyāv, 8 351]
tasyaitadanubhāvena pānīyaṃ rañjitam | [Divyāv, 8 352]
atrāpyanekāni dhātugotrāṇi yaṃ paktvā suvarṇarūpyavaidūryasphaṭikānyabhinirvartante yadeke jāmbudvīpakā manuṣyā ratnānyādāya pratinivartante | [Divyāv, 8 353]
idaṃ badaradvīpamahāpattanasya dvitīyaṃ nimittam | [Divyāv, 8 354]
evaṃ lohaparvatāstāmraparvatā rūpyaparvatāḥ suvarṇaparvatāḥ sphaṭikaparvatā vaidūryaparvatāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 355]
adrākṣīt supriyo mahāsārthavāho nīlapītalohitāvadātaṃ pānīyam antarjale ca dīpārciṣaḥ paśyati dīpyamānāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 356]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarmaghāya sārthavāhāyārocayati yatkhalu mahāsārthavāha jānīyāḥ nīlapītalohitāvadātaṃ pānīyaṃ dṛśyate antarjale ca dīpārciṣo dīpyamānāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 357]
evamukte magho mahāsārthavāhaḥ kathayati naitanmahāsārthavāha nīlapītalohitāvadātaṃ pānīyam nāpyete dīpā iva dīpyante | [Divyāv, 8 358]
paśyasi tvaṃ dakṣiṇakena catūratnamayaṃ parvatam | [Divyāv, 8 359]
tasyaitadanubhāvena pānīyaṃ rañjitam | [Divyāv, 8 360]
ye 'pyete dīpā iva dīpyante ete 'ntargatā auṣadhyo dīpyante | [Divyāv, 8 361]
atrāpyanekāni dhātugotrāṇi yaṃ paktvā suvarṇarūpyavaidūryasphaṭikānyabhinirvartante yatraike jāmbudvīpakā manuṣyā ratnānyādāya pratinivartante | [Divyāv, 8 362]
idaṃ badaradvīpamahāpattanasya daśamaṃ nimittam | [Divyāv, 8 363]
api tu mahāsārthavāha iyantyevāhaṃ badaradvīpamahāpattanasya daśa nimittāni jāne gamanaṃ prati ataḥ pareṇa na jāne | [Divyāv, 8 364]
evamukte supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ kathayati kadā badaradvīpamahāpattanasya gamanāyānto bhaviṣyati evamukte maghaḥ sārthavāhaḥ kathayati mayāpi supriya badaradvīpamahāpattanaṃ kārtsnena na dṛṣṭam | [Divyāv, 8 365]
api tu mayā śrutaṃ paurāṇānāṃ mahāsārthavāhānām antikājjīrṇānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ mahallakānām ito jalamapahāya paścimāṃ diśaṃ sthalena gamyate | [Divyāv, 8 366]
tena caivamabhihitam maraṇāntikāccāsya vedanāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 367]
tataḥ supriyāya mahāsārthavāhāya kathayati maraṇāntikā me vedanāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 368]
etattvaṃ maṅgalapotaṃ tīramupanīya vetrapāśaṃ baddhvā maccharīre śarīrapūjāṃ kuruṣva | [Divyāv, 8 369]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāhastaṃ maṅgalapotaṃ tīramupanīya vetrapāśaṃ badhnāti | [Divyāv, 8 370]
atrāntare magho mahāsārthavāhaḥ kālagataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 371]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāho maghaṃ sārthavāhaṃ kālagataṃ viditvā sthale utthāpya śarīre śarīrapūjaṃ kṛtvā cintayati maṅgalapotamāruhya yāsyāmīti | [Divyāv, 8 372]
sa ca poto vāyunā vetrapāśaṃ chittvā apahṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 373]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāhaścatūratnamayasya parvatasya dakṣiṇena pārśvenāṭavyāṃ sthalena samprasthito mūlaphalāni bhakṣayamāṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 374]
anekāni yojanāni gatvā adrākṣīt ślakṣṇaṃ parvatam anupūrvapravaṇamanupūrvaprāgbhāram | [Divyāv, 8 375]
na śakyate 'bhiroḍhum | [Divyāv, 8 376]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāho madhunā pādau pralipyābhirūḍhaśca avatīrṇaśca anekāni yojanāni gatvā mūlaphalāhāro gataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 377]
sa tatra paśyati mahāntaṃ parvatamuccaṃ ca pragṛhītaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 8 378]
niḥsaraṇaṃ paryeṣamāṇo na labhate na cāsya kaścinniḥsaraṇavyapadeṣṭā | [Divyāv, 8 379]
tataścintāparaḥ śayitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 380]
tatra ca parvate nīlādo nāma yakṣaḥ prativasati | [Divyāv, 8 381]
sa saṃlakṣayati ayaṃ bodhisattvo lokahitārthamudyataḥ parikliśyate yannvahamasya sāhāyyaṃ kalpayeyam | [Divyāv, 8 382]
idamanucintya supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhamidamavocat ito mahāsārthavāha pūrveṇa yojanaṃ gatvā trīṇi parvataśṛṅgāṇy anupūrvanimnānyanupūrvapravaṇānyanupūrvaprāgbhārāṇi | [Divyāv, 8 383]
tatra tvayā vetraśiṭām baddhvā atikramitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 384]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ suptaprabuddho vetraśiṭām baddhvā tāni parvataśṛṅgāṇyatikrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 385]
bhūyaḥ samprasthito 'drākṣīt supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ sphaṭikaparvataṃ ślakṣṇaṃ nirālambamagamyaṃ manuṣyamātrasya | [Divyāv, 8 386]
na cāsyopāyaṃ paśyati taṃ parvatamabhirohaṇāyeti viditvā cintāparo 'horātramavasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 387]
tasmiṃśca parvate candraprabho nāma yakṣaḥ prativasati | [Divyāv, 8 388]
sa cintāparaṃ sārthavāhaṃ viditvā lokahitārthamabhyudyataṃ mahāyānasamprasthitaṃ prasannacittaṃ copetyāśvāsayati na khalu mahāsārthavāhena viṣādaḥ karaṇīya iti | [Divyāv, 8 389]
pūrveṇa krośamātraṃ gatvā mahaccandanavanam | [Divyāv, 8 390]
tasmiṃśca candanavane mahatyaśmaśilā | [Divyāv, 8 391]
tāṃ vīryabalenotpāṭya guhāṃ drakṣyasi | [Divyāv, 8 392]
tasyāṃ guhāyāṃ prabhāsvarā nāmauṣadhī pañcaguṇopetā | [Divyāv, 8 393]
tayā gṛhītayā nāsya kāye śastraṃ kramiṣyati amanuṣyāścāvatāraṃ na lapsyante balaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca saṃjanayati ālokaṃ ca karoti | [Divyāv, 8 394]
tenālokena drakṣyasi catūratnamayaṃ sopānam | [Divyāv, 8 395]
tena sopānena sphaṭikaparvatamatikramitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 396]
sphaṭikaparvatamatikrāntasya te prabhāsvarā auṣadhyantardhāsyati | [Divyāv, 8 397]
tatra te na śocitavyaṃ na kranditavyaṃ na paridevitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 398]
atha candraprabho yakṣaḥ supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhaṃ samanuśāsya tatraivāntarhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 399]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāhaścandraprabheṇa mahāyakṣeṇa samāśvāsya ādeśitamārgo yathoktena vidhinā sphaṭikaparvatamatikrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 400]
atikrāntasya cāsya prabhāsvarā auṣadhyantarhitā | [Divyāv, 8 401]
bhūyaḥ samprasthito 'drākṣīt supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ sauvarṇaṃ mahānagaramārāmasampannaṃ puṣkariṇīsampannam | [Divyāv, 8 402]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāho nagaradvāraṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 403]
yāvadbaddhaṃ nagaraṃ paśyati | [Divyāv, 8 404]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarudyānaṃ gatvā cintayati yadyapyahaṃ nagaramadrākṣam tadapi śūnyam | [Divyāv, 8 405]
kadā badaradvīpasya mahāpattanasyāgamanāyādhvā bhaviṣyatīti viditvā śayitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 406]
atha sā pūrvadevatā supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhaṃ durmanasaṃ viditvā rātryāḥ pratyūṣasamaya upasaṃkramya samāśvāsya utkarṣayati sādhu sādhu mahāsārthavāha nistīrṇāni te mahāsamudraparvatanadīkāntārāṇi manuṣyāmanuṣyāgamyāni | [Divyāv, 8 407]
samprāpto 'si badaradvīpamahāpattanaṃ manuṣyāmanuṣyānavacaritaṃ maheśākhyapuruṣādhyuṣitam | [Divyāv, 8 408]
kiṃ tarhi na sāmpratamaprasādaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 409]
indriyāṇi ca gopayitavyāni cakṣurādīni kāyagatā smṛtirbhāvayitavyā | [Divyāv, 8 410]
śvobhūte nagaradvāraṃ trikoṭayitavyam | [Divyāv, 8 411]
tataścatasraḥ kinnarakanyā nirgamiṣyanti abhirūpā darśanīyāḥ prāsādikāścāturyamādhuryasampannāḥ sarvāṅgapratyaṅgopetāḥ paramarūpābhijātāḥ sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitā hasitaramitaparicāritanṛttagītavāditrakalāsvabhijñāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 412]
tāstvāmatyarthamupalālayanti evaṃ ca vakṣyanti etu mahāsārthavāhaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 413]
svāgataṃ mahāsārthavāha asmākam asvāminīnāṃ svāmī bhava apatikānāṃ patiralayanānāṃ layano 'dvīpānāṃ dvīpo 'trāṇānāṃ trāṇo 'śaraṇānāṃ śaraṇamaparāyaṇānāṃ parāyaṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 414]
imāni ca te 'nnagṛhāṇi pānagṛhāṇi vastragṛhāṇi śayanagṛhāṇyārāmaramaṇīyāni prabhūtāni ca jāmbudvīpakāni ratnāni tadyathā maṇayo muktā vaidūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālarajatajātarūpamaśmagarbhamusāragalvo lohitikā dakṣiṇāvartāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 415]
etāni ca te ratnāni | [Divyāv, 8 416]
tvaṃ cāsmābhiḥ sārdhaṃ krīḍasva ramasva paricārayasva | [Divyāv, 8 417]
tatra te tāsu mātṛsaṃjñā upasthāpayitavyā bhaginīsaṃjñā duhitṛsaṃjñā upasthāpayitavyā | [Divyāv, 8 418]
daśākuśalāḥ karmapathā vigarhitavyāḥ daśa kuśalāḥ karmapathāḥ saṃvarṇayitavyāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 419]
subahvapi te pralobhyamānena rāgasaṃjñā notpādayitavyā | [Divyāv, 8 420]
sacedutpādayiṣyasi tatraivānayena vyasanamāpatsyase | [Divyāv, 8 421]
sūpasthitasmṛtestava saphalaḥ śramo bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 422]
yadyapi te subhāṣitasyārghamaṇiṃ prayaccheyuḥ tatastvayā nipuṇaṃ praṣṭavyāḥ asya ratnasya bhaginyaḥ ko 'nubhāva iti | [Divyāv, 8 423]
evaṃ dvitīyaṃ kinnaranagaramanuprāptasyāṣṭau kinnarakanyā nirgamiṣyanti tāsāṃ pūrvikānāmantikādabhirūpatarāśca | [Divyāv, 8 424]
tatrāpi te eṣānupūrvī karaṇīyā | [Divyāv, 8 425]
yāvaccaturthakinnaranagaraprāptasya te dvātriṃśat kinnarakanyā nirgamiṣyanti tāsāṃ pūrvikānāmantikādabhirūpatarāśca darśanīyatarāśca prāsādikatarāścāpsarasaḥ pratispardhinyaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 426]
śatasahasraśobhitā bhaviṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 427]
tatrāpi te eṣaivānupūrvī karaṇīyā | [Divyāv, 8 428]
ityuktvā sā devatā tatraivāntarhitā | [Divyāv, 8 429]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ pramuditamanāḥ sukhapratibuddhaḥ kālyamevotthāya sauvarṇaṃ kinnaranagaramanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 430]
dvāramūlamupasaṃkramya trikoṭayati | [Divyāv, 8 431]
tataḥ supriyeṇa mahāsārthavāhena trikoṭite dvāre catasraḥ kinnarakanyā nirgatā abhirūpā darśanīyāḥ prāsādikāścāturyamādhuryasampannāḥ sarvāṅgapratyaṅgopetāḥ paramarūpābhijātā hasitaramitaparicāritanṛttagītavāditrakalāsvabhijñāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 432]
tā evamāhuḥ etu mahāsārthavāhaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 433]
svāgataṃ mahāsārthavāha | [Divyāv, 8 434]
asmākam asvāminīnāṃ svāmī bhava apatīnāṃ patiralayanānāṃ layano 'dvīpānāṃ dvīpo 'śaraṇānāṃ śaraṇo 'trāṇānāṃ trāṇo 'parāyaṇānāṃ parāyaṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 435]
imāni ca te 'nnagṛhāṇi pānagṛhāṇi vastragṛhāṇi śayanagṛhāṇyārāmaramaṇīyāni vanaramaṇīyāni puṣkariṇīramaṇīyāni ca | [Divyāv, 8 436]
jāmbudvīpakāni ratnāni tadyathāmaṇayo muktā vaidūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālarajatajātarūpamaśmagarbho musāragalvo lohitikā dakṣiṇāvartā etāni ca | [Divyāv, 8 437]
tvaṃ cāsmābhiḥ sārdhaṃ krīḍasva ramasva paricārayasva | [Divyāv, 8 438]
atha supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhaṃ sūpasthitasmṛtiṃ tāḥ kinnarakanyāḥ sarvāṅgairanuparigṛhya sauvarṇaṃ kinnaranagaraṃ praveśya prāsādamabhiropya prajñapta evāsane niṣādayanti | [Divyāv, 8 439]
niṣaṇṇaḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāho daśākuśalān karmapathān vigarhati daśa kuśalān karmapathān saṃvarṇayati subahvapi pralobhyamāno na śakyate skhalayitum | [Divyāv, 8 440]
tuṣṭāśca tāḥ kinnarakanyāḥ kathayanti āścaryam yatredānīṃ daharaśca bhavān dharmakāmaśca | [Divyāv, 8 441]
na ca kāmeṣu sajjase vā badhyase vā | [Divyāv, 8 442]
prabhūtaiśca ratnaiśca pravārayanti | [Divyāv, 8 443]
dharmadeśanāvarjitāśca ekaṃ saubhāsinikaṃ ratnamanuprayacchanti | [Divyāv, 8 444]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāhastasya ratnasya prabhāvānveṣī kathayati asya ratnasya bhaginyaḥ ko 'nubhāva iti | [Divyāv, 8 445]
tāḥ kathayanti yatkhalu sārthavāha jānīyāḥ tadeva poṣadhe pañcadaśyāṃ śiraḥsnāta upoṣadhoṣita idaṃ maṇiratnaṃ dhvajāgre āropya yojanasahasraṃ sāmantakena yo yenārthī bhavati hiraṇyena vā suvarṇena vā annena vā vastreṇa vā pānena vā alaṃkāraviśeṣeṇa vā dvipādena vā catuṣpādena vā yānena vā vāhanena vā dhanena vā dhānyena vā sa cittamutpādayatu vācaṃ ca niścārayatu | [Divyāv, 8 446]
sahacittotpādād vāgniścāraṇena yathepsitāścopakaraṇaviśeṣā ākāśādavatariṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 447]
ayamasya ratnasyānubhāvaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 448]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāhastāḥ kinnarakanyā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya mātṛbhaginīduhitṛvat pratisaṃmodya sauvarṇāt kinnaranagarāt pratiniṣkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 449]
adrākṣīt supriyo mahāsārthavāho rūpyamayaṃ kinnaranagaramārāmasampannaṃ vanasampannaṃ puṣkariṇīsampannam | [Divyāv, 8 450]
tatrāpi supriyeṇa sārthavāhena trikoṭite dvāre'ṣṭau kinnarakanyā nirgatāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 451]
tā apyevamāhuḥ etu mahāsārthavāhaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 452]
svāgataṃ mahāsārthavāhāya | [Divyāv, 8 453]
asmākamasvāmikānāṃ svāmī bhava pūrvavadyāvattābhirapi dharmadeśanāvarjitābhistadviśiṣṭataraṃ dvisāhasrayojanavarṣakaṃ maṇiratnamanupradattam | [Divyāv, 8 454]
tatrāpi supriyo mahāsārthavāhastāḥ kinnarakanyā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya mātṛbhaginīduhitṛvat pratisaṃmodya rūpyamayāt kinnaranagarāt pratiniṣkrānto yāvat tṛtīyaṃ vaiḍūryamayaṃ kinnaranagaramanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 455]
tatrāpi supriyeṇa sārthavāhena trikoṭite dvāre ṣoḍaśa kinnarakanyā nirgatāḥ tāsāṃ pūrvikānāmantikādabhirūpatarāśca prāsādikatarāśca | [Divyāv, 8 456]
tā api dharmadeśanāvarjitāstata eva viśiṣṭataraṃ saubhāsinikaṃ trisāhasrayojanikaṃ ratnamanuprayacchanti | [Divyāv, 8 457]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāhastasya ratnasya prabhāvānveṣī kathayati asya ratnasya bhaginyaḥ ko'nubhāva iti kinnarakanyāḥ kathayanti pūrvavat | [Divyāv, 8 458]
supriyo mahāsārthavāhastāḥ kinnarakanyā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya mātṛbhaginīduhitṛvat pratisaṃmodya tṛtīyāt kinnaranagarāt pratiniṣkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 459]
adrākṣīt supriyo mahāsārthavāhaścaturthaṃ catūratnamayaṃ kinnaranagaram ārāmodyānaprāsādadevakulapuṣkariṇītaḍāgasuvibhaktarathyāvīthīcatvaraśṛṅgāṭakāntarāpaṇasuracitagandhojjvalaṃ nānāgītavāditayuvatimadhurasvaravajravaiḍūryaśātakumbhamayaprākāratoraṇopaśobhitam | [Divyāv, 8 460]
dvāraṃ trirākoṭayati | [Divyāv, 8 461]
tataḥ supriyeṇa sārthavāhena trirākoṭite dvāre dvātriṃśat kinnarakanyā nirgatāḥ tāsāṃ pūrvikāṇāmantikādabhirūpatarāśca darśanīyatarāścāpsarasaḥ pratispardhinyaḥ śatasahasraśobhitāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 462]
tā apyevamāhuḥ etu mahāsārthavāhaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 463]
svāgataṃ mahāsārthavāhāya | [Divyāv, 8 464]
asmākam asvāmikānāṃ svāmī bhava apatīnāṃ patir alayanānāṃ layano 'dvīpānāṃ dvīpo 'śaraṇānāṃ śaraṇo 'trāṇānāṃ trāṇo 'parāyaṇānāṃ parāyaṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 465]
imāni ca te 'nnagṛhāṇi pānagṛhāṇi vastragṛhāṇi śayanagṛhāṇyārāmaramaṇīyāni vanaramaṇīyāni puṣkariṇīramaṇīyāni | [Divyāv, 8 466]
prabhūtāni ca jāmbudvīpakāni ratnāni tadyathā maṇayo muktā vaiḍūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālarajataṃ jātarūpamaśmagarbho musāragalvo lohitikā dakṣiṇāvartāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 467]
etāni ca te vayaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 8 468]
asmābhiḥ sārdhaṃ krīḍasva ramasva paricārayasva | [Divyāv, 8 469]
tatrāpi supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ sūpasthitasmṛtistāḥ kinnarakanyā vividhairdharmapadavyañjanaiḥ paritoṣayāmāsa | [Divyāv, 8 470]
tuṣṭāśca tāḥ kinnarakanyāḥ supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhaṃ sarvāṅgairanuparigṛhya catūratnamayaṃ kinnaranagaramanupraveśya prāsādamabhiropya prajñapta evāsane niṣādayanti | [Divyāv, 8 471]
niṣaṇṇaḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāho daśākuśalān karmapathān vigarhati daśa kuśalān karmapathān saṃvarṇayati subahvapi pralobhyamāno na śakyate skhalayitum | [Divyāv, 8 472]
tuṣṭāśca tāḥ kinnarakanyāḥ kathayanti āścaryam yatredānīṃ daharaśca bhavān dharmakāmaśca | [Divyāv, 8 473]
na ca kāmeṣu sajjase vā badhyase vā | [Divyāv, 8 474]
prabhūtaiśca ratnaiḥ pravārayanti | [Divyāv, 8 475]
tā api dharmadeśanāvarjitāḥ saubhāsinikaṃ jāmbudvīpapradhānam anargheyamūlyam anantaguṇaprabhāvaṃ badaradvīpamahāpattane sarvasvabhūtaṃ ratnamanuprayacchanti | [Divyāv, 8 476]
evaṃ ca kathayanti idamasmākaṃ mahāsārthavāha maṇiratnaṃ badareṇa bhrātrā kinnararājñā anupradattam asmin badaradvīpamahāpattane cihnabhūtamālakṣyabhūtaṃ maṇḍanabhūtaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 8 477]
tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ kathayati asya ratnasya ko 'nubhāva iti tāḥ kathayanti yatkhalu mahāsārthavāha jānīyāḥ idaṃ maṇiratnaṃ tadeva poṣadhoṣito dhvajāgre baddhvā āropya kṛtsne jambudvīpe ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ karaṇīyam śṛṇvantu bhavanto jambudvīpanivāsinaḥ strīmanuṣyāḥ yuṣmākam yo yenārthī upakaraṇaviśeṣeṇa hiraṇyena vā suvarṇena vā ratnena vā annena vā pānena vā vastreṇa vā bhojanena vā alaṃkāraviśeṣeṇa vā dvipadena vā catuṣpadena vā vāhanena vā yānena vā dhanena vā dhānyena vā sa cittamutpādayatu vacanaṃ ca niścārayatu | [Divyāv, 8 478]
sahacittotpādādvāgniścāraṇena ca yathepsitāścopakaraṇaviśeṣā asya ratnasyānubhāvādākāśādavatariṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 479]
ayaṃ tu prativiśeṣaḥ yāni cāsya lokasya bhavanti mahābhayāni tadyathā rājato vā caurato vā agnito vā udakato vā manuṣyato vā amanuṣyato vā siṃhato vā vyāghrato vā dvipatarakṣuto vā yakṣarākṣasapretapiśācakumbhāṇḍapūtanakaṭapūtanato vā ītayopadravo vā upasargo vā anāvṛṣṭirvā durbhikṣabhayāni vā asminnucchrite ratnaviśeṣe ima ītayopadravā na bhaviṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 480]
ityuktvā tāḥ kinnarakanyāḥ supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhaṃ saṃrādhayāmāsuḥ sādhu sādhu mahāsārthavāha nistīrṇāni mahāsamudraparvatanadīkāntārāṇi | [Divyāv, 8 481]
pūritā te dṛḍhasupratijñā | [Divyāv, 8 482]
saphalīkṛtā te śraddhā | [Divyāv, 8 483]
te gopitānīndriyāṇi | [Divyāv, 8 484]
sādhitā badaradvīpamahāpattanayātrā | [Divyāv, 8 485]
adhigataṃ te sarvajanamanorathasampādakaṃ jambudvīpapradhānaṃ ratnaviśeṣam | [Divyāv, 8 486]
api tu yena tvaṃ pathenāgataḥ amanuṣyāstāvat pralayaṃ gaccheyuḥ prāgeva manuṣyāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 487]
anyadeva vayaṃ sanmārgaṃ vyapadekṣyāmaḥ kṣipraṃ vārāṇasīgamanāya | [Divyāv, 8 488]
tacchṛṇu manasi kuru bhāṣiṣyāmaḥ itaḥ paścime digbhāge sapta parvatānatikramya mahāparvata uccaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 489]
tasmin parvate lohitākṣo nāma rākṣasaḥ prativasati raudraḥ paraprāṇaharaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 490]
sa ca parvato 'manuṣyāvacaritaḥ kṛṣṇamandhakāraṃ savisphuliṅgaṃ vāyuṃ mokṣayati | [Divyāv, 8 491]
tatra te etadeva ratnaṃ dhvajāgre 'varopayitvā gantavyam | [Divyāv, 8 492]
ratnaprabhāvācca te ītayo vilayaṃ gamiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 8 493]
mahāparvatamatikramya aparaparvataḥ | [Divyāv, 8 494]
tasmin parvate 'gnimukho nāgaḥ prativasati | [Divyāv, 8 495]
sa tava gandhamāghrāya sapta rātriṃdivasānyaśaniṃ pātayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 496]
tatra ratnaguhāṃ samanviṣya praveṣṭavyam | [Divyāv, 8 497]
saptarātrasya cātyayādduṣṭanāgaḥ svapiṣyati | [Divyāv, 8 498]
śayite duṣṭanāge parvatamadhiroḍhavyam | [Divyāv, 8 499]
tatra drakṣyasi samaṃ bhūmipradeśamakṛṣṭoptaṃ ca taṇḍulaphalaśālim akaṇakamatuṣaṃ śuciṃ niṣpūtigandhikaṃ caturaṅgulaparyavanaddham | [Divyāv, 8 500]
yastamaṣṭamyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ vā bālāho'śvarājaḥ paribhujya sukhī arogo balavān prīṇitendriyaḥ pūrvakāyamabhyunnamayyodānamudānayati kaḥ pāragāmī kaḥ pāragāmī kaṃ pāraṃ nayāmi svastikṣemābhyāṃ jambudvīpamanuprāpayāmi sa tvayopasaṃkramya idaṃ syādvacanīyam ahaṃ pāragāmī māṃ pāraṃ naya māṃ svastikṣemābhyāṃ vārāṇasīmanuprāpaya | [Divyāv, 8 501]
atha sa supriyo mahāsārthavāhastāḥ kinnarakanyā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya mātṛduhitṛvat pratisaṃmodya yathoddiṣṭena mārgeṇa yathoktena vidhinā anupūrveṇa taṃ bhūmipradeśamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 502]
sa ca bālāho'śvarājaścarannevamāha kaḥ pāragāmī kaḥ pāragāmī kaṃ pāraṃ nayāmi svastikṣemābhyāṃ jambudvīpamanuprāpayāmi tataḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāho yena bālāho 'śvarājastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 503]
upasaṃkramya ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇaṃ jānumaṇḍalaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yena bālāho 'śvarājastenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bālāhamaśvarājamidamavocat ahaṃ pāragāmī ahaṃ pāragāmī naya mām | [Divyāv, 8 504]
svastikṣemābhyāṃ vārāṇasīmanuprāpaya | [Divyāv, 8 505]
evamukte bālāho 'śvarājaḥ supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhamidamavocat na te mahāsārthavāha mama pṛṣṭhādhirūḍhena diśo nāvalokayitavyāḥ nimīlitākṣeṇa te stheyam | [Divyāv, 8 506]
ityuktvā bālāho'śvarājaḥ pṛṣṭhamupanāmayati | [Divyāv, 8 507]
atha supriyo mahāsārthavāho bālāhasyāśvarājasya pṛṣṭhamadhiruhya yathānuśiṣṭo 'lpaiśca kṣaṇalavamuhūrtairvārāṇasīmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 508]
sva udyāne 'vataritaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 509]
avatīrya supriyo mahāsārthavāho bālāhāśvarājapṛṣṭhād bālāhāśvarājaṃ tripradakṣiṇīkṛtya pādābhivandanaṃ karoti | [Divyāv, 8 510]
tato bālāho 'śvarājaḥ supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhaṃ saṃrādhayāmāsa sādhu sādhu mahāsārthavāha | [Divyāv, 8 511]
nistīrṇāni te mahāsamudraparvatanadīkāntārāṇi | [Divyāv, 8 512]
pūritā te dṛḍhapratijñā | [Divyāv, 8 513]
saphalīkṛtaste 'dhvā | [Divyāv, 8 514]
gopitānīndriyāṇi | [Divyāv, 8 515]
sādhitā te badaradvīpamahāpattanayātrā | [Divyāv, 8 516]
adhigataste sarvajanamanorathasampādako jambudvīpasya pradhāno ratnaviśeṣaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 517]
evaṃ hi parahitārthamabhyudyatāḥ kurvanti sattvaviśeṣāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 518]
ityuktvā bālāho 'śvarājaḥ prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 519]
athāciraprakrānte bālāhe 'śvarājani supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ svagṛhaṃ praviṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 520]
aśrauṣurvārāṇasīnivāsinaḥ paurā brahmadattaśca kāśirājaḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ pūrṇena varṣaśatena saṃsiddhayātraḥ pūrṇamanorathaḥ svagṛhamanuprāpta iti | [Divyāv, 8 521]
śrutvā ca punarbrahmadattaḥ kāśirāja ānanditaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 522]
pauravargaḥ supriyaṃ sārthavāhaṃ saṃrādhayāmāsa | [Divyāv, 8 523]
aśrauṣīt tat pūrvakaṃ caurasahasramanyaśca jano dhanārthī supriyo mahāsārthavāhaḥ saṃsiddhayātraḥ paripūrṇamanoratha āgata iti | [Divyāv, 8 524]
srutvā ca punarupasaṃkramya supriyaṃ mahāsārthavāhamidamavocan parikṣīṇadhanāḥ sma iti | [Divyāv, 8 525]
evamukte mahāsārthavāhastān sarvān maitreṇa cakṣuṣā vyavalokya vijñāpayati gacchantu bhavantaḥ svakasvakeṣu vijiteṣu | [Divyāv, 8 526]
yo yenārthī upakaraṇaviśeṣeṇa bhavati sa tasyārthe cittamutpādayatu vācaṃ ca niścārayatu | [Divyāv, 8 527]
śrutvā ca punaḥ prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 528]
