atha supriyo mahāsārthavāhastadeva poṣadhe pañcadaśyāṃ śiraḥsnāta upoṣadhoṣito yattatprathamalabdhaṃ maṇiratnaṃ dhvajāgre āropya vācaṃ ca niścārayati yojanasahasrasāmantakena yathepsitāni sattvānāmupakaraṇānyutpadyante sahābhidhānācca yo yenārthī tasya tadvarṣaṃ bhavati | [Divyāv, 8 529]
tataḥ paripūrṇamanorathāste sattvāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 530]
taccaurasahasraṃ supriyeṇa mahāsārthavāhena daśasu kuśaleṣu karmapatheṣu pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 531]
atrāntarāt kālagate brahmadatte kāśirājani paurāmātyaiḥ supriyo mahāsārthavāho rājābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 532]
mahābhiṣiktena supriyeṇa mahārājñā dvitīyaṃ maṇiratnaṃ dhvajāgre āropya pūrvavidhinā dviyojanasahasrasāmantakena yathepsitāni sattvānāmupakaraṇānyutpadyantāmiti sahābhidhānācca yo yenārthī tasya tadvarṣati | [Divyāv, 8 533]
tṛtīyena maṇiratnena yathoktena vidhinā dhvajāgrocchritena yathepsitopakaraṇaviśeṣavarṣaṇāni sampannāni | [Divyāv, 8 534]
evaṃ triyojanasahasrasāmantakenopakaraṇaiḥ strīmanuṣyāḥ saṃtarpitāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 535]
tato 'nupūrveṇa jambudvīpaiśvaryabhūtena supriyeṇa mahārājñā tadeva poṣadhe pañcadaśyāṃ śiraḥsnātenopoṣadhoṣitena kṛtsne jambudvīpe ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā upakaraṇotpannābhilāṣiṇāṃ strīmanuṣyāṇāṃ jambudvīpanivāsinām yanmaṇiratnaṃ badaradvīpamahāpattanasarvasvabhūtam yathepsitam sarvopakaraṇavarṣiṇaṃ dhvajāgre āropayāmāsa | [Divyāv, 8 536]
samanantaraṃ dhvajāgrāvaropite tasmiñ jambudvīpapradhānamaṇiratne kṛtsno jambudvīpanivāsī mahājanakāyo yathepsitairupakaraṇaviśeṣaiḥ saṃtarpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 537]
upakaraṇasaṃtarpitaśca jambudvīpanivāsī janakāyaḥ supriyeṇa rājñā daśasu kuśaleṣu karmapatheṣu pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 538]
tato jyeṣṭhaṃ kumāraṃ rājyaiśvaryādhipatye pratiṣṭhāpya rājarṣibrahmacaryaṃ caritvā caturo brāhmān vihārān bhāvayitvā kāmeṣu kāmacchandaṃ prahāya tadbahulavihārī brahmalokasabhāgatāyāṃ copapanno mahābrahmā saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 539]
bhagavānāha kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau supriyo nāma mahāsārthavāhaḥ ahameva tena kālena tena samayena bodhisattvacaryāyāṃ vartitavān | [Divyāv, 8 540]
yattaccaurasahasram etadeva bhikṣusahasram | [Divyāv, 8 541]
yā sā pūrvadevatā kāśyapaḥ samyaksambuddho bodhisattvabhūtaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 8 542]
yaścāsau magho mahāsārthavāhaḥ eṣa eva śāriputro bhikṣuḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 8 543]
yaścāsau nīlādo nāma mahāyakṣaḥ eṣa evānando bhikṣustena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 8 544]
yaścāsau candraprabho yakṣaḥ eṣa evāniruddho bhikṣuḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 8 545]
yaścāsau lohitākṣo nāma mahāyakṣaḥ sa eṣa eva devadattastena kalena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 8 546]
yaścāsau agnimukho nāma nāgaḥ eṣa eva māraḥ pāpīyān sa tena kalena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 8 547]
yaścāsau bālāho 'śvarājaḥ maitreyo bodhisattvastena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 8 548]
tadā tāvanmayā bhikṣavo dṛḍhapratijñena pratijñāpūraṇārthaṃ saptavārāṃścaurasahasrāt sārthaḥ paritrātaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 549]
aparituṣṭāṃśca caurān viditvā dṛḍhapratijñā kṛtā | [Divyāv, 8 550]
kṛtvā cānekairduṣkaraśatasahasrair badaradvīpamahāpattanasya yātrāṃ sādhayitvā caurasahasrapramukhaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jambudvīpaṃ dhanena saṃtarpayitvā daśasu kuśaleṣu karmapatheṣu pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 551]
idānīmapi mayā anekairduṣkaraśatasahasrairanuttaraṃ jñānamadhigamya maitrāyatā karuṇayā saptakṛtvaścaurasahasrasakāśāt sārthaḥ paritrātaḥ | [Divyāv, 8 552]
aparituṣṭaṃ ca caurasahasraṃ viditvā yāvadāptaṃ dhanena saṃtarpayitvā atyantaniṣṭhe 'nuttare yogakṣeme nirvāṇe pratiṣṭhāpitāḥ | [Divyāv, 8 553]
anekāni ca devamanuṣyaśatasahasrāṇi yakṣarākṣasapretapiśācakumbhāṇḍapūtanakaṭapūtanakoṭiśatasahasrāṇi śaraṇagamanaśikṣāpadeṣu pratiṣṭhāpitāni | [Divyāv, 8 554]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 8 555]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 8 556]
{Divyāv, 9}
śrāvastyāṃ nidānam | [Divyāv, 9 1]
tena khalu samayena bhadraṃkare nagare ṣaḍ janā mahāpuṇyāḥ prativasanti meṇḍhako gṛhapatir meṇḍhakapatnī meṇḍhakaputro meṇḍhakasnuṣā meṇḍhakadāso meṇḍhakadāsī | [Divyāv, 9 2]
kathaṃ meṇḍhako gṛhapatirjñāto mahāpuṇyaḥ sa yadi riktakāni kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇi paśyati sahadarśanādeva pūryante | [Divyāv, 9 3]
evaṃ meṇḍhako gṛhapatirjñāto mahāpuṇyaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 4]
kathaṃ meṇḍhakapatnī sā ekasyārthāya sthālikāṃ sādhayati śatāni sahasrāṇi ca bhuñjate | [Divyāv, 9 5]
evaṃ meṇḍhakapatnī | [Divyāv, 9 6]
kathaṃ meṇḍhakaputraḥ tasya pañcaśatiko nakulako kaṭyāṃ baddhastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 9 7]
sa yadi śataṃ sahasraṃ vā parityajati tadā pūrṇa eva tiṣṭhati na parikṣīyate | [Divyāv, 9 8]
evaṃ meṇḍhakaputraḥ | [Divyāv, 9 9]
kathaṃ meṇḍhakasnuṣā sā ekasyārthāya gandhaṃ sampādayati śatasahasrasya paryāptirbhavati | [Divyāv, 9 10]
evaṃ meṇḍhakasnuṣā | [Divyāv, 9 11]
kathaṃ meṇḍhakadāsaḥ sa yadaikaṃ halasīraṃ kṛṣati tadā sapta sīrāḥ kṛṣṭā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 9 12]
evaṃ meṇḍhakadāsaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 13]
kathaṃ meṇḍhakadāsī mahāpuṇyā sā yadaikaṃ vastu rakṣati tatsaptaguṇaṃ syāt | [Divyāv, 9 14]
yadā ekamātraṃ pratijāgarti tadā sapta mātrāḥ saṃpadyante | [Divyāv, 9 15]
evaṃ meṇḍhakadāsī mahāpuṇyā | [Divyāv, 9 16]
dharmatā khalu buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ mahākāruṇikānāṃ caturoghottīrṇānāṃ caturṛddhipādacaraṇatalasupratiṣṭhitānāṃ caturṣu saṃgrahavastuṣu dīrgharātrakṛtaparicayānāṃ pañcāṅgavipratihīnānāṃ pañcagatisamatikrāntānāṃ ṣaḍaṅgasamanvāgatānāṃ ṣaṭpāramitāparipūrṇānāṃ saptabodhyaṅgakusumāḍhyānām aṣṭāṅgamārgadeśikānāṃ navānupūrvasamāpattikuśalānāṃ daśabalabalināṃ daśadiksamāpūrṇayaśasāṃ daśaśatavaśavartiprativiśiṣṭānāṃ trī rātrestrirdivasasya ṣaṭkṛtvo rātriṃdivasasya buddhacakṣuṣā lokaṃ vyavalokya jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate ko hīyate ko vardhate kaḥ kṛcchraprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃkaṭaprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃbādhaprāptaḥ kaḥ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhaprāptaḥ ko 'pāyanimnaḥ ko 'pāyapravaṇaḥ ko 'pāyaprāgbhāraḥ kamahamapāyamārgādvyutthāpya svargaphale mokṣe ca pratiṣṭhāpayeyam kasya kāmapaṅkanimagnasya hastoddhāramanupradadyām | [Divyāv, 9 17]
kamāryadhanavirahitam āryadhanaiśvaryādhipatye pratiṣṭhāpayāmi kasyānavaropitāni kuśalamūlānyavaropayeyam kasyāvaropitāni paripācayeyam kasya pakvāni vimocayeyam kasyājñānatimirapaṭalaparyavanaddhanetrasya jñānāñjanaśalākayā cakṣurviśodhayeyam | [Divyāv, 9 18]
apyevātikramedvelāṃ sāgaro makarālayaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 19.1]
na tu vaineyavatsānāṃ buddho velāmatikramet | [Divyāv, 9 19.2]
sarvajñasaṃtānanivāsinī hi kāruṇyadhenur mṛgayatyakhinnā | [Divyāv, 9 20.1]
vaineyavatsān bhavadurganaṣṭān vatsān praṇaṣṭāniva vatsalā gauḥ | [Divyāv, 9 20.2]
bhagavān saṃlakṣayati ayaṃ meṇḍhako gṛhapatiḥ saparivāro bhadraṃkare nagare prativasati | [Divyāv, 9 21]
tasya vaineyakālaṃ pakvamiva gaṇḍaṃ śastrābhinipātamavekṣate | [Divyāv, 9 22]
yannvahaṃ bhadraṃkareṣu janapadeṣu cārikām careyam | [Divyāv, 9 23]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate gaccha tvamānanda bhikṣūṇāmārocaya tathāgato bhikṣavo bhadraṃkareṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cariṣyati | [Divyāv, 9 24]
yo yuṣmākamutsahate tathāgatena sārdhaṃ bhadraṃkareṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cartum sa cīvarakāṇi pratigṛhṇātu iti | [Divyāv, 9 25]
evaṃ bhadantetyāyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya bhikṣūṇāmārocayati tathāgata āyuṣmanto bhadraṃkareṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cariṣyati | [Divyāv, 9 26]
yo yuṣmākamutsahate tathāgatena sārdhaṃ bhadraṃkareṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ caritum sa cīvarakāṇi pratigṛhṇātu iti | [Divyāv, 9 27]
evamāyuṣmanniti te bhikṣava āyuṣmata ānandasya pratiśrutya pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddhā gacchanti | [Divyāv, 9 28]
atha bhagavān dānto dāntaparivāraḥ śāntaḥ śāntaparivāro mukto muktaparivāra āśvasta āśvastaparivāro vinīto vinītaparivāro 'rhannarhatparivāro vītarāgo vītarāgaparivāraḥ prāsādikaḥ prāsādikaparivāraḥ vṛṣabha iva gogaṇaparivṛtaḥ siṃha iva daṃṣṭrigaṇaparivāraḥ haṃsarāja iva haṃsagaṇaparivṛtaḥ suparṇa iva pakṣigaṇaparivṛtaḥ vipra iva śiṣyagaṇaparivṛtaḥ suvaidya ivāturagaṇaparivṛtaḥ śūra iva yodhagaṇaparivṛtaḥ deśika ivādhvagaṇaparivṛtaḥ sārthavāha iva vaṇiggaṇaparivṛtaḥ śreṣṭhīva paurajanaparivṛtaḥ koṭṭarāja iva mantrigaṇaparivṛtaḥ cakravartīva putrasahasraparivṛtaḥ candra iva nakṣatragaṇaparivṛtaḥ sūrya iva raśmisahasraparivṛtaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra iva gandharvagaṇaparivṛtaḥ virūḍhaka iva kumbhāṇḍagaṇaparivṛto virūpākṣa iva nāgagaṇaparivṛtaḥ dhanada iva yakṣagaṇaparivṛtaḥ vemacitrir ivāsuragaṇaparivṛtaḥ śakra iva tridaśagaṇaparivṛtaḥ brahmeva brahmakāyikaparivṛtaḥ stimita iva jalanidhiḥ sajala iva jalanidhiḥ vimada iva gajapatiḥ sudāntairindriyair asaṃkṣobhiteryāpathapracāro dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇair aśītyānuvyañjanairvirājitagātro daśabhirbalaiścaturbhirvaiśāradyaistribhiḥ smṛtyupasthānairmahākaruṇayā ca | [Divyāv, 9 29]
evamanekaguṇagaṇasamanvāgato buddho bhagavāñ janapadacārikayā bhadraṃkaraṃ nagaraṃ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 30]
yadā bhagavatā śrāvastyāṃ mahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitam nirbhartsitā ānanditā devamanuṣyāḥ toṣitāni sajjanahṛdayāni tadā bhagnaprabhāvāstīrthyāḥ pratyantān saṃśritāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 31]
tataḥ kecidbhadraṃkaraṃ nagaraṃ gatvā avasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 32]
taiḥ śrutaṃ śramaṇagautama āgacchatīti | [Divyāv, 9 33]
śrutvā ca punarvyathitāste parasparaṃ kathayanti pūrvaṃ tāvadvayaṃ śramaṇena gautamena madhyadeśānnirvāsitāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 34]
sa yadīhāgamiṣyati niyatamito 'pi nirvāsayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 9 35]
tadupāyasaṃvidhānaṃ kartavyamiti | [Divyāv, 9 36]
te kulopakaraṇaśālā upasaṃkramya kathayanti dharmalābho dharmalābhaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 37]
te kathayanti kimidam avalokitā gamiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 38]
kasyārthāya dṛṣṭā asmābhiryuṣmākaṃ saṃpattiḥ yāvadvipattiṃ na paśyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 39]
āryakāḥ asmākaṃ vipattirbhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 9 40]
bhavantaḥ śramaṇo gautamaḥ kṣurāśaniṃ pātayannanekā aputrikā apatikāśca kurvannāgacchati | [Divyāv, 9 41]
āryāḥ yadyevam yasminneva kāle sthātavyaṃ tasminneva kāle 'smākaṃ parityāgas kriyate | [Divyāv, 9 42]
tiṣṭhata na gantavyam | [Divyāv, 9 43]
te kathayanti kiṃ vayaṃ na tiṣṭhāmaḥ na yūyamasmākaṃ śroṣyatha | [Divyāv, 9 44]
āryāḥ kathayata śroṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 45]
te kathayanti bhadraṃkarasāmantakena sarvajanakāyamudvāsya bhadraṃkaraṃ nagaraṃ pravāsayata | [Divyāv, 9 46]
śādvalāni kṛṣata | [Divyāv, 9 47]
sthaṇḍilāni pātayata | [Divyāv, 9 48]
puṣpaphalavṛkṣaṃ chedayata | [Divyāv, 9 49]
pānīyāni viṣeṇa dūṣayata | [Divyāv, 9 50]
te kathayanti āryāḥ tiṣṭhata sarvamanutiṣṭhāma iti | [Divyāv, 9 51]
te 'vasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 52]
tatastairbhadraṃkaranagarasāmantakena sarvo janakāya udvāsya bhadraṃkaraṃ nagaraṃ pravāsitaḥ śādvalāni kṛṣṭāni sthaṇḍilāni pātitāni puṣpaphalavṛkṣāśchinnāḥ pānīyāni viṣadūṣitāni | [Divyāv, 9 53]
tataḥ śakro devendraḥ saṃlakṣayati na mama pratirūpam yadahaṃ bhagavato 'satkāramadhyupekṣeyam | [Divyāv, 9 54]
yena nāma bhagavatā tribhiḥ kalpāsaṃkhyeyairanekair duṣkaraśatasahasraiḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ paripūryānuttarajñānamadhigatam sa nāma bhagavān sarvalokaprativiśiṣṭaḥ sarvavādavijayī śūnye janapade cārikāṃ cariṣyati | [Divyāv, 9 55]
yannvahaṃ bhagavataḥ saśrāvakasaṃghasya sukhasparśārthāya autsukyamāpadyeyamiti | [Divyāv, 9 56]
tena vātabalāhakānāṃ devaputrāṇāmājñā dattā gacchata bhadraṃkaranagarasāmantakena viṣapānīyāni śoṣayata iti | [Divyāv, 9 57]
varṣabalāhakānāṃ devaputrāṇāmājñā dattā aṣṭāṅgopetasya pānīyasyāpūryateti | [Divyāv, 9 58]
cāturmahārājikā devā uktāḥ yūyaṃ bhadraṃkarāṇāṃ janapadānāṃ vāsayateti | [Divyāv, 9 59]
tato vātabalāhakair devaputrairviṣadūṣitāni pānīyāni śoṣitāni varṣabalāhakaistānyeva kūpodapānavāpīsarastaḍāgānyaṣṭāṅgopetasya pānīyasya pūritāni | [Divyāv, 9 60]
cāturmahārājikairdevair bhadraṃkaranagarasāmantakaṃ sarvamāvāsitam | [Divyāv, 9 61]
janapadā ṛddhāḥ sphītāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 62]
tīrthyair nagarajanakāyasametair avacarakāḥ preṣitāḥ gatvā paśyata kīdṛśā janapadā iti | [Divyāv, 9 63]
te gatāḥ paśyantyatiśayena janapadān ṛddhān sphītān | [Divyāv, 9 64]
tata āgatya kathayanti bhavantaḥ na kadācidasmābhirevaṃrūpā janapadā ṛddhāḥ sphītā dṛṣṭapūrvā iti | [Divyāv, 9 65]
tīrthyāḥ kathayanti bhavantaḥ vo yastāvadacetanān bhāvānanvāvartayati sa yuṣmānnānvāvartayiṣyatīti kuta etat sarvathā avalokitā bhavantaḥ apaścimaṃ vo darśanam gacchāma iti | [Divyāv, 9 66]
te kathayanti āryāḥ tiṣṭhata kim yuṣmākaṃ śramaṇo gautamaḥ karoti so 'pi pravrajitaḥ yūyamapi pravrajitā bhikṣācarāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 67]
kimasau yuṣmākaṃ bhikṣāṃ cariṣyatīti tīrthyāḥ kathayanti samayena tiṣṭhāmo yadi yūyaṃ kriyākāraṃ kuruta na kenacicchramaṇaṃ gautamaṃ darśanāyopasaṃkramitavyam | [Divyāv, 9 68]
ya upasaṃkrāmati sa ṣaṣṭikārṣāpaṇo daṇḍya iti | [Divyāv, 9 69]
taiḥ pratijñātaṃ kriyākāraśca kṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 70]
tato janapadacārikāṃ caran bhadraṃkaraṃ nagaramanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 71]
bhadraṃkare nagare viharati dakṣiṇāyatane | [Divyāv, 9 72]
tena khalu samayena kapilavastuno brāhmaṇadārikā bhadraṃkare nagare pariṇītā | [Divyāv, 9 73]
tayā prākārasthayā bhagavānandhakāre dṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 74]
sā saṃlakṣayati ayaṃ bhagavāñ śākyakulanandanaḥ śākyakulādrājyamapahāya pravrajitaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 75]
sa idānīmandhakāre tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 9 76]
yadyatra sopānaṃ syāt ahaṃ pradīpamādāyāvatareyamiti | [Divyāv, 9 77]
tato bhagavatā tasyāścetasā cittamājñāya sopānaṃ nirmitam | [Divyāv, 9 78]
tato hṛṣṭatuṣṭapramuditā pradīpamādāya sopānenāvatīrya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntā | [Divyāv, 9 79]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ purastāt pradīpaṃ sthāpayitvā pādau śirasā vanditvā niṣaṇṇā dharmaśravaṇāya | [Divyāv, 9 80]
tato bhagavatā tasyā āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī caturāryasatyasamprativedhikī pūrvavadyāvaccharaṇagatāmabhiprasannāmiti | [Divyāv, 9 81]
atha bhagavāṃstāṃ dārikāmidamavocat ehi tvaṃ dārike yena meṇḍhako gṛhapatistenopasaṃkrama upasaṃkramyaivaṃ madvacanādārogyāpaya evaṃ ca vada gṛhapate tvāmuddiśyāhamihāgataḥ tvaṃ ca dvāraṃ baddhvā sthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 82]
yuktametadevamatitheḥ pratipattum yathā tvam pratipanna iti yadi kathayati gaṇena kriyākāraḥ kṛta iti vaktavyas tava putrasya pañcaśatiko nakulakaḥ kaṭyāṃ baddhastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 9 83]
sa yadi śataṃ vā sahasraṃ vā vyayīkaroti pūryata eva na parikṣīyate | [Divyāv, 9 84]
na śaknoṣi ṣaṣṭikārṣāpaṇaṃ dattvā āgantumiti evaṃ bhadanteti sā dārikā bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya samprasthitā | [Divyāv, 9 85]
yathāparijñātaiva kenacideva meṇḍhakasya gṛhapateḥ sakāśaṃ gatā | [Divyāv, 9 86]
gatvā ca kathayati gṛhapate bhagavāṃsta ārogyayati | [Divyāv, 9 87]
sa kathayati vande buddhaṃ bhagavantam | [Divyāv, 9 88]
gṛhapate bhagavānevamāha tvāmevāhamuddiśyāgataḥ tvaṃ ca dvāraṃ baddhvā avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 89]
yuktametadevamatitheḥ pratipattum yathā tvaṃ pratipanna iti sa kathayati dārike gaṇena kriyākāraḥ kṛtaḥ na kenacicchramaṇaṃ gautamaṃ darśanāya upasaṃkramitavyam | [Divyāv, 9 90]
ya upasaṃkrāmati sa gaṇena ṣaṣṭikārṣāpaṇo daṇḍya iti | [Divyāv, 9 91]
gṛhapate bhagavān kathayati tava putrasya pañcaśatiko nakulakaḥ kaṭyāṃ baddhastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 9 92]
sa yadi śataṃ vā sahasraṃ vā vyayīkaroti pūryata eva na parikṣīyate | [Divyāv, 9 93]
na śaknoṣi tvaṃ ṣaṣṭikārṣāpaṇaṃ dattvā āgantumiti sa saṃlakṣayati na kaścidetajjānīte | [Divyāv, 9 94]
nūnaṃ sarvajñaḥ sa bhagavān | [Divyāv, 9 95]
gacchāmīti | [Divyāv, 9 96]
sa ṣaṣṭikārṣāpaṇān dvāre sthāpayitvā brāhmaṇadārikopadiṣṭena sopānenāvatīrya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 97]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavataḥ purastānniṣaṇṇo dharmaśravaṇāya | [Divyāv, 9 98]
tato bhagavatā meṇḍhakasya gṛhapaterāśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī caturāryasatyasamprativedhikī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā meṇḍhakena gṛhapatinā yāvacchrotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 9 99]
sa dṛṣṭasatyaḥ kathayati bhagavan kimeṣo 'pi bhadraṃkaranagaranivāsī janakāya evaṃvidhānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ lābhīti bhagavānāha gṛhapate tvāmāgamya bhūyasā sarva eva janakāyo lābhīti | [Divyāv, 9 100]
tato meṇḍhako gṛhapatirbhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato 'ntikāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 101]
svagṛhaṃ gatvā nagaramadhye kārṣāpaṇānāṃ rāśiṃ vyavasthāpya gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 9 102]
yo draṣṭumicchati jinaṃ jitarāgadoṣaṃ nirbandhamapratisamaṃ karuṇāvadātam | [Divyāv, 9 103.1]
so 'niścareṇa hṛdayena suniścitena kṣipraṃ prayātu dhanamasya mayā pradeyam | [Divyāv, 9 103.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 9 103.3]
janakāyaḥ kathayati gṛhapate śreyaḥ śramaṇasya gautamasya darśanam sa kathayati śreyaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 104]
te kathayanti yadyevam gaṇenaivaṃ kriyākāraḥ kṛto gaṇa eva udghāṭayatu | [Divyāv, 9 105]
ko 'tra virodhas te kriyākāramudghāṭya nirgantumārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 106]
tataḥ parasparaṃ saṃghaṭṭanena na śaknuvanti nirgantumiti vajrapāṇinā yakṣeṇa vineyajanānukampayā vajraḥ kṣiptaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 107]
prākārasya khaṇḍaḥ patitaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 108]
anekāni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi nirgatāni kānicit kutūhalajātāni kānicit pūrvakaiḥ kuśalamūlaiḥ saṃcodyamānāni | [Divyāv, 9 109]
te gatvā bhagavataḥ pādābhivandanaṃ kṛtvā purato niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 9 110]
yāvadbhagavataḥ sāmantakena parṣat saṃnipatitā | [Divyāv, 9 111]
atha bhagavāṃstāṃ parṣadamabhyavagāhya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣadyānekasattvasaṃtānakuśalamūlasamāropikāṃ dharmadeśanāṃ kṛtavān yām śrutvā kaiścicchrotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam kaiściccharaṇagamanaśikṣāpadāni gṛhītāni | [Divyāv, 9 112]
bhagavato 'ciraṃ dharmaṃ deśayato bhojanakālo 'tikrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 113]
meṇḍhako gṛhapatiḥ kathayati bhagavan bhaktakṛtyaṃ kriyatāmiti | [Divyāv, 9 114]
bhagavānāha gṛhapate bhojanakālo 'tikrānta iti | [Divyāv, 9 115]
sa kathayati bhagavan kimakāle kalpate bhagavānāha ghṛtaguḍaśarkarāpānakāni ceti | [Divyāv, 9 116]
tato meṇḍhakena gṛhapatinā śilpina āhūya uktāḥ bhagavato 'kālakhādyakāni śīghraṃ sajjīkuruteti | [Divyāv, 9 117]
tairakālakāni sajjīkṛtāni | [Divyāv, 9 118]
tato meṇḍhakena gṛhapatinā buddhapramukho bhikṣusaṃgho 'kālakhādyakairakālapānakaiśca saṃtarpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 119]
tato bhagavān meṇḍhakaṃ gṛhapatiṃ saparivāraṃ satyeṣu pratiṣṭhāpitaṃ karvaṭanivāsinaṃ janakāyam yathābhavyatayā vinīya prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 9 120]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 9 121]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 9 122]
{Divyāv, 10}
bhikṣavaḥ saṃśayajātāḥ sarvasaṃśayacchettāraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ papracchuḥ kiṃ bhadanta meṇḍhakena meṇḍhakapatnyā meṇḍhakaputreṇa meṇḍhakasnuṣayā meṇḍhakadāsena meṇḍhakadāsyā karma kṛtam yena ṣaḍabhijñātā mahāpuṇyāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ bhagavato 'ntike satyāni dṛṣṭāni bhagavāṃścaibhirārāgito na virāgita iti bhagavānāha ebhireva bhikṣavaḥ karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni labdhasambhārāṇi pariṇatapratyayāni oghavatpratyupasthitānyavaśyambhāvīni | [Divyāv, 10 1.1]
ebhiḥ karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni ko 'nyaḥ pratyanubhaviṣyati na bhikṣavaḥ karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni bāhye pṛthivīdhātau vipacyante nābdhātau na tejodhātau na vāyudhātau api tūpātteṣveva skandhadhātvāyataneṣu karmāṇi kṛtāni vipacyante śubhānyaśubhāni ca | [Divyāv, 10 2.1]
na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatairapi | [Divyāv, 10 3.1]
sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti khalu dehinām | [Divyāv, 10 3.2]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani vārāṇasyāṃ nagaryāṃ brahmadatto nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati ṛddhaṃ ca sphītaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca praśāntakalikalahaḍimbaḍamarataskararogāpagataṃ śālīkṣugomahiṣīsampannamakhilamakaṇṭakam | [Divyāv, 10 4.1]
ekaputramiva rājyaṃ pālayati | [Divyāv, 10 5.1]
tena khalu samayena vārāṇasyāṃ naimittikairdvādaśavarṣikā anāvṛṣṭirvyākṛtā | [Divyāv, 10 6.1]
trividhaṃ durbhikṣaṃ bhaviṣyati cañcu śvetāsthi śalākāvṛtti ca | [Divyāv, 10 7.1]
tatra cañcu ucyate samudgake tasmin manuṣyā bījāni prakṣipya anāgate sattvāpekṣayā sthāpayanti mṛtānām anena te bījakāyaṃ kariṣyantīti | [Divyāv, 10 8.1]
idaṃ samudgakaṃ baddhvā cañcu ucyate | [Divyāv, 10 9.1]
śvetāsthi nāma durbhikṣam tasmin kāle manuṣyā asthīnyupasaṃhṛtya tāvat kvāthayanti yāvat tānyasthīni śvetāni saṃvṛttānīti | [Divyāv, 10 10.1]
tatastatkvāthaṃ pibanti | [Divyāv, 10 11.1]
idaṃ śvetāsthi durbhikṣamityucyate | [Divyāv, 10 12]
śalākāvṛttir nāma tasmin kāle manuṣyāḥ khalu bilebhyo dhānyaguḍakāni śalākayā ākṛṣya bahūdakasthālyāṃ kvāthayitvā pibanti | [Divyāv, 10 13]
iyaṃ śalākāsambaddhatvācchalākāvṛttirityucyate | [Divyāv, 10 14.1]
tato rājñā brahmadattena vārāṇasyāṃ ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kāritam śṛṇvantu bhavanto vārāṇasīnivāsinaḥ paurāḥ | [Divyāv, 10 15.1]
naimittikairdvādaśavarṣikā anāvṛṣṭirvyākṛtā śalākāvṛtti durbhikṣaṃ cañcu śvetāsthi ca | [Divyāv, 10 16.1]
yeṣāṃ vo dvādaśavarṣikaṃ bhaktamasti taiḥ sthātavyam | [Divyāv, 10 17.1]
yeṣāṃ nāsti te yatheṣṭaṃ gacchantu | [Divyāv, 10 18.1]
vigatadurbhikṣabhayāḥ subhikṣe punarapyupāgamiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 10 19.1]
tasmiṃśca samaye vārāṇasyāmanyatamo gṛhapatirāḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vistīrṇaparivāraḥ | [Divyāv, 10 20.1]
tena koṣṭhāgārika āhūya uktaḥ bhoḥ puruṣa bhaviṣyati me saparivārāṇāṃ dvādaśa varṣāṇi bhaktamiti sa kathayati ārya bhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 10 21.1]
sa tatraivāvasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 22.1]
samanantarānubaddhaṃ caitat durbhikṣam | [Divyāv, 10 23.1]
tasya kośakoṣṭhāgārāḥ parikṣīṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 10 24.1]
sarvaśca parijanaḥ kālagataḥ | [Divyāv, 10 25.1]
ātmanā ṣaṣṭho vyavasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 26.1]
tatastena gṛhapatinā kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇi śodhayitvā dhānyaprastha upasaṃhṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 27.1]
so 'sya patnyā sthālyāṃ prakṣipya sādhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 28.1]
asati buddhānāmutpāde pratyekabuddhā loka utpadyante hīnadīnānukampakāḥ prāntaśayanabhaktā ekadakṣiṇīyā lokasya | [Divyāv, 10 29.1]
yāvadanyatamaḥ pratyekabuddho janapadacārikāṃ caran vārāṇasīmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 30.1]
sa pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya vārāṇasīṃ piṇḍāya praviṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 31.1]
sa ca gṛhapatirātmanā ṣaṣṭho 'vasthito bhoktum | [Divyāv, 10 32.1]
sa ca pratyekabuddho 'nupūrveṇa piṇḍapātamaṭaṃs tasya gṛhapater niveśanamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 33.1]
sa tena gṛhapatinā dṛṣṭaścittaprāsādikaḥ kāyaprāsādikaśca | [Divyāv, 10 34.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ saṃlakṣayati etadapyahaṃ parityajya niyataṃ prāṇairviyokṣye yannvahaṃ svapratyaṃśamasmai pravrajitāya dadyāmiti | [Divyāv, 10 35.1]
tena bhāryā abhihitā bhadre yo mama pratyaṃśastamahamasmai pravrajitāyānuprayacchāmīti | [Divyāv, 10 36.1]
sā saṃlakṣayati mama svāmī na paribhuṅkte kathamahaṃ paribhokṣya iti | [Divyāv, 10 37.1]
sā kathayati āryaputra ahamapi pratyaṃśamasmai prayacchāmi | [Divyāv, 10 38.1]
evaṃ putreṇa snuṣayā dāsena dāsyā ca vicārya svasvapratyaṃśāḥ parityaktāḥ | [Divyāv, 10 39.1]
tatastaiḥ sarvaiḥ sambhūya pratyekabuddhaḥ piṇḍakena pratipāditaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 40.1]
kāyikī teṣāṃ mahātmanāṃ dharmadeśanā na vācikī | [Divyāv, 10 41.1]
sa vitatapakṣa iva haṃsarāja upari vihāyasamudgamya jvalanatapanavarṣaṇavidyotanaprātihāryāṇi kartumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 42.1]
āśu pṛthagjanāvarjanakarī ṛddhiḥ | [Divyāv, 10 43.1]
te mūlanikṛttā iva drumāḥ pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 10 44.1]
gṛhapatiḥ praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ yanmayā evaṃvidhe sadbhūtadakṣiṇīye kāraḥ kṛtaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena yadi riktakāni kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇi sahadarśanānme pūrṇāni syur evaṃvidhānāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ lābhī syām prativiśiṣṭataraṃ cātaḥ śāstāramārāgayeyaṃ mā virāgayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 10 45.1]
patnī praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhā yanmayā evaṃvidhe sadbhūtadakṣiṇīye kāraḥ kṛtaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena yadyekasyārthāya sthālīṃ paceyam sā śatenāpi paribhujyeta sahasreṇāpi na parikṣayaṃ gacchet yāvanmayā prayogo 'pratipraśrabdhaḥ ityevaṃvidhānāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ lābhinī syām prativiśiṣṭataraṃ cātaḥ śāstāramārāgayeyaṃ mā virāgayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 10 46.1]
putraḥ praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdho yanmayā evaṃvidhe sadbhūtadakṣiṇīye kāraḥ kṛtaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena pañcaśatiko nakulakaḥ kaṭyāmuparibaddhastiṣṭhet yadi ca śataṃ vā sahasraṃ vā tato vyayaṃ kuryāt pūrṇa eva tiṣṭhet mā parikṣayaṃ gacchet evaṃvidhānāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ lābhī syām prativiśiṣṭataraṃ cātaḥ śāstāramārāgayeyaṃ mā virāgayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 10 47.1]
snuṣā praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhā yanmayā evaṃvidhe sadbhūtadakṣiṇīye kāraḥ kṛtaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena yadyekasya gandham yojayeyam śataṃ vā gandhaṃ ghrāsyati taṃ na ca parikṣayaṃ gaccheyuryāvanmayā apratipraśrabdham evaṃvidhānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ lābhinī syām prativiśiṣṭataraṃ cātaḥ śāstāramārāgayeyaṃ mā virāgayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 10 48.1]
dāsaḥ praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ yanmayā evaṃvidhe sadbhūtadakṣiṇīye kāraḥ kṛtaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena yadyekahalasīraṃ kṛṣeyam sapta sīrāḥ kṛṣṭāḥ syuḥ evaṃvidhānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ ca lābhī syāṃ prativiśiṣṭataraṃ cātaḥ śāstāramārāgayeyaṃ mā virāgayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 10 49.1]
dāsī praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdhā evaṃvidhe sadbhūtadakṣiṇīye kāraḥ kṛtaḥ anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena yadyekāṃ mātrāmārabheyam sapta mātrāḥ saṃpadyeran evaṃvidhānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ ca lābhinī syāṃ prativiśiṣṭataraṃ cātaḥ śāstāramārāgayeyaṃ mā virāgayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 10 50.1]
taiścaivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ kṛtam | [Divyāv, 10 51.1]
sa ca mahātmā pratyekabuddhasteṣāmanukampayā ṛddhyā upari vihāyasā rājakulasyopariṣṭāt samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 52.1]
tena khalu samayena rājā brahmadatta upariprāsādatalagatastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 10 53.1]
tasya ṛddhyā gacchato rājño brahmadattasyopari chāyā nipatitā | [Divyāv, 10 54.1]
sa ūrdhvamukho nirīkṣitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 55.1]
paśyati taṃ pratyekabuddham | [Divyāv, 10 56.1]
tasyaitadabhavat kasyāpyanena mahātmanā ṛddhimahālāṅgalairdāridryamūlānyutpāṭitāni | [Divyāv, 10 57.1]
balavatī āśā | [Divyāv, 10 58.1]
tato 'sau gṛhapatiḥ kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇi pratyavekṣitumārabdho yāvatpūrṇāni paśyati | [Divyāv, 10 59.1]
sa patnīmāmantrayate mama tāvat praṇidhānaṃ pūrṇam yuṣmākamapīdānīṃ paśyāma iti | [Divyāv, 10 60.1]
tato dāsyā dhānyānāmekāṃ mātrāmārabdhvā parikarmayitum sapta mātrāḥ sampannāḥ | [Divyāv, 10 61.1]
patnyā ekasyārthāya sthālī sādhitā sarvais taiḥ paribhuktaṃ tathaivāvasthitā prātiveśyairanekaiśca prāṇiśatasahasraiḥ paribhuktam tathaivāvasthitā | [Divyāv, 10 62.1]
tathaiva putrasya snuṣāyā dāsasya praṇidhiḥ siddhā | [Divyāv, 10 63.1]
tato gṛhapatinā ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kāritaṃ vārāṇasyām yo bhavanto 'nnenārthī sa āgacchatu iti | [Divyāv, 10 64.1]
vārāṇasyāmuccaśabdo mahāśabdo jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 65.1]
rājñā śrutam | [Divyāv, 10 66.1]
kathayati kimeṣa bhavanta uccaśabdo mahāśabda iti amātyaiḥ samākhyātam deva amukena gṛhapatinā kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇi udghāṭitānīti | [Divyāv, 10 67.1]
rājā tamāhūya kathayati yadā eva lokaḥ kālagataḥ tadā tvayā kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇyudghāṭitānīti | [Divyāv, 10 68.1]
deva kasya kośakoṣṭhāgārāṇyudghāṭitāni api tu adyaiva me bījamuptamadyaiva phaladāyakamiti | [Divyāv, 10 69.1]
rājā pṛcchati yathā katham sa etat prakaraṇaṃ vistareṇārocayati | [Divyāv, 10 70.1]
rājā kathayati gṛhapate tvayā asau mahātmā piṇḍakena pratipāditaḥ deva mayaiva pratipāditaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 71.1]
so 'bhiprasanno gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 10 72.1]
aho guṇamayaṃ kṣetraṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitam | [Divyāv, 10 73.1]
yatroptaṃ bījamadyaiva adyaiva phaladāyakam | [Divyāv, 10 73.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 10 73.3]
kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau gṛhapatirgṛhapatipatnī gṛhapatiputro gṛhapatisnuṣā gṛhapatidāso gṛhapatidāsī ayameva meṇḍhako gṛhapatir meṇḍhakapatnī meṇḍhakaputro meṇḍhakasnuṣā meṇḍhakadāso meṇḍhakadāsī ca | [Divyāv, 10 74.1]
yadebhiḥ pratyekabuddhe kārān kṛtvā praṇidhānaṃ kṛtam tasya karmaṇo vipākena ṣaḍ mahāpuṇyā jātāḥ mamāntike dṛṣṭasatyāni | [Divyāv, 10 75.1]
ahaṃ caibhiḥ pratyekabuddhakoṭiśatasahasrebhyaḥ prativiśiṣṭaḥ śāstā ārāgito na virāgitaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 76.1]
iti hi bhikṣava ekāntakṛṣṇānāṃ karmaṇāmekāntakṛṣṇo vipākaḥ ekāntaśuklānāṃ karmaṇāmekāntaśuklaḥ vyatimiśrāṇāṃ vyatimiśraḥ | [Divyāv, 10 77.1]
tasmāttarhi evaṃ śikṣitavyam yadekāntakṛṣṇāni karmāṇyapāsya vyatimiśrāṇi ca ekāntaśukleṣveva karmasvābhogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [Divyāv, 10 78.1]
ityevaṃ vo bhikṣavaḥ śikṣitavyam | [Divyāv, 10 79.1]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 10 80.1]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 10 81.1]
{Divyāv, 11}
evaṃ mayā śrutam | [Divyāv, 11 1.1]
ekasmin samaye bhagavān satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrairdhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhairdevair nāgairasurairyakṣairgaruḍaiḥ kinnarairmahoragairiti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavāñ jñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃgho vaiśālyāṃ viharati sma markaṭahradatīre kūṭāgāraśālāyām | [Divyāv, 11 2.1]
tena khalu samayena vaiśālikā licchavaya idamevaṃrūpaṃ kriyākāramakārṣuḥ pañcadaśyāṃ bhavantaḥ pakṣasya aṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ ca prāṇino hantavyā yatkāraṇameyurmanuṣyā māṃsamanveṣanta iti | [Divyāv, 11 3.1]
tena khalu samayena anyatamo goghātako mahāntaṃ vṛṣabhamādāya nagarānniṣkramati praghātayitum | [Divyāv, 11 4.1]
tamenaṃ mahājanakāyaḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddho māṃsārthī kathayati śīghramenaṃ vṛṣaṃ ghātaya vayaṃ māṃsenārthina iti | [Divyāv, 11 5.1]
sa kathayati evaṃ kariṣyāmi kiṃtu muhūrtamudīkṣadhvamiti | [Divyāv, 11 6.1]
tato vṛṣa īdṛśamanāryaṃ vaco duruktaṃ śrutvā bhītastrastaḥ saṃvigna āhṛṣṭaromakūpa itaścāmutaśca saṃbhrānto nirīkṣate cintayati ca ko māṃ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhaprāptamatrāṇamaśaraṇamiṣṭena jīvitenācchādayediti | [Divyāv, 11 7.1]
sa caivaṃ vihvalavadanastrāṇānveṣī tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 11 8.1]
bhagavāṃśca pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto vaiśālīṃ piṇḍāya prāviśat | [Divyāv, 11 9.1]
athāsau dadarśa buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam aśītyānuvyañjanairvirājitagātraṃ vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtaṃ sūryasahasrātirekaprabhaṃ jaṅgamamiva ratnaparvataṃ samantato bhadrakam | [Divyāv, 11 10.1]
sahadarśanaiścāsya bhagavato 'ntike cittamabhiprasannam | [Divyāv, 11 11.1]
prasannacittaśca saṃlakṣayati prāsādiko 'yaṃ sattvaviśeṣaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 12.1]
śakṣyatyeṣo mama prāṇaparitrāṇaṃ kartum | [Divyāv, 11 13.1]
yannvahamenamupasaṃkrameyamiti | [Divyāv, 11 14.1]
atha sa vṛṣo bhagavatyavekṣāvān pratibaddhacitta eṣo me śaraṇamiti sahasaiva tāni dṛḍhāni varatrakāṇi bandhanāni chittvā pradhāvan yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 15.1]
upasaṃkramyobhābhyāṃ jānubhyāṃ bhagavataḥ pādayor nipatya pādau jihvayā nileḍhumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 16.1]
sa cāsya raudrakarmā goghātakaḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddha eva śastravyagrahastaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 17.1]
tato bhagavāṃstaṃ raudrakarmāṇaṃ goghātakamidamavocat kuruṣva tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa anena govṛṣabheṇa sārdhaṃ sātmyam | [Divyāv, 11 18.1]
jīvitenāchādayeti | [Divyāv, 11 19.1]
sa kathayati nāhaṃ bhadanta prabhavāmyenaṃ jīvitenāchādayitum | [Divyāv, 11 20.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ mayā eṣa bahunā mūlyena krītaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 21.1]
putradāraṃ ca me bahu poṣitavyamiti | [Divyāv, 11 22.1]
bhagavānāha yadi mūlyaṃ dīyate pratimuñcasīti | [Divyāv, 11 23.1]
sa kathayati pratimokṣyāmi bhagavanniti | [Divyāv, 11 24.1]
atha bhagavāṃllaukikacittamutpādayati aho bata śakro devendrastrīṇi kārṣāpaṇasahasrāṇyādāyāgacchediti | [Divyāv, 11 25.1]
sahacittotpādādbhagavataḥ śakro devendraḥ kārṣāpaṇasahasratrayamādāya bhagavataḥ purastādasthāt | [Divyāv, 11 26.1]
atha bhagavāñśakraṃ devendramidamavocat anuprayaccha kauśika asya goghātakasya triguṇaṃ mūlyam | [Divyāv, 11 27.1]
adācchakro devendrastasya goghātakasya kārṣāpaṇatrayasahasraṃ vṛṣamūlyam | [Divyāv, 11 28.1]
atha goghātakaḥ kārṣāpaṇasahasratrayaṃ vṛṣamūlyaṃ gṛhītvā hṛṣṭastuṣṭaḥ pramudito bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā taṃ govṛṣaṃ bandhanānmuktvā prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 29.1]
śakro devendro bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā tatraivāntarhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 30.1]
atha govṛṣo gatapratyāgataprāṇo bhūyasyā mātrayā bhagavatyabhiprasanno bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddho bhagavato mukhaṃ vyavalokayamāno 'sthāt | [Divyāv, 11 31.1]
atha bhagavān smitamakārṣīt | [Divyāv, 11 32.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātāḥ puṣparāgapadmarāgavajravaiḍūryamusāragalvārkalohitakādakṣiṇāvartaśaṅkhaśilāpravālajātarūparajatavarṇā arciṣo mukhānniścārya kāścidadhastādgacchanti kāścidupariṣṭādgacchanti | [Divyāv, 11 33.1]
yā adhastādgacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanamavīcimarbudaṃ nirarbudamaṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhuvamutpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaparyantān narakān gatvā ye uṣṇanarakāsteṣu śītībhūtvā nipatanti ye śītanarakāsteṣūṣṇībhūtvā nipatanti | [Divyāv, 11 34.1]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabhyante | [Divyāv, 11 35.1]
teṣāmevaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaścyutāḥ āhosvidanyatropapannā iti | [Divyāv, 11 36.1]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [Divyāv, 11 37.1]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvā evaṃ bhavati na hyeva vayaṃ bhavanta itaścyutāḥ nāpyanyatropapannā iti | [Divyāv, 11 38.1]
api tvayamapūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvenāsmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [Divyāv, 11 39.1]
te nirmite cittamabhiprasādya tannarakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisaṃdhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 11 40.1]
yā upariṣṭādgacchanti tāścāturmahārājakāyikān devāṃstrāyastriṃśān yāmāṃstuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhānābhāsvarān parīttaśubhānapramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnānanabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalānabṛhānatapān sudṛśān sudarśanānakaniṣṭhaparyantān devān gatvā anityaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyamanātmetyudghoṣayanti | [Divyāv, 11 41.1]
gāthādvayaṃ bhāṣante | [Divyāv, 11 42.1]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [Divyāv, 11 43.1]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāramiva kuñjaraḥ | [Divyāv, 11 43.2]
yo hyasmin dharmavinaye apramattaścariṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 44.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 44.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 11 45.1]
atha tā arciṣastrisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātumanvāhiṇḍya bhagavantameva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [Divyāv, 11 46.1]
tadyadi bhagavānatītaṃ karma vyākartukāmo bhavati bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 47.1]
anāgataṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati purastādantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 48.1]
narakopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādatale 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 49.1]
tiryagupapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pārṣṇyāmantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 50.1]
pretopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati pādāṅguṣṭhe 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 51.1]
manuṣyopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati jānunorantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 52.1]
balacakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati vāme karatale 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 53.1]
cakravartirājyaṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati dakṣiṇe karatale 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 54.1]
devopapattiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati nābhyāmantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 55.1]
śrāvakabodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati āsye 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 56.1]
pratyekāṃ bodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati ūrṇāyāmantardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 57.1]
anuttarāṃ samyaksambodhiṃ vyākartukāmo bhavati uṣṇīṣe 'ntardhīyante | [Divyāv, 11 58.1]
atha tā arciṣo bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavata ūrṇāyāmantarhitāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 59.1]
athāyuṣmānānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [Divyāv, 11 60.1]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarānniṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 61.1]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantāddivākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [Divyāv, 11 61.2]
gāthāṃ ca bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 11 62.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagatyuttamahetubhūtāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 63.1]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitamupadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 63.2]
tatkālaṃ svayamadhigamya dhīrabuddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇajinendrakāṅkṣitānām | [Divyāv, 11 64.1]
dhīrābhirmunivṛṣa vāgbhiruttamābhirutpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [Divyāv, 11 64.2]
nākasmāllavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitamupadarśayanti nāthāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 65.1]
yasyārthe smitamupadarśayanti dhīrāstaṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 65.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 11 65.3]
bhagavānāha evametadānanda evametat | [Divyāv, 11 66.1]
nāhetvapratyayamānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksambuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [Divyāv, 11 67.1]
dṛṣṭaste ānanda ayaṃ govṛṣaḥ dṛṣṭo bhadanta | [Divyāv, 11 68.1]
eṣa ānanda govṛṣastathāgatasyāntike prasannacittaḥ saptame divase kālaṃ kṛtvā cāturmahārājikeṣu deveṣūpapatsyate | [Divyāv, 11 69.1]
vaiśravaṇasya mahārājasya putro bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 70.1]
tataścyutvā trāyastriṃśeṣu deveṣūpapatsyate | [Divyāv, 11 71.1]
śakrasya devendrasya putro bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 72.1]
tataścyutvā yāmeṣu deveṣūpapatsyate | [Divyāv, 11 73.1]
yāmasya devasya putro bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 74.1]
tataścyutvā tuṣiteṣu deveṣūpapatsyate | [Divyāv, 11 75.1]
sa tuṣitasya devasya putro bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 76.1]
tataścyutvā nirmāṇaratiṣu deveṣūpapatsyate | [Divyāv, 11 77.1]
sunirmitasya devaputrasya putro bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 78.1]
tataścyutvā parinirmitavaśavartiṣu deveṣūpapatsyate | [Divyāv, 11 79.1]
vaśavartino devaputrasya putro bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 80.1]
tadanayā saṃtatyā navanavatikalpasahasrāṇi vinipātaṃ na gamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 81.1]
tataḥ kāmāvacareṣu deveṣu divyaṃ sukhamanubhūya paścime bhave paścime nikete samucchraye paścime ātmabhāvapratilambhe manuṣyatvaṃ pratilabhya rājā bhaviṣyati aśokavarṇo nāma cakravartī caturarṇavāntavijetā dhārmiko dharmarājaḥ saptaratnasamanvāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 11 82.1]
tasyemānyevaṃrūpāṇi sapta ratnāni bhaviṣyanti | [Divyāv, 11 83.1]
tadyathā cakraratnaṃ hastiratnamaśvaratnaṃ maṇiratnaṃ strīratnaṃ gṛhapatiratnaṃ pariṇāyakaratnameva saptamam | [Divyāv, 11 84.1]
pūrṇaṃ cāsya bhaviṣyati sahasraṃ putrāṇāṃ śūrāṇāṃ vīrāṇāṃ varāṅgarūpiṇāṃ parasainyapramardakānām | [Divyāv, 11 85.1]
imāmeva samudraparyantāṃ mahāpṛthivīmakhilām akaṇṭakām anutpīḍām adaṇḍenāśastreṇa dharmyeṇa samayenābhinirjitya adhyāvatsyati | [Divyāv, 11 86.1]
so 'pareṇa samayena dānāni dattvā cakravartirājyamapahāya keśaśmaśrūṇyavatārya kāṣāyāṇi vastrāṇi samyageva śraddhayā agārādanagārikāṃ pravrajya pratyekāṃ bodhiṃ sākṣātkariṣyati aśokavarṇo nāma pratyekabuddho bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 87.1]
athāyuṣmānānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha kiṃ bhadanta anena govṛṣeṇa karma kṛtam yena tiryagyonāvupapannaḥ kiṃ karma kṛtam yena divyamānuṣasukhamanubhūya pratyekāṃ bodhimadhigamiṣyati bhagavānāha anenaiva ānanda govṛṣeṇa karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni labdhasambhārāṇi pariṇatapratyayāni oghavatpratyupasthitānyavaśyambhāvīni | [Divyāv, 11 88.1]
govṛṣeṇa karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni ko 'nyaḥ pratyanubhaviṣyati na hyānanda karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni bāhye pṛthivīdhātau vipacyante nābdhātau na tejodhātau na vāyudhātau api tūpātteṣveva skandhadhātvāyataneṣu karmāṇi kṛtāni vipacyante śubhāśubhāni ca | [Divyāv, 11 89.1]
na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi api kalpaśatairapi | [Divyāv, 11 90.1]
sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti khalu dehinām | [Divyāv, 11 90.2]
bhūtapūrvamānanda atīte 'dhvani ekanavate kalpe vipaśyī nāma samyaksambuddho loka udapādi vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devamanuṣyāṇāṃ buddho bhagavān | [Divyāv, 11 91.1]
sa bandhumatīṃ rājadhānīmupaniśritya viharati anyatamasmin vanaṣaṇḍe | [Divyāv, 11 92.1]
tasya nātidūre ṣaṣṭibhikṣavaḥ prativasantyāraṇyakāḥ piṇḍapātikāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 93.1]
sarve ca vītarāgā vigatadveṣā vigatamohā yāvat pañcamātrāṇi dhūrtakaśatāni tena tenāhiṇḍyamānāni taṃ pradeśamanuprāptāni | [Divyāv, 11 94.1]
teṣāmetadabhavat ete hi pravrajitā mahātmāna īdṛśeṣu sthāneṣvabhiramante | [Divyāv, 11 95.1]
yadyeṣāṃ jīvitopacchedaṃ na kariṣyāmaḥ na bhūya etasmin pradeśe svasthairvihartavyaṃ bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 96.1]
yadyapyete mahātmānaḥ sarvasattvahitodayapravṛttā na pareṣāmārocayiṣyanti tathāpyeṣāṃ pradhānapuruṣā upasaṃkramiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 11 97.1]
te 'smākaṃ rājñaḥ samarpayiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 11 98.1]
tatrāsmābhiścārakāvaruddhairmartavyaṃ bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 99.1]
kathamatra pratipattavyamiti ekastatraiva nirghṛṇahṛdayastyaktaparalokaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 100.1]
sa kathayati aghātayitvā etān kutaḥ kṣema iti taiste jīvitādvyaparopitāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 101.1]
te caitatkarma kṛtvā pāpakamakuśalam ekanavatikalpān apāyeṣūpapannāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 102.1]
yadbhūyasā tu narakeṣu tiryagyonau upapannāśca santo nityaṃ śastreṇa praghātitāḥ | [Divyāv, 11 103.1]
tatra yo 'sau caurasteṣāṃ samādāpakaḥ sa evāyaṃ govṛṣaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 104.1]
tasya karmaṇo vipākena iyantaṃ kālaṃ na kadācit sugatau upapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 105.1]
yatpunaridānīṃ mamāntike cittaṃ prasāditam tasya karmaṇo vipākena divyaṃ mānuṣaṃ sukhamanubhūya pratyekāṃ bodhimadhigamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 11 106.1]
evaṃ hi ānanda tathāgatānāṃ cittaprasādo 'pyacintyavipākaḥ kiṃ punaḥ praṇidhānam | [Divyāv, 11 107.1]
tasmāttarhi ānanda evaṃ śikṣitavyam yatstokastokaṃ muhūrtamuhūrtamantato 'cchaṭāsaṃghātamātramapi tathāgatamākārataḥ samanusmariṣyāmītyevaṃ te ānanda śikṣitavyam | [Divyāv, 11 108.1]
athāyuṣmān ānando bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyānandyānumodya bhikṣūṇāṃ purastādgāthā bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 11 109.1]
aho nāthasya kāruṇyaṃ sarvajñasya hitaiṣiṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 110.1]
sukṛtenaiva vātsalyam yasyedṛśamahādbhutam | [Divyāv, 11 110.2]
āpanno hi paraṃ kṛcchraṃ govṛṣo yena mocitaḥ | [Divyāv, 11 111.1]
vyākṛtaśca bhave divye pratyekaśca jino hyasau | [Divyāv, 11 111.2]
iti | [Divyāv, 11 111.3]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 11 112.1]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 11 113.1]
{Divyāv, 12}
sa bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati veṇuvane kalandakanivāpe satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājabhī rājamātrairdhanibhiḥ pauraiḥ śreṣṭhibhiḥ sārthavāhairdevair nāgairyakṣairasurairgaruḍaiḥ kinnarairmahoragairiti devanāgayakṣāsuragaruḍakinnaramahoragābhyarcito buddho bhagavāñjñāto mahāpuṇyo lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ saśrāvakasaṃgho divyānāṃ mānuṣyāṇāṃ ca bhagavānanupalipto viharati padmapatramivāmbhasā | [Divyāv, 12 1.1]
tena khalu samayena rājagṛhe nagare ṣaṭ pūrṇādyāḥ śāstāro 'sarvajñāḥ sarvajñamāninaḥ prativasanti sma | [Divyāv, 12 2.1]
tadyathā pūrṇaḥ kāśyapaḥ maskarī gośālīputraḥ saṃjayī vairaṭṭīputraḥ ajitaḥ keśakambalaḥ kakudaḥ kātyāyanaḥ nirgrantho jñātiputraḥ | [Divyāv, 12 3.1]
atha ṣaṇṇāṃ pūrṇādīnāṃ tīrthyānāṃ kutūhalaśālāyāṃ saṃniṣaṇṇānāṃ saṃnipatitānām ayam evaṃrūpo 'bhūd antarākathāsamudāhāraḥ yatkhalu bhavanto jānīran yadā śramaṇo gautamo loke 'nutpannas tadā vayaṃ satkṛtāścābhūvan gurukṛtāśca mānitāśca pūjitāśca rājñāṃ rājamātrāṇāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ gṛhapatīnāṃ naigamānāṃ jānapadānāṃ śreṣṭhināṃ sārthavāhānām lābhinaścābhūvaṃścīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇām | [Divyāv, 12 4.1]
yadā tu śramaṇo gautamo loke utpannaḥ tadā śramaṇo gautamaḥ satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito rājñāṃ rājamātrāṇāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ gṛhapatīnāṃ janapadānāṃ dhanināṃ śreṣṭhināṃ sārthavāhānām lābhī ca śramaṇo gautamaḥ saśrāvakasaṃghaścīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇām | [Divyāv, 12 5.1]
asmākaṃ ca lābhasatkāraḥ sarveṇa sarvaṃ samucchinnaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 6.1]
vayaṃ sma ṛddhimanto jñānavādinaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 7.1]
śramaṇo 'pi gautama ṛddhimāñjñānavādītyātmānaṃ pratijānīte | [Divyāv, 12 8.1]
arhati jñānavādī jñānavādinā sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 9.1]
yadyekaṃ śramaṇo gautamo 'nuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati vayaṃ dve | [Divyāv, 12 10.1]
dve śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ catvāri | [Divyāv, 12 11.1]
catvāri śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayamaṣṭau | [Divyāv, 12 12.1]
aṣṭau śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ ṣoḍaśa | [Divyāv, 12 13.1]
ṣoḍaśa śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ dvātriṃśaditi yāvacchramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati vayaṃ taddviguṇaṃ tattriguṇaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 14.1]
upārdhaṃ mārgaṃ śramaṇo gautama āgacchatu vayamapyupārdhaṃ mārgaṃ gamiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 15.1]
tatrāsmākaṃ bhavatu śramaṇena gautamena sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 16.1]
atha mārasya pāpīyasa etadabhavat asakṛdasakṛnmayā śramaṇasya gautamasya parākrāntam na ca kadācidavatāro labdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 17.1]
yannvahaṃ tīrthyānāṃ prahareyam | [Divyāv, 12 18.1]
iti viditvā pūraṇavadātmānamabhinirmāya upari vihāyasamabhyudgamya jvalanatapanavarṣaṇavidyotanaprātihāryāṇi kṛtvā maskariṇaṃ gośālīputramāmantrayate yatkhalu maskariñjānīyā aham ṛddhimāñjñānavādī śramaṇo gautama ṛddhimāñjñānavādītyātmānaṃ parijānīte | [Divyāv, 12 19.1]
arhati jñānavādī jñānavādinā sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 20.1]
yadyekaṃ śramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati ahaṃ dve | [Divyāv, 12 21.1]
dve śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahaṃ catvāri | [Divyāv, 12 22.1]
catvāri śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahamaṣṭau | [Divyāv, 12 23.1]
aṣṭau śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahaṃ ṣoḍaśa | [Divyāv, 12 24.1]
ṣoḍaśa śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahaṃ dvātriṃśaditi yāvacchramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati vayaṃ taddviguṇamuttaraṃ manuṣyadharmam ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 25.1]
upārdhaṃ mārgaṃ śramaṇo gautama āgacchatu ahamapyupārdhaṃ mārgaṃ gamiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 26.1]
tatrāsmākaṃ bhavatu śramaṇena gautamena sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 27.1]
atha mārasya pāpīyasa etadabhavat asakṛdasakṛnmayā śramaṇasya gautamasya parākrāntam na ca kadācidavatāro labdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 28.1]
yannvahaṃ tīrthyānāṃ prahareyam | [Divyāv, 12 29.1]
iti viditvā maskarivadātmānamabhinirmāya upari vihāyasamabhyudgamya jvalanatapanavidyotanavarṣaṇaprātihāryāṇi kṛtvā saṃjayinaṃ vairaṭṭīputramāmantrayate yatkhalu saṃjayiñ jānīyā aham ṛddhimāñjñānavādī śramaṇo gautama ṛddhimāñ jñānavādītyātmānaṃ pratijānīte | [Divyāv, 12 30.1]
arhati jñānavādī jñānavādinā sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 31.1]
yadyekaṃ śramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati ahaṃ dve | [Divyāv, 12 32.1]
dve śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahaṃ catvāri | [Divyāv, 12 33.1]
catvāri śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahamaṣṭau | [Divyāv, 12 34.1]
aṣṭau śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahaṃ ṣoḍaśa | [Divyāv, 12 35.1]
ṣoḍaśa śramaṇo gautamaḥ ahaṃ dvātriṃśaditi yāvacchramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati ahaṃ taddviguṇamuttaraṃ manuṣyadharmaprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 36.1]
upārdhaṃ mārgaṃ śramaṇo gautama āgacchatu ahamapyupārdhaṃ mārgaṃ gamiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 37.1]
tatra me bhavatu śramaṇena gautamena sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 38.1]
evamanyonyaṃ sarve viheṭhitāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 39.1]
ekaika evamāharddherlābhī nāhamiti | [Divyāv, 12 40.1]
pūraṇādyāḥ ṣaṭ śāstāraḥ sarvajñajñānino yena rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisārastenopasaṃkrāman | [Divyāv, 12 41.1]
upasaṃkramya rājānaṃ māgadhaṃ śreṇyaṃ bimbisāramidamavocan yatkhalu deva jānīyā vayam ṛddhimanto jñānavādinaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 42.1]
śramaṇo 'pi gautama ṛddhimāñjñānavādītyātmānaṃ pratijānīte | [Divyāv, 12 43.1]
arhati jñānavādī jñānavādinā sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 44.1]
yadyekaṃ śramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati vayaṃ dve | [Divyāv, 12 45.1]
dve śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ catvāri | [Divyāv, 12 46.1]
catvāri śramaṇo gautamo vayamaṣṭau | [Divyāv, 12 47.1]
aṣṭau śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ ṣoḍaśa | [Divyāv, 12 48.1]
ṣoḍaśa śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ dvātriṃśaditi yāvacchramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati vayaṃ taddviguṇaṃ tattriguṇam ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 49.1]
upārdhaṃ mārgaṃ śramaṇo gautama āgacchatu vayamapyupārdhaṃ mārgaṃ gamiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 50.1]
tatrāsmākaṃ bhavatu śramaṇena gautamena sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 51.1]
evamukte rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisārastīrthyānidamavocat yūyamapi śavā bhūtvā bhagavatā sārdham ṛddhiṃ prārabhadhve atha pūraṇādyāḥ ṣaṭ śāstāro 'sarvajñāḥ sarvajñajñānino 'rdhamārge rājānaṃ māgadhaṃ śreṇyaṃ bimbisāraṃ vijñāpayanti vayaṃ smo deva ṛddhimanto jñānavādinaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 52.1]
śramaṇo 'pi gautama ṛddhimāñjñānavādītyātmānaṃ pratijānīte | [Divyāv, 12 53.1]
arhati jñānavādī jñānavādinā sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 54.1]
yāvat tatrāsmākaṃ bhavatu śramaṇena gautamena sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 55.1]
evamukte rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisārastāṃstīrthikaparivrājakānidamavocat yadyevaṃ trirapyetamarthaṃ vijñāpayiṣyatha nirviṣayān vaḥ kariṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 56.1]
atha tīrthyānāmetadabhavat ayaṃ rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisāraḥ śramaṇasya gautamasya śrāvakaḥ bimbisārastiṣṭhatu | [Divyāv, 12 57.1]
rājā prasenajit kauśalo madhyasthaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 58.1]
yadā śramaṇo gautamaḥ śrāvastīṃ gamiṣyati tatra vayaṃ gatvā śramaṇaṃ gautamamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihārye āhvayiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 59.1]
ityuktvā prakrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 60.1]
atha rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisāro 'nyatamaṃ puruṣamāmantrayate gaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa kṣipram | [Divyāv, 12 61.1]
bhadraṃ yānaṃ yojaya yatrāhamadhiruhya bhagavantaṃ darśanāyopasaṃkramiṣyāmi paryupāsanāyai | [Divyāv, 12 62.1]
evaṃ deveti sa puruṣo rājño māgadhasya śreṇyasya bimbisārasya pratiśrutya kṣipraṃ bhadraṃ yānaṃ yojayitvā yena rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 63.1]
upasaṃkramya rājānaṃ māgadhaṃ śreṇyaṃ bimbisāramidamavocat yuktaṃ devasya bhadraṃ yānaṃ yasyedānīṃ devaḥ kālaṃ manyata iti | [Divyāv, 12 64.1]
atha rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisāro bhadraṃ yānamabhiruhya rājagṛhānniryāti bhagavato 'ntikaṃ bhagavantaṃ darśanāyopasaṃkramituṃ paryupāsanāya | [Divyāv, 12 65.1]
tasya yāvatī yānasya bhūmistāvadyānena gatvā yānādavatīrya padbhyāmevārāmaṃ prāvikṣat | [Divyāv, 12 66.1]
antarā rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisāro bhagavantamadrākṣīt | [Divyāv, 12 67.1]
tadantarā pañca kakudānyapanīya tadyathā uṣṇīṣaṃ chatraṃ khaḍgamaṇiṃ vālavyajanaṃ citre copānahau sa pañca kakudānyapanīya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 68.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 69.1]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇaṃ viditvā rājānaṃ māgadhaṃ śreṇyaṃ bimbisāraṃ bhagavān dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 12 70.1]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 12 71.1]
atha rājā māgadhaḥ śreṇyo bimbisāro bhagavantamabhyānandyānumodya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato 'ntikāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 72.1]
atha bhagavata etadabhavat kutra pūrvakaiḥ samyaksambuddhairmahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitaṃ hitāya prāṇinām devatā bhagavata ārocayanti śrutapūrvaṃ bhadanta pūrvakaiḥ samyaksambuddhairmahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitaṃ hitāya prāṇināmiti | [Divyāv, 12 73.1]
bhagavato jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate śrāvastyāṃ pūrvakaiḥ samyaksambuddhairmahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitaṃ hitāya prāṇināmiti | [Divyāv, 12 74.1]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate gaccha tvamānanda bhikṣūṇāmārocaya | [Divyāv, 12 75.1]
tathāgataḥ kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cariṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 76.1]
yo yuṣmākamutsahate tathāgatena sārdhaṃ kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cartum sa cīvarakāṇi dhāvatu sīvyatu rañjayatu | [Divyāv, 12 77.1]
evaṃ bhadantetyāyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya bhikṣūṇāmārocayati bhagavānāyuṣmantaḥ kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ cariṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 78.1]
yo yuṣmākamutsahate tathāgatena sārdhaṃ kośaleṣu janapadeṣu cārikāṃ caritum sa cīvarāṇi dhāvatu sīvyatu rañjayatu iti | [Divyāv, 12 79.1]
te bhikṣava āyuṣmata ānandasya pratyaśrauṣuḥ | [Divyāv, 12 80.1]
atha bhagavān dānto dāntaparivāraḥ śāntaḥ śāntaparivāro mukto muktaparivāra āśvasta āśvastaparivāro vinīto vinītaparivāro 'rhannarhatparivāro vītarāgo vītarāgaparivāraḥ prāsādikaḥ prāsādikaparivāro vṛṣabha iva gogaṇaparivṛto gaja iva kalabhagaṇaparivṛtaḥ siṃha iva daṃṣṭrigaṇaparivṛto rājahaṃsa iva haṃsagaṇaparivṛtaḥ suparṇīva pakṣigaṇaparivṛto vipra iva śiṣyagaṇaparivṛtaḥ suvaidya ivāturagaṇaparivṛtaḥ śūra iva yodhagaṇaparivṛto deśika ivādhvagaṇaparivṛtaḥ sārthavāha iva vaṇiggaṇaparivṛtaḥ śreṣṭhīva pauragaṇaparivṛtaḥ koṭṭarāja iva mantrigaṇaparivṛtaścakravartīva putrasahasraparivṛtaścandra iva nakṣatragaṇaparivṛtaḥ sūrya iva raśmisahasraparivṛto virūḍhaka iva kumbhāṇḍagaṇaparivṛto virūpākṣa iva nāgagaṇaparivṛto dhanada iva yakṣagaṇaparivṛto dhṛtarāṣṭra iva gandharvagaṇaparivṛto vemacitra ivāsuragaṇaparivṛtaḥ śakra iva tridaśagaṇaparivṛto brahmeva brahmakāyikagaṇaparivṛtaḥ stimita iva jalanidhiḥ sajala iva jaladharo vimada iva gajapatiḥ sudāntairindriyair asaṃkṣobhiteryāpathapracāro 'nekairāveṇikairbuddhadharmairmahatā bhikṣusaṃghena ca puraskṛto yena śrāvastī tena cārikāṃ prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 81.1]
anekaiśca devatāśatasahasrairanugamyamāno 'nupūrveṇa cārikāṃ carañ śrāvastīmanuprāptaḥ śrāvastyāṃ viharati jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme | [Divyāv, 12 82.1]
aśrauṣustīrthyāḥ śramaṇo gautamaḥ śrāvastīṃ gata iti | [Divyāv, 12 83.1]
śrutvā ca punaḥ śrāvastīṃ samprasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 84.1]
te śrāvastīṃ gatvā rājānaṃ prasenajitkauśalamidamavocan yatkhalu deva jānīthā vayam ṛddhimanto jñānavādinaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 85.1]
śramaṇo gautama ṛddhimāñ jñānavādītyātmānaṃ pratijānīte | [Divyāv, 12 86.1]
arhati jñānavādī jñānavādinā sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharma ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 87.1]
yadyekaṃ śramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati vayaṃ dve | [Divyāv, 12 88.1]
dve śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ catvāri | [Divyāv, 12 89.1]
catvāri śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayamaṣṭau | [Divyāv, 12 90.1]
aṣṭau śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ ṣoḍaśa | [Divyāv, 12 91.1]
ṣoḍaśa śramaṇo gautamaḥ vayaṃ dvātriṃśaditi yāvacchramaṇo gautama uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati vayaṃ taddviguṇaṃ tattriguṇamuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 92.1]
upārdhaṃ mārgaṃ śramaṇo gautama āgacchatu vayamapyupārdhaṃ mārgaṃ gamiṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 93.1]
tatrāsmākaṃ bhavatu śramaṇena gautamena sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 94.1]
evamukte rājā prasenajit kauśalastīrthyānidamavocat āgamayantu tāvadbhavanto yāvadahaṃ bhagavantamavalokayāmi | [Divyāv, 12 95.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo 'nyatamaṃ puruṣamāmantrayate gaccha tvaṃ bhoḥ puruṣa | [Divyāv, 12 96.1]
kṣipraṃ bhadraṃ yānaṃ yojaya | [Divyāv, 12 97.1]
ahamabhiruhya adyaiva bhagavantaṃ darśanāyopasaṃkramiṣyāmi paryupāsanāyai | [Divyāv, 12 98.1]
evaṃ deveti sa puruṣo rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya pratiśrutya kṣipraṃ bhadraṃ yānaṃ yojayitvā yena rājā prasenajit kauśalastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 99.1]
upasaṃkramya rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamidamavocat yuktaṃ devasya bhadraṃ yānaṃ yasyedānīṃ devaḥ kālaṃ manyate | [Divyāv, 12 100.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo bhadraṃ yānamabhiruhya śrāvastyā niryāti bhagavato 'ntikaṃ bhagavantaṃ darśanāya upasaṃkramituṃ paryupāsanāya | [Divyāv, 12 101.1]
tasya yāvatī yānasya bhūmistāvadyānena gatvā yānādavatīrya pādābhyāmeva ārāmaṃ praviśya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 102.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 103.1]
ekānte niṣaṇṇo rājā prasenajit kauśalo bhagavantamidamavocat ime bhadanta tīrthyā bhagavantamuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryeṇāhvayante | [Divyāv, 12 104.1]
vidarśayatu bhagavānuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 105.1]
nirbhartsayatu bhagavāṃstīrthyān | [Divyāv, 12 106.1]
nandayatu devamanuṣyān | [Divyāv, 12 107.1]
toṣayatu sajjanahṛdayamanāṃsi | [Divyāv, 12 108.1]
evamukte bhagavān rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamidamavocat nāhaṃ mahārāja evaṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ dharmaṃ deśayāmi evam yūyaṃ bhikṣava āgatāgatānāṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatīnāmuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayateti | [Divyāv, 12 109.1]
api tu ahamevaṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ dharmaṃ deśayāmi praticchannakalyāṇā bhikṣavo viharata vivṛtapāpā iti | [Divyāv, 12 110.1]
dvirapi trirapi rājā prasenajit kauśalo bhagavantamidamavocat vidarśayatu bhagavānuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 111.1]
nirbhartsayatu tīrthyān | [Divyāv, 12 112.1]
nandayatu bhagavān devamanuṣyān | [Divyāv, 12 113.1]
toṣayatu sajjanahṛdayamanāṃsi | [Divyāv, 12 114.1]
dharmatā khalu buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ jīvatāṃ tiṣṭhatāṃ dhriyamāṇānām yāpayatām yaduta daśāvaśyakaraṇīyāni bhavanti | [Divyāv, 12 115.1]
na tāvadbuddhā bhagavantaḥ parinirvānti yāvanna buddho buddhaṃ vyākaroti yāvanna dvitīyena sattvenāparivartyamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksambodhau cittamutpāditaṃ bhavati sarvabuddhavaineyā vinītā bhavanti tribhāga āyuṣa utsṛṣṭo bhavati sīmābandhaḥ kṛto bhavati śrāvakayugamagratāyāṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ bhavati sāṃkāśye nagare devatāvataraṇaṃ vidarśitaṃ bhavati anavatapte mahāsarasi śrāvakaiḥ sārdhaṃ pūrvikā karmaplotirvyākṛtā bhavati mātāpitarau satyeṣu pratiṣṭhāpitau bhavataḥ śrāvastyāṃ mahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitaṃ bhavati | [Divyāv, 12 116.1]
atha bhagavata etadabhavat avaśyakaraṇīyametattathāgateneti viditvā rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamāmantrayate gaccha tvaṃ mahārāja | [Divyāv, 12 117.1]
itaḥ saptame divase tathāgato mahājanapratyakṣamuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 118.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo bhagavantamidamavocat yadi bhagavānanujānīyāt ahaṃ bhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍapaṃ kārayeyam | [Divyāv, 12 119.1]
atha bhagavata etadabhavat katarasmin pradeśe pūrvakaiḥ samyaksambuddhairmahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitaṃ hitāya prāṇināmiti devatā bhagavata ārocayanti antarā bhadanta śrāvastīmantarā ca jetavanamatrāntarāt pūrvakaiḥ samyaksambuddhairmahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitaṃ hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 120.1]
bhagavato 'pi jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate antarā ca śrāvastīmantarā ca jetavanamatrāntarāt pūrvakaiḥ samyaksambuddhairmahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśitaṃ hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 121.1]
adhivāsayati bhagavān rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya tūṣṇībhāvena | [Divyāv, 12 122.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo bhagavatas tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavantamidamavocat katamasmin bhadanta pradeśe prātihāryamaṇḍapaṃ kārayāmi antarā ca mahārāja śrāvastīmantarā ca jetavanam | [Divyāv, 12 123.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhinandyānumodya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato 'ntikāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 124.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalastīrthyānidamavocat yatkhalu bhavanto jānīran itaḥ saptame divase bhagavānuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 125.1]
atha tīrthyānāmetadabhavat kiṃ punaḥ śramaṇo gautamaḥ saptabhirdivasairanadhigatamadhigamiṣyati atha vā niṣpalāyiṣyati atha vā pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kartukāmas teṣāmetadabhavat na hyeva śramaṇo gautamo niṣpalāyiṣyati nāpyanadhigatamadhigamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 126.1]
nūnaṃ śramaṇo gautamaḥ pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kartukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 127.1]
vayamapi tāvat pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 128.1]
iti viditvā raktākṣo nāma parivrājaka indrajālābhijñaḥ sa āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 129.1]
raktākṣasya parivrājakasyaitat prakaraṇaṃ vistareṇārocayanti evaṃ cāhur yatkhalu raktākṣa jānīyāḥ śramaṇo gautamo 'smābhirṛddhyā āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 130.1]
sa kathayati itaḥ saptame divase uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 12 131.1]
nūnaṃ śramaṇo gautamaḥ pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kartukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 132.1]
tvamapi tāvat sabrahmacāriṇāṃ pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kuruṣva | [Divyāv, 12 133.1]
tena tatheti pratijñātam | [Divyāv, 12 134.1]
atha raktākṣaḥ parivrājako yena nānātīrthikaśramaṇabrāhmaṇacarakaparivrājakās tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 135.1]
upasaṃkramya nānātīrthikaśramaṇabrāhmaṇacarakaparivrājakānām etatprakaraṇaṃ vistareṇārocayati evaṃ cāha yatkhalu bhavanto jānīran śramaṇo gautamo 'smābhirṛddhyā āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 136.1]
sa kathayati itaḥ saptame divase uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 12 137.1]
nūnaṃ śramaṇo gautamaḥ pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kartukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 138.1]
bhavadbhirapi brahmacāriṇāṃ sāhāyyaṃ karaṇīyam | [Divyāv, 12 139.1]
saptame divase yuṣmābhirbahiḥ śrāvastyā nirgantavyam | [Divyāv, 12 140.1]
taistatheti pratijñātam | [Divyāv, 12 141.1]
athānyatamasmin parvate pañcamātrāṇi ṛṣiśatāni prativasanti | [Divyāv, 12 142.1]
atha raktākṣaḥ parivrājako yena te ṛṣayastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 143.1]
upasaṃkramya teṣāmetatprakaraṇaṃ vistareṇārocayati evaṃ cāha yatkhalu bhavanto jānīran śramaṇo gautama ṛddhyā āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 144.1]
sa kathayati itaḥ saptame divase uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 12 145.1]
nūnaṃ śramaṇo gautamaḥ pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kartukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 146.1]
bhavadbhirapi sabrahmacāriṇāṃ sāhāyyaṃ karaṇīyam | [Divyāv, 12 147.1]
saptame divase yuṣmābhiḥ śrāvastīmāgantavyam | [Divyāv, 12 148.1]
taistatheti pratijñātam | [Divyāv, 12 149.1]
tena khalu samayena subhadro nāma parivrājakaḥ pañcābhijñaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 150.1]
tasya kuśinagaryāmāvasatho 'navatapte mahāsarasi divā vihāraḥ | [Divyāv, 12 151.1]
atha raktākṣaḥ parivrājako yena subhadraḥ parivrājakastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 152.1]
upasaṃkramya etatprakaraṇaṃ vistareṇārocayati evaṃ cāha yatkhalu subhadra jānīyāḥ śramaṇo gautamo 'smābhir ṛddhyā āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 153.1]
sa kathayati itaḥ saptame divase uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 12 154.1]
nūnaṃ śramaṇo gautamaḥ pakṣaparyeṣaṇaṃ kartukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 155.1]
tvayā sabrahmacāriṇāṃ sāhāyyaṃ karaṇīyam | [Divyāv, 12 156.1]
saptame divase tvayā śrāvastīmāgantavyam | [Divyāv, 12 157.1]
subhadreṇābhihitam na śobhanaṃ bhavadbhiḥ kṛtam yadyuṣmābhiḥ śramaṇo gautamo ṛddhyā āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 158.1]
tatkasya hetor mama tāvat kuśinagaryāmāvāso 'navatapte mahāsarasi divā vihāraḥ | [Divyāv, 12 159.1]
śramaṇasya gautamasya śāriputro nāma śiṣyastasya cundo nāma śrāmaṇerakastasyāpi tatraivānavatapte mahāsarasi divā vihāraḥ | [Divyāv, 12 160.1]
na tathānavataptakāyikā devatā api kārān kartavyān manyante yathā tasya | [Divyāv, 12 161.1]
eko 'yaṃ samayaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 162.1]
ihāhaṃ kuśinagarīṃ piṇḍāya caritvā piṇḍapātamādāya anavataptaṃ mahāsarasaṃ gacchāmi | [Divyāv, 12 163.1]
tasya mamānavataptakāyikā devatā anavataptānmahāsarasaḥ pānīyamuddhṛtya ekānte na prayacchati | [Divyāv, 12 164.1]
cundaḥ śramaṇoddeśaḥ pāṃśukūlānyādāyānavataptaṃ mahāsaro gacchati | [Divyāv, 12 165.1]
tasyānavataptakāyikā devatā pāṃśukūlāni dhāvayitvā tena pānīyenātmānaṃ siñcati | [Divyāv, 12 166.1]
yasya tāvadvayaṃ śiṣyapratiśiṣyakayāpi na tulyāḥ sa yuṣmābhiruttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryeṇāhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 167.1]
na śobhanaṃ bhavadbhiḥ kṛtam yacchramaṇo gautamo ṛddhiprātihāryeṇāhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 168.1]
evamahaṃ jāne yathā maharddhikaḥ śramaṇo gautamo mahānubhāva iti | [Divyāv, 12 169.1]
raktākṣeṇābhihitaṃ tvaṃ tāvacchramaṇasya gautamasya pakṣaṃ vadasi | [Divyāv, 12 170.1]
tvayā tāvanna gantavyam | [Divyāv, 12 171.1]
subhadreṇābhihitam naiva gamiṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 12 172.1]
atha rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya kālo nāmnā bhrātā abhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ śrāddho bhadraḥ kalyāṇāśayaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 173.1]
sa rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya niveśanadvāreṇābhiniṣkrāmati | [Divyāv, 12 174.1]
anyatamayā cāvaruddhikayā prāsādatalagatayā rājakumāraṃ dṛṣṭvā sragdāmaṃ kṣiptam | [Divyāv, 12 175.1]
tat tasyopari nipatitam | [Divyāv, 12 176.1]
mitrārimadhyamo lokaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 177.1]
tai rājñe niveditaṃ yatkhalu deva jānīthāḥ kālena devasyāntaḥpuraṃ prārthitam | [Divyāv, 12 178.1]
rājā prasenajit kauśalaścaṇḍo rabhasaḥ karkaśaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 179.1]
tenāparīkṣya pauruṣeyāṇāmājñā dattā gacchantu bhavantaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 180.1]
śīghraṃ kālasya hastapādāṃś chindantu | [Divyāv, 12 181.1]
evaṃ deveti pauruṣeyai rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya pratiśrutya kālasya vīthīmadhye hastapādāśchinnāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 182.1]
sa ārtasvaraṃ krandate duḥkhāṃ tīvrāṃ kharāṃ kaṭukāmamanāpāṃ vedanāṃ vedayate | [Divyāv, 12 183.1]
kālaṃ rājakumāraṃ dṛṣṭvā mahājanakāyo vikroṣṭumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 184.1]
pūraṇādayaśca nirgranthāstaṃ pradeśamanuprāptāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 185.1]
kālasya jñātibhirabhihitam etamāryāḥ kālaṃ rājakumāraṃ satyābhiyācanayā yathāpaurāṇaṃ kurudhvamiti | [Divyāv, 12 186.1]
pūraṇenābhihitam eṣa śramaṇasya gautamasya śrāvakaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 187.1]
śramaṇadharmeṇa gautamo yathāpaurāṇaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 188.1]
atha kālasya rājakumārasyaitadabhavat kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhaprāptaṃ māṃ bhagavān na samanvāharatīti viditvā gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 12 189.1]
imāmavasthāṃ mama lokanātho na vetti saṃbādhagatasya kasmāt | [Divyāv, 12 190.1]
namo 'stu tasmai vigatajvarāya sarveṣu bhūteṣvanukampakāya | [Divyāv, 12 190.2]
asaṃmoṣadharmāṇo buddhā bhagavantaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 191.1]
tatra bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate sma gaccha tvamānanda saṃghāṭimādāya anyatamena bhikṣuṇā paścācchramaṇena yena kālo rājabhrātā tenopasaṃkrāma | [Divyāv, 12 192.1]
upasaṃkramya kālasya rājakumārasya hastapādān yathāsthāne sthāpayitvā evaṃ vada ye kecit sattvā apadā vā dvipadā vā bahupadā vā arūpiṇo vā rūpiṇo vā saṃjñino vā asaṃjñino vā naivasaṃjñino vā nāsaṃjñinaḥ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddhasteṣāṃ sattvānāmagra ākhyāyate | [Divyāv, 12 193.1]
ye kecid dharmā asaṃskṛtā vā saṃskṛtā vā virāgo dharmasteṣāmagra ākhyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 194.1]
anena satyena satyavākyena tava śarīram yathāpaurāṇaṃ syāt | [Divyāv, 12 195.1]
evaṃ bhadantetyāyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya saṃghāṭīmādāyānyatamena bhikṣuṇā paścācchramaṇena yena rājabhrātā kālastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 196.1]
upasaṃkramya kālasya rājakumārasya hastapādān yathāsthāne sthāpayitvā evamāha ye kecit sattvā apadā vā dvipadā vā catuṣpadā vā bahupadā vā yāvannaivasaṃjñino nāsaṃjñinaḥ tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddhasteṣāṃ sattvānāmagra ākhyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 197.1]
ye keciddharmāḥ saṃskṛtā vā asaṃskṛtā vā virāgo dharmasteṣāmagra ākhyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 198.1]
ye kecit saṃghā vā gaṇā vā pūgā vā parṣado vā tathāgataśrāvakasaṃghasteṣāmagra ākhyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 199.1]
anena satyena satyavākyena tava śarīram yathāpaurāṇaṃ bhavatu | [Divyāv, 12 200.1]
sahābhidhānāt kālasya rājakumārasya śarīram yathāpaurāṇaṃ saṃvṛttam yathāpi tatra buddhasya buddhānubhāvena devatānāṃ ca devatānubhāvena | [Divyāv, 12 201.1]
kālena kumāreṇa tenaiva saṃvegena anāgāmiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam ṛddhiścāpi nirhṛtā | [Divyāv, 12 202.1]
tena bhagavata ārāmo niryātitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 203.1]
sa bhagavata upasthānaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 204.1]
yatrāsya śarīraṃ gaṇḍagaṇḍaṃ kṛtaṃ tasya gaṇḍaka ārāmika iti saṃjñā saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 12 205.1]
atha rājñā prasenajitā kauśalena sarvopakaraṇaiḥ sa pravāritaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 206.1]
kālenābhihitam na mama tvayā prayojanam | [Divyāv, 12 207.1]
bhagavata evopasthānaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 12 208.1]
rājñā prasenajitā kauśalena antarā ca śrāvastīmantarā ca jetavanamatrāntarādbhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍapaḥ kāritaḥ śatasahasrahastacaturṇāṃ maṇḍapo vitataḥ | [Divyāv, 12 209.1]
bhagavataḥ siṃhāsanaṃ prajñaptam | [Divyāv, 12 210.1]
anyatīrthikaśrāvakairapi pūrṇādīnāṃ nirgranthānāṃ pratyekapratyekamaṇḍapaḥ kāritaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 211.1]
rājñā prasenajitā kauśalena saptame divase yāvajjetavanaṃ yāvacca bhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍapo 'ntarāt sarvo 'sau pradeśo 'pagatapāṣāṇaśarkarakaṭhalyo vyavasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 212.1]
dhūpacūrṇāndhakāraḥ kṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 213.1]
chatradhvajapatākāgandhodakapariṣikto nānāpuṣpābhikīrṇo ramaṇīyaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 214.1]
antarāntarā ca puṣpamaṇḍapāḥ sajjīkṛtāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 215.1]
atha bhagavān saptame divase pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya śrāvastīṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat | [Divyāv, 12 216.1]
śrāvastīṃ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyaḥ paścādbhaktapiṇḍapātapratikrāntaḥ pātracīvaraṃ pratiśrāmya bahirvihārasya pādau prakṣālya vihāraṃ praviṣṭaḥ pratisaṃlayanāya | [Divyāv, 12 217.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalo 'nekaśataparivāro 'nekasahasraparivāro 'nekaśatasahasraparivāro yena bhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍapastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 218.1]
upasaṃkramya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 219.1]
tīrthyā api mahājanakāyaparivṛtā yena maṇḍapastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 220.1]
upasaṃkramya pratyekapratyekasminnāsane niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 221.1]
niṣadya rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamidamavocan yatkhalu deva jānīyā ete vayamāgatāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 222.1]
kutra etarhi śramaṇo gautamas tena bhavanto muhūrtamāgamayata | [Divyāv, 12 223.1]
eṣa idānīṃ bhagavānadhigamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 224.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśala uttaraṃ māṇavamāmantrayate ehi tvamuttara yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāma | [Divyāv, 12 225.1]
upasaṃkramyāsmākaṃ vacanena bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā alpābādhatāṃ ca pṛccha alpātaṅkatāṃ ca laghūtthānatāṃ ca yātrāṃ ca balaṃ ca sukhaṃ ca anavadyatāṃ ca sparśavihāratāṃ ca | [Divyāv, 12 226.1]
evaṃ ca vada rājā bhadanta prasenajit kauśala evamāha ime bhadanta tīrthyā āgatā yasyedānīṃ kālaṃ manyate | [Divyāv, 12 227.1]
evaṃ devetyuttaro māṇavo rājñaḥ prasenajitaḥ kauśalasya pratiśrutya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 228.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavatā sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃmodanīṃ saṃrañjanīṃ vividhāṃ kathāṃ vyatisārya ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 229.1]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇa uttaro māṇavo bhagavantamidamavocat rājā bhadanta prasenajit kauśalo bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vandate alpābādhatāṃ ca pṛcchati alpātaṅkatāṃ ca laghūtthānatāṃ ca yātrāṃ ca balaṃ ca sukhaṃ ca anavadyatāṃ ca sparśavihāratāṃ ca | [Divyāv, 12 230.1]
sukhī bhavatu māṇava rājā prasenajit kauśalastvaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 12 231.1]
rājā bhadanta prasenajit kauśala evamāha ime bhadanta tīrthyā āgatā yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyate | [Divyāv, 12 232.1]
evamukte bhagavānuttaraṃ māṇavamidamavocat māṇava eṣo 'hamadyāgacchāmi | [Divyāv, 12 233.1]
bhagavatā tathādhiṣṭhito yathottaro māṇavastat evoparivihāyasā prakrāntaḥ yena rājā prasenajit kauśalastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 234.1]
adrākṣīdrājā prasenajit kauśala uttaraṃ māṇavakamupari vihāyasā āgacchantam | [Divyāv, 12 235.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punastīrthyānidamavocat vidarśitaṃ bhagavatottare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 236.1]
yūyamapi vidarśayata | [Divyāv, 12 237.1]
tīrthyāḥ kathayanti mahājanakāyo 'tra mahārāja saṃnipatitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 238.1]
kiṃ tvaṃ jñāsyasi kenaitad vidarśitamasmābhirvā śramaṇena gautamena atha bhagavāṃstadrūpaṃ samādhiṃ samāpanno yathā samāhite citte 'rgaḍacchidreṇārciṣo nirgatya bhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍape nipatitāḥ sarvaśca prātihāryamaṇḍapaḥ prajvalitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 239.1]
adrākṣustīrthyā bhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍapaṃ prajvalitam dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamidamavocan eṣa idānīṃ mahārāja śramaṇasya gautamasya prātihāryamaṇḍapaḥ prajvalitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 240.1]
gaccha idānīṃ nirvāpaya | [Divyāv, 12 241.1]
atha so 'gnir aspṛṣṭa eva vāriṇā sarvaprātihāryamaṇḍapam adagdhvā svayameva nirvṛto yathāpi tadbuddhasya buddhānubhāvena devatānāṃ ca devatānubhāvena | [Divyāv, 12 242.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalastīrthyānidamavocat vidarśitaṃ bhagavatottare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 243.1]
yūyamapi vidarśayata | [Divyāv, 12 244.1]
tīrthyāḥ kathayanti mahājanakāyo 'tra mahārāja saṃnipatitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 245.1]
kiṃ tvaṃ jñāsyasi kena etadvidarśitamasmābhirvā śramaṇena gautamena bhagavatā kanakamarīcikāvabhāsā utsṛṣṭāḥ yena sarvaloka udāreṇāvabhāsena sphuṭo 'bhūt | [Divyāv, 12 246.1]
adrākṣīdrājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ sarvalokamudāreṇāvabhāsena sphuṭam | [Divyāv, 12 247.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punastīrthyānāmantrayate vidarśitaṃ bhagavatottare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 248.1]
yūyamapi vidarśayata | [Divyāv, 12 249.1]
tīrthyāḥ kathayanti mahājanakāyo 'tra mahārāja saṃnipatitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 250.1]
kiṃ tvaṃ jñāsyasi kena etadvidarśitamasmābhirvā śramaṇena gautamena | [Divyāv, 12 251.1]
gaṇḍakenārāmikenottarakauravād dvīpāt karṇikāravṛkṣamādāya bhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍapasyāgrataḥ sthāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 252.1]
ratnakenāpyārāmikena gandhamādanādaśokavṛkṣamānīya bhagavataḥ prātihāryamaṇḍapasya pṛṣṭhataḥ sthāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 253.1]
atha rājā prasenajit kauśalastīrthyānidamavocat vidarśitaṃ bhagavatottare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 254.1]
yūyamapi vidarśayata | [Divyāv, 12 255.1]
tīrthyāḥ kathayanti mahājanakāyo 'tra saṃnipatitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 256.1]
kiṃ tvaṃ jñāsyasi kena etadvidarśitamasmābhirvā śramaṇena gautamena bhagavatā sābhisaṃskāreṇa pṛthivyāṃ pādau nyastau | [Divyāv, 12 257.1]
mahāpṛthivīcālaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 258.1]
ayaṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhāturiyaṃ mahāpṛthivī ṣaḍvikāraṃ kampati prakampati samprakampati | [Divyāv, 12 259.1]
calati saṃcalati saṃpracalati | [Divyāv, 12 260.1]
vyathati saṃvyathati saṃpravyathati | [Divyāv, 12 261.1]
pūrvāvanamati paścimonnamati | [Divyāv, 12 262.1]
pūrvonnamati paścimāvanamati | [Divyāv, 12 263.1]
dakṣiṇonnamati uttarāvanamati | [Divyāv, 12 264.1]
uttaronnamati dakṣiṇāvanamati | [Divyāv, 12 265.1]
madhye unnamati ante 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 12 266.1]
madhye 'vanamati ante unnamati | [Divyāv, 12 267.1]
imau sūryacandramasau bhāsatastapato virocataḥ | [Divyāv, 12 268.1]
vicitrāṇi ca āścaryādbhutāni prādurbhūtāni | [Divyāv, 12 269.1]
gaganatalasthā devatā bhagavata upariṣṭāddivyānyutpalāni kṣipanti padmāni kumudāni puṇḍarīkānyagarucūrṇāni candanacūrṇāni tagaracūrṇāni tamālapatrāṇi divyāni māndārakāṇi puṣpāṇi kṣipanti divyāni ca vāditrāṇi saṃpravādayanti cailavikṣepaṃ cākārṣuḥ | [Divyāv, 12 270.1]
atha teṣām ṛṣīṇāmetadabhavat kimarthaṃ mahāpṛthivīcālaḥ saṃvṛtta iti | [Divyāv, 12 271.1]
teṣāmetadabhavat nūnamasmākaṃ sabrahmacāribhiḥ śramaṇo gautamo ṛddhyā āhūto bhaviṣyatīti viditvā pañca ṛṣiśatāni śrāvastīṃ samprasthitāni | [Divyāv, 12 272.1]
teṣāmāgacchatāṃ bhagavatā ekāyano mārgo 'dhiṣṭhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 273.1]
adrākṣuste ṛṣayo bhagavantaṃ dūrādeva dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaṃ mūrtimantamiva dharmaṃ havyāvasiktamiva hutavahaṃ kāñcanabhājanasthamiva pradīpaṃ jaṅgamamiva suvarṇaparvataṃ nānāratnavicitramiva suvarṇarūpaṃ sphuṭapaṭumahāvimalaviśuddhabuddhiṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantam | [Divyāv, 12 274.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punar na tathā dvādaśavarṣe 'bhyastaśamatho yogācārasya cittasya kalyatāṃ janayati aputrasya vā putraḥ pratilambho daridrasya vā nidhidarśanaṃ rājyābhinandino vā rājyābhiṣeko yathā tatprathamataḥ pūrvabuddhāropitakuśalamūlānāṃ tatprathamato buddhadarśanam | [Divyāv, 12 275.1]
atha te ṛṣayo yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 276.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte sthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 281.1]
ekāntasthitāste ṛṣayo bhagavantamidamavocan labhemahi vayaṃ bhadanta svākhyāte dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasaṃpadaṃ bhikṣubhāvam | [Divyāv, 12 282.1]
carema vayaṃ bhagavato 'ntike pravrajya brahmacaryam | [Divyāv, 12 283.1]
te bhagavatā brāhmeṇa svareṇāhūtāḥ eta bhikṣavaścarata brahmacaryam | [Divyāv, 12 284.1]
sahābhidhānānmuṇḍāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ saṃghāṭīprāvṛtāḥ pātrakaravyagrahastāḥ saptāhāvaropitakeśaśmaśravo varṣaśatopasaṃpannasya bhikṣorīryāpathenāvasthitāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 285.1]
ehīti coktāśca tathāgatena muṇḍāśca saṃghāṭiparītadehāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 286.1]
sadyaḥ praśāntendriyā eva tasthurevaṃ sthitā buddhamanorathena | [Divyāv, 12 287.1]
atha bhagavān divyamānuṣyeṇa pūjāsatkāreṇa satkṛto gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito 'rhannarhatparivāraḥ saptabhiśca nikāyaiḥ saṃpuraskṛto mahatā ca janaughena yena prātihāryamaṇḍapastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 288.1]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 289.1]
bhagavataḥ kāyādraśmayo nirgatya sarvaṃ prātihāryamaṇḍapaṃ suvarṇavarṇāvabhāsaṃ kṛtavatyaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 290.1]
atha lūhasudatto gṛhapatirutthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇaṃ jānumaṇḍalaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocat alpotsuko bhagavān bhavatu | [Divyāv, 12 291.1]
ahaṃ tīrthyaiḥ sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 292.1]
nirbhartsayiṣyāmi tīrthyān | [Divyāv, 12 293.1]
saha dharmeṇa nandayiṣyāmi devamanuṣyān | [Divyāv, 12 294.1]
toṣayiṣyāmi sajjanahṛdayamanāṃsi | [Divyāv, 12 295.1]
na tvaṃ gṛhapate ebhir ṛddhyā āhūtaḥ api tvahaṃ tīrthyaiḥ ṛddhyā āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 296.1]
ahamuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 297.1]
sthānametadvidyate yattīrthyā evaṃ vadeyuḥ nāsti śramaṇasya gautamasyottare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryam | [Divyāv, 12 298.1]
śrāvakasyaiṣā gṛhiṇo 'vadātavasanasya ṛddhiriti | [Divyāv, 12 299.1]
niṣīda tvaṃ gṛhapate yathāsvake āsane | [Divyāv, 12 300.1]
niṣaṇṇo lūhasudatto gṛhapatiryathāsvake āsane | [Divyāv, 12 301.1]
yathā lūhasudatto gṛhapatirevaṃ kālo rājabhrātā rambhaka ārāmikaḥ ṛddhilamātā upāsikā śramaṇoddeśikā cundaḥ śramaṇoddeśaḥ utpalavarṇā bhikṣuṇī | [Divyāv, 12 302.1]
athāyuṣmān mahāmaudgalyāyana utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocat alpotsuko bhagavān bhavatu | [Divyāv, 12 303.1]
ahaṃ tīrthyaiḥ sārdhamuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 304.1]
tīrthyān nigṛhniṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 12 305.1]
saha dharmeṇa nandayiṣyāmi devamanuṣyān | [Divyāv, 12 306.1]
toṣayiṣyāmi sajjanahṛdayamanāṃsi | [Divyāv, 12 307.1]
pratibalastvaṃ maudgalyāyana tīrthyān sahadharmeṇa nigṛhītum | [Divyāv, 12 308.1]
api tu na tvaṃ tīrthyair ṛddhyā āhūtaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 309.1]
ahameṣāmuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayiṣyāmi hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 310.1]
nirbhartsayiṣyāmi tīrthyān | [Divyāv, 12 311.1]
nandayiṣyāmi devamanuṣyān | [Divyāv, 12 312.1]
toṣayiṣyāmi sajjanahṛdayamanāṃsi | [Divyāv, 12 313.1]
niṣīda tvaṃ maudgalyāyana yathāsvake āsane | [Divyāv, 12 314.1]
niṣaṇṇa āyuṣmān mahāmaudgalyāyano yathāsvake āsane | [Divyāv, 12 315.1]
tatra bhagavān rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamāmantrayate ko mahārāja tathāgatamadhyeṣate uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ hitāya prāṇinām atha rājā prasenajit kauśala utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇaṃ jānumaṇḍalaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantametadavocat ahaṃ bhadanta bhagavantamadhyeṣe uttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitum | [Divyāv, 12 316.1]
bhagavānuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryam vidarśayatu hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 317.1]
nirbhartsayatu tīrthyān | [Divyāv, 12 318.1]
nandayatu devamanuṣyān | [Divyāv, 12 319.1]
toṣayatu sajjanahṛdayamanāṃsi | [Divyāv, 12 320.1]
atha bhagavāṃstadrūpaṃ samādhiṃ samāpanno yathā samāhite citte svasminnāsane 'ntarhitaḥ pūrvasyāṃ diśi uparivihāyasamabhyudgamya caturvidhamīryāpathaṃ kalpayati tadyathā caṅkramyate tiṣṭhati niṣīdati śayyāṃ kalpayati | [Divyāv, 12 321.1]
tejodhātumapi sampadyate | [Divyāv, 12 322.1]
tejodhātusamāpannasya buddhasya bhagavato vividhānyarcīṃṣi kāyānniścaranti tadyathā nīlapītāni lohitānyavadātāni mañjiṣṭhāni sphaṭikavarṇāni | [Divyāv, 12 323.1]
anekānyapi prātihāryāṇi vidarśayati | [Divyāv, 12 324.1]
adhaḥkāyaṃ prajvālayati uparimāt kāyācchītalā vāridhārāḥ syandante | [Divyāv, 12 325.1]
yathā pūrvasyāṃ diśi evaṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśīti caturdiśaṃ caturvidham ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ vidarśya tān ṛddhyabhisaṃskārān pratiprasrabhya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 326.1]
niṣadya bhagavān rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamidamavocat iyaṃ mahārāja tathāgatasya sarvaśrāvakasādhāraṇā ṛddhiḥ | [Divyāv, 12 327.1]
tatra bhagavān dvirapi rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamāmantrayate ko mahārāja tathāgatamadhyeṣate 'sādhāraṇāyām ṛddhyāmuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ hitāya prāṇinām atha rājā prasenajit kauśala utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇaṃ jānumaṇḍalaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantamidamavocat ahaṃ bhadanta bhagavantamadhyeṣe 'sādhāraṇāyām ṛddhyāmuttare manuṣyadharme ṛddhiprātihāryaṃ hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 328.1]
nirbhartsayatu tīrthyān | [Divyāv, 12 329.1]
nandayatu devamanuṣyān | [Divyāv, 12 330.1]
toṣayatu sajjanahṛdayamanāṃsi | [Divyāv, 12 331.1]
bhagavatā laukikaṃ cittamutpāditam | [Divyāv, 12 332.1]
dharmatā khalu buddhānāṃ bhagavatām yadi laukikaṃ cittamutpādayanti antaśaḥ kuntapipīliko 'pi prāṇī bhagavataḥ cetasi cittamājānanti | [Divyāv, 12 333.1]
atha lokottaracittamutpādayanti tatrāgatirbhavati pratyekabuddhānāmapi kaḥ punarvādaḥ śrāvakāṇām atha śakrabrahmādīnāṃ devānāmetadabhavat kimarthaṃ bhagavatā laukikaṃ cittamutpāditam teṣāmetadabhavat śrāvastyāṃ mahāprātihāryaṃ vidarśayitukāmo hitāya prāṇinām | [Divyāv, 12 334.1]
atha śakrabrahmādayo devā anekāni ca devatāśatasahasrāṇi bhagavataścetasā cittamājñāya tadyathā balavān puruṣaḥ saṃkuñcitaṃ vā bāhuṃ prasārayet prasāritaṃ vā saṃkuñcayet evameva śakrabrahmādayo devā anekāni ca devatāśatasahasrāṇi ca devaloke 'ntarhitāni bhagavataḥ puratastasthuḥ | [Divyāv, 12 335.1]
atha brahmādayo devā bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvaṃ niśritya niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 336.1]
śakrādayo devā bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā vāmaṃ pārśvaṃ niśritya niṣaṇṇāḥ | [Divyāv, 12 337.1]
nandopanandābhyāṃ nāgarājābhyāṃ bhagavata upanāmitaṃ nirmitaṃ sahasrapatraṃ śakaṭacakramātraṃ sarvasauvarṇaṃ ratnadaṇḍaṃ padmam | [Divyāv, 12 338.1]
bhagavāṃśca padmakarṇikāyāṃ niṣaṇṇaḥ paryaṅkamābhujya ṛjuṃ kāyaṃ praṇidhāya pratimukhaṃ smṛtimupasthāpya padmasyopari padmaṃ nirmitam | [Divyāv, 12 339.1]
tatrāpi bhagavān paryaṅkaniṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 12 340.1]
evamagrataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvataḥ | [Divyāv, 12 341.1]
evaṃ bhagavatā buddhapiṇḍī nirmitā yāvadakaniṣṭhabhavanamupādāya buddhā bhagavanto parṣannirmitam | [Divyāv, 12 342.1]
kecidbuddhanirmāṇāścaṅkramyante kecit tiṣṭhanti kecinniṣīdanti kecicchāyāṃ kalpayanti tejodhātumapi samāpadyante jvalanatapanavarṣaṇavidyotanaprātihāryāṇi kurvanti | [Divyāv, 12 343.1]
anye praśnān pṛcchanti anye visarjayanti | [Divyāv, 12 344.1]
gāthādvayaṃ bhāṣante | [Divyāv, 12 345.1]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [Divyāv, 12 345.2]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāramiva kuñjaraḥ | [Divyāv, 12 345.3]
yo hyasmin dharmavinaye apramattaścariṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 346.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 12 346.2]
