yato bhikṣavaḥ saṃśayajātāḥ sarvasaṃśayacchettāraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ pṛcchanti bhagavan dharmarucirihaiva śrāvastyāṃ jāto 'sminneva jetavane pravrajito na kutaścidāgato na kutracidgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 267.1]
ihaiva tiṣṭhan bhagavatā dharmarucirevamucyate cirasya dharmaruce sucirasya dharmaruce suciracirasya dharmaruce | [Divyāv, 18 268.1]
kiṃ saṃdhāya bhagavān kathayaty evamukte bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma na bhikṣavaḥ pratyutpannaṃ saṃdhāya kathayāmi | [Divyāv, 18 269.1]
atītaṃ saṃdhāya kathayāmi | [Divyāv, 18 270.1]
atītaṃ saṃdhāya mayaivamuktam | [Divyāv, 18 271.1]
icchatha bhikṣavo 'sya dharmaruceḥ pūrvikāṃ karmaplotimārabhya dhārmikathāṃ śrotum etasya bhagavan kāla etasya sugata samayo yadbhagavān dharmarucimārabhya bhikṣūṇāṃ dhārmikathāṃ kuryāt | [Divyāv, 18 272.1]
bhagavataḥ śrutvā bhikṣavo dhārayiṣyanti | [Divyāv, 18 273.1]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani prathame 'saṃkhyeye kṣemaṃkaro nāma tathāgato loka utpanno vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devamanuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [Divyāv, 18 274.1]
sa ca kṣemāvatīṃ rājadhānīmupaniśritya viharati | [Divyāv, 18 275.1]
tasyāṃ ca kṣemāvatyāṃ kṣemo nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati | [Divyāv, 18 276.1]
tasyāṃ ca kṣemāvatyāṃ rājadhānyāmanyatamo vaṇikśreṣṭhī prativasati | [Divyāv, 18 277.1]
tenāsau kṣemaṃkaraḥ samyaksambuddhaḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ traimāsān sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena sarvopakaraṇairupasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 278.1]
yato 'sau śreṣṭhī saṃlakṣayati gacchāmi mahāsamudram | [Divyāv, 18 279.1]
bhāṇḍaṃ samudānīya tasmācca ratnānyānīya saṃghe pañcavārṣikaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 18 280.1]
evaṃ saṃcintya bhāṇḍaṃ samudānīya grāmanigamapallīpattanarājadhānīṣvanupūrveṇa cañcūryamāṇaḥ samudramanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 281.1]
ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā sāmudreṇa yānapātreṇa mahāsamudramavatīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 282.1]
asya tasmin mahāsamudre 'vatīrṇasya kṣemaṃkaraḥ samyaksambuddhaḥ sakalaṃ buddhakāryaṃ kṛtvā nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 283.1]
tasya parinirvṛtasya vaśino bhikṣavaḥ parinirvṛtāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 284.1]
saptāhaparinirvṛtasya śāsanamantarhitam | [Divyāv, 18 285.1]
sa ca śreṣṭhī saṃsiddhayānapātreṇa devatāmānuṣyaparigṛhītena tasmānmahāsamudrāt tīrṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 286.1]
uttīrya ca taṃ bhāṇḍaṃ śakaṭairuṣṭrairgobhirgardabhaiśca cotkṣipya anupūrveṇa samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 287.1]
sa ca panthānaṃ gacchan prātipathikān pṛcchati kiṃ bhavanto jānīdhvaṃ kṣemāvatyāṃ rājadhānyāṃ pravṛttis tairuktam jānīmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 288.1]
sa kathayaty asti kaścit kṣemāvatyāṃ rājadhānyāṃ kṣemaṃkaro nāma samyaksambuddhas te kathayanti parinirvṛtaḥ sa bhagavān kṣemaṃkaraḥ samyaksambuddhaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 289.1]
sa ca tacchrutvā paraṃ khedamupagataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 290.1]
saṃmūrchitaśca bhūmau patitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 291.1]
tasmācca jalābhiṣekeṇa pratyāgataprāṇo jīvita utthāya bhūyaḥ pṛcchati kiṃ bhavanto jānīdhvaṃ śrāvakā api tāvattasya bhagavatastiṣṭhanti tairuktas te 'pi vaśino bhikṣavaḥ parinirvṛtāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 292.1]
saptāhaparinirvṛtasya ca buddhasya bhagavataḥ kṣemaṃkarasya samyaksambuddhasya kṣemeṇa rājñā caityamalpeśākhyaṃ pratiṣṭhāpitam | [Divyāv, 18 293.1]
tena ca gatvā śreṣṭhinā janapadāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 294.1]
asti bhavantastasya bhagavato buddhasya kiṃcit stūpaṃ pratiṣṭhāpitam | [Divyāv, 18 295.1]
tairuktam asti kṣemeṇa rājñā alpeśākhyaṃ caityaṃ pratiṣṭhāpitam | [Divyāv, 18 296.1]
tasya etadabhavad etaṃ mayā suvarṇaṃ kṣemaṃkaraṃ samyaksambuddham uddiśyānītam | [Divyāv, 18 297.1]
sa ca parinirvṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 298.1]
yannvahametenaiva suvarṇena tasyaiva bhagavataścaityaṃ maheśākhyataraṃ kārayeyam | [Divyāv, 18 299.1]
evaṃ vicintya kṣemaṃ rājānaṃ vijñāpayati mahārāja idaṃ mayā suvarṇaṃ kṣemaṃkaraṃ samyaksambuddhamuddiśyānītam | [Divyāv, 18 300.1]
sa ca bhagavān parinirvṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 301.1]
idānīṃ mahārāja yadi tvamanujānīyād ahametenaiva suvarṇenaitat tasya bhagavataścaityaṃ maheśākhyataraṃ kārayeyam | [Divyāv, 18 302.1]
sa rājñābhihito yathābhipretaṃ kuru | [Divyāv, 18 303.1]
tato brāhmaṇā nagaraṃ prati nivāsinaḥ sambhūya sarve tasya mahāśreṣṭhinaḥ sakāśaṃ gatvā kathayanti bho mahāśreṣṭhin yadā kṣemaṃkaro buddho loke 'nutpanna āsīt tadā vayaṃ lokasya dakṣiṇīyā āsan | [Divyāv, 18 304.1]
yadā tūtpannaḥ tadā dakṣiṇīyo jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 305.1]
idānīṃ tu tasya parinirvṛtasya vayameva dakṣiṇīyāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 306.1]
etat suvarṇamasmākaṃ gamyam | [Divyāv, 18 307.1]
sa teṣāṃ kathayati nāham yuṣmākametat suvarṇaṃ dāsyāmi | [Divyāv, 18 308.1]
te kathayanti yadyasmākaṃ na dāsyasi na vayaṃ tava kāmakāraṃ dāsyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 309.1]
te brāhmaṇā bahavaḥ śreṣṭhī cālpaparivāraḥ | [Divyāv, 18 310.1]
teṣāṃ tathā vyutpadyatāṃ na lebhe taccaityam yathepsitaṃ tena suvarṇena kārayitum | [Divyāv, 18 311.1]
atha sa śreṣṭhī rājñaḥ sakāśaṃ gatvā kathayati mahārāja taccaityaṃ na labhe brāhmaṇānāṃ sakāśādyathābhipretaṃ kārayitum | [Divyāv, 18 312.1]
yato 'sya rājñā svapuruṣo dattaḥ sahasrayodhī | [Divyāv, 18 313.1]
evaṃ ca rājñā svapuruṣa ājñapto yadyasya mahāśreṣṭhinaḥ stūpamabhisaṃskurvataḥ kaścidapanayaṃ karoti sa tvayā mahatā daṇḍena śāsayitavyaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 314.1]
evaṃ deveti sahasrayodhī puruṣo rājñaḥ pratiśrutya nirgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 315.1]
nirgamya ca tān brāhmaṇānevaṃ vadati śṛṇvantu bhavanto 'haṃ rājñāsya mahāśreṣṭhinaḥ svapuruṣo datto yadyasya stūpamabhisaṃskurvataḥ kaścidvighātaṃ kuryāt sa tvayā mahatā daṇḍena śāsayitavya iti | [Divyāv, 18 316.1]
yadi yūyamatra kiṃcid vighnaṃ kariṣyatha ahaṃ vo mahatā daṇḍenānuśāsayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 18 317.1]
te brāhmaṇāḥ sahasrayodhinaḥ puruṣasyaivaṃ śrutvā bhītāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 318.1]
yatastena mahāśreṣṭhinā saṃcintya yathaitat suvarṇaṃ tatraiva garbhasaṃsthaṃ syāt tathā kartavyamiti tasya stūpasya sarvaireva caturbhiḥ pārśvaiḥ pratikaṇṭhukayā catvāri sopānāni ārabdhāni kārayitum | [Divyāv, 18 319.1]
yāvadanupūrveṇa prathamā meḍhī tato 'nupūrveṇa dvitīyā tatastṛtīyā meḍhī yāvadanupūrveṇāṇḍam | [Divyāv, 18 320.1]
tathāvidhaṃ ca stūpasyāṇḍaṃ kṛtam yatra sā yūpayaṣṭirabhyantare pratipāditā | [Divyāv, 18 321.1]
paścāt tasyātinavāṇḍasyopari harmikā kṛtā | [Divyāv, 18 322.1]
anupūrveṇa yaṣṭyāropaṇaṃ kṛtam | [Divyāv, 18 323.1]
varṣasthāle mahāmaṇiratnāni tānyāropitāni | [Divyāv, 18 324.1]
tatra ca kriyamāṇe sahasrayodhinaḥ puruṣasyaivamutpannaṃ nātra kaścididānīṃ prahariṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 325.1]
viśvastamanāḥ kenacitkāryeṇa janapadeṣu gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 326.1]
tena ca mahāśreṣṭhinā tasya stūpasya caturbhiḥ pārśvaiścatvāro dvārakoṣṭhakā māpitāḥ caturbhiḥ pārśvaiścatvāri mahācaityāni kāritāni tadyathā jātirabhisambodhirdharmacakrapravartanaṃ parinirvāṇam | [Divyāv, 18 327.1]
tacca stūpāṅgaṇaṃ ratnaśilābhiścitam | [Divyāv, 18 328.1]
catvāraścopāṅgāścaturdiśaṃ māpitāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 329.1]
puṣkariṇyaścaturdiśamanupārśvena māpitāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 330.1]
tatra ca vividhāni jalajāni mālyāni ropitāni tadyathā utpalaṃ padmaṃ kumudaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ sugandhikaṃ mṛdugandhikam | [Divyāv, 18 331.1]
vividhāni ca puṣkariṇītīreṣu sthalajāni mālyāni ropitāni tadyathā atimuktakaṃ campakapāṭalāvārṣikāmallikāsumanāyūthikā dhātuṣkārī | [Divyāv, 18 332.1]
sarvartukālikāḥ puṣpaphalāḥ stūpapūjārtham | [Divyāv, 18 333.1]
sthāvarāvṛttiprajñaptāḥ stūpadāsā dattāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 334.1]
śaṅkhapaṭahavādyāni tūryāṇi dattāni | [Divyāv, 18 335.1]
ye tasmiṃścaitye gandhairdhūpairmālyaiśca cūrṇaiḥ kārāḥ kurvanti | [Divyāv, 18 336.1]
tasmāccādhiṣṭhānādviṣayāccāgamya janapadā gandhairmālyairdhūpaiścūrṇaistasmiṃścaitye kāraṃ kurvanti | [Divyāv, 18 337.1]
yadi ca dakṣiṇo vāyurvāti dakṣiṇena vāyunā sarvapuṣpajātīnāṃ gandhena taccaityamaṅgaṇaṃ cāsya sphuṭaṃ bhavatyanubhāvitam | [Divyāv, 18 338.1]
evaṃ paścimena vāyunā anupūrveṇāpi ca vāyunā | [Divyāv, 18 339.1]
vāyatā vāyatā taccaityāṅgaṇaṃ ca tena vividhena gandhamālyena sphuṭaṃ bhavatyanubhāvitam | [Divyāv, 18 340.1]
tasmiṃśca stūpe sarvajātakṛtaniṣṭhite sahasrayodhī abhyāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 341.1]
sa taṃ stūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvajātakṛtaniṣṭhitaṃ kathayaty asmiṃścaitye kārāṃ kṛtvā kimavāpyate yato 'sau śreṣṭhī buddhodāharaṇaṃ pravṛttaḥ kartum evaṃ tribhirasaṃkhyeyairvīryeṇa vyāyamatānuttarā bodhiravāpyate | [Divyāv, 18 342.1]
sa taṃ śrutvā viṣādamāpanno hīnotsāhatayā kathayati nāhaṃ śakṣyāmi anuttarāṃ samyaksambodhiṃ samudānayitum | [Divyāv, 18 343.1]
tato 'sau śreṣṭhī pratyekabuddhodāharaṇaṃ pravṛttaḥ kartum evaṃ sahasrayodhī tasyāpi varṇodāharaṇaṃ śrutvā viṣaṇṇacetāḥ kathayaty etāmapyahaṃ pratyekabodhiṃ na śaktaḥ samudānayitum | [Divyāv, 18 344.1]
tataḥ sa mahāśreṣṭhī śrāvakavarṇodāharaṇaṃ kṛtvā kathayaty asminnapi tāvat praṇidhatsva cittam | [Divyāv, 18 345.1]
yataḥ sahasrayodhyāha tvayā punarmahāśreṣṭhin katamasyāṃ bodhau praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ tena mahāśreṣṭhinoktam anuttarasyāṃ bodhau cittamutpāditam | [Divyāv, 18 346.1]
sahasrayodhyāha yadi tvayā anuttarasyāṃ bodhau cittamutpāditam ahaṃ tavaiva śrāvakaḥ syām | [Divyāv, 18 347.1]
tvayāhaṃ samanvāhartavyaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 348.1]
yato 'sya śreṣṭhī āha bahukilbiṣakārī bata bhavān | [Divyāv, 18 349.1]
kiṃtu loke yadā tvaṃ buddhotpādaśabdaṃ śrutvā smṛtiṃ pratilabhethāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 350.1]
sa ca śreṣṭhī taṃ caityaṃ kṛtvā nirīkṣya pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ karoti | [Divyāv, 18 351.1]
anena dānena mahadgatena buddho bhaveyaṃ sugataḥ svayambhūḥ | [Divyāv, 18 352.1]
tīrṇo 'haṃ tārayeyaṃ janaughān atāritā ye paurvakairjinendraiḥ | [Divyāv, 18 352.2]
bhagavānāha yo 'sau atīte 'dhvani śreṣṭhī abhūt ahameva sa tasmin samaye bodhisattvacaryāṃ vartāmi | [Divyāv, 18 353.1]
yo 'sau sahasrayodhī eṣa eva dharmarucistena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 18 354.1]
idaṃ mama prathame 'saṃkhyeye etasya dharmarucerdarśanam | [Divyāv, 18 355.1]
tatsaṃdhāya kathayāmi cirasya dharmaruce | [Divyāv, 18 356.1]
yato dharmarucir ājñāyāha cirasya bhagavan | [Divyāv, 18 357.1]
dvitīye dīpaṃkaro nāma samyaksambuddho loka utpanno vidyācaraṇasamyaksambuddhaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca buddho bhagavān | [Divyāv, 18 358.1]
atha dīpaṃkaraḥ samyaksambuddho janapadeṣu cārikāṃ caran dīpāvatīṃ rājadhānīmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 359.1]
dīpāvatyāṃ rājadhānyāṃ dīpo nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati ṛddhaṃ ca sphītaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 18 360.1]
tatra dīpena rājñā dīpaṃkaraḥ samyaksambuddhaḥ sābhisaṃskāreṇa nagarapraveśenopanimantritaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 361.1]
tasya ca dīpasya rājño vāsavo nāma sāmantarājo 'bhūt | [Divyāv, 18 362.1]
tena tasya dūto 'nupreṣita āgaccha iha mayā dīpaṃkaraḥ samyaksambuddhaḥ sābhisaṃskāreṇa nagarapraveśenopanimantritaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 363.1]
tasya pūjāṃ kariṣyāma iti | [Divyāv, 18 364.1]
tadā ca vāsavena rājñā dvādaśavarṣāṇi yajñamiṣṭvā yajñāvasāne rājñā pañca mahāpradānāni vyavasthāpitāni tadyathā sauvarṇakaṃ daṇḍakamaṇḍalu sauvarṇā sapātrī catūratnamayī śayyā pañca kārṣāpaṇaśatāni kanyā ca sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitā | [Divyāv, 18 365.1]
tena khalu samayena anyeṣu janapadeṣu dvau māṇavakau prativasataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 366.1]
tābhyāṃ copādhyāyasakāśād vedādhyayanaṃ kṛtam | [Divyāv, 18 367.1]
dharmatā ācāryasyācāryadhanam upādhyāyasyopādhyāyadhanaṃ pradeyamiti jñātvā cintayataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 368.1]
tābhyāṃ ca śrutaṃ vāsavena rājñā pañca mahāpradānāni yajñāvasāne samudānītāni yo brāhmaṇaḥ svādhyāyasampanno bhaviṣyati sa lapsyatīti | [Divyāv, 18 369.1]
tayoretadabhavad gacchāvastatra taṃ pradānaṃ pratigṛhṇīvaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 370.1]
ko 'smākaṃ tatra bahuśrutatamo vā svādhyāyatamo bhaviṣyatīti saṃcintya yena vāsavasya rājño mahānagaraṃ tena samprasthitau | [Divyāv, 18 371.1]
tasya ca rājño devatayā ārocitam | [Divyāv, 18 372.1]
yau etau dvau māṇavakau āgacchataḥ sumatiśca matiśca anayordvayoḥ sumateretatpradānaṃ dada | [Divyāv, 18 373.1]
yadevaṃ mahārāja tvayā dvādaśa varṣāṇi yajña iṣṭaḥ asmāt puṇyaphalānmahattamapadasya sumatermāṇavakasya mahāpradānaṃ dāsyasi | [Divyāv, 18 374.1]
sa rājā saṃlakṣayati nūnametau mahātmānau yeṣāmarthāya devatā apyārocayanti | [Divyāv, 18 375.1]
yato 'sau rājā paśyati māṇavakau dūrata evāgacchantau prāsādikāvabhirūpau tau ca gatvā tatra yajñe brāhmaṇapaṅktiṣu prajñapteṣu āsaneṣvagrāsanam abhiruhyāvasthitau | [Divyāv, 18 376.1]
yato rājā vāsavastau sumatiṃ māṇavaṃ pṛcchati bhavān sumatis tenoktam aham | [Divyāv, 18 377.1]
yato rājā vāsavaḥ sumatiṃ māṇavamagrāsane bhojayitvā pañca pradānāni prayacchati | [Divyāv, 18 378.1]
sumatirmāṇavaścatvāri mahāpradānāni gṛhṇāti daṇḍakamaṇḍaluprabhṛtīni ekaṃ kanyāpradānaṃ na pratigṛhṇāti | [Divyāv, 18 379.1]
sa kathayaty ahaṃ brahmacārī | [Divyāv, 18 380.1]
yataḥ sā kanyā sumatiṃ māṇavaṃ prāsādikamabhirūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā lubdhā snehotpannā taṃ sumatiṃ māṇavamevamāha pratigṛhṇa māṃ brāhmaṇa | [Divyāv, 18 381.1]
sa kathayati na śakyaṃ pratigṛhītum | [Divyāv, 18 382.1]
yataḥ sā kanyā rājñā pradānabuddhyā parityaktā na punargṛhītā sumatināpi māṇavenāpratigṛhyamāṇā rājño dīpasya dīpāvatīṃ nagarīṃ gatā | [Divyāv, 18 383.1]
sā tatra gatvā tadātmīyamalaṃkāraṃ śarīrādavatārya mālākārāyānuprayacchaty asyālaṃkārasya mūlyaṃ me pratidivasaṃ devasyārthe nīlotpalāni dadasva | [Divyāv, 18 384.1]
sā tenopakrameṇa tad alaṃkārikaṃ suvarṇaṃ dattvā devaśuśrūṣikā saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 18 385.1]
sa ca māṇavakaḥ sumatistāni catvāri mahāpradānāni gṛhya upādhyāyasakāśaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 386.1]
gatvā copādhyāyāya tāni catvāri mahāpradānānyanuprayacchati | [Divyāv, 18 387.1]
tebhyaścopādhyāyastrīṇi pratigṛhṇāti kārṣāpaṇānāṃ tu pañca śatāni tasyaiva sumaterdadāti | [Divyāv, 18 388.1]
sa ca sumatistasyāmeva rātrau daśa svapnānadrākṣīt mahāsamudraṃ pibāmi vaihāyasena gacchāmi imau candrādityau evaṃ maharddhikau evaṃ mahānubhāvau pāṇinā āmārṣṭi parimārṣṭi rājño rathe yojayāmi ṛṣīn śvetān hastinaḥ haṃsān siṃhān mahāśailaṃ parvatāniti | [Divyāv, 18 389.1]
sa tān dṛṣṭvā pratibuddhaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 390.1]
pratibuddhasyaitadabhavat ka eṣāṃ svapnānāṃ mama vyākaraṇaṃ kariṣyati tatra pañcābhijña ṛṣir nātidūre prativasati | [Divyāv, 18 391.1]
atha sumatirmāṇavaḥ saṃśayanirṇayanārtham ṛṣeḥ sakāśaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 392.1]
sumatistasya ṛṣeḥ pratisaṃmodanaṃ kṛtvā svapnānākhyāyāha kuruṣva me eṣāṃ svapnānāṃ nirṇayam | [Divyāv, 18 393.1]
sa ṛṣirāha nāhameṣāṃ svapnānāṃ vyākaraṇaṃ kariṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 18 394.1]
gaccha dīpāvatīṃ rājadhānīm | [Divyāv, 18 395.1]
tatra dīpena rājñā dīpaṃkaro nāma samyaksambuddhaḥ sābhisaṃskāreṇa nagarapraveśenopanimantritaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 396.1]
sa eṣāṃ svapnānāṃ vyākaraṇaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 397.1]
atha vāsavo rājā tasya dīpasya rājñaḥ pratiśrutya aśītyamātyasahasraparivṛto dīpāvatīṃ rājadhānīmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 398.1]
tena ca dīpena rājñā saptamāddivasāddīpaṃkarasya samyaksambuddhasya sābhisaṃskāreṇa nagarapraveśaṃ kariṣyāmīti sarvaviṣayādhiṣṭhānācca sarvapuṣpāṇāṃ saṃgrahaṃ kartumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 399.1]
tatra ca yasmin divase rājñā dīpena tasya dīpaṃkarasya samyaksambuddhasya sābhisaṃskāreṇa nagarapraveśa ārabdhaḥ kartum tasminneva divase sumatirapi tatraivāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 400.1]
tatra rājñā sarvapuṣpāṇāṃ saṃgrahaḥ kāritaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 401.1]
sā ca devopasthāyikā dārikā mālākārasakāśaṃ gatā prayaccha me nīlotpalāni devārcanaṃ kariṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 18 402.1]
mālākāra āha adya rājñā sarvapuṣpāṇi gṛhītāni dīpaṃkaranagarapraveśasyārthe | [Divyāv, 18 403.1]
sā kathayati gacchata punarapi tatra puṣkiriṇyām yadi matpuṇyair nīlotpalapadmam anuddhṛtamāsādyeta | [Divyāv, 18 404.1]
tatra puṣkiriṇyāṃ sumateḥ puṇyānubhāvāt sapta nīlapadmāni prādurbhūtāni | [Divyāv, 18 405.1]
yataḥ sa mālākāro gataḥ sa tāni paśyati | [Divyāv, 18 406.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca dārikayā mālākārasyoktam uddharaitāni padmāni | [Divyāv, 18 407.1]
mālākāraḥ kathayati nāhamuddhariṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 18 408.1]
rājakulānmamopālambho bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 409.1]
yataḥ sā kathayati na | [Divyāv, 18 410.1]
tvayā sarvapuṣpāṇyuddhṛtya rājñaḥ pūrvaṃ dattānyeva | [Divyāv, 18 411.1]
mālākāra āha dattāni | [Divyāv, 18 412.1]
yataḥ sā dārikā kathayati madīyaiḥ puṇyairetāni prādurbhūtāni prayacchoddhṛtāni mama | [Divyāv, 18 413.1]
mālākāraḥ kathayati kathametāni praveśakāni bhaviṣyantyasaṃviditaṃ rājakulasya dārikāhoddharatu bhavān | [Divyāv, 18 414.1]
ahamudakakumbhe prakṣiptaṃ praveśayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 18 415.1]
tena mālākāreṇaivaṃ śrutvā tasyā dārikāyāstānyuddhṛtya anupradattāni | [Divyāv, 18 416.1]
sā tāni gṛhītvā udakakumbhe prakṣipya tatkumbhamudakasya pūrayitvā adhiṣṭhānaṃ gatā prasthitā | [Divyāv, 18 417.1]
sa ca sumatistatsthānamanusaṃprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 418.1]
tasyaitadabhavat kathamahaṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantam dṛṣṭvā na pūjayāmi sa mālākāragṛhāṇyanvāhiṇḍati sarvapuṣpānveṣaṇaparaḥ na ca kiṃcidekapuṣpamāsādayati | [Divyāv, 18 419.1]
paścād bāhyenādhiṣṭhānānnirgamya ārāmeṇārāmaṃ puṣpāṇi paryeṣamāṇaḥ paryaṭati na caikapuṣpamāsādayati | [Divyāv, 18 420.1]
atha paryaṭamānastadudyānaṃ samprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 421.1]
sā ca dārikā tasmādudyānāt tasya sumater māṇavasyābhimukhamāgatā | [Divyāv, 18 422.1]
yataḥ puṇyānubhāvena tāni nīlapadmāni tasmādudakakumbhādabhyudgatāni | [Divyāv, 18 423.1]
yatastāni sumatirdṛṣṭvā tasyā dārikāyāḥ kathayati prayaccha mamaitāni padmāni | [Divyāv, 18 424.1]
matsakāśādeṣāṃ niṣkrayaṃ pañcakārṣāpaṇaśataṃ gṛhāṇa | [Divyāv, 18 425.1]
sā dārikā tasya sumateḥ kathayati tadā necchasi māṃ pratigṛhītum | [Divyāv, 18 426.1]
idānīṃ māṃ padmāni yācase | [Divyāv, 18 427.1]
nāhaṃ dāsyāmi | [Divyāv, 18 428.1]
evamuktvā taṃ sumatiṃ māṇavamuvāca kimebhiḥ kariṣyasi sumatirāha buddhaṃ bhagavantamarcayiṣyāmi | [Divyāv, 18 429.1]
paścāddārikā kathayati kiṃ mama kārṣāpaṇaiḥ kṛtyam evamahaṃ buddhāya dāsye yadi tvameṣāṃ padmānāṃ pradānaphalena mamāpi jātyāṃ jātyāṃ patnīmicchasi asya dānasya pradānakāle yadyevaṃ praṇidhānaṃ karoṣi jātyāṃ jātyāṃ mama bhāryā syāditi | [Divyāv, 18 430.1]
sumatirāha vayaṃ dānābhiratāḥ svagarbharūpaparityāgaṃ svamāṃsaparityāgaṃ ca kurmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 431.1]
tataḥ sā dārikā sumateḥ kathayati tvamevaṃ praṇidhānaṃ kuru paścād yenābhyarthīyase tasya māmanuprayacchethāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 432.1]
evamukte tayā dārikayā tasya sumateḥ pañca padmānyanupradattāni ātmanā dve gṛhīte | [Divyāv, 18 433.1]
gāthāṃ ca bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 18 434.1]
praṇidhim yatra kuryāstvaṃ buddhamāsādya nāyakam | [Divyāv, 18 435.1]
tatra te 'haṃ bhavet patnī nityaṃ sahadharmacāriṇī | [Divyāv, 18 435.2]
tena rājñā tatra sarvamapagatapāṣāṇaśarkarakapālaṃ kāritam ucchritadhvajapatākātoraṇam āmuktapaṭṭadāmaṃ gandhodakacūrṇapariṣiktam | [Divyāv, 18 436.1]
nagaradvārādārabhya yāvacca vihāro yāvacca nagarametadantaram apagatapāṣāṇaśarkarakapālaṃ kāritamucchritadhvajapatākatoraṇam āmuktapaṭṭadāma gandhodakacūrṇapariṣiktam | [Divyāv, 18 437.1]
sa ca rājā śataśalākaṃ chatraṃ gṛhītvā dīpaṃkarasya samyaksambuddhasya pratyudgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 438.1]
evamevāmātyāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 439.1]
evameva vāsavo rājā amātyaiḥ saha pratyudgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 440.1]
dīpo rājā bhagavato buddhasya pādayor nipatya vijñāpayati bhagavan adhiṣṭhānaṃ praviśa | [Divyāv, 18 441.1]
yataḥ sa bhagavān bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto 'dhiṣṭhānapraveśābhimukhaḥ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 442.1]
sa ca rājā dīpaḥ śataśalākaṃ chatraṃ dīpaṃkarasya samyaksambuddhasya dhārayati | [Divyāv, 18 443.1]
tathaivāmātyā vāsavo rājā amātyasahāyaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 444.1]
bhagavatā ṛddhyā tathādhiṣṭhitaṃ yathā ekaikaḥ saṃlakṣayaty ahaṃ bhagavataśchatraṃ dhārayāmīti | [Divyāv, 18 445.1]
atha bhagavāṃstathāvidhayā śobhayā janamadhyamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 446.1]
tatra bhagavatā sābhisaṃskāra indrakīle pādo vyavasthāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 447.1]
yadaiva bhagavatā indrakīle pādo vyavasthāpitas tadaiva samanantarakālaṃ pṛthivī ṣaḍvikāraṃ prakampitā calitā pracalitā saṃpracalitā vedhitā pravedhitā saṃpravedhitā | [Divyāv, 18 448.1]
dharmatā ca buddhānāṃ bhagavatām yadendrakīle sābhisaṃskāreṇa pādau vyavasthāpayanti citrāṇyāścaryāṇyadbhutadharmāḥ prādurbhavanty unmattāḥ svacittaṃ pratilabhante 'ndhāścakṣūṃṣi pratilabhante badhirāḥ śrotraśravaṇasamarthā bhavanti mūkāḥ pravyāharaṇasamarthā bhavanti paṅgavo gamanasamarthā bhavanti mūḍhā garbhiṇīnāṃ strīṇāṃ garbhā anulomībhavanti haḍinigaḍabaddhānāṃ ca sattvānāṃ bandhanāni śithilībhavanti janmajanmavairānubaddhāstadanantaraṃ maitracittatāṃ pratilabhante vatsā dāmāni chittvā mātṛbhiḥ saṃgacchanti hastinaḥ krośanti aśvā hreṣante ṛṣabhā garjanti śukasārikākokilajīvaṃjīvakā madhuraṃ nikūjanti aneritāni vāditrabhāṇḍāni madhuraśabdān niścārayanti peḍākṛtā alaṃkārā madhuraśabdānniścārayanty unnatāḥ pṛthivīpradeśā avanamanty avanatāśconnamanti apagatapāṣāṇaśarkarakapālāstiṣṭhanty antarikṣāddevatā divyānyutpalāni kṣipanti padmāni kumudāni puṇḍarīkānyagurucūrṇāni candanacūrṇāni tagaracūrṇāni tamālapatrāṇi divyāni mandārakāṇi puṣpāṇi kṣipanti pūrvo digbhāga unnamati paścimo 'vanamati paścima unnamati pūrvo 'vanamati dakṣiṇa unnamatyuttaro 'vanamaty uttara unnamati dakṣiṇo 'vanamati madhya unnamatyanto 'vanamati anta unnamati madhyo 'vanamati | [Divyāv, 18 449.1]
tatra ca dīpāvatyāṃ rājadhānyāmanekāni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi puṣpairdhūpairgandhaiśca kārāṃ kurvanti | [Divyāv, 18 450.1]
te 'pi ca sumatiśca dārikā ca yena dīpaṃkaraḥ samyaksambuddhastenānugacchanti padmāni gṛhya | [Divyāv, 18 451.1]
te ca tatra mahājanakāyena pūjārthaṃ saṃparivṛtasya bhagavata upaśleṣaṃ na labhante | [Divyāv, 18 452.1]
bhagavān saṃlakṣayati bahutaraṃ sumatirmāṇavo 'smānmahājanakāyāt puṇyaprasavaṃ kariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 18 453.1]
matvā mahatīṃ tumulāṃ vātavṛṣṭim abhinirmiṇoti | [Divyāv, 18 454.1]
yatastena janakāyenāvakāśo dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 455.1]
labdhāvakāśaśca sumatirmāṇavo bhagavantamasecanakadarśanaṃ dṛṣṭvā atīva prasādajātaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 456.1]
prasādajātena ca tāni pañca padmāni bhagavataḥ kṣiptāni | [Divyāv, 18 457.1]
tāni ca bhagavatā dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhena tathā adhiṣṭhitāni yathā śakaṭīcakramātrāṇi vitānaṃ baddhvā vyavasthitāni | [Divyāv, 18 458.1]
gacchato 'nugacchanti tiṣṭhato 'nutiṣṭhanti | [Divyāv, 18 459.1]
tathā dṛṣṭvā tayā dārikayā prasādajātayā dvau padmau bhagavataḥ kṣiptau | [Divyāv, 18 460.1]
tau cāpi bhagavatā tathādhiṣṭhitau yathā śakaṭīcakramātrau karṇasamīpe vitānaṃ baddhvā vyavasthitau | [Divyāv, 18 461.1]
tatra ca pradeśe tumulena vātavarṣeṇa kardamo jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 462.1]
paścāt sumatirmāṇavo buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ sakardamaṃ pṛthivīpradeśamupagataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 463.1]
tasmin sakardame pṛthivīpradeśe jaṭāṃ saṃtīrya bhagavato purato gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 18 464.1]
yadi buddho bhaviṣyāmi bodhāya buddhabodhana | [Divyāv, 18 465.1]
ākramiṣyasi me padbhyāṃ jaṭāṃ janmajarāntakām | [Divyāv, 18 465.2]
tatastena dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhena tasya sumatermāṇavasya jaṭāsu pādau vyavasthāpitau | [Divyāv, 18 466.1]
tasya ca sumateḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nubuddha eva matirmāṇavastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 18 467.1]
tena kupitenābhihitaṃ bhagavato dīpaṃkarasya paśya tāvadbhoḥ anena dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhenāsya sumatermāṇavasya tiraścām yathā padbhyāṃ jaṭā avaṣṭabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 468.1]
paścāt dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhena sumatirmāṇavo vyākṛto bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ nṛbhavādvimukto mukto vibhurlokahitāya śāstā | [Divyāv, 18 469.1]
śākyātmajaḥ śākyamunīti nāmnā trilokasāro jagataḥ pradīpaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 469.2]
yadā ca sa sumatirmāṇavo dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhena vyākṛtas tatsamakālameva vaihāyasaṃ saptatālānabhyudgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 470.1]
tāścāsya jaṭāḥ śīrṇā anyāḥ praviśiṣṭatarā jaṭāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 471.1]
sa vaihāyasastho mahatā janakāyena dṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 472.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ yadā anenānuttarajñānamadhigataṃ tadāsya vayaṃ śrāvakā bhavema | [Divyāv, 18 473.1]
sāpi ca dārikā praṇidhānaṃ karoti | [Divyāv, 18 474.1]
praṇidhānam yatra kuryāstvaṃ buddhamāsādya nāyakam | [Divyāv, 18 475.1]
tatra te 'haṃ bhavetpatnī nityaṃ sahadharmacāriṇī | [Divyāv, 18 475.2]
yadā bhavasi saṃbuddho loke jyeṣṭhavināyakaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 476.1]
śrāvikā te bhaviṣyāmi tasmin kāla upasthite | [Divyāv, 18 476.2]
khagasthaṃ māṇavaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasrāṇi śatāni ca | [Divyāv, 18 477.1]
śrāvakatvaṃ prārthayante sarve tatra hyanāgate | [Divyāv, 18 477.2]
yadā bhavasi saṃbuddho loke jyeṣṭhavināyakaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 478.1]
śrāvakāste bhaviṣyāmastasmin kāle hyupasthite | [Divyāv, 18 478.2]
yadā ca sumatirmāṇavo dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhena vyākṛtas tadāsya dīpena rājñā jaṭā gṛhītāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 479.1]
vāsavo rājā kathayati mamaitā jaṭā anuprayaccha | [Divyāv, 18 480.1]
tatastasya dīpena rājñā anupradattāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 481.1]
tena gṛhītvā gaṇitā aśītirvālasahasrāṇi | [Divyāv, 18 482.1]
tasya rājño 'mātyāḥ kathayanti deva asmākamekaikaṃ vālamanuprayaccha | [Divyāv, 18 483.1]
vayameṣāṃ caityāni kariṣyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 484.1]
tena rājñā teṣāṃ bhṛtyānāmekaiko vālo dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 485.1]
tairamātyaiḥ svake vijite gatvā caityāni pratiṣṭhāpitāni | [Divyāv, 18 486.1]
yadā sumatirmāṇavo 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksambuddhau vyākṛtaḥ tadā dīpena rājñā vāsavena ca rājñā tairanekaiśca naigamajānapadaiḥ sarvopakaraṇaiḥ pravārito 'nāgataguṇāvekṣatayā | [Divyāv, 18 487.1]
tataḥ sa matirmāṇava ucyate 'hamanuttarasyāṃ samyaksambodhau vyākṛtas tvayā kutra cittamutpāditaṃ sa kathayati kṣato 'haṃ sumate māṇava | [Divyāv, 18 488.1]
sa kathayati kathaṃ kṛtvā kṣato 'si tataḥ sa kathayati yadā tava dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhena padbhyāṃ jaṭā avaṣṭabdhās tadā kupitena vāṅ niścāritā dīpaṃkareṇa samyaksambuddhena śrotriyasya jaṭā tiraścām yathā padbhyāmavaṣṭabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 489.1]
yatastasya sumatiḥ kathayaty āgacchasva buddhasya bhagavato 'ntike pravrajāvaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 490.1]
tatastau sumatirmatiśca dīpaṃkarasya samyaksambuddhasya pravacane pravrajitau | [Divyāv, 18 491.1]
sumatinā ca pravrajya trīṇi piṭakānyadhītāni dharmeṇa parṣat saṃgṛhītā | [Divyāv, 18 492.1]
sa ca sumatirmāṇavaścyutaḥ kālagatastuṣite devanikāye upapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 493.1]
matirmāṇavaścyutaḥ kālagato narakeṣūpapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 494.1]
bhagavānāha yo 'sau vāsavo rājābhūt tena kālena tena samayena sa rājā bimbisāraḥ | [Divyāv, 18 495.1]
yāni tānyaśītiramātyasahasrāṇi tena kālena tena samayena tānyetarhyaśītirdevatāsahasrāṇi | [Divyāv, 18 496.1]
yo 'sau dīpāvatīyako janakāyaḥ yāsau dārikā eṣaiva sā yaśodharā | [Divyāv, 18 497.1]
yo 'sau sumatir ahameva tasmin samaye bodhisattvacaryāyāṃ vartāmi | [Divyāv, 18 498.1]
yo 'sau matiḥ eṣa eva sa dharmaruciḥ | [Divyāv, 18 499.1]
etaddvitīye 'saṃkhyeye asya ca dharmarucermama ca darśanam yadahaṃ saṃdhāya kathayāmi cirasya dharmaruce sucirasya dharmaruce | [Divyāv, 18 500.1]
tasmādapyarvāk tṛtīye 'saṃkhyeye krakucchando nāma samyaksambuddho loka utpanno vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devamanuṣyāṇāṃ buddho bhagavān | [Divyāv, 18 501.1]
tasyāṃ ca rājadhānyāmanyataro mahāśreṣṭhī prativasati | [Divyāv, 18 502.1]
tena ca sadṛśāt kulāt kalatramānītam | [Divyāv, 18 503.1]
sa ca kalatrasahāyaḥ krīḍati ramate paricārayati | [Divyāv, 18 504.1]
tasya krīḍato ramamāṇasya paricārayataḥ putro jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 505.1]
sa ca gṛhapatiḥ śrāddhaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 506.1]
tasya cārhan bhikṣuḥ kulāvavādako 'sti | [Divyāv, 18 507.1]
sa ca gṛhapatistāṃ patnīmevamāha jāto 'smākam ṛṇadharo dhanaharaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 508.1]
gacchāmyahamidānīṃ bhadre vaṇigdharmāṇāṃ deśāntaraṃ bhāṇḍamādāya | [Divyāv, 18 509.1]
sa ca vaṇiglokenāvṛto dūrataraṃ gato bhāṇḍamādāya | [Divyāv, 18 510.1]
yato 'sya na bhūyaściramapyāgacchati | [Divyāv, 18 511.1]
sa ca dārakaḥ kālāntareṇa mahān saṃvṛtto 'bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 512.1]
tato 'sau mātaraṃ pṛcchaty amba kimasmākaṃ kulārthāgataṃ karma sā kathayati vatsa pitā tava āpaṇaṃ vāhayannāsīt | [Divyāv, 18 513.1]
tataḥ sa dāraka āpaṇamārabdho vāhayitum | [Divyāv, 18 514.1]
sā ca mātā asya kleśairbādhyamānā cintayituṃ pravṛttā ka upāyaḥ syāt yadahaṃ kleśān vinodayeyaṃ na ca me kaścijjānīyāt tayā saṃcintyaivamadhyavasitam evameva putrakāmahetostathā paricarāmi yathā anenaiva me sārdhaṃ rogavinodakaṃ bhavati naiva svajanasya śaṅkā bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 515.1]
tatastayā vṛddhayuvatī āhūya bhojayitvā dvis triḥ paścānnavena paṭenācchāditā | [Divyāv, 18 516.1]
tasyāḥ sā vṛddhā kathayati kena kāryeṇaiva mamānupradānādinā upakrameṇānupravṛttiṃ karoṣi sā tasyā vṛddhāyā viśvastā bhūtvā evamāha amba śṛṇu vijñāpyam | [Divyāv, 18 517.1]
kleśairatīva bādhye priyatāṃ mamotpādya manuṣyānveṣaṇaṃ kuru yo 'bhyantara eva syānna ca śaṅkanīyo janasya | [Divyāv, 18 518.1]
vṛddhā kathayati neha gṛhe tathāvidho manuṣyaḥ saṃvidyate nāpi praṇayavān kaścit praviśati yo janasyāśaṅkanīyo bhavet | [Divyāv, 18 519.1]
katamaḥ sa manuṣyo bhaviṣyati yasyāhaṃ vakṣyāmi tataḥ sā vaṇikpatnī tasyā vṛddhāyāḥ kathayati yadyanyo manuṣya evaṃvidhopakramayukto nāsty eṣa eva me putro bhavati naiṣa lokasya śaṅkanīyo bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 520.1]
tasyāstayā vṛddhayā abhihitaṃ kathaṃ nu putreṇa sārdhaṃ ratikrīḍāṃ gamiṣyasi yuktaṃ syādanyena manuṣyeṇa sārdhaṃ ratikrīḍāmanubhavitum | [Divyāv, 18 521.1]
tataḥ sā vaṇikpatnī kathayati yadyanyo 'bhyantaro manuṣyo na saṃvidyate bhavatu eṣa eva me putraḥ | [Divyāv, 18 522.1]
tayā vṛddhayā abhihitaṃ yathepsitaṃ kuru | [Divyāv, 18 523.1]
tataḥ sā vṛddhayuvatī tasya vaṇijaḥ putrasyaivāgamya pṛcchati vatsa taruṇo 'si rūpavāṃśca | [Divyāv, 18 524.1]
kiṃ pratiṣṭhito 'syārthena tena tasyā abhihitaṃ kimetat tataḥ sā vṛddhā kathayati bhavānevamabhirūpaśca yuvā ca asmin vayasi taruṇayuvatyā sārdhaṃ śobhethāḥ krīḍan raman paricārayan kimeva kāmabhogaparihīnastiṣṭhasi vaṇigdārakastaṃ śrutvā lajjāvyapatrāpyasaṃlīnacetāstasyā vṛddhāyāstadvacanaṃ nādhivāsayati | [Divyāv, 18 525.1]
tataḥ sā vṛddhā evaṃ dvirapi trirapi tasya dārakasya kathayati taruṇayuvatistavārthe kleśairbādhyate | [Divyāv, 18 526.1]
sa vaṇigdārako dvirapi trirapyucyamānastasyā vṛddhāyāḥ kathayaty amba kiṃ tasyāstaruṇayuvatyāḥ sannimitte kiṃcidabhihitaṃ tataḥ sā vṛddhā kathayaty uktaṃ tasyā mayā tannimittam | [Divyāv, 18 527.1]
tayā mama nimitte na pratijñātam | [Divyāv, 18 528.1]
sā ca dārikā hrīvyapatrāpyagṛhītā na kiṃcidvakṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 529.1]
na ca śarīramāvṛtaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 530.1]
na tvayā tasyā vānveṣaṇe yatnaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 531.1]
tatastena vaṇigdārakeṇa tasyā vṛddhāyā abhihitaṃ kutrāsmākaṃ saṃgataṃ bhaviṣyati tayā abhihitaṃ madīye gṛhe | [Divyāv, 18 532.1]
tenoktaṃ kutrāvakāśe tava gṛhaṃ tato 'sya tayā vṛddhayā gṛhaṃ vyapadiṣṭam | [Divyāv, 18 533.1]
sā ca vṛddhā tasyā vaṇikpatnyāḥ sakāśaṃ gatvā kathayati icchāpitaḥ sa vo 'yaṃ dārakaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 534.1]
sā kathayati kutrāvakāśe saṃgataṃ bhaviṣyati madīye gṛhe | [Divyāv, 18 535.1]
sa ca dārakaḥ kāryāṇi kṛtvā gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 536.1]
anupūrveṇa bhuktvā tasyā mātuḥ kathayati gacchāmyaham | [Divyāv, 18 537.1]
vayasyagṛhe svapsye | [Divyāv, 18 538.1]
tato 'sya mātrāpyanujñātaṃ gaccha | [Divyāv, 18 539.1]
sa dārako labdhānujñastasyā vṛddhāyā gṛhaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 540.1]
tasya dārakasya tasmin gṛhe gatasya ratikrīḍākālamāgamayamānasya tiṣṭhato niśi kālamapratyabhijñātam | [Divyāv, 18 541.1]
rūpe kāle sā mātā asya vaṇigdārakasya tasminneva gṛhe ratikrīḍāmanubhavanārthaṃ tatraiva gatā | [Divyāv, 18 542.1]
gatvā ca tasmin gṛhe vikālam avyaktiṃ vibhāvyamāne rūpākṛtau nirgūḍhenopacārakrameṇa ratikrīḍāṃ putreṇa sārdhamanubhavituṃ pravṛttā pāpakenāsaddharmeṇa | [Divyāv, 18 543.1]
sā ca parikṣīṇāyāṃ rātrau anubhūtaratikrīḍā satamo'ndhakāre kālāyāmeva rajanyām avibhāvyamānarūpākṛtau svagṛhaṃ gacchati | [Divyāv, 18 544.1]
sa cāpi vaṇigdārako ratikrīḍāmanubhūya prabhātāyāṃ rajanyāṃ bhāṇḍāvāriṃ gatvā kuṭumbakāryāṇi karoti | [Divyāv, 18 545.1]
evaṃ dvirapi trirapi | [Divyāv, 18 546.1]
tatra vṛddhāyā gṛhe ratikrīḍāmanubhavaṃśca cirakālamevaṃ vartamānena ratikrīḍākrameṇa tasya dārakasya sā mātā cintayituṃ pravṛttā kiyatkālam anyadgṛham ahamevam avibhāvyamānarūpā ratikrīḍāmanubhaviṣyāmi yannvahamasyaitat ratikrīḍākramaṃ tathāvidhaṃ krameṇa saṃvedayeyaṃ yathā ihaiva gṛhe ratikrīḍā bhavet | [Divyāv, 18 547.1]
iti saṃcintya tatraiva vṛddhāgṛhe gatvā ratikrīḍāṃ putreṇa sārdhamanubhūya rajanyāḥ kṣaye satamo'ndhakārakāle tasya dārakasyoparimaṃ prāvaraṇaṃ nivasyātmanīyāṃ ca śirottarapaṭṭikāṃ tyaktvā svagṛhaṃ gatā | [Divyāv, 18 548.1]
sa ca dārakaḥ prabhātakāle tāṃ paṭṭikāṃ śirasi mañcasyāvatiṣṭhantīṃ saṃpaśyati | [Divyāv, 18 549.1]
ātmīyāmevopariprāvaraṇapotrīm alabhamānastatraiva tāṃ paṭṭikāṃ saṃlakṣya tyaktvā bhāṇḍāvārīṃ gatvā yugalamanyaṃ prāvṛtya svagṛhaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 550.1]
tatra ca gataḥ saṃpaśyati tamevātmīyaṃ prāvaraṇaṃ tasyā mātuḥ śirasi prāvṛtam | [Divyāv, 18 551.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca tāṃ mātaraṃ pṛcchaty amba kuto 'yaṃ śirasi prāvaraṇo 'bhyāgato yatastayā abhihitam adyāpyahaṃ tavāmbā evaṃ cirakālaṃ tava mayā sārdhaṃ kāmān paribhuñjato 'dyāpyahaṃ tava saivāmbā yataḥ sa vaṇigdārakastathāvidhaṃ mātṛvacanamupaśrutya saṃmūḍho vihvalacetā bhūmau nipatitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 552.1]
tatastayā sa mātrā ghaṭajalapariṣekeṇāvasiktaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 553.1]
sa jalapariṣekāvasikto dārakaścireṇa kālena pratyāgataprāṇastayā mātrā samāśvāsyate kimevaṃ khedamupāgatastvam asmadīyaṃ vacanamupaśrutya dhīramanā bhavasva | [Divyāv, 18 554.1]
na te viṣādaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 555.1]
sa dārakastasyāḥ kathayati kathamahaṃ khedaṃ na kariṣyāmi saṃmohaṃ vā yena mayā evaṃvidhaṃ pāpakaṃ karma kṛtaṃ tataḥ sa tayābhihito na te manaḥśūkam asminnarthe utpādayitavyam | [Divyāv, 18 556.1]
panthāsamo mātṛgrāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 557.1]
yenaivaṃ hi yathā pitā gacchati putro 'pi tenaiva gacchati | [Divyāv, 18 558.1]
na cāsau panthā putrasyānugacchato doṣakārako bhavaty evameva mātṛgrāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 559.1]
tīrthasamo 'pi ca mātṛgrāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 560.1]
yatraiva hi tīrthe pitā snāti putro 'pi tasmin snāti na ca tīrthaṃ putrasya snāyato doṣakārakaṃ bhavati | [Divyāv, 18 561.1]
evameva mātṛgrāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 562.1]
api ca pratyanteṣu janapadeṣu dharmataivaiṣā yasyāmeva pitā asaddharmeṇābhigacchati tāmeva putro 'pyadhigacchati | [Divyāv, 18 563.1]
evamasau vaṇigdārako mātrā bahuvidhairanunayavacanairvinītaśokastayā mātrā tasmin pātake 'saddharme punaḥ punaratīva saṃjātarāgaḥ pravṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 564.1]
tena ca śreṣṭhinā gṛhe lekhyo 'nupreṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 565.1]
bhadre dhīrorjitamahotsāhā bhavasva | [Divyāv, 18 566.1]
ahamapi lekhānupadamevāgamiṣye | [Divyāv, 18 567.1]
sā vaṇikpatnī tathāvidhaṃ lekhārthaṃ śrutvā vaimanasyajātā cintayituṃ pravṛttā mahāntaṃ kālaṃ mama tasyāgamanamudīkṣamāṇāyāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 568.1]
tadā nāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 569.1]
idānīṃ mayā evaṃvidhenopakrameṇa putraṃ ca paricaritvā sa cāgamiṣyati | [Divyāv, 18 570.1]
ka upāyaḥ syāt yadahaṃ tamihāsamprāptameva jīvitāt vyaparopayeyam iti saṃcintya taṃ putramāhūya kathayati pitrā te lekhyo 'nupreṣita āgamiṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 18 571.1]
jānase 'smābhiridānīṃ kiṃ karaṇīyamiti gacchasva pitaramasamprāptameva ghātaya | [Divyāv, 18 572.1]
sa kathayati kathamahaṃ pitaraṃ ghātayiṣye yadā asau na prasahate pitṛvadhaṃ kartum tadā tayā mātrā bhūyo 'nuvṛttivacanairabhihitas tasyānuvṛttivacanairucyamānasya kāmeṣu saṃraktasyādhyavasāyo jātaḥ pitṛvadhaṃ prati | [Divyāv, 18 573.1]
kāmān khalu pratisevato na hi kiṃcit pāpakaṃ karmākaraṇīyamiti vadāmi | [Divyāv, 18 574.1]
tatastenoktaṃ kenopāyena ghātayāmi tayā abhihitam ahamevopāyaṃ saṃvidhāsye | [Divyāv, 18 575.1]
ityuktvā viṣamādāya samitāyāṃ miśrayitvā maṇḍilakān paktvā anye 'pi ca nirviṣāḥ paktāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 576.1]
yatastaṃ dārakamāhūya kathayati gacchasva | [Divyāv, 18 577.1]
amī saviṣā maṇḍilakā nirviṣāśca | [Divyāv, 18 578.1]
gṛhya pitṛsakāśaṃ gatvā ca tasya viśvastasyaikatra bhuñjata etān saviṣān maṇḍilakān prayacchasva ātmanā ca nirviṣān bhakṣaya | [Divyāv, 18 579.1]
tataḥ sa dārakastena lekhavāhikamanuṣyeṇa sārdhaṃ tān maṇḍilakān gṛhya gataḥ pitṛsakāśam | [Divyāv, 18 580.1]
āgamya pitā asya atīva taṃ putraṃ dṛṣṭvā abhirūpaprāsādikaṃ maheśākhyaṃ prāmodyaṃ prāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 581.1]
sahyāsahyaṃ pṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ teṣāṃ vaṇijāmākhyāty ayaṃ bhavanto 'smākaṃ putraḥ | [Divyāv, 18 582.1]
yadā tena dārakeṇa saṃlakṣitaṃ sarvatra ahamanena pitrā pratisaṃvedita iti tatastaṃ pitaramāha tāta ambayā maṇḍilakāḥ praheṇakamanupreṣitam | [Divyāv, 18 583.1]
tattātaḥ paribhuñjatu | [Divyāv, 18 584.1]
paścāttena pitrā sārdhamekaphalāyāṃ bhuñjatā tasya pituḥ saviṣā maṇḍilakā dattāḥ ātmanā nirviṣāḥ prabhakṣitāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 585.1]
yato 'sya pitā tān saviṣān maṇḍilakān bhakṣayitvā mṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 586.1]
tasya ca pituḥ kāladharmaṇā yuktasya ca dārako na kenacit pāpakaṃ karma kurvāṇo 'bhiśaṅkito vā pratisaṃvedito vā | [Divyāv, 18 587.1]
paścāttairiṣṭasnigdhasuhṛdbhirvaṇigbhiḥ śocayitvā yattattu kiṃcittasya vaṇijo bhāṇḍamāsīddhiraṇyasuvarṇaṃ vā tattasya dārakasya dattam | [Divyāv, 18 588.1]
sa dārakastaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ hiraṇyasuvarṇaṃ paitṛkaṃ gṛhya svagṛhamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 589.1]
tasya ca gatasya svagṛhaṃ sā mātā pracchannāsaddharmeṇa taṃ putraṃ paricaramāṇā ratiṃ nādhigacchaty anabhiratarūpā ca taṃ putraṃ vadati kiyatkālaṃ vayamevaṃ pracchannena krameṇa ratikrīḍāmanubhaviṣyāmo yannu vayamasmāddeśādanyadeśāntaraṃ gatvā prakāśakrameṇa niḥśaṅkā bhūtvā jāyāpatīti vikhyātadharmāṇaḥ sukhaṃ prativasema | [Divyāv, 18 590.1]
tatastau gṛhaṃ tyaktvā mitrasvajanasambandhivargānapahāya purāṇadāsīdāsakarmakarāṃstyaktvā yāvadarthajātaṃ hiraṇyasuvarṇaṃ ca gṛhya anyaviṣayāntaraṃ gatau | [Divyāv, 18 591.1]
tatra gatvā janapadeṣu vikhyāpayamānau jāyāṃpatikamiti ratikrīḍāmanubhavamānau vyavasthitau | [Divyāv, 18 592.1]
yāvadarhan bhikṣuḥ kenacit kālāntareṇa janapadacārikāṃ caraṃs tamadhiṣṭhānamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 593.1]
tena tatra piṇḍapātamanvāhiṇḍatā vīthyāṃ niṣadyāyaṃ vaṇigdharmaṇā saṃvyavahāramāṇaḥ sa dārako dṛṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 594.1]
dṛṣṭvā cārogyayitvā cābhibhāṣyokto mātuste kuśalam sa ca dārakastamarhantaṃ tathā abhivadamānamupaśrutya saṃbhinnacetāḥ svena duścaritena karmaṇā śaṅkitamanāścintayituṃ pravṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 595.1]
sa vicintya mātṛsakāśaṃ gatvā saṃvedayati yatirabhyāgato yo 'sau asmadgṛhamupasaṃkrāmaty eṣa sa ihādhiṣṭhāne pratisaṃvedayiṣyati eṣā asya dārakasya māteti | [Divyāv, 18 596.1]
vayaṃ ceha jāyāṃpatikamiti khyātau | [Divyāv, 18 597.1]
kathameṣa śakyaṃ ghātayituṃ tatastayoḥ saṃcintya taṃ gṛhamenamupanimantrayitvā bhuñjānaṃ ghātayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 598.1]
tatastayorevaṃ saṃcintya so 'rhan bhikṣurantargṛhamupanimantrayitvā bhojayitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 599.1]
sa dārako gūḍhaśastro bhūtvā arhantaṃ bhojayituṃ mātrā saha nirjanaṃ gṛhaṃ kṛtvā sa cārhadbhikṣurbhuktvā tasmādgṛhādviśrabdhacārakrameṇa pratinirgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 600.1]
tatastena dārakeṇainaṃ antargṛhaviśrabdhacārakramam avekṣya nirgacchantaṃ parāpṛṣṭhībhūtvā śarīre 'sya śastraṃ nipātya jīvitād vyaparopayati | [Divyāv, 18 601.1]
kāmāśca lavaṇodakasadṛśāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 602.1]
yathā yathā sevyanti tathā tathā tṛṣṇāvṛddhimupayānti | [Divyāv, 18 603.1]
tasya dārakasya sā mātā taṃ putramasaddharmeṇānuvartamānā tasminnevādhiṣṭhāne śreṣṭhiputreṇa sārdhaṃ pracchannakāmā asaddharmeṣu saktacittā jātā | [Divyāv, 18 604.1]
tasya dārakasya tathāvidha upakramaḥ pratisaṃviditaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 605.1]
tatastena tasya māturuktam amba nivartasvedṛśāddoṣāt | [Divyāv, 18 606.1]
sā ca tasmiñ śreṣṭhiputre saṃraktacittā dvirapi trirapyucyamānā na nirvartate | [Divyāv, 18 607.1]
tatastena niṣkoṣamasiṃ kṛtvā sā mātā jīvitādvyaparopitā | [Divyāv, 18 608.1]
yadā tasya trīṇyānantaryāṇi paripūrṇāni tadā devatābhirjanapadeṣvārocitaṃ pāpa eṣa pitṛghātako 'rhadghātako mātṛghātakaśca | [Divyāv, 18 609.1]
trīṇyanenānantaryāṇi narakakarmasaṃvartanīyāni karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni | [Divyāv, 18 610.1]
tatastenādhiṣṭhānajanena tacchrutvā tadadhiṣṭhānānnirvāsitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 611.1]
sa yadā nirvāsitastasmādadhiṣṭhānāt tadā cintayituṃ pravṛtto 'sti cāsya buddhaśāsane kaścidevānunaya evaṃ manasi kṛtaṃ gacchāmi idānīṃ pravrajāmīti | [Divyāv, 18 612.1]
sa ca vihāraṃ gatvā bhikṣusakāśamupasaṃkramya evaṃ kathayaty ārya pravrajeyam | [Divyāv, 18 613.1]
tatastena bhikṣuṇā uktaṃ mā tāvat pitṛghātako 'si tena bhikṣurabhihito 'sti mayā ghātitaḥ pitā | [Divyāv, 18 614.1]
tataḥ punaḥ pṛṣṭo mā tāvanmātṛghātako 'si tenoktam ārya ghātitā mayā mātā | [Divyāv, 18 615.1]
sa bhūyaḥ pṛṣṭo mā tāvadarhadvadhaste kṛtas tataḥ sa kathayaty arhannapi ghātitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 616.1]
tatastena bhikṣuṇābhihita ekaikena eṣāṃ karmaṇāmācaraṇānna pravrajyārho bhavasi prāgeva samastānām | [Divyāv, 18 617.1]
gaccha vatsa nāhaṃ pravrājayiṣye | [Divyāv, 18 618.1]
tataḥ sa puruṣo 'nyasya bhikṣoḥ sakāśamupasaṃkramya kathayaty ārya pravrajeyam | [Divyāv, 18 619.1]
tatastenāpi bhikṣuṇā anupūrveṇa pṛṣṭvā pratyākhyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 620.1]
tataḥ paścādanyasya bhikṣoḥ sakāśaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 621.1]
tamapi tathaiva pravrajyāmāyācate | [Divyāv, 18 622.1]
tenāpi tathā anupūrvakrameṇa pṛṣṭvā pratyākhyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 623.1]
sa yadā dvirapi trirapi pravrajyāmāyācamāno 'pi bhikṣubhir na pravrājitas tadā amarṣajātaścintayituṃ pravṛtto yā api sarvasādhāraṇā pravrajyā tāmahamapyāyācanna labhāmi | [Divyāv, 18 624.1]
tatastena tasmin vihāre śayitānāṃ bhikṣūṇāmagnirdattaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 625.1]
tasmin vihāre 'gniṃ dattvā anyatra vihāraṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 626.1]
tatrāpi gatvā bhikṣūṇāmupasaṃkramya pravrajyāmāyācate | [Divyāv, 18 627.1]
tairapi tathaivānupūrveṇa pṛṣṭvā pratyākhyātaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 628.1]
tatrāpi tena tathaiva pratihatacetasā agnirdattaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 629.1]
tatrāpi vihāre bahavo bhikṣavaḥ śaikṣāśaikṣāśca dagdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 630.1]
evaṃ tasyānekān vihārān dahataḥ sarvatra śabdo visṛta evaṃvidhaścaivaṃvidhaśca pāpakarmakārī puruṣo bhikṣubhyaḥ pravrajyāmalabhan vihārān bhikṣūṃśca dahatīti | [Divyāv, 18 631.1]
sa ca puruṣo 'nyavihāraṃ prasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 632.1]
tatra ca vihāre bodhisattvajātīyo bhikṣuḥ prativasati tṛpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 633.1]
tena śrutaṃ sa evaṃ duṣkarakarmakārī puruṣa ihāgacchatīti | [Divyāv, 18 634.1]
yataḥ sa bhikṣustasya puruṣasyāsamprāptasyaiva tasmin vihāre pratyudgataḥ | [Divyāv, 18 635.1]
sa taṃ puruṣaṃ sametya kathayati bhadramukha kimetad yato 'sya puruṣeṇoktam ārya pravrajyāṃ na labhāmi | [Divyāv, 18 636.1]
tatastena bhikṣuṇoktam āgaccha vatsa ahaṃ te pravrājayāmīti | [Divyāv, 18 637.1]
paścāt tena bhikṣuṇā tasya puruṣasya śiro muṇḍāpayitvā kāṣāyāṇi vastrāṇi dattāni | [Divyāv, 18 638.1]
paścāt sa puruṣaḥ kathayaty ārya śikṣāpadāni me 'nuprayaccha | [Divyāv, 18 639.1]
tatastena bhikṣuṇā uktaḥ kiṃ te śikṣāpadaiḥ prayojanam evaṃ sarvakālaṃ vadasva namo buddhāya namo dharmāya namaḥ saṃghāyeti | [Divyāv, 18 640.1]
paścāt sa bhikṣustasya puruṣasya dharmadeśanāmārabdhaḥ kartum tvamevaṃvidhaścaivaṃvidhaśca pāpakarmakārī sattvo yadi kadācidbuddhaśabdaṃ śṛṇoṣi smṛtiṃ pratilabhethāḥ | [Divyāv, 18 641.1]
athāsau tripiṭo bhikṣuścyutaḥ kālagato deveṣūpapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 642.1]
sa cāpi puruṣaścyutaḥ kālagato narakeṣūpapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 18 643.1]
yato bhagavānāha kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau atīte 'dhvani bhikṣus tripiṭa āsa ahameva sa tena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 18 644.1]
yo 'sau pāpakarmakārī sattvo mātāpitrarhadghātakaḥ eṣa eva dharmaruciḥ | [Divyāv, 18 645.1]
idaṃ mama tṛtīye 'saṃkhyeye 'sya dharmarucerdarśanam | [Divyāv, 18 646.1]
tadahaṃ saṃdhāya kathayāmi cirasya dharmaruce sucirasya dharmaruce suciracirasya dharmaruce | [Divyāv, 18 647.1]
yāvacca mayā bhikṣavastribhirasaṃkhyeyaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ pāramitābhiranyaiśca duṣkaraśatasahasrairanuttarā samyaksambodhiḥ samudānītā tāvadanena dharmarucinā yadbhūyasā narakatiryakṣu kṣapitam | [Divyāv, 18 648.1]
idamavocadbhagavān āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 18 649.1]
{Divyāv, 19}
buddho bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati veṇuvane kalandakanivāpe | [Divyāv, 19 1.1]
rājagṛhe nagare subhadro nāma gṛhapatiḥ prativasati āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 2.1]
so 'tyarthaṃ nirgrantheṣvabhiprasannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 3.1]
tena sadṛśāt kulāt kalatramānītam | [Divyāv, 19 4.1]
sa tayā sārdhaṃ krīḍati ramate paricārayati | [Divyāv, 19 5.1]
tasya krīḍato ramamāṇasya paricārayataḥ kālāntareṇa kālāntareṇa patnī āpannasattvā saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 19 6.1]
bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya rājagṛhaṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat | [Divyāv, 19 7.1]
rājagṛhaṃ piṇḍāya caran yena subhadrasya gṛhapater niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 8.1]
adrākṣīt subhadro gṛhapatirbhagavantaṃ dūrādeva | [Divyāv, 19 9.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ patnīmādāya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 10.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavantamidamavocad bhagavan iyaṃ me patnī āpannasattvā saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 19 11.1]
kiṃ janayiṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 12.1]
bhagavānāha gṛhapate putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 13.1]
tena bhagavataḥ śucinaḥ praṇītasya khādanīyabhojanīyasya pātrapūro dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 14.1]
bhagavānārogya ityuktvā piṇḍapātamādāya prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 15.1]
tasya nātidūre bhūrikastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 19 16.1]
sa saṃlakṣayati yadapyasmākamekaṃ bhaikṣākulam tadapi śramaṇo gautamo 'nvāvartayati | [Divyāv, 19 17.1]
gacchāmi paśyāmi kiṃ śramaṇena gautamena vyākṛtamiti | [Divyāv, 19 18.1]
sa tatra gatvā kathayati gṛhapate śramaṇo gautama āgata āsīt āgataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 19.1]
kiṃ tena vyākṛtam ārya mayā tasya patnī darśitā kiṃ janayiṣyati sa kathayati putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 20.1]
sa bhūriko gaṇitre kṛtāvī śvetavarṇāṃ gṛhītvā gaṇayitumārabdhaḥ paśyati yathā bhagavatā vyākṛtaṃ tatsarvaṃ tathaiva | [Divyāv, 19 21.1]
sa saṃlakṣayati yadi anusaṃvarṇayiṣyāmyahaṃ gṛhapatirbhūyasyā mātrayā śramaṇasya gautamasyābhipraśaṃsyati | [Divyāv, 19 22.1]
tadatra kiṃcid saṃvarṇayitavyaṃ kiṃcit vivarṇayitavyamiti viditvā hastau saṃparivartayati mukhaṃ ca vibhaṇḍayati | [Divyāv, 19 23.1]
subhadro gṛhapatiḥ kathayati ārya kiṃ hastau saṃparivartayasi mukhaṃ ca vibhaṇḍayasīti sa kathayati gṛhapate atra kiṃcit satyaṃ kiṃcinmṛṣā | [Divyāv, 19 24.1]
ārya kiṃ satyaṃ kiṃ vā mṛṣā gṛhapate yadanenoktaṃ putraṃ janayiṣyatīti idaṃ satyaṃ kathayati | [Divyāv, 19 25.1]
kulamuddyotayiṣyatītīdamapi satyam | [Divyāv, 19 26.1]
agrajyotiriti saṃjñā | [Divyāv, 19 27.1]
mandabhāgyaḥ sa sattvo jātamātra evāgninā kulaṃ dhakṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 28.1]
yat kathayati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyatīti idaṃ mṛṣā | [Divyāv, 19 29.1]
gehapate asti kaścit tvayā dṛṣṭo manuṣyabhūto divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhavan yatkathayati mama śāsane pravrajiṣyatīti idaṃ satyam | [Divyāv, 19 30.1]
yadā asya na bhaktaṃ na vastram tadā niścayena śramaṇasya gautamasyāntike pravrajiṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 31.1]
sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyatīti idaṃ mṛṣā | [Divyāv, 19 32.1]
śramaṇasyaiva tāvadgautamasya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ nāsti prāgevāsya bhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 33.1]
subhadro viṣādamāpannaḥ kathayati ārya atra mayā kathaṃ pratipattavyamiti bhūrikaḥ kathayati gṛhapate vayaṃ pravrajitāḥ śamānuśikṣāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 34.1]
tvameva jānīṣe | [Divyāv, 19 35.1]
ityuktvā prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 36.1]
subhadraḥ saṃlakṣayati sarvathā parityājyo 'sau iti viditvā sa bhaiṣajyaṃ dātumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 37.1]
caramabhaviko 'sau sattvaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 38.1]
tadasya bhaiṣajyārthāya syāditi | [Divyāv, 19 39.1]
sa tasyā vāmakukṣiṃ marditumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 40.1]
sa garbho dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣiṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 41.1]
subhadro dakṣiṇakukṣiṃ marditumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 42.1]
sa vāmaṃ kukṣiṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 43.1]
asthānametadanavakāśo yaccaramabhavikaḥ sattvo 'ntarāducchidya kālaṃ kariṣyati aprāpte āśravakṣaye | [Divyāv, 19 44.1]
sā gṛhapatipatnī kukṣiṇā mṛdyamānena vikroṣṭumārabdhā | [Divyāv, 19 45.1]
prātiveśyaiḥ śrutam | [Divyāv, 19 46.1]
te tvaritatvaritaṃ gatāḥ pṛcchanti bhavantaḥ kimiyaṃ gṛhapatipatnī virauti subhadraḥ kathayati kukṣimatyeṣā | [Divyāv, 19 47.1]
nūnamasyāḥ prasavakāla iti | [Divyāv, 19 48.1]
te prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 49.1]
subhadraḥ saṃlakṣayati na śakyamasyā atropasaṃkramaṃ kartum | [Divyāv, 19 50.1]
araṇyaṃ nayāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 51.1]
sā tenāraṇyaṃ nītvā tathopakrāntā yathā kālagatā | [Divyāv, 19 52.1]
sa tāṃ pracchannaṃ gṛhamānīya suhṛtsambandhibāndhavānāṃ prātiveśakānāṃ ca kathayati bhavantaḥ patnī me kālagateti | [Divyāv, 19 53.1]
te vikroṣṭumārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 54.1]
sā tairvikrośadbhir nīlapītalohitāvadātairvastraiḥ śibikāmalaṃkṛtya śītavanaṃ śmaśānamabhinirhṛtā | [Divyāv, 19 55.1]
nirgranthaiḥ śrutaṃ te hṛṣṭatuṣṭapramuditāśchatrapatākā ucchrayitvā rājagṛhasya nagarasya rathyāvīthīcatvaraśṛṅgāṭake upāhiṇḍamānā ārocayanti śṛṇvantu bhavantaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 56.1]
śramaṇena gautamena subhadrasya gṛhapateḥ patnī vyākṛtā putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 57.1]
sā ca kālagatā śītavanaśmaśānamabhinirhṛtā | [Divyāv, 19 58.1]
yasya tāvadvṛkṣamūlameva nāsti kutastasya śākhāpatraphalaṃ bhaviṣyatīti atrāntare nāsti kiṃcidbuddhānāṃ bhagavatāmajñātamadṛṣṭamaviditamavijñātam | [Divyāv, 19 59.1]
dharmatā khalu buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ mahākāruṇikānāṃ lokānugrahapravṛttānām ekārakṣāṇāṃ śamathavipaśyanāvihāriṇāṃ tridamathavastukuśalānāṃ caturoghottīrṇānām ṛddhipādacaraṇatalasupratiṣṭhitānāṃ caturṣu saṃgrahavastuṣu dīrgharātrakṛtaparicayānāṃ caturvaiśāradyaviśāradānāṃ pañcāṅgaviprahīṇānāṃ pañcagatisamatikrāntānāṃ ṣaḍaṅgasamanvāgatānāṃ ṣaṭpāramitāparipūrṇānām asaṃhatavihāriṇāṃ saptabodhyaṅgakusumāḍhyānām aṣṭāṅgamārgadeśikānāṃ navānupūrvavihārasamāpattikuśalānāṃ daśabalabalināṃ daśadiksamāpūrṇayaśasāṃ daśaśatavaśavartiprativiśiṣṭānāṃ trī rātres trirdivasasya buddhacakṣuṣā lokaṃ vyavalokya jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate ko hīyate ko vardhate kaḥ kṛcchraprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃkaṭaprāptaḥ kaḥ saṃbādhaprāptaḥ kaḥ kṛcchrasaṃkaṭasambādhaprāptaḥ ko 'pāyanimnaḥ ko 'pāyapravaṇaḥ ko 'pāyaprāgbhāraḥ kamahamapāyāduddhṛtya svarge mokṣe ca pratiṣṭhāpayeyaṃ kasyānavaropitāni kuśalamūlānyavaropayeyaṃ kasyāvaropitāni paripācayeyam kasya paripakvāni vimocayeyam | [Divyāv, 19 60.1]
āha ca | [Divyāv, 19 61.1]
apyevātikramedvelāṃ sāgaro makarālayaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 61.2]
na tu vaineyavatsānāṃ buddho velāmatikramet | [Divyāv, 19 61.3]
atha bhagavānanyatarasmin pradeśe smitamakārṣīt | [Divyāv, 19 62.1]
dharmatā khalu yasmin samaye buddhā bhagavantaḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti tasmin samaye nīlapītalohitāvadātā arciṣo mukhānniścārya kāścidadhastādgacchanti kāścidupariṣṭādgacchanti | [Divyāv, 19 63.1]
yā adhastādgacchanti tāḥ saṃjīvaṃ kālasūtraṃ saṃghātaṃ rauravaṃ mahārauravaṃ tapanaṃ pratāpanamavīcimarbudaṃ nirarbudamaṭaṭaṃ hahavaṃ huhavamutpalaṃ padmaṃ mahāpadmaṃ narakaṃ gatvā ye uṣṇanarakāsteṣu śītībhūtā nipatanti | [Divyāv, 19 64.1]
tena teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 65.1]
teṣāmevaṃ bhavati kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanta itaścyutāḥ āhosvidanyatropapannā iti | [Divyāv, 19 66.1]
teṣāṃ prasādasaṃjananārthaṃ bhagavān nirmitaṃ visarjayati | [Divyāv, 19 67.1]
teṣāṃ nirmitaṃ dṛṣṭvā evaṃ bhavati na hyeva vayaṃ bhavanta itaścyutāḥ nāpyanyatropapannāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 68.1]
api tvayamapūrvadarśanaḥ sattvaḥ asyānubhāvādasmākaṃ kāraṇāviśeṣāḥ pratiprasrabdhā iti | [Divyāv, 19 69.1]
te nirmite cittamabhiprasādya tannarakavedanīyaṃ karma kṣapayitvā devamanuṣyeṣu pratisaṃdhiṃ gṛhṇanti yatra satyānāṃ bhājanabhūtā bhavanti | [Divyāv, 19 70.1]
yā upariṣṭādgacchanti tāścāturmahārājakāyikān devāṃstrāyastriṃśān yāmāṃstuṣitānnirmāṇaratīn paranirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhānapramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnānanabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalānatapān sudṛśān sudarśanānakaniṣṭhān devān gatvā duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmetyudghoṣayanti | [Divyāv, 19 71.1]
gāthādvayaṃ ca bhāṣante | [Divyāv, 19 72.1]
ārabhadhvaṃ niṣkrāmata yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane | [Divyāv, 19 72.2]
dhunīta mṛtyunaḥ sainyaṃ naḍāgāramiva kuñjaraḥ | [Divyāv, 19 72.3]
yo hyasmin dharmavinaye apramattaścariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 73.1]
prahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 73.2]
atha tā arciṣastrisāhasramahāsāhasraṃ lokadhātumanvāhiṇḍya bhagavantameva pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanugacchanti | [Divyāv, 19 74.1]
bhagavata āsye 'ntarhitāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 75.1]
athāyuṣmānānandaḥ kṛtakarapuṭo bhagavantaṃ papraccha | [Divyāv, 19 76.1]
nānāvidho raṅgasahasracitro vaktrāntarānniṣkasitaḥ kalāpaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 77.1]
avabhāsitā yena diśaḥ samantāddivākareṇodayatā yathaiva | [Divyāv, 19 77.2]
gāthāśca bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 19 78.1]
vigatodbhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagatyuttamahetubhūtāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 78.2]
nākāraṇaṃ śaṅkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitamupadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 78.3]
tatkālaṃ svayamadhigamya dhīrabuddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇajinendra kāṅkṣitānām | [Divyāv, 19 79.1]
dhīrābhirmunivṛṣa vāgbhiruttamābhirutpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ | [Divyāv, 19 79.2]
nākasmāllavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitamupadarśayanti dhīrāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 80.1]
yasyārthe smitamupadarśayanti nāthāstaṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti te janaughāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 80.2]
bhagavānāha evametadānanda evametat | [Divyāv, 19 81.1]
nāhetupratyayamānanda tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksambuddhāḥ smitaṃ prāviṣkurvanti | [Divyāv, 19 82.1]
gaccha ānanda bhikṣūṇāmārocaya tathāgato bhikṣavaḥ śmaśānacārikāṃ gantukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 83.1]
yo yuṣmākamutsahate tathāgatena sārdhaṃ śmaśānacārikāṃ gantum sa cīvarakāṇi gṛhṇātu | [Divyāv, 19 84.1]
evaṃ bhadantetyāyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya bhikṣūṇāmārocayati tathāgata āyuṣmantaḥ śmaśānacārikāṃ gantukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 85.1]
yo yuṣmākamutsahate tathāgatena sārdhaṃ śmaśānacārikāṃ gantum sa cīvarakāṇi gṛhṇātu | [Divyāv, 19 86.1]
evamāyuṣmanniti te bhikṣavaḥ sarve saṃśrutya bhagavatsakāśamupagatāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 87.1]
atha bhagavān dānto dāntaparivāraḥ śāntaḥ śāntaparivāro mukto muktaparivāra āśvasta āśvastaparivāro vinīto vinītaparivāro 'rhannarhatparivāro vītarāgo vītarāgaparivāraḥ prāsādikaḥ prāsādikaparivāro vṛṣabha iva gogaṇaparivṛto gajarāja iva kalabhagaṇaparivṛtaḥ siṃha iva daṃṣṭrigaṇaparivṛto haṃsarāja iva haṃsagaṇaparivṛtaḥ suparṇīva pakṣigaṇaparivṛto vipra iva śiṣyagaṇaparivṛtaḥ suvaidya ivāturagaṇaparivṛtaḥ śūra iva yodhagaṇaparivṛto deśika ivādhvagaṇaparivṛtaḥ sārthavāha iva vaṇiggaṇaparivṛtaḥ śreṣṭhīva paurajanaparivṛtaḥ koṭṭarāja iva mantrigaṇaparivṛtaścakravartīva putrasahasraparivṛtaścandra iva nakṣatragaṇaparivṛtaḥ sūrya iva raśmisahasraparivṛto dhṛtarāṣṭra iva gandharvagaṇaparivṛto virūḍhaka iva kumbhāṇḍagaṇaparivṛto dhanada iva yakṣagaṇaparivṛto vemacitrīvāsuragaṇaparivṛtaḥ śakra iva tridaśagaṇaparivṛto brahmeva brahmakāyikaparivṛtaḥ stimita iva jalanidhiḥ sajala iva jaladharo vimada iva gajapatiḥ sudāntairindriyair asaṃkṣobhiteryāpathapracāro dvātriṃśatā mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛto 'śītyā cānuvyañjanairvirājitagātro vyāmaprabhālaṃkṛtamūrtiḥ sūryasahasrātirekaprabho jaṅgama iva ratnaparvataḥ samantato bhadrako daśabhirbalaiścaturbhirvaiśāradyaistribhirāveṇikaiḥ smṛtyupasthānairmahākaruṇayā ca samanvāgata ājñātakauṇḍinyāśvajidbāṣpamahānāmabhadrikaśāriputramaudgalyāyanakāśyapayaśaḥpūrṇaprabhṛtimahāśrāvakaiḥ parivṛto 'nyena ca mahatā bhikṣusaṃghena anekaiśca prāṇiśatasahasraiḥ śītavanaṃ mahāśmaśānaṃ samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 88.1]
aṣṭādaśānuśaṃsā buddhacārikāyāmityanekāni devatāśatasahasrāṇi bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nubaddhāni | [Divyāv, 19 89.1]
śītavanānuguṇāśca vāyavo vāyitumārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 90.1]
rājagṛhāt dvau bāladārakau brāhmaṇadārakaḥ kṣatriyadārakaśca bahir nirgatya krīḍataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 91.1]
tayoḥ kṣatriyadārako 'vagāḍhaśrāddho brāhmaṇadārako na tathā | [Divyāv, 19 92.1]
sa brāhmaṇadārakaḥ kṣatriyadārakasya kathayati vayasya bhagavatā subhadrasya gṛhapateḥ patnī vyākṛtā putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 93.1]
sā ca mṛtā kālagatā śītavanaṃ śmaśānaṃ nirhṛtā mā haiva bhagavatā bhāṣitaṃ vitathaṃ syāditi | [Divyāv, 19 94.1]
sa kṣatriyadārako gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 19 95.1]
sacandratāraṃ prapatedihāmbaraṃ mahī saśailā savanā nabho vrajet | [Divyāv, 19 96.1]
mahodadhīnāmudakaṃ kṣayaṃ vrajenmaharṣayaḥ syur na mṛṣābhidhāyinaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 96.2]
sa ca brāhmaṇadārakaḥ kathayati vayasya yadyevaṃ gacchāmaḥ śītavanaṃ mahāśmaśānaṃ paśyāmaḥ vayasya gacchāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 97.1]
tau samprasthitau | [Divyāv, 19 98.1]
bhagavāṃśca rājagṛhānnirgataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 99.1]
adrākṣīt sa kṣatriyadārako bhagavantaṃ dūrādeva | [Divyāv, 19 100.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punargāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 19 101.1]
anuddhato vigatakutūhalo muniryathā vrajatyeṣa janaughasaṃvṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 102.1]
niḥsaṃśayaṃ paragaṇavādimardano nadasyate mṛgapatinādamuttamam | [Divyāv, 19 102.2]
yathā hyamī śītavanonmukhotsukāḥ pravānti vātā himapaṅkaśītalāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 103.1]
prayānti nūnaṃ bahavo divaukaso nirīkṣituṃ śākyamunervikurvitam | [Divyāv, 19 103.2]
rājñā bimbisāreṇa śrutaṃ bhagavatā subhadrasya gṛhapateḥ patnī vyākṛtā putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 104.1]
sā ca mṛtā kālagatā śītavanaṃ śmaśānamabhinirhṛtā | [Divyāv, 19 105.1]
bhagavāṃśca saśrāvakasaṃghaḥ śītavanaṃ samprasthita iti | [Divyāv, 19 106.1]
śrutvā ca punarasyaitadabhavan na bhagavān nirarthakaṃ śītavanaṃ gacchati | [Divyāv, 19 107.1]
nūnaṃ bhagavān subhadrasya gṛhapateḥ patnīmāgamya mahadvineyakāryaṃ kartukāmo bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 108.1]
paśyāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 109.1]
so 'pyantaḥpurakumārāmātyapaurajānapadaparivṛto rājagṛhānnirgantumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 110.1]
adrākṣīt sa kṣatriyakumārako rājānaṃ māgadhaśreṇyaṃ bimbisāraṃ dūrādeva | [Divyāv, 19 111.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punargāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 19 112.1]
yathā hi śreṇyo magadhādhipo hyayaṃ viniryayau rājagṛhāt sabāndhavaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 113.1]
pravartate me hṛdi niścitā matir mahājanasyābhyudayo bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 113.2]
janakāyena bhagavantaṃ dṛṣṭvā vivaramanupradattam | [Divyāv, 19 114.1]
bhagavān smitonmukho mahājanamadhyaṃ praviṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 115.1]
nirgranthā bhagavantaṃ smitonmukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃlakṣayanti yathā śramaṇo gautamaḥ smitonmukho mahājanamadhyaṃ praviṣṭaḥ nūnamayaṃ bodhisattvo na kālagataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 116.1]
taiḥ subhadro gṛhapatirukto gṛhapate nanvayaṃ sattvo mandabhāgyo na kālagata iti | [Divyāv, 19 117.1]
sa kathayati ārya yadyevaṃ kathamatra pratipattavyamiti te kathayanti gṛhapate vayaṃ śamāttaśikṣās tvameva jñāsyasīti | [Divyāv, 19 118.1]
sa tāṃ patnīṃ citāyāmāropya dhmāpayitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 119.1]
tasyāḥ sarvaḥ kāyo dagdhaḥ sthāpayitvā kukṣisāmantakam | [Divyāv, 19 120.1]
tathāsau kukṣiḥ sphuṭitaḥ padmaṃ prādurbhūtam | [Divyāv, 19 121.1]
tasya coparipadmakarṇikāyāṃ kumāro niṣaṇṇo 'bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 122.1]
taṃ dṛṣṭvā anekāni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi paraṃ vismayamupagatāni | [Divyāv, 19 123.1]
nirgranthā nipātamadamānā na ca prabhāvāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 124.1]
tatra bhagavān subhadraṃ gṛhapatimāmantrayate gṛhapate gṛhāṇa kumāram | [Divyāv, 19 125.1]
sa nirgranthānāṃ mukhamavalokitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 126.1]
te kathayanti gṛhapate yadi prajvalitāmetāṃ citāṃ pravekṣyasi sarveṇa sarvaṃ na bhaviṣyasīti | [Divyāv, 19 127.1]
sa na pratigṛhṇāti | [Divyāv, 19 128.1]
tatra bhagavāñ jīvakaṃ kumārabhūtamāmantrayate gṛhāṇa jīvaka kumārakamiti | [Divyāv, 19 129.1]
sa saṃlakṣayati asthānamanavakāśo bhagavān māmasthāne niyokṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 130.1]
gṛhṇāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 131.1]
tena nirviśaṅkena citāṃ vigāhya gṛhītaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 132.1]
vigāhatastasya jinājñayā citāṃ pratigṛhṇataścāgnigataṃ kumārakam | [Divyāv, 19 133.1]
jinaprabhāvānmahato hutāśanaḥ kṣaṇena jāto himapaṅkaśītalaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 133.2]
tato jīvakaṃ kumārabhūtamidamavocaj jīvaka māsi kṣata upahato veti sa kathayati rājakule 'haṃ bhadanta jāto rājakule vṛddhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 134.1]
nābhijānāmi gośīrṣacandanasyāpīdṛśaṃ śaityam yadbhagavatā adhiṣṭhitāyāścitāyāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 135.1]
tatra bhagavān subhadraṃ gṛhapatimāmantrayate gṛhāṇedānīṃ gṛhapate kumāramiti | [Divyāv, 19 136.1]
sa mithyādarśanavihataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 137.1]
tathāpi na sampratipadyate | [Divyāv, 19 138.1]
nirgranthānāmeva mukhaṃ vyavalokayati | [Divyāv, 19 139.1]
te kathayanti gṛhapate ayaṃ sattvo 'tīva mandabhāgyo yo hi nāma sarvabhakṣeṇāpyagninā na dagdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 140.1]
kiṃ bahunā yadyevaṃ gṛhaṃ praveśayasi nīyatām | [Divyāv, 19 141.1]
te gṛhamutsādayad bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ ca prāṇairviyujyasa iti | [Divyāv, 19 142.1]
nāsti ātmasamaṃ premeti | [Divyāv, 19 143.1]
tenāsau na pratigṛhītaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 144.1]
tatra bhagavān rājānaṃ bimbisāramāmantrayate gṛhāṇa mahārāja kumāramiti | [Divyāv, 19 145.1]
tena sasambhrameṇa hastau prasārya gṛhītaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 146.1]
tataḥ samantato nirīkṣya kathayati bhagavan kiṃ bhavatu asya dārakasya nāmeti bhagavān āha mahārāja yasmādayaṃ dārako jyotirmadhyāllabdhastasmādbhavati dārakasya jyotiṣka iti nāmeti | [Divyāv, 19 147.1]
tasya jyotiṣka iti nāmadheyaṃ vyavasthāpitam | [Divyāv, 19 148.1]
tato bhagavatā tasya janakāyasyāśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca jñātvā tādṛśī dharmadeśanā kṛtā yāṃ śrutvā bahubhiḥ sattvaśatairmahān viśeṣo 'dhigataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 149.1]
kaiścicchrotāpattiphalaṃ sākṣātkṛtam kaiścit sakṛdāgāmiphalaṃ kaiścidanāgāmiphalaṃ kaiścit sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtaṃ kaiścidūṣmagatāni kuśalamūlānyutpāditāni kaiścinmūrdhānaḥ kaiścit mṛdumadhyāḥ kṣāntayaḥ kaiścicchrāvakabodhau cittānyutpāditāni kaiścit pratyekabodhau kaiścidanuttarāyāṃ samyaksambodhau kaiściccharaṇagamanāni kaiścicchikṣāpadāni | [Divyāv, 19 150.1]
yadbhūyasā sā parṣadbuddhanimnā dharmapravaṇā saṃghaprāgbhārā vyavasthitā | [Divyāv, 19 151.1]
jyotiṣko dārako rājñā bimbisāreṇa aṣṭābhyo dhātrībhyo 'nupradatto dvābhyām aṃsadhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ kṣīradhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ maladhātrībhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ krīḍanikābhyāṃ dhātrībhyām | [Divyāv, 19 152.1]
so 'ṣṭābhirdhātrībhir unnīyate vardhate kṣīreṇa dadhnā navanītena sarpiṣā sarpimaṇḍena anyaiścottaptottaptairupakaraṇaviśeṣaiḥ | [Divyāv, 19 153.1]
āśu vardhate hradasthamiva paṅkajam | [Divyāv, 19 154.1]
tasya mātulaḥ paṇyamādāya deśāntaraṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 155.1]
tena śrutaṃ yathā mama bhaginī sattvavatī saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 19 156.1]
sā bhagavatā vyākṛtā putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 157.1]
sa paṇyaṃ visarjayitvā pratipaṇyamādāya rājagṛhamāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 158.1]
tena śrutaṃ yathā sā asmākaṃ bhaginī kālagateti | [Divyāv, 19 159.1]
śrutvā ca punaḥ saṃlakṣayati bhagavatā asau vyākṛtā putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyāṃ mānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 160.1]
mā haiva tadbhagavato bhāṣitaṃ vitathaṃ syāt | [Divyāv, 19 161.1]
tena tiraḥprātiveśyāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ śrutaṃ mayā asmākaṃ bhaginī sattvavatī saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 19 162.1]
sā bhagavatā vyākṛtā putraṃ janayiṣyati kulamuddyotayiṣyati divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyati mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 163.1]
śrutvā vayaṃ parituṣṭāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 164.1]
sā ca śrūyate mṛtā kālagateti | [Divyāv, 19 165.1]
mā haiva bhagavato bhāṣitaṃ vitathaṃ syāditi | [Divyāv, 19 166.1]
te gāthāṃ bhāṣante | [Divyāv, 19 167.1]
sacandratāraṃ prapatedihāmbaraṃ mahī saśailā savanā nabho vrajet | [Divyāv, 19 168.1]
mahodadhīnāmudakaṃ kṣayaṃ vrajenmaharṣayaḥ syur na mṛṣābhidhāyinaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 168.2]
na bhagavato bhāṣitaṃ vitatham | [Divyāv, 19 169.1]
kathaṃ bhagavato bhāṣitaṃ vitathaṃ bhaviṣyati kiṃtu tena svāmināpi asau tathā tathā upakrāntā yathā kālagatā | [Divyāv, 19 170.1]
sa dārako maharddhiko mahānubhāvaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 171.1]
agninā na dagdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 172.1]
adyāpi rājakule saṃvardhata iti | [Divyāv, 19 173.1]
sa subhadrasya gṛhapateḥ sakāśaṃ gatvā kathayati na yuktaṃ gṛhapate tvayā kṛtam | [Divyāv, 19 174.1]
kiṃ kṛtaṃ asmākaṃ sattvavatī bhaginī tvayā nirgranthavigrāhitena tathā tathā upakrāntā yathā kālagatā | [Divyāv, 19 175.1]
sa dārako maharddhiko mahānubhāvaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 176.1]
agnināpi na dagdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 177.1]
adyāpi rājakule saṃvardhate | [Divyāv, 19 178.1]
tadgatametat | [Divyāv, 19 179.1]
yadi tāvatkumāramānayasi ityevaṃ kuśalam | [Divyāv, 19 180.1]
no cedvayaṃ tvāṃ jñātimadhyādutkṣipāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 181.1]
salokānām saṃkāraṃ pātayāmaḥ rathyāvīthīcatvaraśṛṅgāṭakeṣu cāvaraṇaṃ niścārayāmo 'smākaṃ bhaginī subhadreṇa gṛhapatinā praghātitā | [Divyāv, 19 182.1]
strīghātako 'yam | [Divyāv, 19 183.1]
na kenacidābhāṣitavyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 184.1]
rājakule ca te 'narthaṃ kārayāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 185.1]
sa śrutvā vyathitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 186.1]
yathaiṣa paribhāṣate nūnamevaṃ karomīti viditvā rājñaḥ pādayor nipatya kathayati deva mama jñātaya evaṃ paribhāṣante yadi tāvat kumāramānayasītyevaṃ kuśalaṃ no cedānayasi vayaṃ tvāṃ jñātimadhyādutkṣipāmaḥ saṃkāraṃ pātayāmo rathyāvīthīcatvaraśṛṅgāṭakeṣu cāvaraṇaṃ niścārayāmo 'smākaṃ bhaginī subhadreṇa gṛhapatinā praghātitā | [Divyāv, 19 187.1]
strīghātako 'yam | [Divyāv, 19 188.1]
na kenacidābhāṣitavyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 189.1]
rājakule ca te 'narthaṃ kārayāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 190.1]
tadarhasi jyotiṣkaṃ kumāraṃ dātumiti | [Divyāv, 19 191.1]
rājā kathayati gṛhapate na mayā tvatsakāśāt jyotiṣkaḥ kumāro gṛhītaḥ kiṃtu bhagavatā mama nyastaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 192.1]
yadi tvaṃ kumāreṇārthī bhagavatsakāśaṃ gaccheti | [Divyāv, 19 193.1]
sa bhagavatsakāśaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 194.1]
pādayor nipatya kathayati bhagavan mama jñātaya evaṃ paribhāṣante yadi tāvat kumāramānayasītyevaṃ kuśalam | [Divyāv, 19 195.1]
no cedānayasi vayaṃ tvāṃ jñātimadhyādutkṣipāmaḥ saṃkāraṃ pātayāmaḥ rathyāvīthīcatvaraśṛṅgāṭakeṣu cāvaraṇaṃ niścārayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 196.1]
asmākaṃ bhaginī subhadreṇa gṛhapatinā praghātitā | [Divyāv, 19 197.1]
strīghātako 'yam | [Divyāv, 19 198.1]
na kenacidābhāṣitavya iti | [Divyāv, 19 199.1]
rājakule cānarthaṃ kārayāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 200.1]
tadarhasi jyotiṣkaṃ kumāraṃ dāpayitumiti | [Divyāv, 19 201.1]
bhagavān saṃlakṣayati yadi subhadro jyotiṣkaṃ kumāraṃ na labhate sthānametadvidyate yaduṣṇaṃ rudhiraṃ chardayitvā kālaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 202.1]
iti viditvā āyuṣmantamānandamāmantrayate gaccha ānanda rājānaṃ bimbisāraṃ madvacanenārogyaya evaṃ ca vada anuprayaccha mahārāja subhadrasya gṛhapaterjyotiṣkaṃ kumāram | [Divyāv, 19 203.1]
yadi subhadro gṛhapatirjyotiṣkaṃ kumāraṃ na labhate sthānametadvidyate yaduṣṇaṃ śoṇitaṃ chardayitvā kālaṃ kariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 204.1]
evaṃ bhadantetyāyuṣmānānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya yena rājā bimbisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 205.1]
upasaṃkramya rājānaṃ bimbisārametadavocad bhagavāṃste mahārāja ārogyayati kathayati ca anuprayaccha mahārāja subhadrasya gṛhapaterjyotiṣkaṃ kumāram | [Divyāv, 19 206.1]
yadi subhadro gṛhapatirjyotiṣkaṃ kumāraṃ na labhate sthānametadvidyate yat subhadro gṛhapatiruṣṇaṃ śoṇitaṃ chardayitvā kālaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 207.1]
rājā kathayati vande bhadantānanda buddhaṃ bhagavantam | [Divyāv, 19 208.1]
yathā bhagavānājñāpayati tathā kariṣye | [Divyāv, 19 209.1]
ārogyamityuktā āyuṣmānānandaḥ prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 210.1]
rājā bimbisāraḥ kathayati gṛhapate mayā ayaṃ kumāraḥ saṃvardhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 211.1]
priyaśca me manāpaśca | [Divyāv, 19 212.1]
samayato 'haṃ muñcāmi yadi māṃ divase divase triṣkālaṃ darśanāyopasaṃkrāmatīti | [Divyāv, 19 213.1]
sa kathayati deva upasaṃkramiṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 214.1]
ko 'nya upasaṃkramitavya iti sa rājñā sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitaṃ kṛtvā hastiskandha āropya visarjitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 215.1]
ācaritametallokasya na tāvat putrasya nāma prajñāyate yāvat pitā jīvati | [Divyāv, 19 216.1]
yāvadapareṇa samayena subhadro gṛhapatiḥ kālagataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 217.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kumāraḥ svagṛhe pratiṣṭhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 218.1]
sa buddhe 'bhiprasanno dharme saṃghe 'bhiprasannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 219.1]
buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gato dharmaṃ saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 220.1]
tena yasmin pradeśe tena subhadreṇa patnī āghātitā tasmin pradeśe vihāraṃ kārayitvā sarvopakaraṇasampūrṇaś cāturdiśāryabhikṣusaṃghāya niryātitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 221.1]
tathā sthavirairapi sūtrānta upanibaddhaṃ bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati mṛditakukṣike dāva iti | [Divyāv, 19 222.1]
subhadrasya gṛhapateḥ pauruṣeyā ye paṇyamādāya deśāntaraṃ gatās taiḥ śrutaṃ subhadro gṛhapatiḥ kālagataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 223.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kumāraḥ svagṛhe pratiṣṭhitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 224.1]
sa buddhe 'bhiprasanno dharme saṃghe 'bhiprasanno buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gato dharmaṃ saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ gata iti | [Divyāv, 19 225.1]
teṣāṃ ca gośīrṣacandanamayaṃ pātraṃ sampannam | [Divyāv, 19 226.1]
taistadratnānāṃ pūrayitvā jyotiṣkasya gṛhapateḥ prābhṛtamanupreṣitam | [Divyāv, 19 227.1]
tena taddīrghe stambhe āropya sthāpitam | [Divyāv, 19 228.1]
ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kāritaṃ nedaṃ kenacit viṣṭayā vā śiṭayā vā karkaṭakena vā gṛhītavyam | [Divyāv, 19 229.1]
ya etacchramaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā maharddhiko vā mahānubhāva ṛddhyā gṛhṇāti tasyedam yathāsukhamiti | [Divyāv, 19 230.1]
tīrthyāḥ kalyamevotthāya tīrthyasparśanaṃ gacchanti | [Divyāv, 19 231.1]
taistad dṛṣṭam | [Divyāv, 19 232.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarjyotiṣkasya gṛhapateḥ kathayanti gṛhapate kimetaditi tena teṣāṃ vistareṇārocitam | [Divyāv, 19 233.1]
te kathayanti gṛhapate tvaṃ śramaṇaśākyaputreṣvabhiprasannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 234.1]
te evaṃ grahīṣyantītyuktvā prakrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 235.1]
yāvat sthavirasthavirā bhikṣavo rājagṛhaṃ piṇḍāya praviṣṭāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 236.1]
tairdṛṣṭvā tairapi jyotiṣko gṛhapatiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kimetaditi tena tathaiva vistareṇa samākhyātam | [Divyāv, 19 237.1]
te kathayanti gṛhapate kiṃ pātramātrasyārthāyātmānaṃ saṃprakāśayāma uktaṃ bhagavatā pracchannakalyāṇairvo bhikṣavo vihartavyaṃ dhūtapāpair ityuktvā prakrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 238.1]
yāvadāyuṣmān daśabalaḥ kāśyapastamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 239.1]
sa pṛcchati gṛhapate kimetaditi tena yathāvṛttamārocitam | [Divyāv, 19 240.1]
āyuṣmān daśabalakāśyapaḥ saṃlakṣayati yena mayā anādikālopacitaṃ kleśagaṇaṃ vāntaṃ tyaktaṃ charditaṃ pratinisṛṣṭaṃ taṃ māṃ gṛhapatistīrthikasādhāraṇayā ṛddhyā āhvayati | [Divyāv, 19 241.1]
tadasya manorathaṃ pūrayāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 242.1]
tena gajabhujasadṛśaṃ bāhumabhiprasārya tatpātraṃ gṛhītam | [Divyāv, 19 243.1]
sa tadgṛhītvā vihāraṃ gato bhikṣubhirucyate sthavira kutastava gośīrṣacandanamayaṃ pātramiti tena yathāvṛttamārocitam | [Divyāv, 19 244.1]
bhikṣavaḥ kathayanti sthavira kalpate tava pātramātrasyārthāya ṛddhiṃ vidarśayitumiti kathayati āyuṣmantaḥ kalpatu vā mā vā | [Divyāv, 19 245.1]
kṛtamidānīm | [Divyāv, 19 246.1]
kiṃ kriyatāmiti etat prakaraṇaṃ bhikṣavo bhagavata ārocayanti | [Divyāv, 19 247.1]
bhagavānāha na bhikṣuṇā āgārikasya purastāt ṛddhirvidarśayitavyā | [Divyāv, 19 248.1]
darśayati sātisāro bhavati | [Divyāv, 19 249.1]
api tu catvāri pātrāṇi suvarṇamayaṃ rūpyamayaṃ vaiḍūryamayaṃ sphaṭikamayam | [Divyāv, 19 250.1]
aparāṇyapi catvāri pātrāṇi rītimayaṃ tāmramayaṃ kaṃsamayam abhramayaṃ ca | [Divyāv, 19 251.1]
tatra yāni pūrvakāṇi catvāri pātrāṇi etānyanupasthāpitāni nopasthāpayitavyāni upasthāpitāni visarjayitavyāni | [Divyāv, 19 252.1]
yāni paścimāni catvāri pātrāṇi etānyanupasthāpitāni nopasthāpayitavyāni upasthāpitāni tu bhaiṣajyaśarāvaparibhogena paribhoktavyāni | [Divyāv, 19 253.1]
api tvadhīṣṭāni te dve pātre āyasaṃ mṛṇmayam | [Divyāv, 19 254.1]
yāvadapareṇa samayena jyotiṣkasya gṛhapaterdivyamānuṣī śrīḥ prādurbhūtā | [Divyāv, 19 255.1]
antarā ca rājagṛhamantarā ca campāmatrāntare śulkaśālā | [Divyāv, 19 256.1]
tasyāṃ śulkaśālikaḥ kālagataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 257.1]
sa vyālayakṣeṣūpapannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 258.1]
tena putrāṇāṃ svapnadarśanaṃ dattaṃ putrā yūyam etasmin sthāne yakṣasthānaṃ kārayata tatra ca ghaṇṭāṃ baddhvā lambayata yaḥ kaścit paṇyamaśulkayitvā gamiṣyati sā ghaṇṭā tāvadviraviṣyati yāvadasau nivartya śulkaṃ dāpayitavyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 259.1]
taistaṃ svapnaṃ saṃbandhibāndhavānāṃ nivedya divasatithimuhūrtena tasmin pradeśe yakṣasthānaṃ kāritam | [Divyāv, 19 260.1]
tatra ca ghaṇṭā baddhvā lambitā | [Divyāv, 19 261.1]
campāyāmanyatamo brāhmaṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 262.1]
tena sadṛśāt kulāt kalatramānītam | [Divyāv, 19 263.1]
sā brāhmaṇī saṃlakṣayati ayaṃ brāhmaṇo yaistairupāyairdhanopārjanaṃ karoti | [Divyāv, 19 264.1]
ahaṃ bhakṣayāmi | [Divyāv, 19 265.1]
na mama pratirūpaṃ yad aham akarmikā tiṣṭheyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 266.1]
tayā vīthīṃ gatvā karpāsaḥ krītaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 267.1]
taṃ parikarmayitvā ślakṣṇam sūtraṃ kartitam | [Divyāv, 19 268.1]
śobhanena kuvindena kārṣāpaṇasahasramūlyā yamalī vāyitā | [Divyāv, 19 269.1]
tayā brāhmaṇa ukto brāhmaṇa asyā yamalyāḥ kārṣāpaṇasahasraṃ mūlyam | [Divyāv, 19 270.1]
gṛhītvā vīthīṃ gaccha | [Divyāv, 19 271.1]
yadi kaścit yācati kārṣāpaṇasahasreṇa dātavyā no ced apattanaṃ ghoṣayitvā anyatra gantavyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 272.1]
sa tāṃ gṛhītvā vīthīṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 273.1]
na kaścit kārṣāpaṇasahasreṇa gṛhṇāti | [Divyāv, 19 274.1]
so 'pattanaṃ ghoṣayitvā tām yamalīṃ chatradaṇḍe prakṣipya sārthena sārdhaṃ rājagṛhaṃ samprasthito yāvadanupūrveṇa śulkaśālāmanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 275.1]
śulkaśālikena sārthaḥ śulkitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 276.1]
sa śulkaṃ dattvā samprasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 277.1]
ghaṇṭā raṭitumārabdhā | [Divyāv, 19 278.1]
śaulkikāḥ kathayanti bhavantaḥ yatheyaṃ ghaṇṭā raṇati nūnaṃ sārtho na nipuṇaṃ śulkitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 279.1]
bhūyaḥ śulkayāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 280.1]
tairasau sārthaḥ punaḥ pratinivartya śulkitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 281.1]
nāsti kiṃcid aśulkitam | [Divyāv, 19 282.1]
ghaṇṭā raṭatyeva | [Divyāv, 19 283.1]
tairasau sārtho bhūyaḥ pratinivartya pratyavekṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 284.1]
nāstyevakiṃcit | [Divyāv, 19 285.1]
sārthikā avadhyātumārabdhāḥ kim yūyamasmān mūṣitukāmā yena bhūyo bhūyaḥ pratinivartayadhvamiti tairasau dvidhā kṛtvā muktaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 286.1]
yeṣāṃ madhye sa brāhmaṇo nāsti te 'tikrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 287.1]
anyeṣāṃ gacchatāṃ sā ghaṇṭā tathaiva raṭitumārabdhā | [Divyāv, 19 288.1]
taiste punaḥ pratyavekṣitāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 289.1]
evaṃ tāvat dvidhākṛtāḥ yāvat sa caiko brāhmaṇo 'vasthita iti | [Divyāv, 19 290.1]
sa tairgṛhītaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 291.1]
sa kathayati pratyavekṣata yadi mama kiṃcidastīti | [Divyāv, 19 292.1]
taiḥ sarvataḥ pratyavekṣya muktaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 293.1]
sā ghaṇṭā raṭatyeva | [Divyāv, 19 294.1]
tairasau brāhmaṇaḥ pratinivartyokto bho brāhmaṇa kathaya naiva śulkaṃ dāpayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 295.1]
kiṃtu devasyaiva sānnidhyaṃ jñātaṃ bhavatīti | [Divyāv, 19 296.1]
kathayati satyaṃ na dāpayatha na dāpayāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 297.1]
tena chatradaṇḍādapanīya sā yamalī darśitā | [Divyāv, 19 298.1]
te paraṃ vismayamāpannā bhavantaḥ īdṛśamapi devasya sānnidhyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 299.1]
taistat ekaṃ vastramudghāṭya devaḥ prāvṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 300.1]
brāhmaṇaḥ kathayati yūyaṃ kathayatha śulkaṃ na dāpayāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 301.1]
idānīṃ sarvasvamapaharatha iti | [Divyāv, 19 302.1]
te kathayanti brāhmaṇa nāsmābhirgṛhītam | [Divyāv, 19 303.1]
api devasyaitat sānnidhyamiti kṛtvā asmābhiḥ prāvṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 304.1]
gṛhītvā gaccheti | [Divyāv, 19 305.1]
sa taṃ punargṛhītvā punaśchatranāḍikāyāṃ prakṣipya prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 306.1]
anupūrveṇa rājagṛhamanuprāptaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 307.1]
sa vīthyāṃ prasāryāvasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 308.1]
tatrāpi tāṃ na kaścit kārṣāpaṇasahasreṇa yācate | [Divyāv, 19 309.1]
sa rājagṛhamapyapattanaṃ ghoṣayitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 310.1]
jyotiṣkaśca kumāro rājakulānniṣkramya hastiskandhābhirūḍho vīthīmadhyena svagṛhaṃ gacchati | [Divyāv, 19 311.1]
tena śrutam | [Divyāv, 19 312.1]
sa taiḥ śabditaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 313.1]
jyotiṣkeṇokto bho brāhmaṇa kimarthaṃ tvam apattanaṃ ghoṣayasi gṛhapate asyā yamalyāḥ kārṣāpaṇasahasraṃ mūlyam | [Divyāv, 19 314.1]
na ca kaścidyācata iti | [Divyāv, 19 315.1]
sa kathayati ānaya paśyāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 316.1]
tenopadarśitā | [Divyāv, 19 317.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kathayati astyetadeva | [Divyāv, 19 318.1]
kiṃtu atraikaṃ vastraṃ paribhuktakam | [Divyāv, 19 319.1]
ekamaparibhuktakam | [Divyāv, 19 320.1]
yad aparibhuktam asya pañcakārṣāpaṇaśatāni mūlyam | [Divyāv, 19 321.1]
yattu paribhuktakam asyārdhatṛtīyāni | [Divyāv, 19 322.1]
brāhmaṇaḥ kathayati kimetadevaṃ bhaviṣyati jyotiṣkaḥ kathayati brāhmaṇa tava pratyakṣīkaromi | [Divyāv, 19 323.1]
paśyeti | [Divyāv, 19 324.1]
tenāsau aparibhukta uparivihāyasā kṣiptaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 325.1]
vitānaṃ kṛtvā avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 326.1]
paribhuktaḥ kṣiptaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 327.1]
kṣiptamātraka eva patitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 328.1]
brāhmaṇo dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayamāpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 329.1]
kathayati gṛhapate maharddhikastvam mahānubhāva iti | [Divyāv, 19 330.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kathayati brāhmaṇa punaḥ paśyainaṃ yo 'sau aparibhuktaka iti sa kaṇṭakavāṭasyopariṣṭāt kṣipto 'sajjamāno gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 331.1]
so 'nyaḥ kṣiptaḥ kaṇṭake lagnaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 332.1]
sa brāhmaṇo bhūyasyā mātrayā abhiprasannaḥ kathayati gṛhapate maharddhikastvaṃ mahānubhāvaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 333.1]
yat tavābhipretaṃ tatprayaccheti | [Divyāv, 19 334.1]
sa kathayati brāhmaṇa atithistvam | [Divyāv, 19 335.1]
tavaiva pūjā kṛtā bhavati | [Divyāv, 19 336.1]
sahasrameva prayacchāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 337.1]
tena tasya kārṣāpaṇasahasraṃ dattam | [Divyāv, 19 338.1]
brāhmaṇastamādāya prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 339.1]
jyotiṣkeṇa tato yaḥ paribhuktakaḥ sa dārakāya datto 'paribhuktakastu snānaśāṭakaḥ kṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 340.1]
yāvadapareṇa samayena rājā bimbisāra upariprāsādatalagato 'mātyagaṇaparivṛtastiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 19 341.1]
jyotiṣkasya sa snānaśāṭaka upari gṛhasyābhyavakāśe śoṣito vāyunā hriyamāṇo rājño bimbisārasyopari patitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 342.1]
rājā kathayati bhavantaḥ rājārhamidaṃ vastram | [Divyāv, 19 343.1]
kuta etaditi | [Divyāv, 19 344.1]
te kathayanti deva śrūyate rājño māndhātuḥ saptāhaṃ hiraṇyavarṣaṃ patitam | [Divyāv, 19 345.1]
devasyāpi vastravarṣaḥ patitumārabdham | [Divyāv, 19 346.1]
nacirāddhiraṇyavarṣaḥ patiṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 347.1]
rājā kathayati bhavantaḥ jyotiṣko gṛhapatirbhagavatā vyākṛto divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 348.1]
idaṃ ca divyaṃ vastramākāśāt patitam | [Divyāv, 19 349.1]
sthāpayata | [Divyāv, 19 350.1]
tasyaivāgatasya dāsyāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 351.1]
te caivamālāpaṃ kurvanti jyotiṣkaścāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 352.1]
rājā kathayati kumāra tvaṃ bhagavatā vyākṛto divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 353.1]
mama cedaṃ divyaṃ vastramākāśāt patitam | [Divyāv, 19 354.1]
gṛhāṇeti | [Divyāv, 19 355.1]
tena hastaḥ prasāritaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 356.1]
deva ānaya paśyāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 357.1]
sa nirīkṣitumārabdho yāvat paśyatyātmīyaṃ snānaśāṭakam | [Divyāv, 19 358.1]
sa vismṛtya kathayati deva madīyo 'yaṃ snānaśāṭako vāyunopakṣipta ihāgata iti | [Divyāv, 19 359.1]
kumāra tava divyamānuṣyakī śrīḥ prādurbhūtā deva prādurbhūtā | [Divyāv, 19 360.1]
kumāra yadyevam kimarthaṃ na nimantrayasi deva nimantrito bhava | [Divyāv, 19 361.1]
gaccha bhaktaṃ sajjīkuru | [Divyāv, 19 362.1]
deva yasya divyamānuṣī śrīḥ prādurbhūtā kiṃ tena sajjīkartavyam nanu sajjīkṛtameva gaccheti | [Divyāv, 19 363.1]
sa jyotiṣkasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 364.1]
rājā bāhyaṃ parijanaṃ dṛṣṭvā indriyāṇyutkṣipati | [Divyāv, 19 365.1]
deva kimarthamindriyāṇyutkṣipasi | [Divyāv, 19 366.1]
sa kathayati kumāra vadhūjano 'yamiti kṛtvā | [Divyāv, 19 367.1]
deva nāyaṃ vadhūjanaḥ bāhyo 'yaṃ parijanaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 368.1]
sa paraṃ vismayamāpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 369.1]
punarmadhyaṃ janaṃ dṛṣṭvā indriyāṇyutkṣiptumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 370.1]
tathaiva pṛcchati | [Divyāv, 19 371.1]
rājā api tathaiva kathayati | [Divyāv, 19 372.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kathayati deva ayamapi na vadhūjanaḥ kiṃtu madhyo 'yaṃ janaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 373.1]
sa bhūyasyā mātrayā paraṃ vismayamāpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 374.1]
tasya madhyamāyāṃ dvāraśālāyāṃ maṇibhūmiruparacitā | [Divyāv, 19 375.1]
tasyāṃ matsyā udakapūrṇāyāmiva yantrayogenoparibhramanto dṛśyante | [Divyāv, 19 376.1]
rājā praveṣṭukāmo vāpīti kṛtvopānahau moktumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 377.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kathayati deva kasyārthe upānahau apanayasīti sa kathayati kumāra pānīyamuttartavyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 378.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kathayati deva nedaṃ pānīyaṃ maṇibhūmireṣā | [Divyāv, 19 379.1]
sa kathayati kumāra ime matsyā upari bhramantaḥ paśyanti | [Divyāv, 19 380.1]
deva yantrayogenaite paribhramanti | [Divyāv, 19 381.1]
sa na śraddhatte | [Divyāv, 19 382.1]
tenāṅgulimudrā kṣiptā | [Divyāv, 19 383.1]
sā raṇaraṇāśabdena bhūmau patitā | [Divyāv, 19 384.1]
tato vismayamāpannaḥ praviśya siṃhāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 385.1]
vadhūjanaḥ pādābhivandana upasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 386.1]
tāsāmaśrupāto jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 387.1]
rājā kathayati kumāra kasmādayaṃ vadhūjano roditi deva nāyaṃ roditi kiṃtu devasya kāṣṭhadhūmena vastrāṇi dhūpitāni tena āsāmaśrupato jāta iti | [Divyāv, 19 388.1]
rājā tatra divyamānuṣyā śriyā upacaryamāṇaḥ pramatto na niṣkrāmati | [Divyāv, 19 389.1]
rājakṛtyāni rājakaraṇīyāni parihātumārabdhāni | [Divyāv, 19 390.1]
amātyairajātaśatruḥ kumāro 'bhibhūtaḥ kumāra devo jyotiṣkasya gṛhaṃ praviśya pramattaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 391.1]
gaccha nivedayeti | [Divyāv, 19 392.1]
tena gatvā ukto deva kimatra praviśyāvasthito 'mātyāḥ kathayanti rājakṛtyāni rājakaraṇīyāni parihīyanta iti | [Divyāv, 19 393.1]
sa kathayati kumāra na śaknoṣi tvamekaṃ divasaṃ rājyaṃ kārayitum kiṃ devo jānīte mamaiko divasaḥ praviṣṭasya adya devasya saptamo divaso vartate | [Divyāv, 19 394.1]
rājā jyotiṣkasya mukhaṃ nirīkṣya kathayati kumāra satyam deva satyam | [Divyāv, 19 395.1]
saptama eva divaso vartate | [Divyāv, 19 396.1]
kumāra kathaṃ rātrirjñāyate divaso vā deva puṣpāṇāṃ saṃkocavikāsānmaṇīnāṃ jvalanājvalanayogācchakunīnāṃ ca kūjanākūjanāt | [Divyāv, 19 397.1]
