santi tāni puṣpāṇi yāni rātrau vikasanti divā mlāyanti santi yāni divā vikasanti rātrau mlāyanti santi te maṇayo ye rātrau jvalanti na divā santi ye divā jvalanti na rātrau santi te śakunayo ye rātrau kūjanti na divā santi ye divā kūjanti na rātrau rājā vismayamāpannaḥ kathayati kumāra avitathavādī bhagavān | [Divyāv, 19 398.1]
yathā tvaṃ bhagavatā vyākṛtastathaiva nānyathetyuktvā jyotiṣkagṛhāt niṣkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 399.1]
ajātaśatrukumāreṇa jyotiṣkasantako maṇirapahṛtya dārakasya haste dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 400.1]
tena yata eva gṛhītastatraiva gatvāvasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 401.1]
ajātaśatruḥ kathayati dāraka ānaya taṃ maṇiṃ paśyāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 402.1]
sa muṣṭiṃ vighāṭya kathayati kumāra na jāne kutra gata iti | [Divyāv, 19 403.1]
sa taṃ tāḍayitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 404.1]
jyotiṣkaḥ kathayati kumāra kimarthamenaṃ tāḍayasi gṛhapate ahaṃ cauraḥ eṣa mahācauraḥ | [Divyāv, 19 405.1]
mayā tvadīyo maṇirapahṛtaḥ so 'pyanenāpahṛta iti | [Divyāv, 19 406.1]
sa kathayati kumāra na tvayā apahṛto nāpyanena api tu yata eva tvayā gṛhītastatraiva gatvā avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 407.1]
api tu kumāra svakaṃ te gṛham | [Divyāv, 19 408.1]
yāvadbhirmaṇibhiranyena vā prayojanaṃ tāvadgṛhāṇa yathāsukhamiti | [Divyāv, 19 409.1]
sa pratibhinnakaḥ saṃlakṣayate yadā pituratyayādrājā bhaviṣyāmi tadā grahīṣyāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 410.1]
yadā ajātaśatruṇā devadattavigrāhitena pitā dhārmiko dharmarājo jīvitād vyaparopitaḥ svayameva ca paṭṭaṃ baddhvā pratiṣṭhitas tadā tena jyotiṣko 'bhihito gṛhapate tvaṃ mama bhrātā bhavasi | [Divyāv, 19 411.1]
gṛhaṃ bhājayāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 412.1]
sa saṃlakṣayati yena pitā dhārmiko dharmarājaḥ praghātitaḥ sa māṃ marṣayatīti kuta etan nūnamayaṃ madgṛhamāgacchatu kāmaṃ prayacchāmīti viditvā kathayati deva vibhaktameva kimatra vibhaktavyam madīyaṃ gṛhamāgaccha ahaṃ tvadīyaṃ gṛhamāgacchāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 413.1]
ajātaśatruḥ kathayati śobhanam | [Divyāv, 19 414.1]
evaṃ kuru | [Divyāv, 19 415.1]
sa tasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 416.1]
jyotiṣko 'pyajātaśatrorgṛhaṃ gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 417.1]
sā śrīstasmādgṛhādantarhitā yatra jyotiṣkastatraiva gatā | [Divyāv, 19 418.1]
evam yāvat saptavārānantarhitā prādurbhūtā ca | [Divyāv, 19 419.1]
ajātaśatruḥ saṃlakṣayate evamapi mayā na śakitaṃ jyotiṣkasya maṇīnapahartum | [Divyāv, 19 420.1]
anyadupāyaṃ karomi | [Divyāv, 19 421.1]
tena dhūrtapuruṣāḥ prayuktā gacchata jyotiṣkasya gṛhānmaṇīnapaharateti | [Divyāv, 19 422.1]
te hi śiṭākarkaṭakaprayogenābhiroḍhum ārabdhāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 423.1]
te 'ntaḥpurikayā upariprāsādatalagatayā dṛṣṭāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 424.1]
tayā dhūrtadhūrtakā iti nādo muktaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 425.1]
jyotiṣkeṇa śrutam | [Divyāv, 19 426.1]
tenāśayato vāṅniścāritā tiṣṭhantu dhūrtakā iti | [Divyāv, 19 427.1]
teṣām yo yatrābhirūḍhaḥ sa tatraivāsthito yāvat prabhātā rajanī saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 19 428.1]
mahājanakāyena dṛṣṭāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 429.1]
te kathayanti bhavantaḥ anena kalirājena pitā dhārmiko dharmarājo jīvitād vyaparopitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 430.1]
idānīṃ gṛhāṇyapi moṣayati | [Divyāv, 19 431.1]
tatkiṃ na me moṣiṣyata iti purakṣobho jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 432.1]
ajātaśatruṇā jyotiṣkasya dūto 'nupreṣito muñcata mamāyaṃ khalīkāra saṃlakṣayate yena nāma pitā jīvitād vyaparopitaḥ sa māṃ na praghātayiṣyatīti kuta etat sarvathā ahaṃ bhagavatā vyākṛto mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkariṣyatīti | [Divyāv, 19 433.1]
gacchāmi pravrajāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 434.1]
tena sarvaṃ ghanajātaṃ dīnānāthakṛpaṇebhyo dattam | [Divyāv, 19 435.1]
adhanāḥ sadhanā vyavasthāpitāḥ | [Divyāv, 19 436.1]
atha jyotiṣko gṛhapatiḥ suhṛtsambandhibāndhavānavalokya yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 437.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 438.1]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇo jyotiṣko gṛhapatirbhagavantamidamavocal labheyāhaṃ bhadanta svākhyāte dharmavinaye pravrajyāmupasampadaṃ bhikṣubhāvam | [Divyāv, 19 439.1]
careyamahaṃ bhagavato 'ntike brahmacaryamiti | [Divyāv, 19 440.1]
sa bhagavatā ehibhikṣukayā ābhāṣita ehi bhikṣo cara brahmacaryamiti | [Divyāv, 19 441.1]
bhagavato vācāvasānameva muṇḍaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 442.1]
saṃghāṭīprāvṛtaḥ pātrakaravyagrahastaḥ saptāhāvaropitakeśaśmaśrurvarṣaśatopasaṃpannasya bhikṣurīryāpathenāvasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 443.1]
ehīti coktaḥ sa tathāgatena muṇḍaśca saṃghāṭiparītadehaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 444.1]
sadyaḥ praśāntendriya eva tasthāvupasthito buddhamanorathena | [Divyāv, 19 444.2]
tasya bhagavatā avavādo dattaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 445.1]
tenodyacchamānena vyāyacchamānena idameva pañcagaṇḍakaṃ saṃsāracakraṃ calācalaṃ viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatīḥ śatanapatanavikiraṇavidhvaṃsanadharmatayā parāhatya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 19 446.1]
arhan saṃvṛttastraidhātukavītarāgaḥ samaloṣṭakāñcana ākāśapāṇitalasamacitto vāsīcandanakalpo vidyāvidāritāṇḍakośo vidyābhijñāpratisaṃvitprāpto bhavalābhalobhasatkāraparāṅmukhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 447.1]
sendropendrāṇāṃ devānāṃ pūjyo mānyo 'bhivādyaśca saṃvṛttaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 448.1]
bhikṣavaḥ saṃśayajātāḥ sarvasaṃśayacchettāraṃ buddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ papracchuḥ kiṃ bhadanta āyuṣmatā jyotiṣkeṇa karma kṛtam yena citāmāropitaḥ divyamānuṣī śrīḥ prādurbhūtā bhagavataḥ śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtamiti bhagavānāha jyotiṣkeṇaiva bhikṣavaḥ karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni labdhasaṃhārāṇi pariṇatapratyayānyoghavatpratyupasthitānyavaśyambhāvīni | [Divyāv, 19 449.1]
jyotiṣkeṇa karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni | [Divyāv, 19 450.1]
ko 'nyaḥ pratyanubhaviṣyati na bhikṣavaḥ karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni pṛthivīdhātau vipacyante nābdhātau na tejodhātau na vāyudhātau api tūpātteṣveva skandhadhātvāyataneṣu karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni vipacyante śubhānyaśubhāni ca | [Divyāv, 19 451.1]
na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatairapi | [Divyāv, 19 452.1]
sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti khalu dehinām | [Divyāv, 19 452.2]
bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣava ekanavatikalpe vipaśyī nāma śāstā loka udapādi tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddho vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devamanuṣyāṇāṃ buddho bhagavān | [Divyāv, 19 453.1]
dvāṣaṣṭibhikṣusahasraparivāro janapadacārikāṃ caran bandhumatīṃ rājadhānīmanuprāpto bandhumatyāṃ viharati sma bandhumatīyake dāve | [Divyāv, 19 454.1]
tena khalu samayena bandhumatyāṃ rājadhānyāṃ bandhumān nāma rājā rājyaṃ kārayati ṛddhaṃ ca sphītaṃ ca kṣemaṃ ca subhikṣaṃ ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyaṃ ca praśāntakalikalahaḍimbaḍamaraṃ taskararogāpagataṃ śālīkṣugomahiṣīsampannam | [Divyāv, 19 455.1]
dhārmiko dharmarājā dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kārayati | [Divyāv, 19 456.1]
tasyānaṅgaṇo nāma gṛhapatirāḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogo vistīrṇaviśālaparigraho vaiśravaṇadhanasamudito vaiśravaṇadhanapratispardhī | [Divyāv, 19 457.1]
sa saṃlakṣayate bahuśo mayā vipaśyī samyaksambuddho 'ntargṛhe upanimantrya bhojitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 458.1]
na tu kadācit traimāsīṃ sarvopakaraṇaiḥ pravāritaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 459.1]
yannvahaṃ vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ traimāsīṃ sarvopakaraṇaiḥ pravārayeyam | [Divyāv, 19 460.1]
iti viditvā yena vipaśyī samyaksambuddhastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 461.1]
upasaṃkramya vipaśyinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 462.1]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇamanaṅgaṇaṃ gṛhapatiṃ vipaśyī samyaksambuddho dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 19 463.1]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 19 464.1]
athānaṅgaṇo gṛhapatirutthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena vipaśyī samyaksambuddhastenāñjaliṃ praṇamya vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhamidamavocad adhivāsayatu me bhagavāṃs traimāsīṃ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃgheneti | [Divyāv, 19 465.1]
adhivāsayati vipaśyī samyaksambuddho 'naṅgaṇasya gṛhapatestūṣṇīmbhāvena | [Divyāv, 19 466.1]
athānaṅgaṇo gṛhapatirbhagavatas tūṣṇībhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā vipaśyinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā utthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 467.1]
aśrauṣīdbandhumān rājā vipaśyī samyaksambuddho dvāṣaṣṭibhikṣusahasraparivāro janapadacārikāṃ caran bandhumatīmanuprāpto bandhumatyāṃ viharati bandhumatīye dāve iti | [Divyāv, 19 468.1]
śrutvā ca punarasyaitadabhavad bahuśo mayā bhagavānantargṛhe upanimantrya bhojitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 469.1]
na tu kadācit traimāsīṃ sarvopakaraṇaiḥ pravāritaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 470.1]
yannvahaṃ vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ sarvopakaraṇaiḥ pravārayeyam | [Divyāv, 19 471.1]
iti viditvā yena vipaśyī samyaksambuddhastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 472.1]
upasaṃkramya vipaśyinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 473.1]
ekāntaniṣaṇṇaṃ bandhumantaṃ rājānaṃ bhagavān dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 19 474.1]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samādāpya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya tūṣṇīm | [Divyāv, 19 475.1]
atha bandhumān rājā utthāyāsanād ekāṃsamuttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena vipaśyī samyaksambuddhastenāñjaliṃ praṇamya vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhamidamavocad adhivāsayatu me bhagavāṃstraimāsīṃ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena | [Divyāv, 19 476.1]
upanimantrito 'smi mahārāja tvatprathamato 'naṅgaṇena gṛhapatinā | [Divyāv, 19 477.1]
adhivāsayatu bhagavān ahaṃ tathā kariṣye yathā anaṅgaṇo gṛhapatirājñāsyati | [Divyāv, 19 478.1]
sacet te mahārāja anaṅgaṇo gṛhapatiranujānīte evaṃ te 'hamadhivāsayāmi | [Divyāv, 19 479.1]
atha bandhumān rājā vipaśyinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya pādau śirasā vanditvā utthāyāsanāt prakrānto yena svaṃ niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 480.1]
bandhumān rājā anaṅgaṇaṃ gṛhapatiṃ dūtena prakrośyedamavocad yatkhalu gṛhapate jānīyād ahaṃ tvatprathamato vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ bhojayāmi tataḥ paścāt tavāpi na duṣkaraṃ bhaviṣyati vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ bhojayitumiti | [Divyāv, 19 481.1]
sa kathayati deva mayā vipaśyī samyaksambuddhastvatprathamata upanimantritaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 482.1]
ahameva bhojayāmi | [Divyāv, 19 483.1]
rājā kathayati gṛhapate yadyapyevaṃ tathāpi tvaṃ mama viṣayanivāsī | [Divyāv, 19 484.1]
nārhāmyahaṃ tvatprathamato bhojayitum deva yadyapyahaṃ tava viṣayanivāsī tathāpi yena pūrvanimantritaḥ sa eva bhojayati | [Divyāv, 19 485.1]
nātra devasya nirbandho yuktaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 486.1]
na te gṛhapate kāmakāraṃ dadāmi | [Divyāv, 19 487.1]
api tu yo bhaktottarikayā jeṣyati so 'vaśiṣṭaṃ kālaṃ bhojayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 488.1]
tathā bhavatu ityanaṅgaṇo gṛhapatiḥ pratyaśrauṣīt | [Divyāv, 19 489.1]
tathā anaṅgaṇo gṛhapatistāmeva rātriṃ śuciṃ praṇītaṃ khādanīyaṃ bhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyamevotthāyodakamaṇīn pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālamārocayati samayo bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyate | [Divyāv, 19 490.1]
atha vipaśyī samyaksambuddhaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto yenānaṅgaṇasya gṛhapaterbhaktābhisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 491.1]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 492.1]
athānaṅgaṇo gṛhapatiḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpayati saṃpravārayati | [Divyāv, 19 493.1]
anekaparyāyeṇa śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ saṃtarpya saṃpravārya bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastamapanītapātraṃ nīcataramāsanaṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purastānniṣaṇṇo dharmaśravaṇāya | [Divyāv, 19 494.1]
atha vipaśyī samyaksambuddho 'naṅgaṇaṃ gṛhapatiṃ dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati | [Divyāv, 19 495.1]
anekaparyāyeṇa dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśya samuttejya saṃpraharṣya prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 496.1]
evaṃ bandhumatā rājñā bhojitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 497.1]
eṣa eva grantho vistareṇa kartavyaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 498.1]
na kvacidbhaktottarikayā parājayati | [Divyāv, 19 499.1]
tato bandhumān rājā kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 500.1]
amātyāḥ kathayanti deva kasmāt tvaṃ kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparastiṣṭhasīti sa kathayati bhavantaḥ kathamahaṃ na cintāparastiṣṭhāmi yo 'haṃ mama viṣayanivāsinaṃ kuṭumbinaṃ na śaknomi bhaktottarikayā parājayitum te kathayanti deva tasya gṛhapateḥ kāṣṭhaṃ nāsti | [Divyāv, 19 501.1]
kāṣṭhavikrayo vidhāryatāmiti | [Divyāv, 19 502.1]
rājñā ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kāritam | [Divyāv, 19 503.1]
bhavanto na kenacit madviṣayanivāsinā kāṣṭhaṃ vikretavyam | [Divyāv, 19 504.1]
yo vikrīṇīte tena madviṣaye na vastavyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 505.1]
anaṅgaṇo gṛhapatirgandhakāṣṭhairbhaktaṃ sādhayitumārabdhaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 506.1]
sugandhatailena ca vastrāṇi tīmayitvā khādyakānyullāḍayitum | [Divyāv, 19 507.1]
surabhiṇā gandhena sarvā bandhumatī nagarī sphuṭā saṃvṛttā | [Divyāv, 19 508.1]
bandhumān rājā pṛcchati bhavantaḥ kuta eṣa manojñagandha iti tairvistareṇa samākhyātam | [Divyāv, 19 509.1]
sa kathayati ahamapyevaṃ karomi | [Divyāv, 19 510.1]
kiṃ mama vibhavo nāstīti amātyāḥ kathayanti deva kasyārthe evaṃ kriyate ayaṃ gṛhapatiraputro nacirāt kālaṃ kariṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 511.1]
devasyaiva sarvaṃ santaḥsvāpateyaṃ bhaviṣyati | [Divyāv, 19 512.1]
kāṣṭhavikrayo 'nujñāsyatām iti | [Divyāv, 19 513.1]
tena kāṣṭhavikrayo 'nujñātaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 514.1]
anaṅgaṇena gṛhapatinā śrutaṃ rājñā kāṣṭhavikrayo 'nujñāta iti | [Divyāv, 19 515.1]
tena cittaṃ pradūṣya kharā vāṅ niścāritā tāvanme bhaktakāṣṭhamasti yenāham enaṃ sahāmātyaṃ citāmāropya dhmāpayāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 516.1]
rājā kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparo vyavasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 517.1]
amātyāḥ kathayanti deva kimarthaṃ kare kapolaṃ dattvā cintāparastiṣṭhasīti tena vistareṇa samākhyātam | [Divyāv, 19 518.1]
te kathayanti deva alaṃ viṣādena | [Divyāv, 19 519.1]
vayaṃ tathā kariṣyāmo yathā devaścānaṅgaṇaṃ gṛhapatiṃ parājayatīti | [Divyāv, 19 520.1]
tairaparasmin divase bandhumatī rājadhānī apagatapāṣāṇaśarkarakaṭhalyā vyavasthāpitā candanavāripariṣiktā surabhidhūpaghaṭikopanibaddhā āmuktapaṭṭadāmakalāpā ucchritadhvajapatākā nānāpuṣpāvakīrṇā nandanavanodyānasadṛśā | [Divyāv, 19 521.1]
tatpratispardhaśobhāvibhūṣito maṇḍavāṭaḥ kāritaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 522.1]
tasmin nānāratnavibhūṣitāsanavasanasampannaśobhāsanaprajñaptiḥ kāritā | [Divyāv, 19 523.1]
mṛduviśadasurabhigandhasampanno vividhabhaktavyañjanasahito divyasudhāmanojñasaṃkāśas trailokyaguroranurūpa āhāra upasamanvāhṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 524.1]
tato bandhumān rājā dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayamāpannaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 525.1]
tato vismayāvarjitacittasaṃtatirvipaśyinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya dūtena kālamārocayati samaye bhadanta sajjaṃ bhaktam yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyata iti | [Divyāv, 19 526.1]
atha vipaśyī samyaksambuddhaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya bhikṣugaṇaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena bandhumato rājño bhaktābhisārastenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 527.1]
upasaṃkramya purastādbhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 528.1]
bandhumato rājño maṅgalyābhiṣeko hastināgo vipaśyinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya śataśalākaṃ chatramupari mūrdhno dhārayati avaśiṣṭā hastināgā bhikṣūṇām | [Divyāv, 19 529.1]
bandhumato rājño 'gramahiṣī vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ sauvarṇena maṇivālavyajanena vījayati avaśiṣṭā antaḥpurikā avaśiṣṭānāṃ bhikṣūṇām | [Divyāv, 19 530.1]
anaṅgaṇena gṛhapatinā avacarakaḥ puruṣaḥ preṣito gaccha bhoḥ puruṣa paśya kīdṛśenāhāreṇa bandhumān rājā buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ bhojayatīti | [Divyāv, 19 531.1]
sa gatastāṃ vibhūtiṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayāvarjitamanāstatraivāvasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 532.1]
evaṃ dvitīyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ preṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 533.1]
so 'pi tatraiva gatvā avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 534.1]
tato 'naṅgaṇo gṛhapatiḥ svayameva gataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 535.1]
so 'pi tāṃ vibhūtiṃ dṛṣṭvā paraṃ viṣādamāpannaḥ saṃlakṣayati śakyamanyat saṃpādayitum | [Divyāv, 19 536.1]
kiṃtu hastināmantaḥpurasya ca kuto mama vibhava iti viditvā niveśanaṃ gato dauvārikaṃ puruṣamāmantrayate bhoḥ puruṣa yadi kaścidyācanaka āgacchati sa yat prārthayate taddātavyaṃ no tu praveśaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 537.1]
ityuktvā śokāgāraṃ praviśya avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 538.1]
śakrasya devendrasyādhastāt jñānadarśanaṃ pravartate | [Divyāv, 19 539.1]
sa saṃlakṣayati ye kecilloke dakṣiṇīyā vipaśyī samyaksambuddhasteṣāmagro dānapatīnāmapyanaṅgaṇo gṛhapatiḥ | [Divyāv, 19 540.1]
sāhāyyamasya kalpayitavyam | [Divyāv, 19 541.1]
iti viditvā kauśiko brāhmaṇaveṣamabhinirmāya yenānaṅgaṇasya gṛhapater niveśanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 542.1]
upasaṃkramya dauvārikaṃ puruṣamāmantrayate gaccha bhoḥ puruṣa anaṅgaṇasya gṛhapateḥ kathaya kauśikagotro brāhmaṇo dvāre tiṣṭhati bhavantaṃ draṣṭukāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 543.1]
sa kathayati brāhmaṇa gṛhapatinā ahaṃ sthāpito yaḥ kaścid yācanaka āgacchati sa yat prārthayate taddātavyaṃ na tu praveśa iti | [Divyāv, 19 544.1]
yena te prayojanaṃ tadgṛhītvā gaccha | [Divyāv, 19 545.1]
kiṃ te gṛhapatinā dṛṣṭeneti sa kathayati bhoḥ puruṣa na mama kenacit prayojanam | [Divyāv, 19 546.1]
ahaṃ gṛhapatimeva draṣṭukāmaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 547.1]
gaccheti | [Divyāv, 19 548.1]
tenānaṅgaṇasya gṛhapatergatvā niveditam ārya kauśikasagotro brāhmaṇo dvāre tiṣṭhati āryaṃ draṣṭukāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 549.1]
sa kathayati gaccha bhoḥ puruṣa yena tasya prayojanaṃ tat prayaccha kiṃ tenātra praviṣṭeneti sa kathayati ārya ukto mayā evaṃ kathayati nāhaṃ kiṃcit prārthayāmi api tu gṛhapatimeva draṣṭukāma iti | [Divyāv, 19 550.1]
sa kathayati bhoḥ puruṣa yadyevam praveśaya | [Divyāv, 19 551.1]
sa tena praveśitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 552.1]
brāhmaṇaḥ kathayati kasmāt tvaṃ gṛhapate kare kapolaṃ cintāparastiṣṭhasīti sa gṛhapatirgāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 19 553.1]
na tasya kathayecchokaṃ yaḥ śokānna pramocayet | [Divyāv, 19 554.1]
tasmai tu kathayecchokaṃ yaḥ śokātsaṃpramocayet | [Divyāv, 19 554.2]
śakraḥ kathayati gṛhapate kastava śokaḥ kathaya ahaṃ te śokātpramocayāmīti | [Divyāv, 19 555.1]
tena vistareṇa samākhyātam | [Divyāv, 19 556.1]
atha śakro devendraḥ kauśikabrāhmaṇarūpamantardhāpya svarūpeṇa sthitvā kathayati gṛhapate viśvakarmā te devaputraḥ sāhāyyaṃ kalpayiṣyatītyuktvā prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 557.1]
atha śakro devendro devāṃstrāyastriṃśān gatvā viśvakarmāṇaṃ devaputramāmantrayate gaccha viśvakarman anaṅgaṇasya gṛhapateḥ sāhāyyaṃ kalpaya | [Divyāv, 19 558.1]
paraṃ bhadraṃ tava kauśiketi viśvakarmaṇā devaputreṇa śakrasya devendrasya pratiśrutya āgataḥ | [Divyāv, 19 559.1]
prativiśiṣṭatarā nagaraśobhā nirmitā divyo maṇḍalavāṭo divyāsanaprajñaptirdivya āhāraḥ samanvāhṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 560.1]
airāvaṇo nāgarājo vipaśyinaḥ samyaksambuddhasya śataśalākaṃ chatramupari mūrdhno dhārayati avaśiṣṭā nāgā avaśiṣṭānāṃ bhikṣūṇām | [Divyāv, 19 561.1]
śacī devakanyā vipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhaṃ sauvarṇena maṇivālavyajanena vījayati avaśiṣṭā apsaraso bhikṣūn | [Divyāv, 19 562.1]
bandhumatā rājñā avacarakaḥ puruṣaḥ preṣito gaccha bhoḥ puruṣa kīdṛśenāhāreṇānaṅgaṇo gṛhapatir buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ tarpayatīti sa puruṣastatra gatastāṃ vibhūtiṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraiva avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 563.1]
tenāmātyaḥ preṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 564.1]
so 'pi tatraivāvasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 565.1]
kumāraḥ preṣitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 566.1]
so 'pi tatraivāvasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 567.1]
tato bandhumān rājā svayameva taddvāraṃ gatvā avasthitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 568.1]
vipaśyī samyaksambuddhaḥ kathayati gṛhapate bandhumān rājā dṛṣṭasatyaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 569.1]
tasyāntike tvayā kharavākkarma niścāritam | [Divyāv, 19 570.1]
sa eva dvāre tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 19 571.1]
gaccha kṣamayeti | [Divyāv, 19 572.1]
tenāsau nirgatya kṣamita uktaśca mahārāja praviśa svahastena pariveṣaṇaṃ kuru | [Divyāv, 19 573.1]
sa praviṣṭaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 574.1]
paśyati divyāṃ vibhūtim | [Divyāv, 19 575.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca paraṃ vismayamāpannaḥ kathayati gṛhapate tvamevaiko 'rhasi dine dine buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ bhojayituṃ na vayam iti | [Divyāv, 19 576.1]
athānaṅgaṇo gṛhapatirvipaśyinaṃ samyaksambuddhamanayā vibhūtyā traimāsyaṃ praṇītenāhāreṇa saṃtarpya pādayor nipatya praṇidhānaṃ kartumārabdho yanmayā evaṃvidhe sadbhūtadakṣiṇīye kārā kṛtā anenāhaṃ kuśalamūlena āḍhye mahādhane mahābhoge kule jāyeyaṃ divyamānuṣīṃ śriyaṃ pratyanubhaveyam evaṃvidhānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ lābhī syām evaṃvidhameva śāstāramārāgayeyaṃ mā virāgayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 19 577.1]
kiṃ manyadhve bhikṣavo yo 'sau anaṅgaṇo nāma gṛhapatir eṣa evāsau jyotiṣkaḥ kulaputrastena kālena tena samayena | [Divyāv, 19 578.1]
yadanena bandhumato rājño dṛṣṭasatyasyāntike kharā vāṅniścāritā tasya karmaṇo vipākena pañcaśatāni samātṛkaścitāyāmāropya dhmāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 579.1]
yāvadetarhi api citāmāropya dhmāpitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 580.1]
yadvipaśyini tathāgate kārāṃ kṛtvā praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ tasya karmaṇo vipākena āḍhye mahādhane mahābhoge kule jātaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 581.1]
divyamānuṣī śrīḥ prādurbhūtā | [Divyāv, 19 582.1]
mama śāsane pravrajya sarvakleśaprahāṇādarhattvaṃ sākṣātkṛtam | [Divyāv, 19 583.1]
ahamanena vipaśyinā samyaksambuddhena sārdhaṃ samajavaḥ samabalaḥ samadhuraḥ samasāmānyaprāptaḥ śāstā ārāgito na virāgitaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 584.1]
iti hi bhikṣava ekāntakṛṣṇānāṃ karmaṇāmekāntakṛṣṇo vipāka ekāntaśuklānāmekāntaśuklo vyatimiśrāṇāṃ vyatimiśraḥ | [Divyāv, 19 585.1]
tasmāt tarhi bhikṣava ekāntakṛṣṇāni karmāṇyapāsya vyatimiśrāṇi ca ekāntaśukleṣveva karmasvābhogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [Divyāv, 19 586.1]
ityevaṃ vo bhikṣavaḥ śikṣitavyam | [Divyāv, 19 587.1]
idamavocadbhagavān | [Divyāv, 19 588.1]
āttamanasaste bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitamabhyanandan | [Divyāv, 19 589.1]
{Divyāv, 20}
evaṃ mayā śrutam | [Divyāv, 20 1.1]
ekasmin samaye bhagavāñ śrāvastyāṃ viharati sma jetavane 'nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme mahatā bhikṣusaṃghena sārdhamardhatrayodaśabhirbhikṣuśataiḥ | [Divyāv, 20 2.1]
satkṛto bhagavān gurukṛto mānitaḥ pūjito bhikṣubhirbhikṣuṇībhirupāsakairupāsikābhī rājabhī rājamātrair nānātīrthikaśramaṇabrāhmaṇacarakaparivrājakair devair nāgairyakṣairasurairgaruḍairgandharvaiḥ kinnarairmahoragaiḥ | [Divyāv, 20 3.1]
lābhī bhagavān prabhūtānāṃ praṇītānāṃ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārāṇāṃ divyānāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca | [Divyāv, 20 4.1]
taiśca bhagavān anupaliptaḥ padmamiva vāriṇā | [Divyāv, 20 5.1]
bhagavataścāyamevaṃrūpo digvidikṣu udārakalyāṇakīrtiśabdaśloko 'bhyudgata ityapi sa bhagavāṃstathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddho vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devamanuṣyāṇāṃ buddho bhagavān | [Divyāv, 20 6.1]
sa imaṃ sadevakaṃ lokaṃ samārakaṃ sabrahmakaṃ saśramaṇabrāhmaṇīṃ prajāṃ sadevamānuṣīṃ dṛṣṭa eva dharme svayamabhijñāya sākṣātkṛtvopasaṃpadya pravedayate | [Divyāv, 20 7.1]
sa dharmaṃ deśayati ādau kalyāṇaṃ madhye paryavasāne kalyāṇam | [Divyāv, 20 8.1]
svarthaṃ suvyañjanaṃ kevalaṃ paripūrṇaṃ pariśuddhaṃ paryavadātaṃ brahmacaryaṃ saṃprakāśayati | [Divyāv, 20 9.1]
tatra bhagavān bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma sacedbhikṣavaḥ sattvā jānīyurdānasya phalaṃ dānasaṃvibhāgasya ca phalavipākaṃ yathāhaṃ jānāmi dānasya phalaṃ dānasaṃvibhāgasya ca phalavipākam apīdānīm yo 'sau apaścimaḥ kavaḍaś carama ālopas tato 'pyadattvā asaṃvibhajya na paribhuñjīran sacellabheran dakṣiṇīyaṃ pratigrāhakam | [Divyāv, 20 10.1]
na caiṣāmutpannaṃ mātsaryaṃ cittaṃ paryādāya tiṣṭhet | [Divyāv, 20 11.1]
yasmāt tarhi bhikṣavaḥ sattvā na jānante dānasya phalaṃ dānasaṃvibhāgasya ca phalavipākaṃ yathāhaṃ jānāmi dānasya phalaṃ dānasaṃvibhāgasya ca phalavipākaṃ tasmāddhetor adattvā asaṃvibhajya paribhujyante āgṛhītena cetasā | [Divyāv, 20 12.1]
utpannaṃ caiṣāṃ mātsaryaṃ cittaṃ paryādāya tiṣṭhati | [Divyāv, 20 13.1]
tatkasya hetor bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo 'tīte 'dhvani rājābhūt kanakavarṇo nāma abhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ paramayā suvarṇapuṣkalatayā samanvāgataḥ | [Divyāv, 20 14.1]
rājā bhikṣavaḥ kanakavarṇa āḍhyo mahādhano mahābhogaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 15.1]
prabhūtasattvasvāpateyaḥ prabhūtavittopakaraṇaḥ prabhūtadhanadhānyahiraṇyasuvarṇamaṇimuktāvaiḍūryaśaṅkhaśilāpravālarajatajātarūpaḥ prabhūtahastyaśvagaveḍakaḥ paripūrṇakośakoṣṭhāgāraḥ | [Divyāv, 20 16.1]
rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya khalu bhikṣavaḥ kanakāvatī nāma rājadhānī babhūva pūrveṇa paścimena ca dvādaśa yojanānyāyāmena dakṣiṇenottareṇa ca sapta yojanāni ca vistāreṇa | [Divyāv, 20 17.1]
ṛddhā ca sphītā ca kṣemā ca subhikṣā ca ākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyā ca ramaṇīyā ca | [Divyāv, 20 18.1]
rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyāśītir nagarasahasrāṇyabhūvan | [Divyāv, 20 19.1]
aṣṭādaśa kulakoṭī ṛddhāni sphītāni kṣemāṇi subhikṣāṇyākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṇi | [Divyāv, 20 20.1]
saptapañcāśadgrāmakoṭya ṛddhāḥ sphītāḥ kṣemāḥ subhikṣā ramaṇīyā mahājanākīrṇamanuṣyāḥ | [Divyāv, 20 21.1]
ṣaṣṭiḥ karvaṭasahasrāṇyabhūvann ṛddhāni sphītāni kṣemāṇi subhikṣāṇyākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṇi | [Divyāv, 20 22.1]
rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyāṣṭādaśāmātyasahasrāṇy abhūvan | [Divyāv, 20 23.1]
viṃśatistrīsahasrāṇyantaḥpuramabhūt | [Divyāv, 20 24.1]
rājā bhikṣavaḥ kanakavarṇo dhārmiko babhūva | [Divyāv, 20 25.1]
dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kārayati | [Divyāv, 20 26.1]
athāpareṇa samayena rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya ekākino rahogatasya pratisaṃlīnasya evaṃ cetasi cetaḥparivitarkamudapādi yannvahaṃ sarvavaṇijo 'śulkānagulmān muñceyam | [Divyāv, 20 27.1]
sarvajāmbudvīpakān manuṣyān akārānagulmān muñceyamiti | [Divyāv, 20 28.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇo gaṇakamahāmātrāmātyadauvārikapāriṣadyān āmantrayate adyāgreṇa vo grāmaṇyaḥ sarvavaṇijo 'śulkān muñcāmi sarvajāmbudvīpakān manuṣyān akārānaśulkān muñcāmi | [Divyāv, 20 29.1]
tasyānenopāyena bahūni varṣāṇi rājyaṃ kārayato 'pareṇa samayena nakṣatraṃ viṣamībhūtaṃ dvādaśa varṣāṇi devo na varṣati | [Divyāv, 20 30.1]
atha brāhmaṇā lakṣaṇajñā naimittikā bhūmyantarikṣamantrakuśalā nakṣatraśukragrahacariteṣu tat saṃlakṣayitvā yena rājā kanakavarṇaḥ tenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 20 31.1]
upasaṃkramya rājānaṃ kanakavarṇamidamavocan yatkhalu devo jānīyān nakṣatraṃ viṣamībhūtam dvādaśa varṣāṇi devo na varṣiṣyati | [Divyāv, 20 32.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇa idamevaṃrūpaṃ nirghoṣaṃ śrutvā aśrūṇi pravartayati aho bata me jāmbudvīpakā manuṣyāḥ aho bata me jambudvīpa ṛddhaḥ sphītaḥ kṣemaḥ subhikṣo ramaṇīyo bahujanākīrṇamanuṣyo nacirādeva śūnyo bhaviṣyati rahitamanuṣyaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 33.1]
atha rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya muhūrtaṃ śocitvā etadabhavat ya ime āḍhyā mahādhanā mahābhogās te śakṣyanti yāpayitum | [Divyāv, 20 34.1]
ya ime daridrā alpadhanā alpānnapānabhogāḥ te katham yāpayiṣyanti tasyaitadabhavad yannvahaṃ jambudvīpādannādyaṃ saṃhareyaṃ sarvajāmbudvīpān sattvān gaṇayeyam | [Divyāv, 20 35.1]
atha gaṇayitvā māpayeyaṃ māpayitvā sarvagrāmanagaranigamakarvaṭarājadhānīṣvekaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ kārayeyam | [Divyāv, 20 36.1]
ekaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ kārayitvā sarvajāmbudvīpakānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ samaṃ bhaktaṃ pratyarpayeyamiti | [Divyāv, 20 37.1]
atha kanakavarṇo rājā gaṇakamahāmātrāmātyadauvārikapāriṣadyān āmantrayate gacchata yūyaṃ grāmaṇyaḥ sarvajambudvīpādannādyaṃ saṃhṛtya gaṇayata gaṇayitvā māpayata māpayitvā sarvagrāmanagaranigamakarvaṭarājadhānīṣvekaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ sthāpayata | [Divyāv, 20 38.1]
paraṃ deveti gaṇakamahāmātrāmātyadauvārikapāriṣadyā rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya pratiśrutya sarvajambudvīpādannādyaṃ gaṇayanti gaṇayitvā māpayanti māpayitvā sarvagrāmanagaranigamakarvaṭarājadhānīṣvekasmin koṣṭhāgāre sthāpayanti | [Divyāv, 20 39.1]
ekasmin koṣṭhāgāre sthāpayitvā yena rājā kanakavarṇaḥ tenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 20 40.1]
upasaṃkramya rājānaṃ kanakavarṇamidamavocad yat khalu deva jānīyāḥ sarvagrāmanagaranigamakarvaṭarājadhānīṣv annādyaṃ saṃhṛtam saṃhṛtya gaṇitam gaṇayitvā māpitam māpayitvā sarvagrāmanagaranigamarājadhānīṣvekasmin koṣṭhāgāre sthāpitaṃ yasyedānīṃ devaḥ kālaṃ manyate | [Divyāv, 20 41.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇaḥ saṃkhyāgaṇakalipikapauruṣeyānāmantrayitvā etadavocad gacchata yūyaṃ grāmaṇyaḥ sarvajāmbudvīpakān manuṣyān gaṇayata gaṇayitvā grāmaṇyaḥ sarvajāmbudvīpakānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ samaṃ bhaktaṃ prayacchata | [Divyāv, 20 42.1]
paraṃ deveti saṃkhyāgaṇakalipikapauruṣeyā rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya pratiśrutya sarvajāmbudvīpakān manuṣyān gaṇayanti saṃgaṇya rājānaṃ kanakavarṇamādau kṛtvā sarvajāmbudvīpakānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ samaṃ bhaktaṃ prajñapayanti | [Divyāv, 20 43.1]
te yāpayantyekādaśavarṣāṇi dvādaśavarṣaṃ na yāpayanti | [Divyāv, 20 44.1]
nirgato dvādaśasya varṣasyaiko māso yāvadbahavaḥ strīpuruṣadārakadārikā jighatsitāḥ pipāsitāḥ kālaṃ kurvanti | [Divyāv, 20 45.1]
tena khalu punaḥ samayena sarvajambudvīpādannādyaṃ parikṣīṇamanyatra rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyaikā mānikā bhaktasyāvaśiṣṭā | [Divyāv, 20 46.1]
tena khalu samayena anyatamaścatvāriṃśatkalpasamprasthito bodhisattva imāṃ sahālokadhātumanuprāpto babhūva | [Divyāv, 20 47.1]
adrākṣīd bodhisattvo 'nyatarasmin vanaṣaṇḍe putraṃ mātrā sārdhaṃ vipratipadyamānam | [Divyāv, 20 48.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarasyaitadabhavat kliśyanti bateme sattvāḥ saṃkliśyanti bateme sattvā yatra hi nāma asyāmeva nava māsān kukṣau uṣitvā asyā eva stanau pītvā atraiva kālaṃ kariṣyati iti | [Divyāv, 20 49.1]
alaṃ me īdṛśaiḥ sattvair adhārmikair adharmarāgaraktair mithyādṛṣṭakair viṣamalobhābhibhūtair amātṛjñair aśrāmaṇyair abrāhmaṇyair akule jyeṣṭhāpacāyakaiḥ | [Divyāv, 20 50.1]
ka utsahata īdṛśānāṃ sattvānāmarthāya bodhisattvacaryāṃ carituṃ yannvahaṃ svake kārye pratipadyeyam | [Divyāv, 20 51.1]
atha bodhisattvo yenānyataradvṛkṣamūlaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 52.1]
upasaṃkramya tasmin vṛkṣamūle niṣaṇṇaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 53.1]
paryaṅkamābhujya ṛjukāyaṃ praṇidhāya pratimukhaṃ smṛtimupasthāpya pañcasūpādānaskandheṣūdayavyayānudarśī viharati yadutedaṃ rūpam ayaṃ rūpasamudayaḥ ayaṃ rūpasyāstaṃgamaḥ iyaṃ vedanā iyaṃ saṃjñā ime saṃskārāḥ idaṃ vijñānam ayaṃ vijñānasamudayaḥ ayaṃ vijñānasyāstaṃgama iti | [Divyāv, 20 54.1]
sa evaṃ pañcasūpādānaskandheṣūdayavyayānudarśī viharannacirādeva yatkiṃcit samudayadharmakaṃ tat sarvaṃ nirodhadharmakamiti viditvā tatraiva pratyekāṃ bodhimadhigatavān | [Divyāv, 20 55.1]
atha bhagavān pratyekabuddho yathāprāptānavalokya tasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 20 56.1]
saṃsevamānasya bhavanti snehāḥ snehānvayaṃ sambhavatīha duḥkham | [Divyāv, 20 57.1]
ādīnavaṃ snehagataṃ viditvā ekaścaret khaḍgaviṣāṇakalpaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 57.2]
atha tasya bhagavataḥ pratyekabuddhasyaitadabhavad bahūnāṃ me sattvānāmarthāya duṣkarāṇi cīrṇāni na ca kasyacit sattvasya hitaṃ kṛtam | [Divyāv, 20 58.1]
kamadyāham anukampeyaṃ kasyāhamadya piṇḍapātamāhṛtya paribhuñjīya atha bhagavān pratyekabuddho divyena cakṣuṣā viśuddhenātikrāntamānuṣeṇa sarvāvantamimaṃ jambudvīpaṃ samantādanuvilokayannadrākṣīt sa bhagavān pratyekabuddhaḥ sarvajambudvīpādannādyaṃ parikṣīṇam anyatra rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyaikā mānikā bhaktasyāvaśiṣṭā | [Divyāv, 20 59.1]
tasyaitadabhavad yannvahaṃ rājānaṃ kanakavarṇamanukampeyam | [Divyāv, 20 60.1]
yannvahaṃ rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya niveśanāt piṇḍapātamapahṛtya paribhuñjīya | [Divyāv, 20 61.1]
atha bhagavān pratyekabuddhastat eva ṛddhyā vihāyasamabhyudgamya dṛśyatā kāyena śakuniriva ṛddhyā yena kanakāvatī rājadhānī tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 62.1]
tena khalu samayena rājā kanakavarṇa upariprāsādatalagato 'bhūt pañcamātrairamātyasahasraiḥ parivṛtaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 63.1]
adrākṣīdanyatamo mahāmātrastaṃ bhagavantaṃ pratyekabuddhaṃ dūrata evāgacchantam | [Divyāv, 20 64.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca punarmahāmātrānāmantrayate paśyata paśyata grāmaṇyaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 65.1]
dūrata eva lohitapakṣaḥ śakunta ihāgacchati | [Divyāv, 20 66.1]
dvitīyo mahāmātra evamāha naiṣa grāmaṇyo lohitapakṣaḥ śakuntaḥ rākṣasa eva ojohāra ihāgacchati | [Divyāv, 20 67.1]
eṣo 'smākaṃ bhakṣayiṣyati | [Divyāv, 20 68.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇa ubhābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ mukhaṃ saṃparimārjya mahāmātrānāmantrayate naiṣa grāmaṇyo lohitapakṣaḥ śakuntaḥ na ca rākṣasa ojohāraḥ | [Divyāv, 20 69.1]
ṛṣireṣo 'smākamanukampayehāgacchati | [Divyāv, 20 70.1]
atha sa bhagavān pratyekabuddho rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya prāsāde pratyaṣṭhāt | [Divyāv, 20 71.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇastaṃ bhagavantaṃ pratyekabuddhamutthāyāsanāt pratyudgamya pādau śirasā vanditvā prajñapta evāsane niṣīdayati | [Divyāv, 20 72.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇastaṃ bhagavantaṃ pratyekabuddhamidamavocat kimartham ṛṣe ihābhyāgamanaṃ bhojanārthaṃ mahārāja | [Divyāv, 20 73.1]
evamukte rājā kanakavarṇaḥ prārodīt | [Divyāv, 20 74.1]
aśrūṇi pravartayannevamāha aho me dāridryam aho dāridryaṃ yatra hi nāma jambudvīpaiśvaryādhipatyaṃ kārayitvā ekasyāpi ṛṣerasamarthaḥ piṇḍapātaṃ pratipādayitum | [Divyāv, 20 75.1]
atha yā kanakāvatyāṃ rājadhānyāmadhyuṣitā devatā sā rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya purastādgāthāṃ bhāṣate | [Divyāv, 20 76.1]
kiṃ duḥkhaṃ dāridryaṃ kiṃ duḥkhataraṃ tadeva dāridryam | [Divyāv, 20 77.1]
maraṇasamaṃ dāridryam | [Divyāv, 20 78.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇaḥ koṣṭhāgārikaṃ puruṣamāmantrayate asti bhoḥ puruṣa mama niveśane kiṃcidbhaktaṃ yadahamasya ṛṣeḥ pradāsyāmi sa evamāha yat khalu deva jānīyāḥ sarvajambudvīpādannādyaṃ parikṣīṇam anyatra devasyaikā mānikā bhaktasyāvaśiṣṭā | [Divyāv, 20 79.1]
atha rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyaitadabhavat sacet paribhuñje jīviṣye | [Divyāv, 20 80.1]
atha na paribhokṣye mariṣye | [Divyāv, 20 81.1]
tasyaitadabhavad yadi paribhokṣye yadi vā na paribhokṣye avaśyaṃ mayā kālaḥ kartavyaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 82.1]
alaṃ me jīvitena | [Divyāv, 20 83.1]
kathaṃ nāmehedṛśa ṛṣiḥ śīlavān kalyāṇadharmā mama niveśane 'dya yathādhautena pātreṇa nirgamiṣyati atha rājā kanakavarṇo gaṇakamahāmātrāmātyadauvārikapāriṣadyān saṃnipātyaivamavocad anumodata yūyaṃ grāmaṇyaḥ ayaṃ rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyāpaścima odanātisargaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 84.1]
anena kuśalamūlena sarvajāmbudvīpakānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ dāridryasamucchedaḥ syāt | [Divyāv, 20 85.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇastasya maharṣestat pātraṃ gṛhītvā ekāṃ mānikāṃ bhaktasya pātre prakṣipya ubhābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ pātraṃ gṛhītvā jānubhyāṃ nipatya tasya bhagavataḥ pratyekabuddhasya dakṣiṇe pāṇau pātraṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [Divyāv, 20 86.1]
dharmatā punarbhagavatāṃ pratyekabuddhānāṃ kāyikī dharmadeśanā na vācikī | [Divyāv, 20 87.1]
atha bhagavān pratyekabuddho rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyāntikāt piṇḍapātramādāya tat eva ṛddhyā uparivihāyasā prakrāntaḥ | [Divyāv, 20 88.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇaḥ prāñjalirbhūtvā tāvadanimiṣaṃ prekṣamāṇo 'sthāt yāvaccakṣuṣpathādatikrānta iti | [Divyāv, 20 89.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇo gaṇakamahāmātrāmātyadauvārikapāriṣadyān āmantrayate gacchata grāmaṇyaḥ svakasvakāni niveśanāni | [Divyāv, 20 90.1]
mā ihaiva prāsāde jighatsāpipāsābhyāṃ sarva eva kālaṃ kariṣyatha | [Divyāv, 20 91.1]
ta evamāhur yadā devasya śrīsaubhāgyasampadāsīt tadā vayaṃ devena sārdhaṃ krīḍatā ramatā kathaṃ punarvayamidānīṃ devaṃ paścime kāle paścime samaye parityakṣyāma iti | [Divyāv, 20 92.1]
atha rājā kanakavarṇaḥ prārodīt | [Divyāv, 20 93.1]
aśrūṇi pravartayati | [Divyāv, 20 94.1]
aśrūṇi saṃparimārjya gaṇakamahāmātrāmātyadauvārikapāriṣadyān idamavocad gacchata grāmaṇyo yathāsvakasvakāni niveśanāni | [Divyāv, 20 95.1]
mā ihaiva prāsāde jighatsāpipāsābhyāṃ sarva eva kālaṃ kariṣyatha | [Divyāv, 20 96.1]
evamuktā gaṇakamahāmātrāmātyadauvārikapāriṣadyāḥ prarudanto 'śrūṇi pravartayanto 'śrūṇi saṃparimārjya yena rājā kanakavarṇastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [Divyāv, 20 97.1]
upasaṃkramya rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasya pādau śirasā vanditvā añjaliṃ kṛtvā rājñaḥ kanakavarṇasyaitadūcuḥ kṣantavyaṃ te yadasmābhiḥ kiṃcidaparāddham | [Divyāv, 20 98.1]
adyāsmākaṃ devasyāpaścimaṃ darśanam | [Divyāv, 20 99.1]
tadyathā tena bhagavatā pratyekabuddhena sa piṇḍapātraḥ paribhuktaḥ atha tasminneva kṣaṇe samantāccatasṛṣu dikṣu catvāryabhrapaṭalāni vyutthitāni śītalāśca vāyavo vātumārabdhāḥ ye jambudvīpādaśuciṃ vyapanayanti meghāśca pravarṣayantaḥ pāṃśūñ śamayanti | [Divyāv, 20 100.1]
